jeewathweema yanu ayathana walin 
-adhyathmika ayathana 6 
--asa kana nawsaya diwa shareeraya manasa
-bahira ayathana 6
-- warna roopa, shabda roopa, gandha roopa, rasa roopa, pottabba roopa (maha butha 3k, 
----patavi (thada,mrudu,ralu,gana, sahallu bawa), 
----thejo (unusuma, seethala) 
----wayu (pimbena , hamana gathiya) walin.  
----apo (galana wagirena sukuma roopa, very sium, indriyanta danenne na) dathuwa nathuwa)

bahira ayathana wala sapa duka mukuth na
api hithana apita sapa enne bahirin. 
 for example : muhudu sulaga sapai, but api hithanawa sapa therenne  hulaga handa but eka ehema nevi
 
sapa tiyenne athule, e point e point eka thamai api study karanna oni.


sanyojana 10 (badeem) (kama lokaya ta badena widiha) kama lokaya kiyana where we are today.

we devide it to two 5 point categories
first category - oram baageeya
second category - uddam baageeya

example - 
gahak polawe tiyenne mul walin ne, oram baageeya kiyanna hariyata mula wage.
if we have heleum baloons  connected to that tree, such as uddam baageeya (always pull upwords, roopa loka , aroopa loka, divya loka)

swayan boo gyanaya ( samma sambudda, thaniyama soyaa gath nisa)

*********
dasa sanyojana (ten hindrands) hara , ithiri pawathina dharmayo, hadunnawanne , sanyoja-neeya dharma
*****
example : adaraneeya amma kiwwahama, ammata godak hithai (lengathui) kiyala.
sanyoja-neeya yanu sanyojana walata hithawath wuu dharamayooya. ( ithuru okkoma)
reason only talk about 10 is that those are the ones we focus on niwan maga.


more examples : 
roopa
wedana
sagya (signal)
sankaara (sakaskarana lada)
wynyaana (hitha)

all of above are sonyoga-neeya dharama we.

for example, there is a chair, ( its a roopa, so its a sonyoja-neeya dharma), so sanyojana sahitha manasakata, anek siyalla sanyojaneeya we.
rahathan wahanse siyalu sonyojana duru karala,  so sonyoja-neeya dharmayak nemei.
e nisa mona putuwe wadi unath, mind status eka wenas nowe.

sanyogana dharma nikan glue ekak wage, sanjo-neeya darma ape ayathana walin awith eke alenawa.

dharmaya anu monawada , kohomada meka igena ganne.

dharmaya ahanawa widihaya 
-> suthaa (ahanna)
-> dhathaa (dharnaya -mathaka tiya gannawa)
-> wachasaa parichithaa (wachanayen bawitha karanna oni)
-> manasaa upekithaa (hithin mathak karanna)
-> dhittiyaa suppati viddaa ( athma drushtiyata ahu novi, sakkaya dittiya duru wena widihata dakma ridju karanna oni)

dharmaya deshana kala widiha
->aadhi kalyanam ( mula)
-> madhya kalyanam (mada)
-> pariyo-saana kalyanam (aga) ( yahapath)

--> saathtam ( artha sathithai)
--> sabyanjanam (anu kotas sahithai)
--> kewala paripurnnam ( haath pasin paripuranam)
--> paarisuddam bhramachariyan ( pirisidu , usas hasireema )
--> prakaa sethi ( prakasha kalaa)

pruthakjana manussayek,hama tissema
aayathana 6 ta athiwena roopa walata ahuwenawa
ex:
manasata danne dhamma roopa walata ahuwenawa

(mekata ahu wenne, aththa athi satiyena ahu noweema, pirisidu sath dharmaya ahala naa.)
mekata ahu wenna serama aththai kiyala ganna eka 
deviyan sahitha lokayama me mulawe watila inne
meken gala wenna nam - dharmaya hodata , above fine points widihata ahanna oni. ( mekata oni , viirya oni)

ai rawatenne
roopa nimiththak api allanne vindeemakuth, haduna ganeemakuth, sithuwili mawillakuth, sanskaranayakuth (direction) ekka
meka mehema allala denne manasikaraya.
manasikaraya kiyanne pudgalayeku nevi, dharmathawak.
me dharmathawayen karana de, mamai hoo, pudgala widihata gannawa, ( aathma drushtiyen gannawa).

dharmathawaya --> loku galak , loku lidakata atharinawa. dennek prarthanawath karnaawa , gala paawenna kiyala, anika kiyanawa eka yatata yanna kiyala. namuth gala yata giye ai.  me dennagema balapama nisa nevi eka dharmathawayak nisa.  ( nature.)
ex:
bath kanawa - api action eka gana thamai awadaanaya karanna oni, methana action ekathamai, bath kana eka, not about the bath. bath gana hoyanawa nam, kuburata yanakan yanna wenwa, eka iwarayak na. wadak na. 


api samudaya  ( me hataganna deya / origin) kiyala kiyanne me manisikarayen allala dena gathi sobahawayata. samudaya dannawa nam nirodaya therum ganna puluwan.


api danata hoyana widiha
>>api hoyanne siyawath gananakata eha  wechcha dewal gana.
>> dharmayen katha karanne , me dan, me mohothe wena wadak thamai api atheethaya, anagathaya gana plan kaleth me mohothe mai.
>> budun dharmaya deshana karanna thrushnawa nathi karanna. me mohothe sihiyen yukthawa jeewithaya dakinne kohomada kiyana eka thamai budun sakachcha karanne.

me mohothe, 
ditta (pena / chakka ayathana), 
sutha (ahanna / sootha ayathana  ), 
mutha ( daneema, nasaya, diwa , body /ghaana ayathan,jivha ayathana, kaayaa thanaya) 
wyn-yaatha ( mana aayathana) washayen apa thula yamak samudaya wanne nam,  e pilibadawa, chanda raagaya ain kara ganna , yoniso (hoda paththa) manisikaaraya ( mana ehi karya menehi kirima) pawichchi karanna oni.
ehema kaloth niwana purna wenawa. (meke anith paththa , ayooniso manisikaraya, waradi widihata mana ehi karya meheni kirima)

yoniso manisikaaraya ( anather definition) - sihi path kala yuthu de sihi karnawa , nokala yuthu de sihi nokireema.
ayoniso manisikaaraya- vice versa.

dharmatha has 4 common features 
- anithya
- dukkai
- anathmai
- asubai

namuth, api thula wippallaasa hada gannawa,  mewa wenas aakarayata therum ganeemen. ewa thamai
nithaya, suka,aathma, subha


akusalaya - suba nimiththa (wipallaasayak) + ayoniso manasikaraya.
kusalaya - asuba nimiththa + yooniso manasikaaraya

me mohothe wana de ganamai api katha karanne - pachchuppannaya ( prathyen upan) ( dharmathawayan nisa hataganna wenas dharmathawayan  /sadena de) ( meka adyathmaka paththa wiya yuthui, bath ate kathaawa.)
asa explain karanna ba, roopaye upakarayak nathuwa.  asa ta roopayata prathyai ( supported element)
roopaya explain karanna ba asa nathuwa, so  roopaya ta asa prathyai.

asai , roopayai gana katha karanna ba, wyn-yaanaya nathuwa.
wyn-yaanaya poshana labanne asa haa roopaya athi witai.

wyn-yaanaya example : A yakadaya and B yakadaya happawana, is sound coming from A or B ?
wyn-yaanayata names 9k tiyenwa. 

ethakota apita pena dewal okkoma tiyenna nam roopai,asai, wyn-yaanayai thuna ekata pawathinna oni. - api mekata kiyana sprshaya kiyala.  ( thinnan sungathi passo) ( sprsha ayathana 6 mese saade)
me widihata anith ayathana sade,
ithuruwa mama danna oni.
sithiwili (dhamma/ aramunu) + manasa + wyn-yaanayai -> mono sammpassaya .


madu-pindika ( pani kalla) -suthraya ahanna oni. majjima nikaaya.



viirya 
- nupan akusal noipadeema pinisa, 
- upan akusal prahaanaya pinisa,
- nupan kusal ipadeema pinisa,
- upan kusal wadi diunu kirima pinisa.

niwana 
kenek, deyak, yamak, thanak , pudgalayek ahu nowana widihata thamai wada karanna oni, lokayata ahuwela inne.

hitha gaththahama karna dekak wenawa
- hithana eka 
-danaganna eka

hithe eka awasthawak
1) Sanjaanathi ( wenas wana dathu aakara nisa , different identification athiweema)
bahira deyak dakkama-
- ahata warnayak penanawa, 
( jaanaathi)== ( vija-naathi)== ( san-jaa-naathi) kiyalath hadunwanawa , 
- ahata warnayak penakota , sithe aaga,idwesha, moha  or anusaya 7 hadilath na ( so sitha pirisidui).
- meka keles mukuth nathi pirisidu awasthawak.
--- kenek bannoth , dewani parata dakkoth mathu wela ena gathi api anusa kiyala hadunnawana
- mewa (saptha anusaya)
--- kama raga anusaaya, ( pancha kaamaya pina weeme anusaya) (kama loka)
--- patiga annusaya ( gatenawa , idwesaya anusaya)
--- ditti anusaya ( dakina widihata anuwa peneema, hari widihata dakkoth hariyata penawa, waradi widihata dakkoth ehema penenawa)
--- wichikittiya anusaya ( sakayak hithunoth e widihata thamai penne)
--- maana anusaya ( manayak , wynaanaya nathi thana maanaya pamine)
--- bawa raga anusaya ( divloka wala ipadeemata kamaththa )(roopa loka, aroopa loka)
--- awijja anusaya ( chathura arya sathya gana nodanna kama)

me keles mukuth nathi pirisidu awasthawata api wipaaka awasthawa kiyala kiyanawa. ( meka rahathan wahansetath tiyenawa)

2) withak kethi 
methanin passe thamai api witharaka karanne, ( api kalpana karanne.)
-e kiyanne , kenek deyak , thanak ,kiyala innawa se aduna gaththa welawa. ( mewa witharka kiyala kiyanne)

3) panpanchethi ( me kotasaya ahu wunoth api pramada wadi, sasarata adila yanawa , thun kalaya tiyenawa bayata alenawa) ( sathiya nathu unahama thamai meka wenne, api normally kiyanne mekata asihiyen wada kireema)- [budu rajanam wahanse , appamado amathapadan, pamaado machchudo padan kiyala kiwwe methanata]

-methana thamai mama (maanaya), mage(thanhawa), mage athmaya(ditti, illution of control) kiyaa badenawa
-- tripitakaye majjima nikaahe tiyenawa.

(withakka-santhana suthraya) - balanna , for sithuwillak apuwahama
ekath ekka digatama yana eka ,
apu eka yatapath karanne kohomada kiyala.

pruthak jana - dharma awabodayak na
eya jewath wenne , tiyenawa kiyala understand karapu lokeka
gewal tiyenawa , yaluwo innawa, tiyena nathi wana swabawaya upathin pawathinawa

ex: idamak tiyenawa nam, eka mage nam, mage kiyala kiyanne thawa oppuwakin, habai e kole idamak na
ethkota mage kiyana adahasa athi wenne me lokeye tiyena dewala ekinek badena widhata api ganna handa
meka thamai api samaja sammmathaya ( smmuthiya) / sampradaya thula sathyak .
ethkota aththa baluweth - kenekuth na, thanakuth naha, eka handa aithiyakuth na

but eka nevi budun deshana kala sathya. budun deshana kale paramartha sathya.

------------------------pena-pindu-pama suthra-------------------------------------<<<<<<<<<

roopaya - pena pindayakata (like soap form)
ex: if we go to see waterwall, wathura galata waddidi athi wena pena, apita pena washayen ganna deyak na. ethana tiyenne , mohothin mohotha wenas we, sarawath bawak na nisarui. sarawath waben empty (his), sathwa
pudgala bawayen empty.

wedanawa - diya bubulak wage 
ex: meka ganna oni thani darmathawak widihata, bade wedanawa, dannise kakkuma ...(kaaya +manasa ekathu wela) ganne nathuwa thani darmathawayak lesa dakinna oni. ethkota eka sarawath bawayak na, apita oni welawata aran tiyanna use karanna ba. api hama tissema athireka dharmayak ekathu karan thamai katha karanne. but athireka dharmayak nathi unahama , methana deyak na.

sanyaa - miriguwak wage
ex: miriguwaka , wathura wage penunawa wathura, ehema naththam hoyagena gihin baluwata hambuwenne na.

sanskaaran kandaloopama-- sanskaaraya kehel kadak wage
ex: layers walin hadila tiyenne , wena wenama gaththahama ath ideyak na, aratuwak na. prayojanak karaganna 
bari gahak. ( sanskaaraka - hadala gaththa, sanjaanathi, withakkethi,papanchethi wela sankaranaya wechchi de)

me karana siyalla dana ganne winyanayen- hithe kriyawak. (roopa,wedana, sankara)
maayu-pamancha wynyaanan.
ex: genapu dekuth nathiwa, aranyana dekuth nathi mawana de. nimithi kisiwak nathiwa athi bawata maweema.
-meka normal majician karana de nevi ( its a false direction). this is not that
-irdi balayen mawana deyak wage. sanjaa walata gochara wana paata, widihata bahirin athi bawata mawanawa.

sanjaawata gochara wana pata,hadayaa apita bahirin tyiena deyak tiyenawa, innawa , thanak kiyala mawala denawa. (winyanayen)


asa + roopaya athi kalhi wynyaanaya atha. (imasmin sathi, idan hoothi) (meya athi kalhi meya we)
 asa - chakku parasadaya (opawath baya, dilisena bawa, like a glass, bahira roopa asa thulata wadda ganeeme power eka)
 ethkota chakku prasadaya athi kali , roopa atha
 wynaayaawa chakku prasadaya saha roopaya athi kali , atha.
 
 ex: if we take a cup. apita penne color, hadaya ( shape) hadala denne manasen ( color eka distribute wela tiyena outline eka penne manasata) ( sanjaanathi awasthawa)
 
 color+ shape ekak dakka kiyala, raaga,idwesha, moha  or anusaya 7 hadilath na.
 
 ex: dhaathu nanathwya nisa, synyaa nanathwaya athiwe. ( hageema, feeling/sensation)
 mati guliyakin kenek pot , ekak , huttiyak, budu roopayak, haduwama eka dakina hithata athi wena synyaawak / feeling eka wenas.
 habai thunama mati, pihitala tiyenawa widiha wena.
 anna e pihiti akaraye wena nisa- different identification tiyenawa.
 
 ethkota patisothagaami weema sadaha, kramayen arambaka awasthawata paminiya uthui. ewita bahira kiyana praknyapthi kisiwak hamu nove.
ex: roopaya penawa kiyana eka , patisothagami lesi balapuwahama, eka parakp manak wana bawa wataha gatha yuthui.
kanata nam shabdayak.
nasayata nam rasayak
diwata nam rasayak
kayata nam pahasak
sitha nam dhamma roopayak (dharmathawak)

me sansiddiya -> wyn-yaanaya athi wita meya wei. (nathi wita nohata gani)
atha saha natha yanu lokaya thula wuu dahamaki
ewa anthawadi dharshanayaki.
budun deshana kale , meya athi kal hi meya wei. ( antha dekatama nogihin)

wyn-yaanaya karana maayawa haduna gaththe nathi nisa, bahira dewal atha/natha kiyalamai gaththe.

dahama ganeema ma yanu,
me wyn-yaanaye mayaawa aduna ganna oni mai.

ex: idamak tiyenawa kiyala penawa. ( patak witharai)
sanjaa-naathi - dhaathu nanathwya nisa, synyaa nanathwaya
witharkayedi - idamak
papanchethi - mage idame, tea wawanawa, geyak hadanawa, entrace eka mehemai hadanne

mehema, 
duk godak hada gannawa ( (wipallaasayak) + ayoniso manasikaraya)
hada gaththu duka widinawa ( papanchethi eka athule karakenawa)

me hada gaththu duka , mata witharamai widawanna puluwan.
wena ayata denna ba.
ethkota sapa hoo duka hoo, ehema naththam mada bawa (upekshaawa) api ganne deyak athi / bawa nisa, lokaya athi bawa piligaththu nisa.
naththam, lokaya hada gaththe thamun mai ( meya loka samudayai)
loka nirodaya sadaha (lokoththara weemata ) api me lokaya sadune kelesa dai, nuwanin wimasa balanna oni.
me sadaha
saddawa + panyaawa tibiya uthui.

(anuththara indriya bawanawa hewath - aayathana sanwaraya)
beeja suthraya meka hodata explain karanawa
thawa magandiya kiyana deshanawath wadagath

Roopa -
Warna roopa (roopa roopa)
Ganda roopa
Rasa roopa
Shabda roopa
Pottabba roopa
Dhamma roopa


Thinking about the flower, eka roopayak (Nam + gam okkomata kiyanne roopa)

Eka kotas walata beduwoth. >>
Ethana tiyenne malaka kotas tibbata malak kiyanne na.
Api kiyanne pethi ,renu...etc
So where is the flower ?


me kotas aye Ekathu unahama , hitha athule thamai flower eka tiyenne.

Another example:

Pandama aran rotate faster -> you will see a circle
Nawaththuwahama -> pandama

E circle eka pawatinne naththam, ethana pawathinna karna kisith na.
Dakimak witharai, aththa deyak na, api circle ekak nathi thanakin
Circle ekak hoyanawa, ehema naththam nathi deyak, nathi bawa nodana , soyanawa 
E kiyanne hiss deyak, seweema, anuwana kamak mai.


e wagema thamai, kenek ipadenawa, onna eyata danawa namak, "nimal", nimal hodin jeewath wela marila yanawa, dan marunawama nimal na, body ekak tiyenawa
ipadunu hadaya nevi marila tiyenne, e unata aduna gena tiyenne namakin, 
So aththatama mulin , agin baluwahama nimal kiyala namak tibbe naththam madata nimal kenek awe kohomada.



Ex:
A usai B ta wada. ( methanin usa A)
C usai A ta wada ( dan kawda usa -> dan ethakota A kotai).
Which means there is no evidence of Usaa. so there is no physical thing called hight.
Anything relevant ( saapeksha) does not exist.
Ussa tiyenne miti tiyena kam.
(paali- imasmin sathi idhan hoathi) (meya athi kalhi meya athi wei)
This is the starting theory of pattichcha samuppaadha.
Meke anith pattha thamai, (vice versa)
Imasmin asathi, idan na hoathi → meya nathi kalhi meya hata nogani ( nathi wita hata nogani) (annuppadha nirodhaya)

Ex:
Budu charithaye kathawak tiyenawa nanda prince gana
About the Village beauty.
Budun took him to thawthisa, alone the way showed wadiriyak kalu pata and ask who is beautiful nanda said -> village beauty
Then showed thawthisa dewagana , asked again, then village beauty was like wadiri.

So lassana and awa lassana tiyenne hithe.
Ethakota meka hithe pawathina gathiyak.
So lassana ho awalassana deka tiyenne ekata hithe, 
So bahira tiyena siyaluma de athule ta gannakota oke me idwathawaya (duality) (saapeksha bawa) tiyenawa.

So 
lanweemai tiyena thana duras weemak tiyenawa,
Adara tiyena thana wyraya tiyenawa,
Tharunakama tiyena thana  mahalu kame aduwak tiyenawa

Loke hati mehamai, saama dema idwathaawayaka pawathi…!!!

Conclusion : me dekenma ain una manasa, tiyenne rahathan wahanseta…!!!

Lokaya me widihata dakinna kota , duka ho sathuta mada , nosali seetime gunaya thamai purudu karanna oni.

Me dekatama ahu noweema thamai, Arya shrawakyek widhihata karanna oni. 


Ex:

Take a certain item to the hand. → dan api kiyanawa hand eka uda item ekak tiyenawa kiyala
Now drop that item and see . → dan api kiyanne hand eka uda mukuth na kiyalane

That is wrong -> hand eka uda (mukuth na kiyana eka ) tiyenawa.
Ehema naththam, me nathi swabhawaya meke tiyenawa.

Ethkota me dekama nathi unoth ? eka apita me tiyena jana sammatha words walin wisthara karanna ba. Enam me hiss baawaya api use karana words walin withara karanna ba.
Niwana gana dana ganeeme awabhodaya, yanu, menna me withara kala nohaki de gana nuwana pawathwa ganeemai, ( enlightenment / awabhodayata pathweemai) 
Eka me lokayen ethara sobahawayak. 
Budunta wuwath baga kiyala denna witharai puluwan. Thamaa thulinma dakiya yuthui
(akkaa thaaroo thathaagathoo) 
Meka karanna prakyynaa wanthayata pamanai.
-------------------
Ex:
Api inne dream state ekaka, dreams hamadama patan ganne madin, mulak or agak nopene.
(think about the circle, when pandama karakawana kota). 
Dream ekakath mula and aga hoyanna ba…
Dream ekak kiyala danne , nagittata passe.

kulii gedara and own house. + aithiya

Meken kiyanne mala athaarinna kiyala nevi, ewa tiyena than wala tibunnaawe.
Athaarinna kiyanne aithiya (owner ship)

Ex: 
We blame the rain, because we try to own it, and hope that will work the way we want
It will never work as we want. We should always release the ownership.

Ownership eka enne watinakama handa, ownership eka atharinawa kiyanne watinakam denne nathuwa inna ekata.


Wena paththata wenna arinna. Balen wadanna yanna oni na.
Podi kenek pansale nidahase inna eka saha api balen sanwara weema, athara wenasa api own karana bond ekai, (api bond ekata badila , eka own karanwa, podda bond eka dannawa but nidasase raum gahanawa,) me bond eka athaareema , ownership eka athareemai.

Ex: amude kathawa, amude -> meeya -> cat ->cow -> kolla->girl->child
Internal problem ekata -> external solution ekak hewwa.
External solutions will always populate more problems, as they are external , which are outside our control.
ONLY solution is to give up.  ( belonging / Aithiya) ( meka duty nevi) (watinaakama athaarinna)


Nutshell : aithiya and watinakama atharinna


Ethakota wenaswana swabaawaye tiyena me lokeye hama de ganama sathutin inne kohomada.

Dewal tibbath naththath, sathutata seemawak na… ( niwana kayanne parama sukaya)
Sathuta tiyenna satisfaction eka athule, (thrupthimath weema )

Podi kale kate kadala , satis wenwa, same kate dan kaduwoth , e sathuta ada ganna ba.
Eka enne naththe ai,

Sathute, market value value eka wadi welaa. E kiyanne kate tibba salli walin sathutu karanna bari manasak hadagena ( value increase kara gena), habai me value eka ain kaloth
Labena hama deyakin ma satisfaction eka ganna puluwan.
Puluwan tharam sarala wena tharamata, sathutu wenna lesie.

Ex: kama kanakota labbichcha parippuwa , parana or nolabunu parippu walata compare karanna epa. (tea cup eka thulin parana rasa soyanna epa)
Rahathan wahanseta manik kate and boralu kate athara wenasak na.

kaamayan gen tiyena pahasa, niyama sapan widihata gannawa
ex: 
kushtayak tiyena kenek eka kahanaakota sapak athi wenawa
habai eka nathi wita e ashwadaya digatama tiyenawa kiyala eka api widala na. eka handa kaamayan gen tiyena pahasa niyamai kiyala hithenawa.

ex:
milatary man 45 days work then 7 dayas leave,
dawas 7the sapa kiyana eka eka atharinna puluwan nam , eyata 45 days ma sapai.

ex:
kamata tiyenaw sapa aleema handa, badu genna oni, badu ganna salli oni,salli walata job oni.... me okkoma me kaama handa
kama gana tiyena sapa athariyoth , ara okkoma oni na.

sakkaya dittiya ( sakkaya (pancha upadana skandaya api allan innawa dittiyen ( thanha,dhrushtiya, manna) ), naththam mama , mage , mage athmaya kiyala deyak tiyenawa kiyala gannawa.

---------eelaga session -----maaha bhuutha dhaathu ( sathara maha dhaathu)-------

panchaskandaya - naama roopa deke, ( wyn-yaanayakohatada aithi wenne) ?
--wynyaana ye definition eka (dana ganeema)
 
mama kiyanne kawda
roopya ( meterial) tika mama nevi nam
wedana ( sakas kirima) kiyana ekath mama nevi nam
wyn-yaanaya kiyana eka mama kiyala hithenawa. ( menna meka thamai athma swabaawaya) (hindu and buddhist athara difference eka thamai meka)   

kottika suthraya (maha wedalla suthraya)
roopaya + asa dekama ekatada tiyenne ?
sudu gona and kalu gona ekata lanuwakin badala ( meka thamai chanda raagaya)
me lokayen midenna nam, lanuwa kapanna oni, (chanda raagaya ain karanna oni)(kamaththa)

pana kiyanne mokadda ? pana yanawa kiyanne mokadda,
meka wenama balanna oni ekak.......  (nawa anga sasthroo sasanaya)

kes - patavi dathuwa adika roopa kalaapa hodak tiyenne.
ethakota kes -> nis sathwai (sathwayek, pudgalayak na) -> nis jeewai () -> enam hiis  


------------------------ Skanda----------------------------(pancha + iskanda)

sasarata hethuwa nathakaranna oni --> enam awidyawai thrushnawa nathi karanna oni

awidyawa - pathikada thamai
--niwarna dharmayak
--sanyojana dharmayak
--mulika dharmakyak 
--yooga dharmayak ( ooga - sada pahara , yooga yanu sada paharata thallu kirima)
--prathya wannak.

suthra pitkaya saha abhidarmaya thulin meka withara karla tiyenawa
yamkisi kenekuge dakime pathikata , 
drushti lesi hadin we.




dhrushtiya nisa thamai panchaskandaya hata ganne.

dhrushti (ditti)
- samma dittiya
---laukika ( tibena sansaraya matha hitha pina pawa matha, sapa labanne)
---lokoththara
- mithya dittiya ( maha kachchayana suthraya wisthara wenawa)
----saswatha dhrushti ( sansarayak tiyenawa bawa, methanin pass nithya wu sadakalika thanak tiyenawa kiyala)
----uthcheda dhrushti ( me saren iwarai, me idadeema pamanai kiyana eka)

drushti athi wenna hithakara than 8k tiyenawa
--skanda
--awidiyawa
--sparshaya
--sanyaawa
--witharkaya
--ayoniso manasikaraya
--papa mithra sewanaya
--paratho-goshakaya (anunge haden/ bahira shabda nisa)


skanda
======

drushtiya nikan alokaya wage ( eka athi wenne sknda matha pathitha wela)
- bahira skanda matha pathitha wela dhrushtiya athiwei ( dhrushtiyata , bahira skanda prathyayai)(e nisa skanda tibena thek dhrushtiya athi wei.)
- ex: alokaya penne apita kohe ho pathitha unoth witharai ne. pathita nowunoth, alokaya tibe but apita nopene.


- e wagema athma sahagatha sankalpaya pawatinna nam,
ekko
-roopaya , wedana, sanyaa, sankaara, wynyaana matha pathitha wenna oni (skanda)
ex:
roopaya - kalin dakapu aya thamai adath dakinne, dan asuru karanne. ( thun kalayaka athi weemak widihata dhrushti hadenawa )

enam nithaya kenek innawa kiyala , tiyeanwa kiyala, athma drushtiya athi wenna puluwan.
mehema dhrushti pawathwanna hethu une skanda dharmatha tika.
habai budun deshana kale " me skanda dharmatha wala lakshanaya thamai hata gena niruddawana bawa" ( udaya waya.)
problem eka thamai, skanda tika wenama penneth na , dhrushtiya wenama penneth na.
me dekama ekak widihata ekak penewa. enam sathwak lesa deyak hata gani.
- skanda matha patina wana thanata api kiyanawa wasthuwa kiyala
--me lokaya kiyala pennanne. onna othanata ( skanda prathya kara gena drushti pawathii)
--hoda naraka karma ras kara ganeema siduwanne menna me hada ganna lokaya matha.

ex: budun kale hitiya yamaka kiyala hamudu namak,
me kiwwa "rahathan wahanse namak piriniwan pawa nam aye upadinne na kiyala " -> meka mithya dhrushtiyak

sariuth hamuduruwo meka beakdown karanawa
-- rahathan wahanse kiyanne-roopayatada , wedanawata ,sanya..sankaara, wynaanatada ?
-- me okkoma hari ekak dekak hari da,
-- ehenam mona rahathan wahanseda upadinne naththe ?

e nisa, me skanda paha athule , pudgala bawak panawannata deyak na kiyala.
sammuthiye katha kalata panawanna ba.
ex: 
rahathan wahanse widihata drushtiya pawathwanna hethu une me iskanda panchakaya. namuth me iskanda wenama gaththoth dhrushtiyak panawanna ba.
(me wen karanna bari kama handa thamai, api rahathan wahanse wada innawa kiyala hithanne)
meka danna ganna bari me okkoma ekata ahu wena handa saha , dhrushtiyakin meka wahila inna nisa.
ethkota maranin mathu ipadeema / noopadina bawa, katha kale me dhrushtiya athule idagena

me iskanda dharamathawala nodannakama thamai athma dhrushtiya hethu wenne 
enam
-laukin samma drushtiyai
-mithaya dhrushtiyai athiwe.

ex: podi kale api walakulu wala sathuthu, plane penawa... habai ethana aththa sathek nane.
walakulu wala tibbe, aththatama ekinekata sambandayak nathi pini bindu godak 
habai, ape drushtiyen e aththa swabawaya wahala, eya danna hadayak ( athma dhrushityak) widihata ilibibu karai.

iskanda = pera nothibinemma athi wela - > ayeth sheshayak wath nathiwa niruddawana dharmathawayak (lokoththara samma dittiya) (dharmathwaya / udaya waya) dakkoth, lokayak kiyala pawathina sankalpayata thanak natiwa yanawa.

meka thamai mithaya dittiya. ( ekata hethuawa thamai, pera nothibena lesi athi wela nathi wena bawa ( samma dittiya), notherena kama)(awiddyawa)
drushtiyakin wahila nisa, meke tiyena waradi enam, drushti wena wenamath, skanda wenawena math nopeneemamai.

melesa bahirin dewal tibena bawata gena , dhrushti mata hida gena kusal kusal kala hakie. (laukin samma dittiya) namuth mehi padanama awidyawai.

iskandayan aramunu kota gena yam dhrushtiyak athi wei nam, ema dhrushtiya  bahirin penena wathsuwa nowei. ehema naththam wasthuwa dhrushtiya nevi.
ehenam melese barin penena wathuwa dhrushtiya nowana waga  or ema wasthuwa dhrushitya nowana bawa nuwanin mana kota awaboda karaweemen dhrushtiya duru wei. enam awidyawena galawe.

ex: amma lesa bahira penena wathuwa, drushtiya nevi. enam dhrushtiya wasthuwa nevi.


second part - awidyaawa ( thunkalayei dewal pawathi lesa )
=====================================================

ethkota drushiya sahitha keles tikak sovaan wethdi duru wei. ( sakkaya dittiya duru wei)(anithya de nithya bawa)(anathma de athmai kiala ganeema) duru wei.

awiddyawa nisa, 
pin paw karanwa
dhyaana wadanawa


third - sparshaya
==========================
patiga -sammpassaya ( roopaya+ ayathanaka gatena eka) - prakata wenna naama dharma tiyena kota. ( aadhi wachana sampassaya)
patiga-sampassaya -- adhiwachana sampassaya athi witama pawathi (and vice versa)

api meka gana danne nathi handa 
- api hithanne patiga sammpassaya thula idan
--- bahirin eka digatama tiyeanwa kiyala lokayak dakinne.
- ehema naththam hithanwa siyalla tiyenne hithe kiyala.

me gathi dekama waradie, so sparshaya thamai wenkirimata maruma.
mese wenne udaya waya nodanna kama handamai.

forth sanyaawa
==============
two type of sanyaa
-> ditti sanya
-> wedana sanyaa ( dharmayak, sobhawahak lesa haduna ganeemak)

sanyawa asurukota ganna dhrushti (athmai, nithya lesa ) ganeema ditti sanyaa kiyala kiyanwa.
nawatha nawatha upadawanna puluwan nam api kiyanawa eka ditti sanyaawak kiyala . ( drishtiya hethu wena sanyaa)

ex: camera reel eke, apeture eka open kapuwama phtoto wadila frame eka pichcenawa.  aye photo ganna ba.
ewa parasadayath ath iwenne wedana sanyaa. ( dharmayak, sobhawahak lesa haduna ganeemak)

methana api katha karanne dhrushi athi wena than, so wedana sanyaa ekata watenne na.

fifth withakaya (kalpana kirima)
===============

nithya sanyawata rawatila , atheethaye sita pawathila , thama pawatina bawata kalpana kirima (withakkeiya)

meka duru karanna anithya sanyawa wadanna oni. withakkayata mulika une sanyaawa. 

ex: mama leda une naththam hodai
puthata seth wewaa.. 
mewa hithenne nithya sahagatha sanyaa. ( putha kiyana sanyaawa)

in other terms ( putha kiyana sanyaawa wipareetha wena kota duka gala gena ewanawa)
enam sanyaawai witharkayai thamai in control .

ethkota sanyaawa kiyana eka niwaradi unoth ( witharkayen thora wela) awidyawata thanak nathi wenawa, enam lokoththara samma dittiyata path wenawa.


ayaoniso manasikaraya, papa mithra senawa, paratho-goshakaya
============================================================

nunuwanin (dharmayen sanndadda novi) sitina kenekuta dharmaya weshayen pawa dhrushti hata gani.

paratho-goshaya ( hoda / naraka) dekama pawathi



------------------------------

ex:


hitata dharma (sitiwili) kiyana ewa baahirai. mewa matha pathitha weemen dhrushti athi wenne. (alokaya wage)(pathitha wanne mokadda kiyana eka gochara na)
eka gochara wenne skandayak (sitiwili) tiyana thek witharai.

sithiwili (sknada) -> wathuwak kiyala  realise karanwa 

ex:
amma
hithe pawathina nithya sahagatha kalpanawa hewath athma dhrushiya lesa gaththu eka
samathsa roopa skandaya paththen penena kota eya arabaya labiya hari sapa wedanawa, bahira pawathinnak se danena kota
bahira puthgalaya hata ganeema dhrushtiya pawath weemata upakaara lesa, dharamatha 5ma hewath skanda 5ma upakaaree wei.
roopaya amma nove. warna satahanaki.
sankalpa tikath amma novei.
amma nouna dharmatha matha dhrushtiyak lesa gaththa.

dhrushtiya + wasthuwa = ekak lesa peneema , wedana ,sanyaa ...etc misak oba or mama nove.



-----------------------------------
6 ayathanama swa-yakthai (thaniyama wada karanna)
asata roopa , kanata shabda...etc
yoniso manasikaaraya - kewala darmayak nevi ( thani dharmayak nevi) (swayaktha dharmayak nevi)
e sadahaa, bahirin yamak labiya uthu mai.
e thamai niwaradi budda wachcanaya.

saththdarmaya bahirin asena kotama apita yoniso manasikaaraya upadee. -> meka dammanu damma patipadawen 

niwaradi budu dharamaya deshana karanna kalyana mitharayek pamanai.

kalyana mithra sewanaya -> sathdarmath shrawanaya -> yoniso manisaaraya -> dammanu damma patipadawa ( me karunu sampurna wena wita)
marga pala labennawa.

-------------------------------------

alife  vs dead difference

-unusuma ( temp)
-husma (aayushaa)
-wyn-yaanaya

panaa ( sawinyaanaka) ( wynaanaya sahita) (jeewitha indiya (roopa jeewitha + naama jeewithaya kotas kek tiyenawa)

gaswal (wynaanakai) ( unusuma and husma but wyn-yaana na)
sihiya awa / sihiya na ( kiyanne yamak danaganna kiyana eka)

ethkota pana aththam / sihiya aththama thamai dana gannawa kiyana eka wenne ( enam wynyaanaya pawatinne)


=========================== iskanda panchakaya ==============13/09/2020===========================

iskanda panchakayata enna kalin poddak man me mohotha gana katha karala innam


kenek marenna inna kenek , maara dwya puthrayek awith.
eya lagin pettiyak tiyenawa
meka thamai oyata aithi de,
ethkota marenna innawa kena ahanawa mage adum da kiyala.
adum -> adum nevi nool -> nool nevi pulun -> pulun gadune pulun gahen. -> gaha hadenne diya, sulan, temp, polowen thamai gaha -> gaha marila pass wenawa.

ethkota meke ko oyage adum, adum aith pasata ne.

meke inne mage naayoo da ? ( du daruwan, amma , thaththa)
oyata mathak nathi unoth mokada wenne, ethkota nayek nane da, eka nikan sankalpaya witharai da 

meke tiyenne mage idam kadam, ekathu karapu muthu manik da
geyak -> gadol, ulu, wathura , simenthi tikak -> ethkota geyak kiyala deyak tiyenna bane

ehenam mage shareeraya (body ) eka dannada genawe
meka oyage shareeraya nam -> ai meka leda wenna -> oyata aithi nam oyata kamathi widihata tiyan ganna puluwan wenna epai.
pasen sadena de pasata mai ekathu wenne. ehenam body eka aith pasata

ehenam mage mathakayada ?
oyata mathak karala sathutu wenna puluwan , habai ewa bukti widinna bane, ethkota mathakaya aith kaaalayata

ehenam mage athmayada ?
athmaya kiyana eka oyata aithi nam, oyata kamathi thanakata aran y anna puluwan wenna epai. devlowama inna puluwan wenna epai.

ehenam mata aith deyak nadda othana ?

ehema ekak tiyei, eka athaharala wena wena dewal hoyala aithi kiyala hithala tiyenawa. aithi ekama de therum gaththeth na bukthi windeth na

mokadda e aithi ekama de ?
eka thamai me mohotha, ehenam warthamana mohotha thula me siyalla puwathinawa, nirwaanaya, gala weema, wimukthiya tiyenne me mohothe witharai.
namuth memohethe kapa karala api wena ewa aithi kiyala hithanawa

ex:
patachara -> okkoma nathi wela mentally down -> dan man me mohothe mokadda karanne ?
duwa gena yanwa budun lagata , adum nathuwa pissuwen wage. ( mehe mohothe wana de nodaneema - pissu)
budun wadala
naganiyani sihiya elawa ganna (sathi-pattanaya purudu karanna oni)

ethakota sihiya kiyanne mokadatada ?

sihiya = dana ganeema. (sathiya)

meka kotas walata kadanna puluwan.
1)jaa-naathi (jaanaathi -> vijanaathi -> sanyanaathi (thama witharka wela na))
2)pajaa-naathi ( prakyawen dakinawa)
3)sanpajaa-nathi

(laukika paththen)
ex: yaluwek gamanak yanawa 
api hanawa : koheda yanne ? me answer eka jaa-naathi
next details layer : koheda, kath ekkada , mokatada  ? meka pajaa-naathi
very details layer : all the details on why he is going there ? meka sanpajaa-naathi

(lokoththara paththen)
jaanathi - dannawa kiyana eka
pajanathi - prakyawen dakinawa
sanpajaanaathi - niwan awabodaya sadaha siyalu de wala ekathuwak lesa dakinawa (jaanathi to pajanaathi entire collection)(danna, dakina kena)

ethkota sihiyen me okkoma dana gannawata api kiyanawa (sathi sampajaa-naathi)

ethakode patachara ta kiwwe sihiya elawa ganna kiyala , enam ( me mohotha dana ganna )
1) patachara ge family members marune dan nevie, ( atheethaye , me mohothe nevi)
e kiyanne wela iwarai , wenas karann ba
anaagathaya thama awith na, me mohothe deyak nevi
api atheethaya and anagathaya gana hithanne me mohothe
ethkota una de nisa anagathaya gana baya hithenneth me mohothe.
ethkota atheetha and anagathaya gana hithanneth me mohothe.

ethkota me mohothe kisi problem ekak na , patachara budun diha balan innawa
ethkota duk wena ekai pasu thawili wena ekai nawathwala , me mohothata awa.
enam patachara , sathya awaboda kala.
me mohotha thula kisi prashnayak na nathi bawa awaboda kara gaththa.

ekata udaw kale , sihiya.
enam apith sihiya thulin me mohothe awabodaya laba ganna oni.
me awabodaya labanna punchi dekin puluwan. 
me mohothe innawa nam troubles mukuth na.

ex:
pansalata bawana karanna giyama ,
hamuduro yawanawa , uda maluwata gadol 1000k adinna.

-> dan onna widiwanawa , api awe bawan karanna habai dan gadol adinnalu
-> thawa set ekak, gala gala ganan kara kara , galen galata widawanawa.

habai baawana karanna sihiya purudu karanna , ethkota me gal tika me mohothe sihin adinna puluwan ne
enam me mohothe tiyenne eka galai ne, ethkota me mohothe adinne eka galai. 
aththeethaya adda gala balala adu nam athi duka hithanawa , wadinam anagathaye gal adina eka lesi wenna 

me mohothe inna sihiya gana wishwasaya tiyanna oni.

jiwithe, mo mohothe thula gatha karana wa nam , me mohothata kapa karanawa nam, samada sathuten inna hakiya.

ethkota me mohotha thula api sihiyen sitinawa nam, atheetha , anagatha sithuwili api athara man wenne na,
mehema unahama apita kisiyam wuu aramunak gana wiwida pathikada osse balanna awasthawa habuwenaw

ethakota , yam kisi deyak gana wiwida pathikada walin balanna puluwan.
eka konekin eka widihata dakkinne
thawa konakein wena widihata ,

melesa wiwida pathikada walin balana wihata api widarshanawa kyiala kiyanawa.

ex: bath atayak aragena mulu lokayak mawanna puluwan.

dan api meka hithe tiyagena , panchaskandaya balamu.

abhisamaya sanyuththya  (baguru dhamma / pattichcha sammupada) --> dukka suthraya
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------


api duk widinne nosalakilla nisa, sakillak tibboth duk widinne nathuwa inna puluwan.

jethawanaramaye, sawath nuwata , dhamma mandapaye deshana kala.

prakna jathi 3 (wisdom)
- suthamaya ( ahala dana ganna danuma) ( bahirin udawwak oni mai)
- chittamaya praknaa (sitha wadidiunu kareema)
- bhawanamaya praknaa ( jeewitha abyasayak thula purudu karana lada)

kohomada duka hata gannane ( dukka samudaya)

passa  (thinnam sangathi passo/isparshaya (ekathuwa)) pachchaya wedanaa (aramuna pariharanaya kirima)(ex: roopaya pariharanaya kirima asen.)(ex: lecture ekaka lecturer to amatharawa, thawa admin jobs tiyenawane, ethkota lecture eka pawatinna nam lecture + admin stuff + work flow...) 
wedana pachchara thanhaa 

aryyan ge awabhodaya sanada, suwishesha sathya 4k deshana kala ( chaturarya sathya)
duka -> samudaya -> nirodaya -> maargaya

hethu pala niyaayata anuwa,

duka yanu yamaka prathipalayak (jaathi pi dukka, jara-pi dukka..etc)
-ipadeema , leda weema, wayasata yaama, maranaya  mewa duka

ethkota ipadeema namathi duka hata ganne ai ? 
dukata hethuwa thanhaawa, yali ipadeemata tibu kamaththa
kamaththak naththam iapadeemak na.

ex:
married couple after 5/6 years . no lamai.
me denna lamaita kamathie, namuth kusata enna kamathi kenek naththam enne na.

ethkota there are poeple who doesnt try or not married, doesnt want children
but get pregnant -> ethkota amma thaththa kamathi na, but ena kena kamathie.

ethkota upadeemata athi (jaathiya athi kamaththa hewath thanhaawa )kamaththa tiyenne upadina kena matha.
me jathi thanhawa thamai hethuwa , maw kusta enna 
e hethuwa nathi karanna eka puluwan maarga sathyen witharai. ( arya ashtangika margaya, mulin athi una jathi thanhawa (naththam hethuwa) nasanawa)


niwana namathi palayata, hethuwa thamai marga sathya . namuth marga sathyen nasuwe dukata hethuwa wana thanhawa. (dukka nirodaya)
duka niroda karapuwahama , aye hata ganeemak na, 
namuth niwana kiyana eka hethu palayak nevi. ( namuth sammuthiya thula niwana , hethu palayak lese dakinne , namuth niwana asankatha dhammayaki)

enam sathwaya duk wideema kiyana kriyawa wanne , hethu pala dahamaka kriyawa nisai.

ex: asthrutha ( dhamma asa nathi) pruthak jana kenek, mama kiya kenek pawathwa ganeema
musical function ekak gahththoth, annoucer kenek , voice controller , engineerin kenek , sound system ... so many functions tiyenwane
individual systems do their work to seperatly to get the final out put ekata.
eliye idan balana kena musical function ekak misak ekinekata sambanda nathi groups tikaka ekathuwak lesa dakinne nane.

anna e wage , ape me wena kirawaliya, api ekkenek kiyala gannawa, ayathana 6n wena wenama wada kalata , ekak lesa gannawa.

ethkota me anunge deyak, mama or mage lesa dakinawa. 
mage nowana deyak, mage kiyala thanha upaddawanawa.
e ayathana 6 , mage kiyala thanha upaddanawa.
menna me mage nowana dewal mage karaganeema nisa, duke hethuwa thanhaawa upadinawa
thanhawa upadinawa wita duka hata gannawa.
duka hata sasarata aleema patan gannawa.

pancha+skandaya hata gannawa


aththa athi satiyena nogena, badeemak hata ganeema ( thanhawa) duka athi karanawa
naththama nuwana nathi kenak thanhawen badila tiyenne hama witama
enam me anithya bawa nodanna nisa, mulaawa thula alenawa

anunge deyak ganeema yanu (horakamak) enam waraddak, waraddakata daduwamak tiyenawa. enam nirwanaya block karanawa enam sasaratama badenawa
nuwana thanhawen wahenawa.

badeema mul karagena dirga kaleenawa duk widinawa ( duka upawa gannawa)

ex : passa pachchaya wedana kiwwawata , methana wedanawa athule hugak components tiyenawa . me wedanawa thani ekak nevi.

eka roopayak balala thawa ekak balanawa, ethkota issella balapu eka tiyenawada ?
eka na , roopaye anithya thawaya e widihatath therum gatha hakiya.
e roopaya aye dakithdi , ekamai kiyala hithanawa ( nithya widihata gannawa / wipallaasayak)
issella balapu de nevi dan tiyenne aluth ekak kiyala nuwanin menehi karapu wahama , anithya awaboda wenawa
anithya awabodaya nisa , nithya sanyawen hata ganna thanhawa niroda wenawa

ex: 
lassana kellek ge pinthurayak gannawa, aye aye balanna kiyala laptop eke save karanawa. aye open karala aye balanawa.
eka anithya une naththe ai ?
> me photo eke tiyena eka nithya widihata dakinawa, balana balana hamasarema penne ekamai (nithya kyiala gannawa)
> asa tiyena kan roopa penawa wage, mana tiyenakan sithiwili pahala wei. ( eka karma wipakayak) ( mathak weema yanu peneema, aseema , wage ekak)
> ethkota me pinthuraya dakima thula sithuwili pahala wei. ( meya ape palanayen thorai. (anathmai) )
> eethkota peneema wenas karanna ba, habai hithana eka wenas karanna puluwan. (meka mathakaya nevi)


> peneema apita oni walakwanna ba ( palanaya karannath ba) ( asa+ alokaya tiyenawa nam penawa)
> apita aithi nam , mata oni widihata palanaya karanna puluwan wenna oni
> ehenam katha roopa mata penna epa kiwwoth ewa nopenee tiyenna oni, ehema na , e kiyanne mata aithi na.

sihi nuwana nathi hamathanama
aramunu pariharanaya (wedana pariharanaya) - thanha badimen duk widinawa.

pancha skandaya kotas 2i
---------------------------
drushti athi wenna hethu 8k katha kala  ( iskanda + awiddaya +passa +sanyaa + withakka + ayoniso+ paratho goshaya + paapa mithra )

paramartha dharma-4
sith- 89 ( laukika 81 , lokoththara 8)
chythasika 52, 
roopa 28
niwana 

lokaya = sith 81 + chythasika 52 + roopa 28
chythasika 52 ( 1 wedana + 1 sanyaa + 50 sankaara)
onima sithaka ( 7 sankaara ( meka sabba chichcha sankaara)) (passa, wedana, sanyaa, chathana, manasikara , ekakgratha , jiwitha indriya)
abidharmaye & suthra pitakaye roopa explain karana widi dekak tiyenawa.

1) roopa wedana sanyaa sankaara wyn-yaana (suthra pitakaye)
2) passa wedana sanyaa chethana manasi-kaara (abidharmaye anuwa)(pattichcha samuthpadaya)

-----1-----------------------------------------
 
roopa ( shuddashtakayaki , dirana bawa)
- asa - warnaya
- kana - shabdayak
- diwa - rasa
- kaya - pahasa
- molaya - sithuwili

wedana ( kamaththa akamaththa, upekshawa)
sanyaa ( lakunu kireema)
sankaara ( sakas kirima/ ras kirima)
- pin paw
- kusala akusala
- kaaya, wachi, mano sankara
wynaanaya ( dana ganeema)
- lokaya thula dewal dana ganeema.

me pahen 1k ho 4k ho 5k me wishwaye onima thanaka pawathi. (asannya thayale roopaya witharai(1k),aroopa thala naama skanda 4k witharai tiyenne (wedana, sanya, sankaa , wynaana ), kama loka wala 5ma tibe )

roopa iskanda - asa ,roopa (bahira dewal + ayathanaya) (sathara maha dhathu walin athi wei)
nama isknada - hithe athiwena ewa 
-------------------------------------------------

ex: asa ha roopa, dekama roopa wei
megana tiyena kamaththa akamaththa wedanawa nam wei
asa haa roopa pilibada lakunu/ satahan walata kiyanne sanyaa  
peneema kiyala , sitha sakase nam ( ekata kiyanawa chiththa sankaara kiyala)
penuna kiyala haduna ganne wynaanayen
ehenam peneema mul karagena pancha iskandayak haduna.
enam panchaskandaya yanu body eka nowa hithata namak. (chiththena neeyathi loke, chiththena parikappathi)
enam peneema kiyanne sithak.

sitha kiyanne , aramunak mulika kara gena pahala wanna wuu panchaskandaya ki.

ex: 6inch usa body ekakata , pana athnam, mata lowa penwai.
pana tiyennama oni lokaya penwanna.
pana tiyenawa kiyanne sithak tiyenawa kiyana eka enam pancha iskandayak tiyeanwa kiyana eka.
pana tiyenna oni sithen penwana nisai.

pana tibe nam sitha atha, sitha tibe nam wishwaya atha, (bahira gana dan ganeemak pawathee)

question : sammuthiya athule (ekama) lokaya 6 thanaka pahala wenawa. poduwe sitha kiyanawa.
panchaskandaya | lokaya | siyalla pawathee kiyanawa.

asa -> lokayai
diwa -> lokayai ....etc

panchaskandaya pawathinawa nam pana pawathinawa , enam sitha pawathinawa , me lokaya pawathinaya
(kaayena sanwaraya saadhu
saadhu waachaaya sanwaroo
mansaa sanwaroo sadhu
saadhu sabbathth sanwaroo) (kaya wachara , manasa sanwara nam mulu lokayama sanwara una wei)
ex: as deka wahuwahama lokeyen tikak ain wei, shabda naththam tikak ain wei

ex:
athak isseema karanna puluwan sithak nathuwa.
awidinna puluwan da sithak nathuwa.
ethkota kriyawa yanu sithak. ehema naththam lokayak, panchakayak

ex:
muna kapuna, atha puna,... kana kapanawa kiwwoth adenne sithak.
me sitha hadenne awiddyaawa hinda.
meka niroda karagannai oni.
me karanna nam hama sithakatama (panchaskandaya) aithiya pawara noganna oni 
muna kapuna , methana  mage muna thamai kapune - eka mage muna kiyala gannawa.

------------------------------2---------------------------------

passa wedana sanyaa chethana manasi-kaara

ex:
pol aththe aratuwa ( bidange) wage me chethanawa. waten iratu hai wenawa wage awashya chythasika (sithuwili) ekathu karannawa

kusala / akusala chethana - anuwa chythasika pahala wenawa.
(chethana nam bikkawe, kammain wadami)- chethanawa karmayai.


suthra pitakaye. mona suthrayada?  ( beeja suthraya)
mahaa nidana suthraya

---------------------------------------20/09/2020------------------------
questions to ask from friends ?
1) penne kohadata
2) pihihe muwahathakin e muwahatha kapanna puluwan da
3) ahata aha penawada


kohomada panchaskandaya hithak une ?  මහා හත්ති පදොපම සු thtraya
-------------------------------------------
hitha kiyanne mokadda saha hithe gathi aduna ganna oni

ex:
aliya 4000kg
mama 120kg 
namuth mama awidina kota mata mawa ni-barai, e wagemai aliyatath ?  ethkota apita awidina wita me bara nodanee, sahalluwen yanawa 
ai ei ?

me hithe gathiya, kayen pennanna puluwan

ex: minihek tharaha giyahama, rathu wenawa ( specially you can see on fair skin), 
e wagema sthrii , purusha bawath hithe gathiyak...
hitha swabahawaya gathin pennanna puluwan.

lingika awayawaya ( uthuja roopayak) ( karamaya, hitha, aahara, uthuja (kalaguna, wenaswanasulu swabawika) wihata roopa janitha we, ) me awagayawa, hithe gathiya
handa thamai gahanu pirimi wenne (me hithe gathiya sukuma roopayak (16types), asata nopene)

thawa roopa (okkoma 28) 3k ( lahutha (sahallu bawa), mudutha (mrudu bawa), kammannyatha ( oppersite of akarmanytha/ability of action), hugak welawata hithe balapaama nisa ihata roopa upadina widi 4 walin hata gane.

meeta amatharama , hithenma upadina roopa dekai, (ekaantha chiththaja roopa)
-kaaya wynyaththi (hagaweema)
-wachee wynyaththi
 
ethkota me bara sahallu kiyala therenne , hadena lahutha roopaya nisa.
lahutha roopaya hadenne hithe , eka hithe gathiyak.
kaya pawaththwanna ( ehema naththamam kunu wenne nathuwa pawthwanne) - aahara walin, hitha hadenne ( karmaya nisa, thanhawa nisa, awidyawa nisa)
hithata geyak thamai kaya. ( mata oni wihata me gedara pawathwa ganie, ) mama naththam, me gedara pawathmak na.
me body ekath mohothen mohotha wenas wenawa, kawadawath isthirawa tiyenne na.
isthirawa tiyena ekama de thamai wenas weema.

ex: katta karuwalaka, aatha gini dallak penawa.
e eliya penne ahata, hithenne kawruhari innawa kiyala ( dakkada ?)
ethkota ahata penune eliya + hithen hithuwe (kenek kiyala)
ethkota ayathana dekak ekathu unu swabawayen, eliye kenek athi bawa hithuwa. (dhrushti + wasthuwa)
habai elie me ekekwath na.
enam outside nathi hama ekakma api hithin hadapuwa.

ex:
ahata penne warnaya ne
ahata thamai okkoma roopa penne ? ethkota aha penne kohatada ?
kannadiyakin balapuwa pena ahada ?, kannadiyen penneth roopayak nam aththa aha koheda tiyenne ? ehenam eka penne kokatada ? aththatama aha mokadda koheda tiyenne.
kannadiyen penne boru ahak nam(reflection ekak nam)(roopayak nam), eken pena roopayath ahak nevi. 
enam ahata kawadawath aha penne na ( ani+dassanai) ,aha penne hithata.
me eliye tiyenne aha kiyala hithapu upakarayak witharai.
pena nisa aha tiyenawai kiwwata, aththa peneema tiyenne hithe.

ex: gold walin haduwa nam ranmuwa, ridee nam rideemaya.... wage namak denawa
ekenma hadala nam(raththaranin ma hadapu nisa) - ran-maya
ridiyen hadapu nisa - rideemaya
manasin hadapu nisa - mano+ maya kiyala kiyanawa
ethkota manomaya lesa hadapuwa wenne hithe, hithen hadapuwa, mewa eliye na. eliye bauthika lesa pawathina lesa ganna nuwana mada kama hinda (moda kama nisa)

melesa eliya + athula kiyala (adyathmaya+bahira) kiyala deyak , kenek, thanak tiyenawa innawa kiyala pennuwe wynyaanaya.

ethkota sammuthiye api hithanne
bahirin lokya tiyenawa , tiyena lokaya apita penawa , penne mata kiyala hithenawa
pene loke aththa, ( sakkaya dittiya athi wenne mehemai)

ex:
mama putuwak dakinawa, putuwa dakapu mama thamai biththiya dakkinne, eyama thamai ahasa dakinne
ethkota mama kiyana eka auto register wenawa ( mamath waya) (manyanaa karanawam, oyata 'manyyannda' kiyala ahanne) (mannyethi)(manasen hithanawa)
sowan to rahath margaya dakwa ( ma.. manyathi)(aathwela)
rahathan wahanse (n..manyathi)(ain karala)


ex:
hithen hithuwa rosa malak. 
mewage rosa malak mage, ahawal yaluwaage mal waththe.
apo egollonge amma kamathi na denna kamathi na kiyala hithenawane.
ethkota 
budunta puja karanna kamathie
but illanna kamathie ( hambena eka sure nathi handa)
ethkota hithe amuthu duka swabawayak ( idweshayak) enne.
me welawe mama maloth tharaha sithakin thamai marenne.
enam apaye.

api remote katha karanwa ( kalayakuth na , dura durakuth na), oni welawaka connect wenna puluwan.
e wage me hithata karmaya thulin thawa roopayak allagannawa.
ethkota menna me allaganna ekata kiyanawa upadanaya kiyala. habai eka allagaththe me mohothe me sitha athule.
starting pointing eke sitha hatagaththu swabawaya anuwa thamai hithe allagaththu roopya iwara wenne.




anithya example.

ex: pahanak ude idan hawas wena kan paththu una kiyala kiyanawa.
ethana tibbe dallai,thel,tire emohethe thel bunduwak enawa dawenawa yanawa.
aye binduwak enawa dalwenawa yanawa.
meka hugak wegayen wenawa.


ex: wassa , wahapu wassak gana kiyala , paya dekak widihata hodatama wassa.
palaweni binduwa athi una ( polawata wathuna nathi una)
dewani eka binduwa  (polawata nathi una)
ethkota eka binduwak wath paya dekak tibune na
ethkota mokadda wassa kiyala paya dekak tibune.
ehema ekak tibila na.
ethkota wahi binduwala ( dhathu maathrayak) wenas weeme swabayakak, kriyakarithwak pamanayai, enam pugalayek, sathwayek, kenek , deyak , thanak lesa natha.
kriyawaliyak pamani.
wassa ho wassa nathi kama mawwe wynyaanayen ( me sapeksha bawaya)
me sama sapeksha lokayama pawathinne api wyn-yaana mayawata ahuwela inna handa.


ethkota panchan skanadaya kiyanne mokadda  ?

roopayada ?  (asa + bahira roopaya) eka witharak nevi. kama lokaye api roopen thamai wedanawa enawa kiyala hithanne.
amma thaththa leda una hama apita wedanawak enwa, etha roopaya thula pawathina ekak nevi.  bahira roopaya handa wedanawa awaa nevi , eka hithe upadipu gathiyak.
samaru sambola and bath walata asai, 
pita tiyenawa kota rasa danunne na, enam athulata apuhama thamai rasa dannenne.

roopayata ho wedanawata , panchaskandaya nove.
sanyyawa gaththahama ,
ammage paata , hadaruwa adunawa ganne roopa sanyyawen, namuth sanyyawa witharak handa panchaskandaya hata gannene na.
sankara,
amma hari hodai, mata podi kale idan salakuwa, ithin math salakanna oni , mekath hithe athiwena gathiyak, barira roopaye na
wynaanaya,
amma innawa kiwwe hithen, dana gaththe hithen , eliye roopaye na. 

me okkoma tika tibbe mano+maya roopayakata , ekath eliye na, eka bahira bawthikaya nevi

ema nisa roopaya manomayai, enam panchaskandaya sithaki.
enam panchaskandaya yanu dukaki.
panchaskandaya nisa lokaya atha, enam duka atha. 
panchaskandaya = sitha = lokaya = duka.

panchaskanaya == pancha upadana skandayata ?

upa ~ sameepa ( upa sabapathi , upa kulapathi) (mohoma lagata inna kena)
adaana ~ adinadanaa ( dunne nathi) adhana ( gaththa) > nudun de gaththa gaththa, ethkota 'dana' yanu denawa. 'adana' yanu gannawa kiyan eka  

upa+adana - lagata gannawa (allagannawa)

panchaskanaya manomayai. mohothak wath nopawathi,  nodanna kama nisa
kama loke api , panchaskandaya thulin sathuta hoyanawa . e nisa thanhawen (assawen) badenawa , enisa thadin alla gannawa
enisa sasara yanawa. ( e taste ekama hoyagena yanawa , enam upadana hoya gena yanawa). e gathiya hoyagena yanawa. enam sasara yanawa.

e gathiya maintain karanna nam, yalin me asa, kana, nasaya oni wenawa , e nisa eelaga bawayedi me isknada pahala wenawa ( iskandaandan paathubawoo, ayathanaanam patilaabo)
(ayan wuchchathi jaathi) -jathiya (sasara athi wei) -> duka -> nirodaya sadaha upadanaya nokara yuthuya. (upadana pachchaya bawa, bawa pachchaya jaathi)

enam sasara kiyanneth tiyena ekak nevi, mokada isthira tiyenawa nam nawathwanna bane. sakas wana ekak. upadanaya tiyena thak kal tiyena ekak. me hama bohothakma pawathinne sasare. sitha karamayen badi wenas wemin yana dharma thawayaki. namuth sithak kiyanne nopawathina ekak ( e nisa niwan dakinna puluwan.)


(dharmaya haduna ganeemata ,eya dharma winayata galapiya yuthui)- (sabbaashrawa suthra)
-chathurraya sathya + patichcha samuppadayata galapa baliya
-ahana kenage raga idwesha moha mathu nowiya yuthui. (aashrawa heena wenna oni)


ethkota kohomada meka chathurraya sathya + patichcha samuppadayata galapa baliya yuthui 

chathur + araya sathya
duka -> duka manasika or shaareerika danena deyak novei. 'anithya nodaneemama duka.' , duka yanu deyak, yamak, kenek, thank tiyenawa innawa kiyala piliganeema thamai duka
dukka smudaya -> thanhawa. aththa athi satiyen nodanna kama nisa, penena lokaya aththa washayen piliganeema (awidyawa) nisa aleema. thahawa thamai morala upadana bawata path wenne.
dukka niroda -> nirwanaya. sithak yanu isthira lesa nopawathina dharmathawak bawa nuwanin awabodha kara ganeema (lahu pariwarthanaya) (wegayen wenas wena)
dukka niroda gaameeni patipada -> lokoththara arya ashtangika margaya ( aththa athi satiyen dana ganeema hewath samma dittiya samaga ithuru anga 7)

pattichcha samupannaya

imasmin sathi , idan hothi ( meya athi kalhi meya wei) panchaskanada tibe nam duka atha.
imasmin asathi idan nahothi (meya nathi kalhi meya hata nogani)  panchaskandaya nathi bawa therum giya wita nawatha hata nogayee ( annuppada nirodaya)


athi deyak nathi weema nowa.
athi bawa nathi weema nowa.
athi wana bawa nathiweemai niwana. ( anu (nawatha nathawa)+ uppada nirodaya)(nohata ganna bawa)

--------------------------------24/09/2020---------------------------------------------------------------------

for waradi drushtiya

kenek , deyak, thanak, pudgalyek innawa kiyala gannawa.
eka thamai me sakkaya dittiye hati.

eliya/athula - depaththa pennuwe wynaaneyen.
meka thripitakaye tiyenawa mayawak kiyala .
namuth lokaya aluthe api meka ahttha kiyala aran.


ex:
Apita hithenaවා නේ ඇස කන නාසය දිව සරිරය දරා ගෙන පුංචි දරැවෙක් ලොකෙට ඉපදිලා කියලා
පොඩිදරැවා එහෙම හිතන්නෙනැහැ  දරැවගෙ එහෙම කිසිවක් නැහැ.පලමු සිත පහල වුනා.ඒ සිතේ මොකක් පහල වනවා ඇත්ද?
සිතක් පහල වුන බව දන්නෙ හිතෙන්මයි.සිතෙන් සිත දැන ගත්තා හැර වෙන වචනයක් කියන්න බැහැ.
සිත ඇති කල්හිම මන දමිම මෙික තමයි පටිචිච සමුප්පාදය කිවෙි.
ඉමස්මිං සති ඉදං හොති.
මෙිකම තමයි හේthun පටිචිච සමිබුතං හේ බංගා නිරජ්ති කියලා
හේthu banga nirujjathi kiyala
සිත සකස් වුනේ කොහොමදමන දමිම ඇති කල්හි සිත සකස්වෙනවා viceversa.

Api දුක නැති කරන්න උත්සහ කරනවා.ඒ උනාට දුක කෙලවර කරන්න කාටවත් බැහැ.මෙි නිසයි පහල මධ්‍යම ධනපති කියල පංති භේදය.මෙි නිසා 10අක,සල් පංචනිරණ වලි සිත මැඩගත්ත නිසා ධර්මය වටහගන්න අසිරැයි.මහ වනයක් මැද තනිව සිටියත් නිදහස් උනාට 
අනෙක් පන්සල් වල ඉන්න
අය සමග සංසංදනය කරල  ඒ සැහැල්ලුව තියෙන්නෙ මට කියල දිටිඨි ගත වෙනවා සතර සත්‍ය අවබෝධ නොවෙි.

එහෙනමි සියලුම පැනවිමි කලේ හිතෙන්මයි
ඇස පනවගත්තෙත් හිතෙන්මයි.
පෙනිම ගොඩනංවලා තියෙන්නෙත් හිතමයි
තණ්හාවත් සිතින්මි.
මෙි අනුව පෙනිම ඇති කල්හිමයි ඇස රැප පැනවෙන්නෙ.
පෙනිම ඇහිම දැනිම දැනගැනිම ඇතිකල්හිමයි ආයතන 06 ම.
ඇහැට පතිත වනවිට කයන්නෙ රැප සංgnawa කියල.ඒකම මනස පැත්තෙන් අරමුණු වෙන විට රැපසංචෙිතනා කියනවා.
ඔය විිදිහටම ශබිද සංචෙිතනා ගන්ධසංචෙිතනා ගාණසංචෙිතනා රසසංචෙිතනා පොටිඨභ්බසංචෙිතනා  ධමිමසංචෙිතනා කියල ආයතන 06 මෙන්න මෙි හයම ගන්න පිලිවන් හැකියාව තියෙන්නෙ මනසටයි එතකොට  කියන්නෙ මනෝසංචෙිතනා කියලා.

අපේමතකය මුලුමනින්ම  erase වුනොත් මොනවහරි දැනගැනිමක් එන්නෙ මනසටයි.ඔන්න ඒකත් erase වෙල.ආයිත් හැගිමක් එනවා erase වෙනවා.ඔන්න ඔය phynomina එක තමයි ැම මොහොතකම ඇත්ත .
මොකවත් ගන්න දෙයක් නැහැ හිස්.
ඔිකට තමයි පචිචුප්පන්න කියල කියන්නෙ.ඔන්න ඔතන අපට නතර වන්න බැහැ.මොනවහරි තියෙන්නම ඔිනෙ
ඒ නිසා හැම මොහොතම මුලාවකිහ් වැහිල.ඉතින් කොහොමද ධර්මය තේරෙන්නෙ.
සියලුම ගැටළු මෙි නිසයි නිවනක හුළගක්වත් නැහැමයි

ඔයා ඇස් වහගෙන ඉන්න වෙලාවක හුනෙක් සද්දකරනවා ඇහුණා කියන්නකො.ඹන්න ඔතන සිහියවත් නුවනවත් පිහිටල නැහැ.
එළයෙ හුනෙක් ඉන්නවා කියලා පිළිඅරගත්තනෙ
ඇත්තටම එළි ඉන්න එකා කියල drowing කරල පෙන්නන්නත් පිළිවන්.
ඉතින් ඔයා ඇස්වහගත්තනෙ. කොහොමද එළියෙ කියන්නෙ.
ඇත්ත කඵාව ඒක සිතේම නිර්මාණයක්.පරණ පුරැද්දට එළියෙ කියලා පිළිගත්තෙ.
ඔයා මෙි විධිහට නමි බලන්නෙ ඒකට කියනවා රැපඋපාදාානස්කන්ධය කියලා
හුනගෙ ශරිරය හැදුන  කොටස් බලල නැතිනමි සතරමහ ධාතැවිදිහට බලල සොයන විදිහ බාහිර බැලිමක්. මෙිකත් උවමනයි.
බුදුරජාණන්වහන්සේ පෙන්නුවෙ තමා තලින් බලන්න කියලනෙ.
භාහිරින් බැලිමට කියනවා පුර්ව ප්රතිපදාාව කියලා.  ඒකෙන් නිවරණ යටපත්වෙනවා.ඇතිවනවා නැතිවනවා කියලා වෙනස් වනවා කියලා හිතෙන කොට ඇලිම ගැටිම අඩුවෙනවා.ඒක ලෝකය ඇතලේ කෙරෙන එකක්.
ලෝකොත්තර දහම තේරැමිගැනිමට නමි
බුද්ධචද්සනාවට එකගවන්නඋවමනයි.තමන් තලින් දකින්න උවමනවි

ethkota gaththe eliye tibba deyakda, naththam parana puruddak hinda hithe hada gaththu ( mano+maya) swaroopayak, baahira dhathu wenas weemak nisa aththa kiyala gannawa.

mehema aththatama nathi deyak tiyenawa kiyala ganna eka, api puruddata karana deyak neda, meka moda kamak neda , ekathamai awiddayawa kiyanne.
enam aththa nodanna kama.

me anithya bawa dakala na. sanya wipallaasayak wela.

another way.

mayakarayek kotiyek mawanawa, kotiyai mayakarayai wen karanna puluwan da ?
eka kawadawath karanna ba.
mawanawa kiyala kiwwa gaman api hithanawa aththa deyak mawwe kiyala.
namuth eka aththa nevi
mayaakaraya innakan thamai kotiya inne.
mayakaraya nathi nam kotiya mawanna ba. ( driver wenna car eka tiyenna epai)
ethkota mayakaraya and kotiya dennek kiyala ganna ba. me denna wen karanna ba . ( imasmin sathi , idan hothi)
kotiya inna nam mayakaraya innama oni.

ethanata thamai api kotu wela inne , api rawatila inne.

another way.

as deka wahaganna , dan mokada wenne. ? ethkota penne na kiyala kiyai.
namuth penne nathi as deka tiyenawa ne.
as pillan wahapu aha tibila.
ethkota as deka tiyenawa nam penna epai, habai penne nane, ( imasmin sathi, idan hothi kiyana ekata gala penne na, enam budda wachanayata galapenne na)
enam boruwak, mulawak m awidyawak.
penawa kiyana mohothe thamai asath , roopayath pahala une. ( meya athi kal hi meya athi wei)- isthirawa tiyena thanak ho, kenek na. asa isthirawa tiyenaw ekak nevi.
mechchara kalayak mas asa ahata penawa kiyala hitana widiha waradie.
ahata , kana nasaya diwa shareeraya penne na , ahata penne warna roopaya pamanai.
aniwatath ehemai.

ethkota me aha kiyanne mokadda ?
(ahuthwa sambuthan, puthwa nobawissathi) - ( pera nothibeemenma athi wela, sheshayak wath nathuwa nirudda wana dharma thawayak lesa dakiya uthui )
(mulu wishwayama ehemai)

roopa dakinawa kiyana thana , kriyathmaka wenne  - (roopa wedana sanyaa sankaara wynaana tikai, enam panchaskandayai.)
anith ayathana 6tath mehemai.

penawa kiyana sansiddiya , bulath kolaya.

kola pata kiyala dana gaththe prakyawenda ? wyn-yaanayen da? wynyaneyen( jaanath , sanjanathi, wijanathi)

mama wisin dakeema - wynaanaya kala de (mamathwaya mulika kota goda nageema nisa)

habai nuwanin dakinawa kiyanne (paja nathi)

enam aththa athisatiyen dakima, yatha bootha iswarupayen dakima. (widharshanawa) - methana dakapu pata wala wenasa , eliye bulath kolaya kiyana sanyaawa gannawa , ganne mama kiyala kenek innawa abyantharaya boarder eka widihata.

wynaanaya thulin roopa wedana sanyaa sankara hewath nama roopa pilibada dana gaththa , wynaanayen thorawa me depaththa haduna ganna ba.
wynaanaya athi kali thamai peneema, peneema athi kal hi thamai wasthu saha kenaa namathi depaththak panawanne.

e kriyawaliya thamai nuwanin hewath widarshanawena dakinawa kiyanne.


ex:
pita konde thuwalayak, eka panuwo gahala
thuwale kiyanawa da mata beth danna , kiyala  ?
eka kiwwe kawda ? hitha.
kes kalu wenawa kiyala kes kiyanawada ? naha
kawda kiyanne ? hitha
ehema nam mehama deyakak ma -> hithak -> dukak -> pancha upadana skandayak.
habai hithak kiyala aththa ekak pawathinawada ? 
sitha yanu nopawathina darmathawayak.
apo thejo wayo patawi, dakkinna ba
dakkina bawata penwanne , (wedana sanyaa chethana)->(passa)-> manasikaarayai ( methana gaburu darmayak tiyenne)
(naama kaye patiga sammpassayath
roopa kaye adiwachana sammpassayath kiyala kiyanne mekatai)



---------------------(passa)->(wedana sanyaa chethana)->( manasikaarayai)--------------------------


පස්ස, වෙිදනා, saggna, චෙිතනා,මනසිකාර   =  wedana ,sagga,sankara ( no roopa or wynaana, this is inbetween)

manase - naama dharma witharai, (chythasika witharai, e wala ekathuwak)
onima sithaka - පස්ස, වෙිදනා, saggna, චෙිතනා,මනසිකාර   *(ekakgrathawaya + jeewitha indriya) - sabba chiththa sadarana chythasika.
mewa okkoma chythasika
me sithaka kotas 7n , kriyakari swabawaya pennanne, (පස්ස, වෙිදනා, saggna, චෙිතනා,මනසිකාර )walin pamanai.

me paha thulama wynaanaya bahagannawa.(me 5th ekka wynaanaya wada karanawa) ( mewa wynaanayata pihitala inna puluwan than 5k)


 
 
අතේ මහපට ඇගිල්ල වගේ තමයි මනසිකාරය ඒක නැතිව කිසිදෙයක් අල්ලන්නට බැහැවගේ තමයි 
මනිසිකාරය මුලින්ම යොමුකිරිම කරන්නෙ.
manasikara - mahapata agilla 
passa - sulagilla (alla ganeema)
wedana,sangga , chenatha e deka mada tiyena agili.


ethkota sparshaya yanu - mahapata agilla plus anek agillak.

ex: passa+ manasikara - sparashaya ( alla ganeema)
1 ක් අල්ලගනනවා වගේ තමයි පස්ස කියන්නෙ ( ayathana 6yen apu aramunak alla gaththa)(methana roopaya automatically included becasue we started with a roopa)

roopa kathawen ( patiga sammassaya) + naama paththe (chythasika paththen) ( aadhi wachana sampassaya) -> wynaanaya hadenne
naama roopa pachchaya wynaanam.

enam naama roopa waya wela thamai wynaanaya sade. (wynaaneyen naama and roopa aye wenas karanna puluwanda ?)
ehema ba. 

wynaanaya hadana duwithawaya handa , apita pena roopa eliye innawa, e roopa balana mama kiyala kenek innawa. eka waradi drushtiyak
e namuth api, wynaanaya hadunu me roopaya and namaya eliye nithya dekak washayen (eliye pena roopa, mage hithe naama) kiyala gannawa. ehema ganne me anithya danne nathi handa.
e dana ganeema tiyenawa kiyala hithenawa . eka anithyai.

eliye roopayak tiyenawa kiyala nithya washayen aran e roopa manase gatena eka api sparshaya washayen gannawa.එ⁣කට කැමති අකමැති බව තමයි වෙිදනා කියන්නෙ. ඒ අල්ලගත්ත එකේ පාට හැඩය නැතිනමි කවුද කොතනද කියල හදුනාගැනිම තමයි සංබාර කිවෙ.
ඉහත ආකාර දැනගැනිමට තමයි සිත හෙවත් vinynana කිවෙ.

ex:

eliye wasthuwata (raththaran) api dhrushtiyak (watinakamak) dala , api kiyanawa raththaran watinawa kiyala .
api hithanawa watina raththaran tiyenne eliye kiyala gannawa. (watinakama eliye tiyena ekma tibba kiyala gannawa )
e nisa kamathi wenawa.
e nisa kamaththa radawa ganna , api eka araksha karanawa.
e nisa pidawak hata gannawa
e nisa manasata barak, peedawak awa.
nama roopa wena kara ganna bari una e nisa duka athi une.

me hada gaththu watinakama  , tibunath dukai, nathi unath dukai.
enema lokaya duka matha pihita pawathee.

ex: puthek gaththama 
mage putha (watinakamak da gannawa), so mata mage putha watinawa.
e nisa eyata hoda deyak wenna/wenawata asa wenawa.
putha eliye innawa kiyala gannawa. naama + roopa wen karaganna bari wenawa .
watinakamata allichcha handa putha hitiyath dukai, naththai dukai
lokayama dukai.

duka hataganne thanhawa nisa,

thanha -> upadana -> bawo -> jaathi

ඉපදිම පලයක්, (wipakayak) 
ඉපදුනාට pස්සෙ ලැ⁣බෙන විපාක සැමත් පලයක්  ( wyaadi, jathi , jara marana).
ඉපදෙන කෙනාගෙ ආශාව තමයි ඒකට කාරණය. ( chanda raagaya)
හේතව.
අම්මා තාත්තා අශාඋනත් නැතත් ඒ මත නොවෙයි ජනිතවන්නෙ.
එ අය උපකාරක ධර්මයක් පමනයි.
ඉපදිම දුකක් ඊටහේතව තණ්හාවයි.
වෙිදනා පචිචයා තණ්හා.
වෙිදනා කියන්නෙ කැමති හෝ අකැමති හෝ මධ්‍යසථ බවයි
ඵස්ස පචිචයා වෙිදනා

eliye nithya lesa gath wita, kamathi (lobaya) , akamathi (iwesaya) ho madyathsa bawa ( mohaya) pawathi.

ස්පර්ශය කියන වචනය යෙදෙන තැනේ හැටියටයි තෝරන්නෙ. (bahira roopa , indriya + wynaana) 3 used to create sparshaya.

කෙනෙක්ව ස්පර්ශ කරනවා කියන තැන (තිණ්ණන් සගති කථාව) . (meka pottabbaya roopaya + kaaya indriya + wynaanaya)

දැන් ඵස්ස වෙිදනා සංඣා සඞිකාර කියනතැන මනසට අදාාල කාරණයක්. 
තවත් තෙනක තව විදිහක්
මනසේ කතන්දරය හැදෙන්න ඇස කන ආදිය උපකාර උනාට, ආපසු ඇහැ පැත්ත බලනකොta 
ඉතිරියක් නැතිව නිරවශේෂ නිරෝධය දකින විට 
අල්ලගෙන  උපාදාාන කරන්න දෙයක් නැතිබව දකිනවා. ( meka dakkoth eya niwana dakala. )

e nisa wynaana pachchara namaroopa athi nove.
meka dakinne maarga nynanaya(daham asa) thulin.

api mechchara kal kaleth wynaana pachahara namaroopa kiyala therum gaththu eka.
namuth budu dahame kiyala denne nama roopa pachchaya wynaana widihata.


රත්තරං වටිනවා කියල අපේ හිතේ ඇතිකරගත් දෘෂ්ඨිය රත්තරං අතහැරියා  කියලා නතර වෙන්නේ නැහැ.
ආභරණ කාවදාවත් කියන්නේ නැහැ එයා නයිතවා කියලා  කෙනා කෙනාගෙ සිත මතමයි පැනවිම කලේ.
තණ්හාවත් මෙි සිතමයි තණ්හා කරල තියෙන්නෙත් මෙි හිටමයි.
එහෙමනමි භාහිර හැම දේ තක්සේරැ කලේ සිතමයි.
මෙි සියල්ලම මනසිකාර දෘෂ්ටියක්මයි.
අපි දෘෂ්ඨිකාන්තාරයක අතරමංවෙලා.

ඔලුවේ kakkuma, කොහොමද මේ විඳීමට දකින්නේ?
වෙිදනාව දියබුබුලක් වගේ
ඔලුව කිවිවත් කයේ කොටසක්නෙ.ඇතලේ වෙනස්වන ගතියක් ස්පර්ෂ වෙලා ආව සිද්ධියක්.හැදුනෙ පංචඋපාදානයක්මයි
පංච උපාදානක්ඛන්ධා දුක්කා.
මතකද පුංචි කා ලෙ අහපු කතන්දරයක් අර ලබුංගඩියෙ යාගය කියලා.
වැස්සක් ඇවිත් මුහුදට ගහගෙන ගියා.ඉතින් මාලුවෙක් ඒක ගිත්තා.
අන්න ඔතන ලබුගෙඩිය කිවිවෙ ලොකය ඒ කිවිවෙ පංචඋපාදාානස්කන්ධයටයි.
කෙලෙස් වර්ෂාවට ගහගෙන යනවා.මහ සාගරය වගේ දෘෂ්ඨිකාන්තාරයක මැදිවෙල සසර ගමන යනවා ඉතින් මාඑයා වැනි මාලුවා ගිලගන්නවා
ඔන්න එකමත් එක රටක ලොකතොවිලයක් කරන්න තිබුනා.
තොවිලෙ කරන්න තිබුනෙ ලබුගෙඩියක් ඇතංලේ
ඉතින බෙරකාරයොයි නැටුමිකාරයොයි ආතරයයි ගෙදරඅයයි හැමෝම ලබුගෙඩිය ඇතලට ගිහිල්ලා වහගෙන තොවිලෙ පටන්ගත්තා
මෙහෙම කරනවිට වෙනකායවත් පේන්නෙ නැහැ.බෙරගහනවා නටනවා කවිකියනවා ඉතින් දවස් කිපයක වැඩක් නෙ.ගජරාමෙට ලබිබෙි තොවිලෙ.
එදා දව⁣සෙ හොදටම වැහල ලබිබෙි ගහගෙනගියා මුහුදටම.
විශාල මාලුවෙක් ඇවිල්ල ලබිබෙ ගිල්ලා ඉතින් මෙිකව මලුඅල්ලන කටිටියකගෙ දලට අහුවෙල  ගෙනැහිල්ල උගෙබඩ
පලල බලනකොට ලපුගෙඩියක් ඒක පලල බලනකොටස ඩෙන්න ඩෙනො කියල බෙරකාරයොයි නටිටුවොයි ඔකකොම ආවලු එදා තමයි තොවිලෙ ඉවරවෙචිච දවස.
එ කිසිවෙක් දන්නෙ නැහැ මෙි හාහිර සිදු වු එක සිද්ධියක්වත්.

ex:
මම වෙනමත් ලොකය තව එකක් කියල වෙනම දෙකක් නැහැ.මෙික පංචඋපාදාාස්කන්ධයක්මයිමම සහ භාහිර ලොකය කවිවෙ මහ මුලාවකට අසුවෙලා.
ඒක එහෙම නොවෙයි  ඇස කණ නාසය දිව ශරිරය කියන්නෙම අනිදරශන ධර්ම කියල බුදුරජාණංණ් වහන්සෙ දේසනා කලා.
අපිට දකින්න බැහැ අස නාසය ආදිය කාගෙවත් නොවෙයි.මෙිවා කාලයක් තිස්සෙ තියෙන දෙවලුත් නොනෙයි.
මෙිවා ඒ මොහොතෙ උපදින ධර්මයි.මෙන්න මෙික මුලින්ම තේරැමිගතයුතවෙනවා.
හුගක් අය හිතන්නෙ ඇස කණ ආදියෙන් හැදිචිච මම ඉතින් මගෙ අමිම මගේ දරැවා කියල වෙන්කරගෙනනෙ.
මෙහෙම වර්ගිකරනයක් කරන්නෙ  පංචඋපාදානස්කන්ධය ඇතලේමයි එනමි රැප වෙිදනා සංනා සංකාර වින්නාන ඇතලෙමයි.ලබිබ ඇතලෙමයි.

කෙස් ගසක් ඔළුවෙ තියෙන්නෙ දැනෙන ගතිය සිනිදු ගතියටත් පඨවි කියනවා..

පුලුන් කෑල්ලක් අල්ලන කොට සැහැල්ලු ගතියක්නෙ ඒකටත් පඨවි කියනවා

මස්කෑල්ලක් ඔබන කොට දැනෙන මෘදු ගතියත් පඨවි කියනවා
මෙදේ හයආකාරයක දැනෙන ගතිවලට පඨවි කියනවා මිසක් ඇහැට පෙනෙන භාහිර දේවල් වලට පඨවි කියන්නෙ හැහැ.

පඨවිය විසිරි  යන්නට නොදාි බැද තබන ගතියට කියනවා ආපෝ ස්වවාභාවය කියලා
දැන් ඔන්න පිටි ටිකකට ජලය ටිකක් දැමිමොත් පිටි බෝලයක් හදන්න පුළුවන් වෙන්නෙ ජලයේ ඇති ආපෝ ගතිය නිසයි.
ගලන වැගිරෙන ගති තියෙන්නෙත් ආපෝ ගතිය නිසයි.
ආපෝ ගතිය විශේෂයක් තමයි පංච ඉදුරන්ට ගොචර වෙන්නෙ නැහැ.ඒක මනසින්මයි දැනගන්නෙ. (alena swabahawaya thamai apoo kiyanne, gum wala alena gathiya tiyenawa)
මේනිසා ආපෝ ගති ස්වභාවය  සුඛුම රැපයක් කියනව.
ජලයට ඇගිල්ල ඔබලා බලන්න උණුසුම හෝ සිසිල දැනේවි ඒකට කියනවා තේජෝ ගතිය කියලා.
හුස්මක් ගන්න කොට පිමිබෙන හැකිලෙන ගතිය දැකෙන්නෙ වායෝ ස්වාභාවය නිසයි
සෙලවෙන හමන ගතියටත් වායෝ ස්වාභය කියනවා 
ඒ නිසා පඨවි ආපෝ,තේජෝ,වායෝ ගති ඇහැට පේන්නෙ නැහැ.

පඨවි ආපෝ,තේජෝ,වායෝ ගති  hama dathu iswabawayakama pawathinawa.
මෙි හතර තමයි නියෝජනය වන්නේ rupa කියලා.මෙිවට මහාBhutha rupa කියනවා

මහාbhutha rupa ඇතිතැනක උපාදාාය rupa 4 ක් තියෙනවා.වර්ණ,ගන්ධ, රස ඔිජා කියලා
මෙි 8 ම තනිව පවතින්න බැහැ.එකටමයි තියෙක්නෙ අනුපාතය  වෙනස්වන්න පිළිවන්

මැරිල දිරල දුර්වල  වන තැන් පනගහල ගන්න ගතියට තමයි ඔිජා කියනිනෙ

Rupaya අරඹයා අපේ හිතම විදිමින්,හදුනමින්,ඒ ඒ විධිහට හිතමින් හැසිරෙනබවත් දැතගන්න ඔිනි.
මෙන්න මෙි නාම rupa දෙක නිසයි දැනගැනිල්ලක් ඇතිඋනේ කියල නොදන්න කම නිසා,එයාට පෙනෙන්නෙම මෙි හිතේ ගතිය නාම Rupa දෙකටම අයිතියි කියලමයි.
 
මෙන්න මෙහෙමයි තණ්හාව ඒ කියන්නෙ ලමයෙක් ගේ Ripayak මට ඇතිඋනේ.
නාම Rupa පචිචයා Vignanan  කියලා නොදන්න අවිද්‍යාව නිසා vignana පචිචයා නාම Rupan උනා.
මෙසේ හැදිචිච විදිහ නතර කලොත් මිසක තණ්හාව නතර කරන්න බැහැ.
 
හොදට මතක තියා ගන්න වෙනවා මෙි නාම rupa වැයවෙල තමයි vignanaya හටගත්තෙ කියල.
තම තමුන්මයි හිතලා දුක හදාාගෙන තියෙන්නෙ.
ජිවිතය කියන පංචඋපාදාානස්ඛන්ධ දුක ඔහොමයි හැදෙන්නෙ
වචන ඇතත් නැතත් තිරිසනාට උනත් කැමැත්තෙන් හිත හසුරවන්ට පළිවන් බව අපිට තේරෙනවනෙ

pattichcha sammuppadaya (hethu pala wadaya)

awidya pachchaya sankara
sankara pachchaya wynaana
wynaana pachchaya nama roopan
nama roopa pachchaya salayathanan (ayathana 6)
salayathana pachchaya passo
passa pachchaya wedana 
wedana pachchaya thanha
thanha pachchaya upadana
upadana pachchaya bawo
bawa pachchaya jathi -> duka

wynaana -> nama roopa -> salayathana -> passo

pancha ikandaya = roopa wedana sannya sankara wynaana
pattichca sammupadaya nisa hata gaththu nama roopa nisa pancha upadana iskanaya athi wenawa. ( sitha thula)

pattichcha samuppadaya handa hadenne nama roopayak (manomaya roopayak). bahira roopaisndayak nevi
me namika roopaya allala thamai -> wenda sannya sankara wynaana hadenne. ( pancha upadana ikandayak hata gaththa)


ex: maha gedara amba gahen gediyak genath ape gedara hitawala, parana rasama hoyanawa.

pattichcha samuppadaya bahirin balanna ba. ( purwa prathipadawa) meya eliyen balanna ba.
budun deshana karanne , meya thama thulin balanna kiyala thamai prakasha kale.
apita therena apita galapena widihata hada gena balanna ba. ( purwa prathipadawa)

me example eka awidyawa gana therumak tibbath naththath onima kenekuta therum ganna deyak.

e nisa awidyawe sobawaya dana gaththata passe patisothagami akarayen hithanna patan ganna oni.
laukika lokaya thula tiyena logic and assumptions bahara karala , podi lamayek mula idan igena ganna widihata thamai me dharamaya ahanna oni.

ex:
api gedara mathak kaloth, apita mawenne hithe roopayak neda.
mathak une hithata pena gedara nam , e mathak una hithata, bahirawa gedarak upaddanna ba. enam lokayak upaddanna bari wenawa, enam lokayak pihitanna ba.
manase hadana eka dakinne manasenmai.
aha dakina eka ahen iwarai
kana dakin eka kanek nirodai.
namuth 
awidyawa nisa ayathana dekak ekathuwak washayen api bahirata roopa danawa.
methana incoming and outgoing hith dekak wada karanawa.
kana+ manasa
asa+manasa

ex:
bulath kolayak ganna. aha kiwwada bulath kiyala
diwa bulath kiwwada bulath kiyala 
atha gala baluwath bulath kiwwada
enam pancha indrayan gen lokaya panawanna ba. 
bulath kiyana panaweema kale manasen

enam pancha iduranta (asa, kana, nasaya, diwa shareera) lokaye yamak ath dakinna ba.
enam buluth kathawa awe kohomada
podi kale idan dapu manse sanyaa osse , widima osse, chethana osse lokaya upadinne manasikarayata (menehi karawana) witai.

manasikaaraya job eka thamai , api piligaththu widihata mathak karala denawa
api waradi widihata nam pili aran tiyenne , e widihata mathak karala denawa.
api hari widihata nam pili aran tiyenne , e widihata mathak karla denawa.

enam api bahiren tibba abha hade, ate kiyala pili gaththa nisa mathak karala denawa.
enam mohithin mohotha hata gena niroda wenawa kiyala pili gaththe nathi nisa, apita nithya lesas pawathina bawa mathak karala denawa.

mohothak mohothak marena nama roopa , alla badagena , lokaya kiyala hitha gena innawa.
