pachcha samuppadaye tiyenne wynaana pachchaya namaroopa,
abhidharmaye (wynaanaya hata ganna thana) explain karanne nama roopa pachchaya wynaanan kiyala.

imamsmin sathi idan hothi ( meya athi kal hi meya wei.)

ex:
wynyana athi kalhi nama roopa atha. ( meya athi kalhi meya wei. wynyana tiyena thak kal witharai nama roopa tiyenne, majician inna kal witharai kotiya inne )
enam hethuwen palaya wen karanna ba.

enam kannadiya athi kalhi thamai prathibimbhaya.
kannadiya +  prathibimbhaya , me deka wena karanna ba.
namuth eka dana genath 
wen karala haduna gannawa.
ex:
putha ara kannadiya aran enna kiyala panawanawa
eya kannadiya witharak aran enawa.
dan kannadiya wen karalane. (api drushtiye alila)
kannadiya nathuwa apita prathibimbaya penne na, namuth api hithanawa mama innawa , man gawa thamai prathibimbaya tiyenne . kannadiya karanne eka pennana eka 
kiyala. namuth aththatama
kannadiyen thora prabimbayak tibbe na.


namuth kannadiya witharak genawa kiya hithithanawa , 
kannadiya prathibimmayak nathuwa pawathina bawata wishwasa karanawa.
e wishwasayata hethuwa methek kal api purudu kara gath waradi dakmai (drushtiyai)
enam patichcha samuppadaya hariyata dakala na.
hethuwen thorawa palayak hata ganna ba.
enam prathibimbayak nathuwa kannadiyak tiyenna ba. 

e unata apita oni tharam wena wena ma roopa tiyenawa kiyala pili gannawa ( me lokaya pawathinawa kiyala piliaran) 
kawru hari ahen baluwoth yamak tiyenawa kiyala dana ganna onima kenekuta piliwan kiyala , piligannawa.

namuth pattichchasamuppadaya anuwa hethuwa athi kal hi palaya hata gani.
namuth me wena wena ma gaththu roopa wala hethuwa apita penne na.
enam me roopa wala tiyena pattichcha samuppanna bawa api therum aran na.
enam bahira tibena me dewal wala hethuwa nathuwa palaya pili aran.
 
ethkota,
awiddayawa gana danna kenek saha nodanna kenek gaththath, degollata ma me wena karapu roopa tiyenawa 
enam dharmaya dana genath api thama pruthakjanai.
arya sharawakayek wenna nam , bahira roopa nithya lesa pana wiya nohaki. nama roopaya anithya ( niroda) weema dana gatha uthui.
pancha upadana iskandayath anithyai , dukkai, anathmai ( thrilakshana) kiya datha uthui.
meya dakinne marga pala prakhawen, ehenam daham asen. ( wynaanayen nevi) 


roopaskanda ( roopa wedana sanya sankara wynaana)
11 akarayenkin wihidila tiyenawa ( godak handa isanda kiwwa) ( atheetha, warthamana, anagatha, bahira, athyathmika, gorosu, sium, heena, praneetha,dura,laga) roopa.
iskanda kiyana gathi iwabawaya  me 11 than wala tiyenna puluwan.

namuth naamaroopa (namika roopayak) kiyanne eka nevi ( meka eliyen na) (namika roopayai) (manase hadenne)
namuth me sith paramparawe wegaya handa bara gaththe eliye roopayak kiyala.
methana namayai roopayai kiyala dekata kaduwe wynaanaya. ( majician)

ex: shabdayak ahunawama ( hithuwa eka fan eke sadde kiyala) - ethkota eliye fan eken kiyala hageemak enawa.
eliye kiyala kiwwa gaman, fan eka tiyenne eliye kiyala panawala iwarai. lokaya nithyai kiyala panawala iwarai.
eliya roopaya baara aran iwarai.
ahen warnayak penawa
ethkota eka fan eka wage kiyala hageemak enawa.
onna sanskara dharma, nithya bawata prove kara gaththa. (sadde ahune fan eken bawa.)
thawa kenekuta balannath puluwan.
namuth me sathara maha dhathu roopaya nevi naama roopa kiyanne.
namaroopa ehema karanna ba, bahirata panawanna ba.
wyn-yaana nathi wana wita namaroopa nirodai.

enam
imasmin asathi idan nahothi. ( meya nathi kalhi meya hata nogani)

meka thawa durata explain karanna:

apita saddyak ahuna (danagannawa) : ethana ahuna kiyanne wynaanaya (sithak)
wynaanayak hata gaththa nam wynaana pachchaya namaroopan. ( pachchicha samuppada niyaya)
namaroopaya manomaya fan roopaya. 
wynayanaya lahu pariwaththan ( itha wegayakin wenas wenawa)
athi una thanama nirudda wenawa
wynanaya nirudda unu wita namaroopa hata nogani.

wynaanaya hata gaththe naththam namaroopa hata noganie.
meya anuppada nirodayai. ( uppada novi niroda wei) (niwan awabodaya)
melesa ahuna naththam danagaththu eka ethanama nathi wenawa nam 
thanha karanna thanak na
idesha, mohoyen badenna thanak na

onima aramunak apita pancha upadana iskandayak
mama kiyala aramunu kaloth ekatha pancha upadana iskandayak.
eka warakata enne eka pancha upadana iskanadayak witharai.
kasiyak wage , bima wadinne eka paththak witharai. aramuna (gathi 6, asa kana nasaya..etc) + mamai (bima)

ex:
 tharaha = mama
dekama pancha upadana isknada nisa, eka kasiyaka depaththa.

aramunama pancha upadana iskandayak. (mama ho tharaha ho, ira , handa ... onima ramunak)
ethkota 
tharaha gaththoth tharaha aran tiyenne magema pancha upadana iskanadayata
mage sitha mai mama dakinne.
kenek dakinne thama thaman ge sith wal pamani


asata roopa hambenawa kiyana eka wipakayak
ekata hethuwa thamai pera roopayata tibunu ashawa.
wipaka washayen
ahak hambuna
roopa habenawa (kusala, akusala namaroopa)
apita mewa wipaka washayen nothereema nisa (dan siddawana deyak kiyala hithana handa)
aluthin karma hadanawa
e karmayata wipaka lesa sasara yanawa.
wipakaya e mattamen iwara kirimen duken nidahas wiya haka.
aluth karma nosada sitiya haka.

hadanna bari wenne ai
asa + roopaya handa chakku wynaanaya hata ganeema wipakayak.
wynaanaya nisa namaroopayak athi wenawa.
habai eka eliye tiyena roopayawath asa wath nevi. (meka tiyenne pancha upadana iskanayak, tiyenne hithe)
eka katawath wenas karanna ba
enam pattichcha samuppadayai.


asa aran innkota roopa pena eka apita nawaththawanna ba.
asa+roopya -> wynaanaya haduwa (me thuna ekathu wela isparshaya haduwa)

ex:
ballek innawa, balla wathurata ebenawa
balla hithanne wathure ballek innawa kiyala 
ithin buranawa , pahuru ganawa
balla gedara gawata awith
onna ara wathure ballek innawa kiyala hithala 
aye buranawa uge kama kanna ei kiyala 
apita oka therenawa 
namuth api ballata ochcham karanawa methana ballek na kiyala
eth ballata oka therenne nane.

me wage apith awidyawen, wyn-yaanaya -> nama roopa  -> iskanda panchaya haduna kiyala gannawa 
sansaraye yanawa
- mekata kiyanne anusothagami patichchasamuppadaya
-anith eka patisothagami patichcha samupadaya


incoming and outgoing 

incoming - 
pata kolayak eliye tibba , punchi lamayai , wadihitiyek dakinawa, mokadda dakinne pata kole.
dennatama incoming ekama de (warnaya witharai)
outgoing -
podi lamaka, mukuth na kole iranwa
wadihitiya , kole aran watinakama tiyenawa kiyala.

incoming and outgoing sith dekak.
incoming -> namaroopa waya karala wynaanaya haduwa
outgoing -> watina kama kiyana naama roopayak eliyata damma me kole salli kiyala.

namuth sithak nathi wenna oni sithak upadinna. (chiththa niyamaya)
enam nopawathina sithak.

----------------------------------------

hith paramparawaka hageema yanna kohomada
chiththa withi 17k pancha upadana iskandayaka tiyenawada ?


----------------------------------------------

chichcha veethiya gana balamu

sithiwalin thamai pancha upadana iskandaya hadenne.

ayathanawa walin thamai athdakeem ganne ( enam roopa nimithi 6akarayakin gannawa kiyana eka)
enam e e aya upadinata passe igena gaththu bashawan haraha , manase gabada karagaththu noyek sanyaa tiyenawa.
mechchara kal api kale , chanda ragayek mewata aluna kiyana ekane.
ethakota 
api lokaya allaganne hama tissema
me 6 akarayaka saynyaa walin.
e anuwa thamai , api sithiwili hadanne ( chethana )
enam mohothak mohothak pasaa, api roopa wedana saynyaa sankara wynyaana ta ahuwenawa
eneam pancha upadana iskandayata ahuwenawa.
me mohotha and next mohotha nithya bawa pilligannawa.

bahira deta hani unoth , api asa karapu lokaya gara watenawa, duka pawathinawa.
enam duka yanu sithe athi karagath / pawathina deyak.
enam duka kiyanne api hada gaththu ekak. ( api mawa gaththu ekak)

sankappa rago purisassa kamoo ( purushayage kamaththa moketa hari alennamai) kiyala kiyanne.

mehema wethdi
api thula gathi dekak enawa
1) ahan kara (paliyen ahan yanu mama ta) - awidyawa
2) maman kara (paliyen maman kiyanne mage) - thanhawa

enam ahankara, mamankara hadila tiyenne ( awidiyawa+ thanhawa ekathu wenakota)
ethkota sathwaya kiyala kiyane mama+ mage kiyana saynyaa deke ekathuwata.
ehema naththam (awidyawa+thanhawata)

ethkota 
awidyawa+thanhawata tiyena kam, sathwa pudgala bawaya pawathinawa / hagenawa
me sathwa pudgala bawaya , samawitama niwana yatapath karanawa

ese niwana yatapath dharma (niwana wahana dharma = neewarana dharmatha) - 5k gana api katha karanawa.
1) kama chanda (pancha kamayata kamathi bawa)
2) wyapaada ( tharaha, iweshaya)
3) theena midda ( alasa bawa)
4) uddachcha kukkuchcha ( pasu thawilla) ( nokala kusal ha kala akusal gana sitha sitha pasu thawenawa )
5) wichikichcha (buddadi 8 than kerehi athi sakaya. enam budda,dhamma,sangga,shikksha pada,pattichcha sammupadaya, pachchicha samuppadaya nisa 3akarayakin hata ganna saka)
5.5 pattichcha sammupadaya sakaya nisa hata ganna saka 3i
5.5.1 pubbe kankathi ( pera wisu widiha gana athi sakaya)
5.5.2 aparantha kankathi ( ilagga bawaya kelesa ipadeeda kiyana sakaya)
5.5.3 pubbantha aparantha kankathi ( pera wisu saha anagatha kawru wela ipadee da danne na kiyala sakaya)

 
niwana mathu karannam, me  neewara samuchcheda prahanaya wiya uthui.
enam me mohotha thula pamanayak lokaya pawathi waba therum gatha uthui
me mohotha sakas wana akaraya , awankawa therum ganna oni.
enam pachchuppannaye sakas weema awaboda gara ganeemai. ( enam me mohotha kohomada hadhune kiyala eka)

(budun sitha samadhimath karaganeeme awashathawaya pennuwe ,
enam pas kam sapaye sathutu wana sitha mella karanna oni nisa.
meeta hethuwa ashruthawath pruthak janaya samawitama kancha kaamaye gunenmai sanasilla pawatinne kiyana eka, hithapu nisa)

chiththa samadhiya deshana kirimata hethuwa meyai.
chiththa samadhiye gunaya nisa pattichcha samuppaadha dharmayo therum ganeema sudu parisaraya sakasenawa

me anuwa. 
iskandayan ge samudaya weemada (iskanda hata ganima) saha pattichcha samuppadaya da pachchuppanna bawa therum gatha haka.
(saralawa kiyanawa nam,
iskanda hata ganeemai.
hethu pala dahamai
dekam athi wenne me mohothe bawa)
therum gatha haka.

enam pachchupannaye thamai ( me mohothe) thamai ape sasara goda nagena thana.
enam midimatha  tiyenne me pachchupannaye thamai. (me mohothemai)

asata roopa peneema dharmathawayak. (mamathi roopa witharak mata peniyan kiyala kiyanna ba, so eka dharmathawayak)
ewa allagen ape keles walin abhisanskaranaya ( mathu wipaka pinisa karma sakas weema) weemai problem eka.
apita mula sita tibunu chanda raagaya (alena gathiya) mideemata nam , puhunuwak oni.
mese chanda ragayen iwath weema sadaha thamai thri+lakshanaya hadunwa dunne

mokada me allaganeema ( upadanaya) api bawa ganan huru wela inne, 
budunge sri deshanawa anuwa me siyalla anithyai
enam me mohothath anithyai.
ehema naththam, me mohothawath alla gena sitiya nohakie.

me mohothe, nimiththak alladunna asa
+ asa wisin allala dunna nimiththa + wynaanaya (thinnan sangathi passo)
nisa athia wu passa /iparshaya
nisa mulu siyaluma dharama athiwe. ( passa samudaya sabbe dhamma)

enam me mulu lokaya samudaya (dannene) wenne passayeni (isparshayeni).

mese mulu lokayak peerana danumak awashya na,
thama thulin baleemak pamanamai tiyenne.

ex:

onna motorcyclist kenek enawa . api eyagen ahanawa oya bike eke awe kohomada kiyala
eya kiyanwa bike ekata gahana petrol walin awe kiyala.
dan bike eka nawaththala tiyenne, yanne na.
eth petrol tiyenawa. e kohomada e ?

onna ethkota kiyala nanana awe pichchichcha thel walin kiyala
namuth , pichchichcha thel dapuwahama bike eka wada na
ehenam bike eka awe kohomada
enam e mohothe pichchichcha thel walin.
enam e mohothe pichchena thel walin kiwwahama ekata atheethak, anagathak na
warthamayeth pennanna bari lesa waya wela.
enam kisi deyak ithuru nathi,mohothen mohothata
enam pachchupannai.

metakata kamatahank thamai :

gul 6k tiyena thubasak tiyenawa 
ekata thalagoyek ringanawa 
dan me satha eliyata ganne kohomada ?
hil 5k wahanawa
ethkota eken eliyata enna oni.

anna e wage thamai,
api as wahagena bawana karanakota hithen (mano dwarayen) aramunu enawa iwarak nathuwa.
ena kawulu wahuwa wage, ena ena sithuwili anithyai kiyala dakinna oni.
bana asa dharamatha therena handa
me mohothe, athi wana sithiwili me mohothema nirodaya wana bawa ( sithuwili athi wela nathi wena bawa)
dakinnawa.
enam siyaluma sansara arbuda tiyenne, sithak pahala unoth
enam sansara arbuda tiyenne . menna me wynaana saha namaroopa kriyawaliya nisa bawa
salayathinika nimithi sith pahala weemenmai samudaya wenne.
wynanaa wisin pilibuimbu karana namaroopa saynyaa thamai api haduna ganne  

me sith thamai pahala wenne kiyala danagena
pena kota lassanai kiyala hithunoth , api sansarayata badila
methanin galaweema thaam.

ex:
enam apita mona asawak awath, eka sithak washayen ganna oni
enam awidyawai + thahawamai bawa dana gena prahanaya karanna oni.

panchaskandaya (roopa wedana sayanyaa sankara wynana) kohewath pawathina dharamayak nevi.
kohenwath apu kohatawath yana , pawathina dharamathayak nevi.
sithenma sakas kala roopa sanyawata wedana sanya chethana  kirimen dana ganna wu anathma wu, anithya wu iskanda pahaki.


me nisa tiyena asakwath tiyena roopayak wath methanata sambannda natha.

mese anithya wana iskanda panchakaya, (anithya bawa nodanna nisa) nithya lesa alla ganimen (awidyawen+thanhawen) mama/mage/mage athmaya yanuwen upadanaya kirima nisa
mathu wipaka pinisa karmaya sakas wei.
namuth athiwana ikandaya nirodaya wei.namuth upadana karagath de anithya bawa dakka nisa yali, 31 thalaye onima thanaka upathak labiya haka.
mese panchaskanadayata ena onima aramuk alla ganeemen mathu wipaka sakase.

eya paw /pin/dyaana aramuk ho loba,idwesha,moha,mana,kroda,matchariya aramunak lesa ganimen sasara sakas wei.
alla noganeemen (upadanaya nokirimen) jeewithaya sathuten gatha karamu.

rahathan wahanse namak ,
mama ,mage ,mage athmaya lesa nogena ,
sathwa pudgala drushtiyen thorawa,
awidya thrushnawen nogena,
paraknaawen samawitama (piriniwan paana thek)
upadanaya nokara , ikanda pariharanaya (kaya pariharanaya) kirima sopaadisesha niwana lesa hadunwanu labe.
piriniwan papuwata passe anupadhi sesha niwana lesa hadin wei. ( e ikanda nisa athi una dukath iwarai)-enam parinirwanayai.  

peneema,aseema,daneema(rasaya,pahasa,ganda/suwada(aagrahanaya)), danaganeema ( ayathana 6) siyalla sith wei.
me 6nma ekawarakara eka pancha upadana ikandayak pamani.
enam sithak yanu pancha iskandayak.
api me pancha iskandaya mama/mage/mage athmaya lesa ganeemen pancha upadana ikandayak wei
me anuwa onima aramunak mama/mage/mage athmaya lesa gaththoth eya pancha upadana iskandayak wei.
me anuwa ,raga, idesha,moha sithak sakas wenne 
raga idesha moha mama kiya alla ganeemen.
me upadanaya nathi weemen
anithya dharmathawaya gana awaboda wei.

rahathan wahansa namakata pancha iskandayak pamanai pawathinne, upadanaya novei.

me mohothe athi wu sithe athiya thawaya awankawa wataha gatha uthuya.
evi anathmaya prakata wei. 

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------
mas asa + manasa + panasa kiyanne mokadda ?
maha wedalla suthraya.

asa + roopaya panaweema siduwenne wynaanaya athi kalma wei. (C=A)
wynaaya athi kalhimai naama roopa (A=B)
enam (C=B) - asa+roopaya athi wenne naama roopa

asa + bahira roopya = wynaanaya
me deka ekathu kara hithe hada gannawa 
namaroopa ( asa and bahira roopaya wayawee)
asa + bahira roopya => namaroopa

wyaana and namaroopa ekatamai pawathinne.
wynaanaya athiunoth namaroopa pawathinnama oni
namaroopa  pawathinawa nam wynaanaya pawathinna oni.


aramunak (sama input ekakma ayathana 6yen ena dharamathawayan) -> upadanaya karaganne (mama ,mage ,athmaya kiya) ganne nithya sanyaawak athi wechcha nisa. 
(aramunak nowena kisiwak natha)
nithya wenne ( wynaana + namaroopa wala anithya isbawaya nodanna nisa )
prakshawen (*danuma, enlightment) api awiddawen athi wena me kriyawalin dakinna oni.

yamkisi kenek boruwa boruwak bawa danne nam.
e dana gaththa eka prakshawai.
eya nuwanin kalakirenawa. e nisa nitharama anithya dukka anathma sihi karanawa.

kamatahana-
as deka piyagena.
sathara sathipattanaya purudu wenna oni.
- kaye kayanu passi wiharathi (kaye kaya anuwa danagena jiwwewath weema)
- wedasu wedananu passi wiharathi (wedanawa anuwa balala bala jiwath weema)
- chiththe chiththanu passi wiharathi (sithe sitha anuwa)
- dhammesu dhammanu passi wiharathi (dharmaya anuwa baleema)

pamalu eka wadapuhama anith thuna autoa wadenawa.
kaya prakata handa eka thamai karanna oni.

as deka piya gena samathaya wadanna.(sitha eka thana kata ganna)
dan saddayak ahena kota,
ahuna- mokadda shabbadayak
danagaththa- kohenda manasen
eliyen shabddayak awa kiyala -hithuna
ema bahirin kiyala hithune mage nodanna kamata
kanata ahuwe shabba roopaya pamani
dana gaththe sithen/manasen pamani.
manasin dangaththu de manasata pamanai aithi.
ehema nam bahirin shabbadayak asuna yai sithuwe kohomada ?
enam awidiyawa nisa.
mehema sidda une sootha ayathanaya + mana ayathanaya dekama eka wara gaththu nisa
kisima kaleka sanyaaa dekak ekawara kriyathmaka nove.
enam ayathana iswayakthayai.
me awabodaya menehi karanna 

pass + manasikaraya gana hoyanna.

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

pin paw karala hodin jeewath wenna budun ge deshana awashaya wenne na.
jiwithe api inna position, hodai sansara gamanata.

budun ge paniwidaya sasara nawathweematai.
jiwithe ta dunna watinakama nisa ne sansara gamanata yanne
me watinkama dunne hithen.
ehenam waradeema wenne hithen.

ex:
duriyan, kenekuta hodai kenekuta appriyai.
ehenam me 
watinakama denne hithen
enam 
bahira ta dena wati kama matha hamadama sansaraya sakas wei.
dukak awath, api balanne pancha kamaya thulin thamai eka niwa ganna.
me karameyen nawatha sansaraya digu wena eka witharai wenne.

hitha kiyanne nopawathina dharmathawak ( meka lahu pariwaththan, e nisa examples denna ba)
hitha pawathina ayathana 6k atha.
me ayathana 6 adyathmika and bahira lesa bede.
me ayathana hataganna mohothe, issparashaya athi wenne.
isparashaya athi wenawa kiyanne siyaluma dharma athiwenawa. (madu pindika suthraya)
me isparshaya hata ganeema dharmathawayak.

ex:
eliye kurullek ka ahanawa
mage kanin man ahanawa.
kiyala ne api normally kiyanne. ( mata isthira kanak tibila tiyenawa , plus eliye kurulek idala tiyenawa)

budun kiwwe me karamaya waradie kiyala ne.

siddiya : aseema, danaganeema, peneema, daneema ( mewa okkoma hithe)
aramuna : roopaya (asata,nahayata,kanata)
wedanawa : e roopayata kamathi ho akamathi bawa 
sanyya : mona ayathanayen da awe kiyala haduna ganeema
sankara : haduna gaththu de gana athiwana chethana
wynana : me hama deyakma dana ganna bawa.

hithe tiyena kotas thamai : wedana sanyya sanakara (naama)
isparashaya+ manasikaraya -> pancha upadana iskanadayak


dukka arya sathya yanu -> pancha upadana iskandaya
dukka samudaya sathya yanu -> me duka athi une kohomada kiyala hoya ganna eka(awiddaya nisa nithya lesa ganeema)
dukata hethuwa - bahira roopa tiyenawa , e roopa thulin apita sathutu asathutu wenna puluwan kiyala hageemak ena eka. ewa walata tiyena thanhawa nisa wenasweemata api kamathi na.
dukka nirodaya sathya yanu - > aththa athi satiyen dana ganeema.
dukka niroda gamani patipada sathya yanu - arya ashtangika margaya.

enam dukai dukata hethiwai nitharama api laga tiyenawa.
ein nidas weemata nam ithuru deka gana salakilimath wenna oni.

pattichcha samuppadaya ta anuwa , meya athi kal hi weya wei.
mehi therum ganna oni de thamai , ekama welawe dekama wenne . hethuwa athi wee palaya hata ganna wa nevi
hethuwa and palaya ekama mohothe hata ganna bawa saha niruddawa wana bawa therum gatha uthui.

ex:
eka wata dekak sidda wena ekata ex.

ex:

daspethiya malaka suwada tiyenne mala tiyena kan witharai.
para wechchi male suwada na.
mala pipila athi kalhima suwada atha.
mata pipunata pasuwa nevo suwada.
pipena bawai suwadai ekama mohothe wei.
pipichcha mala tiyena kan suwada atha.
mala wenama ho suwada wenama tibbe na.
kohenwath awath nevi, kohatawath yanawa wath nevi.
athi wita atha,
nathi wita natha.

elasama , iskanda panchakaya athi kalhi, 
mama, mage m mage athmaya kiyana sathwa pudgala bawaya athiwei. ( meya upan gei doshaya lesa hadinwei)
ipadunu gaman api ahu wela. ( prathamayen athi wana puruddak, sakkaya dittiye patan ganeema)
(ethan mama, eso hamasmi ,eso me aththa) - mage,mama,mage athmaya let ganeema.

budun deshana karanwa 
ikandakaya mama,mage athmaya kiyala nogena
(nathan mama, neso hamasmi, nmeso aththa) - lesa ganna lesa.

namuth upan gei dosaya prabala bawaya handa,
pin kalath pawkalath, dhyanan waduwath, mama mage athmaya lesa ganie.
enam lokaya thulamai, 
awdiyawen galaweemak natha.

me swabawaya dana ganne wishesha nuwankin
-lokoththara samma dittiya (+ 7 other factors)

lokothra samma dittiya awaboda kara ganeema sadaha
laukika samma dittiya awashayai.
e nisa pina awashayai. ( kaththabban kusalan bahun)
enam minimum qualification eka laukika samma dittiyamai.

laukika samma dittiya innakota , prakshawena kalakirima thulin
lokoththara sammadittiya sadaha uthsahayan athi wei.

>> mama ho wena kenekuta karadara nowena akarayen jeewithaya aran yatha uthui

ex:
lassana gagak galagena yanawa

dan gana galaka happenawa
wathura dishawa wenas wela turn wenawa 
ethkota aawaata hadenawa (siya suliya)
gaga parana widihata giyata dan diya suliya wate tiyena ewa adala gannawa.
dan me diya suliyata ahuwenawa wage thamai. (mama , mage athmaya kiyala gaththu thana)
namuth gagama thamai pawathinne ( sabawata pawatinne anithya wechcha anathma wechcha swabawaya)
awata tiyena skanda wala gateema hetuwen ( gange dahara thula wenas akara athi wela , diya suliya wage haduna ganeemak enawa)

galala gaga - sabaa lokaya (anithyai, dukai, anathmai)
diya suliya - mage lokaya ( nithyai, sukai, athmai)

budda wachanaya - yankinchi samudaya dhamman, sabbanthan niroda dammanthi
(yamak athi unada, ethiwechcha thanama nirodha wei)

enam api ipadenawa kiyala kiana thana, dharmayedi nirwachanaya wenne
hodin gaburin kalpana kaloth, hata noganna bawai.
meyata anuppada nirodhaya yai kiyana labe.

ex:

duka - kotas 3i
--dukka dukka (kayata manasata danena duka, oluwe kakkuma..etc)
--wiparinama dukka (wenasweeme duka)
--sankara duka (me sasane witharai pawathinne, pancha upadana iskandaya nisa hata ganna duka)

kamatahana-
anithya bawa dakeema thamai wenna oni
enam pancha upadana iskandayata ena sama aramunak ma anithya bawa dakima.

hageemak ekka api purudu wela tiyenne wena wenama dakinna puluwan kiyala.
100km kiwwahama eliye tiyena durak kiyala hageemak apithula athi wenawa.
100 km කිවිවත් හැඟිමක් පමනයි එකම හැඟිම දෙවරක් එන්නෙ නැහැ.හැගිමට නමක් දිල ලෝකයේ පවතින දෙයක් කරල භෞතික දෙයක් හා තැනක් දල.
නොපවතින සිතක් තුන් කාලයක් දිල කරපු වැරද්ද වටහාගත යුතුයි.
අවකාශය කිවිවත් හැගිමක්.ලොකයක් කිවත් හැඟිමක්.
4 මහ ගති ය පවා හැගිමක් භාහිර ස්ථානගත කරල නාමකරනය නිසා.
(patavi,apo ,thejo,wayo) - ehema kiyala  hagenneth hithen mai.
නාමය දැන් තුන්කල් පවතින රුපයක් බවට පත් කරල. එක දිගටම පවතින මෙයයි සමිමුති සත්‍ය මෙිවා ලොකයේ පැවත්මට මිසක් නැවැත්මට නොවෙිමයි.
හැඟිම කියන්නෙත් යමක් කලේ සංනිවෙිදන අවශ්‍යතාවය නිසයි.
යමක් බවට පත් කරල නිවන හෝ බුද්ධ කිවත් එහෙමයි.යමක් නමි අප්පමාන වෙන්න බැහැ.මෙම ස්වාභාවය ඉක්මවල.
කරන්නෙක් කරවන්නෙක් ඇතිවුනෙත් එහෙමයි.
මුලාවෙි තරම කොහොමද මෙි සියල්ල ඉක්මවා යා යුතුයි.
පැනිරහ පොතක  ලියන්නබැහැ.සාපේක්ෂකත්වයෙන් පමනයි කලහැක්කෙ.
හැඟම පවා ආධාරකයක් ලෙස ගෙන කථාකරන්නෙ.
නිවනට  වචන නැහැ.එක තැනකට කොටුකරගෙන ලං කටෙන්ම ගොඩවිමකින් තමයි නාමපද  කුියා පද ඉක්මවා යන්නෙ.
සියලු මුලිවන් ඉක්මවා යා යුතුයි.

sitha kiyana ekata isthira thanak na, (apita hithunata mole kiyala)
sitha nopawathana lahu pariwathanaya wena deyak.

අපේ අරමුණුවල කොටස් 02 ක්  තියෙනවා, ඇස් 02 ක වහගෙන ඛැලුවිට වටපිටාවෙි හැම දෙයක්ම තියෙනවා කියන හැඟිමත් එක එක දේවල් සිහිවන ගතියත් යන ධර්මතා 02 ගැන තමයි කිවෙි,
හරියට ආනාපාන සතිය වැඩුවොත් ඔය ගති 02 න්ම හිත මුදවා ගන්න පිලිවන්.
ආශ්වාස ප්‍රශ්වාස ,සතිනිමිත්ත යන කරුනු අත නොහැර වැඩිය යුතුයි,
දැනෙන බව හා හිතෙන බව නතර වි සිත සමාධිගත වෙයි.

samadi gatha una kiyanne - eliye tiyenawa kiyana gathiyai, sitha athulen katha karana gathiyai nathi wela giyahama.
anapana sathiya waduwoth, hama tissema nahaye eka purukak wadipura dannenawa. ethenata hitha tiya gannawa
hitha e mohothe tiya gannawa.
meka hariyata kaloth sitha wena aramunu walata yanne na.
15 minutes withara idala,
daham karunu gana wisthara kalpana karanne.
me magin pancha neewarna yatapath karanna me sathiya udaw wenawa.


sithata hama dissema hithenne mama hari kiyala
ekata hethuwa athma swabawaya nisa.

enam

enam asa hata gena nirudda una kiyala dana ganna oni.
anith paththen
pudgalekuta hata gaththu aha tiyenne hithe bawa shakshath karanna oni

aththa thathwaya thamai
asa hata ganna thama nirudda wenawa
namuth

menna me dekama sakshath karanna oni.
methana athmayak panawanna bari bawa dakinna oni.

ex:
oyage gedara lassana nam sathutak enawa kiyanna

wali godak gaththoth,
wali ate ate ain kaloth goda na 
enam meka imagination / hageemak (sangyaawa)bawa.

e hageemata nama/kriya padayak dapuwahama thamai deyak bawata pathwenne.
athin allala thadai kiyala gaththu hageema ta thamai ne api wasthu washayen namak denne.

ex: as deka wahagen pansalak allalapuwahama , danena thada gathiya ne ahu une. pansala nevi patavi yane ahu une.
e hageemata namak/kriyawak dammama thamai wasthu washayen enne.

ethkota me hageema kiyanne pansalada ?
ehenam hageema kiyanne mokadda ?
its only a sanyaa, sensation ekak (chathanawak), set of information withrai.
when we add 
nama or kriyawak, eya deyak, thanak, kenek bawata pathwenawa.

pansala istirai kiyana hageemak enne me deka ekata ganna handa.
hageemak+namayak athi thana isthreera lesa pawathina bawa.

meka aththak kiyala piligathoth -> bahira deyak tiyenawa piligannawa ,eka balanna kenek methana innawa kiyala.

ethkota hageema kiyanne 
bahira pena wasthuwa da ? (ehenam ena okkoma hageem pansala wage wenna epai)
naththam mamada ? (mama athi une pansala eliye istira widihata gaththu nisa ne )

e dekama nevi nam

meka athi wenne koheda ? sithe
namuth sitha kiyanne nopawathina dharmathawak ( enam wegayen wenas wana dharmathawayak)
ehenam hageem kiyala dharmathawayak isthira washayen pawathinna ba.
ehenam nathi hageemak padanam karan 
pansalai , mamai athiwena eka mayawak.
avidyawa hinda thamai meka une.

sabbe pruthakjana.. unmaththakaa.... 

ex:
onna sidney kiyana nama padaya ahuna

thanak bawata path una gaman -> durak athi una
durak nisa kalayak athi wenawa. (kalayata sapekshawa dura pawathina nisa)
namuth  dharmaya akalikai. (athi wena thanama nathi wenawa nam kalayak pawathinne bane)
enam ihatha karunu dharmayen awabodakara gaththu wahama , 
siyalla awdiyawen siduwana bawa therenawa ( awiddya pachcha sankara)
meya awaboda karagena karma sakas nowana lesa sathutin jeewath wemu.

karma sakas novi jeewithaya pawathwagena karaganeema , anithya therum ganeemai.

 
=============================== 6/12/2020 udaya-waya part 1-----------------------------------

pancha upadana iskandaye udaya waya (udaya waya -nyanam - pachan upadana iskandaya athi weema saha nathi weema) 

upakalpanaya - imagination ( sithin sitha ganeema)
upakalpanayakin thorawa sathya darshanayata yanna puluwan.

sathwayata ( enam mata) duka prakatai. ( harima purudui , kaika ho manasika peedanaya)
menna me dekatama eha giya dukak thamai sanskaara duka. eka apita prakata na.

api katha kala 
duka - kotas 3i
--dukka dukka (kayata manasata danena duka, oluwe kakkuma..etc)
--wiparinama dukka (wenasweeme duka)
--sankara duka (me sasane witharai pawathinne, pancha upadana iskandaya nisa hata ganna duka)

ada api prakata duka atharala , prakata nowana duka gana thamai katha karanna hadanne.

sankara duka (sakas karagath) - apita prakata nowana duka mokadda ?

pancha upada iskandaye hata ganeema duka enam ( budun deshana kala widihata pancha upadana iskandaa dukka)

pancha upadana isknandaya hata ganeema (sankara duka) hadune kohomada ?

ayathanayaka krikarithwayath ein nidahas weematath.  dana, daka ( jaanatho, passatho) yuththe kumakkda - pancha upana iskandayai.

ex: 
koppayak penena thana , pancha upadana iskandaya mokadda ?

koppaya kiyana roopayata , sanyyawak damma
koppaya mata hamu une sanyaawa haraha.
enam hama roopayak ma hambenne sanyaawa harahamai. (ekinekata prathyai)
me okkoma dana gaththe wynanayen.

me isknada 5 thamai api mechchara kal katha kale.

sanyyawa koppaya lesa ganna eka waradi pili ganeemak.

hithanna api koppaya hodatama kudu karanawa , dan koppaya tiyenawada ?
dan natha.
enam koppaya niruddai, enam koppaya atheethayata gihin.
hatagena pawathina deyak thamai warthamanaya lesa api gaththe.
ehema ganna hethu une, atheethaya saha anagathaya tibunui kiyla wishwasa karapu nisa.
prasent ganna nam past and future nathuwa. ( ekama welawe sidda unata)

kudu kalata passe koppe tiyenawada ? eka atheethaye ne.
atheethaye sathya ( koppaya tiyena bawa soyala) wadak na. eka iwarai.
anagathaya hambela na (ekath hoyala wadak na)
pachchupannaye tiyenne ( warthamana mohothe) tiyena monawada ?
ara koppaya hadichcha dhathu tika witharai.
kudu karana process eka aye aye karagena giya hamath, dhathu nanathwayak witharai hambenne.

eken ekak gamu.
patavi sanyyawa ( thada isbawaya) ekata adala 
(wedana,sanya,sankara,wynana) nama dharama tika tiyenawa
metika okkoma sankalpa.(mental projections)
enam witharka kirimak witharai. (hitha hitha inna eka witharai.)

eka prathyakshayak nevi. (jaanatho passatho dekama thulin  meka dakinna oni ) (dana gannawa, daka ganna)
enam hethuwai , hethuwen upan palayai dakinawa ta thamai prathyaksha wenawa kiyanne. meka sankalpayak nove(kalpanawak nevi)

sankalpayai prathayakshayai athara wenasa mokadda ?

meka api balanna oni ( api hithena widhata nevi budun deshana kale)
budun deshana kala
pattichcha sammupaddye arya niyaya,
"imasmin sathi idan hothi" - hethuwa nam woo meya athi kalhi, palaya nam woo meya athi wei.
"imasmin asathi idan nahothi " - hethuwa nam woo meya nathi kalhi, palaya nam woo meya athi nowei.

koppaya kudu karagena kudu karagena gihin pataviya labuna kiyana eka pattichcha samuppannada ?

koppaya kudu karagena gihyama ithuru une patavi.
ethakota dan
koappaya nathi kalhi pataviya atha ? meka pattichcha samuppana da ? meya budu wadanata ekaga na.
enam pachcha samuppadha niyayata ekaga novei.

enam apita me awith tiyenne sithiwillak witharai.(shdudashshataka kiyala gaththath ekath sanyyawak, apita hethu palaya hambela na neda)
enam apita prathyakshayak wela natha. (parathyakshaya wenna nam meka pattichcha samupanna wenna oni)

mechchara kalayak budda wachanaya mekai kiyala , eka ekkana thama thamun ge matha idiripath kala
budun wachana , athak-kawa-charai (tharka kara kara hasireema awasha noviwei.)(nisha chara - rathiye hasiren, wana chara - wanaye hasirena)
namuth patticha samupanna apply karana widiha therum nogena 
wena wena matha samaja gatha wela
budda wachahraya niyama arthya yatapath wela , edineda katha karana bashawen dharmaya samaja gatha wela.

hari budda wachanaya hoyanne kohomada ?
chathurarya sathya ekaga, pachchicha samuppada niyayata ekaga wiya uthui.

koppaya kadala -> patavi patichcha samupanna naththam , kohomada meka api explain karanne

experiment : "koppaya" kiyala awe kohomada ?

lokaya hadune (adhyathmika,bahira ayathana nisa)
patavi, apo ,thejo, wayo kiyana sobawayan
upanayen hata gaththu ekak. (methana upadaya focus karanna , api dan tiyena danuma bidinna hadanne )

(maha haththi padopama suthraya, mujjima nikaye, muula pannasakaya)

patavi gaththo ehema , budun wisthara karala tiyenne (what is patavi ?)

"ajjaththan pachchaththan , kakkalan karigathan upaadinnan" - methana upaadinnan kiyana eken thamai focus karanna oni, mokada eken thamai apita patavi, apo ,thejo, wayo kiyana sobawayan hamu wenne.

apo walata tiyenne : "ajjaththan pachchaththan , apo gathan upaadinnan"
wayo walata tiyenne : "ajjaththan pachchaththan , wayo gathan upaadinnan"
thejo walata tiyenne : "ajjaththan pachchaththan , thejo gathan upaadinnan"

ajjaththan - adyathmika (thama ge yai ganena)
pachchaththan - prathyen upan
kakkalan - gorosu
karigathan - thada
upaadinnan - alla ganeema (dharmathayak)(meka pudgala bawayen ganna ba)
(maha haththi padoma suthraya / look at dhamma dinna theraniya discussion)


dan chathanaham bikka we kamman wadami ( chethanawa nisa karmak hata gannawamai)(mama pawathinnama oni)
namuth mewa chathana novie. (budun haduna gaththu ekak, personal desires nevi.)



koppaya kudu karala thamai api me dhathu nanathwayata awe.(patavi apo thejo wayo)
dathu nanathwayata apita hambune menna me upadinaya haraha.

methana dhathu nanathwaya kiyanne deyak,pudgalayek wasthuwak novei. eka manatasata ena gathi sobahawayak.
meka apita ahu wennema upadinayak haraha witharamai. ( maha haththi padomaya suthraya balanna detail explanation)

upadanaya kiyanne pattichcha samuppadaye kotas 12n ekak. ( last eka, thanha pachchaya uppadinnan)
me lokaye (budun wahanse kenek sitiya ho natha)
me lokaya pawathina swabawaya, pattichcha sammuppada dharmayata anukulai. (budun meka pennuwe me lokayen ethara weema sandai)
enam me lokaya kiyana eka awaboda karagena loken nidahas weemai.

enam me upadanaya weema haraha dakapu koppaya , tibbeth hithe pamanai.
hithe athi wana ageema , hithen dakeemak witharai, enam eka me lokaye swabawayak.
me lokaya apita ahu wena widihak.

me widiha athule prathyakshayak tiyenna ba. mokada api meka hithen hithapu (sankalpanawak) deyak nisa.
prathyaksha wenna nam, budu rajanan wahanse deshana kale kohomada
kiyala soyanna oni.

mese soyanna patan ganna oni kama -> yoniso manasikarayai.
yoniso manisakaraya diunu weemen praknyawa upadi

ema praknya asen thamai api dana gannai daka ganna oni (jaanatho , passatho)
enam diunu wechcha yoniso manisakaraya praknyawai. (enam wynanayen nevi, me lokada sakinne wynanayen)

wynanaya kiyanne sithak
praknyawa kiyanne chithasikayak

sitha and chithasikayak deka venasa mokadda ?
ex: sitha aroopi dharmayak.
sitha and chithasiyak ekinekata saha jaathai ( ekinekata prathyai)
sithe hata ganna gathi chithasikayak widihata adun wanna puluwan (52 tiyenawa)
ex: sitha mallak nam ekata dana dewal chithasikayak

dan parana example eka gaththama

koppaya kiyapu deta thamai api thanha kale. (lokaya thulin upadanaya nisa thanha kale)
namuth budda wachanaya (pattichcha sammuppadaya anuwa)
wedana pachchaya thanha
thanha pachchaya upadanan

api koppeta asa kala, enam tiyena bandayakata thamai asa karala tiyenne.
api start ekema koppaya isthirawa tiyena bawa dana genamai me asawa athi une.
me nithya bawa gaththe anithya sanyaawa nodanna nisa.

wedana (sensation)
-sapa wedana
-duka wenda
-sapa duka wedana 

menna me sensation eka handa thanhawak athi unata , api gaththe koppaya handa thanhawa athi una kiyala

awidya pachchaya sankara  ( dharmaya nodanna kama nisa sankara (sakasweema) athiuna ( mathu wipaka pinisa karmayak sakas una)
sankara pachchaya wynanam ( enam karmaya handa wipaka wynayaak bihi una , prathisandi sitha  )
wyn-yaana pachchaya naama roopa ( wynanaya tiyena nisa nama roopa athi una)
naama roopa pachchaya salayathana ( nama roopa nisa ayathana 6 pahala wenawa)
salayathana pachchaya passa (ayathana 6 haraha sparshaya siduwenawa)
pass pahchaya wedana ( sparshaya nisa sensation ekak athi wenawa) (weemak daneema)(sensation of something happening)
wedana pachchaya thanha (sensation nisa thanhawa)(internal sensation eka sathwa pudgalayo (kamaththa/akamaththa/madya) lesa sakas karagaththa (aathma washayen gena)

me ekama sensation eka api athma washayen gena sapa, duka, upeksha lesa alenawa (thanha karanawa)
namuth ekama sensation eka.

thanha pachchaya upadanan ( melesa hada gaththu sapa/duka/upeka thanhawa, thadin allagannawa)


api hithuwata koppayata thamai upadana une kiyala , 
aththatama upadanaya une 
sparshaya nisa athi unu wedanawata.

ex:
1st example : lokaye tiyena dewal walata thamai api upadanaya wenawa kiyala lokaya piligannawa , habai eka ehema nevi 

normal people news paper ekak kiyawanakota , wenne ahen dakima pamanai.
namuth wiwida news osse wiwida sanya enawa.
ex: earthquake in lanka
another topic , all people in nz given bonuses.
another topic , climate change rally is happening.

me thunen apita apita awe roopa sanyaa witharai. me roopaya chakkuwe gatila sparshayak manase gata gaththa
hariyata nikan bird kenek aththaka wahuwahama , eyage shadow eka polowe watuna wage . dekama wenne ekata.

 me sparshaya nisa apita ekama widihe wedanawak (hama tissema wipaka wedanawak, upeksha wedanawak)
 karmaya nisa athi wechcha ayathanaya (methana nam chakkuwa) sama witama upekshai. 
 , meka manatasa aluth wedanawak , onna dan manasa simulate una ( hariyata kurulla ge shadow eka polowata watuna wage)
polawata (manasa) aththata roopa samaga gatimak na.
asata roopa wage , manata prathya wenne dhamma (manasata gochara wana sithuwili, aroopi)(kalpa 91ka details eyata ganna puluwan)(meka nikan previous experiance details) - dhamma gana pasuwa detail katha karamu.

manasa , me apu aluth wedanawa , previous experiance attract karanna hakiyawa tiyenawa. e anuwa  manasa+dhamma nisa mano wynaana upadinawa) e nisa api wynaayen aduna 
gannawa sapa,duka,upeka wedanawak kiyala.
namuth e kriyawa manasema iwarai.
namuth e bawa bodanna nisa
bahira wasthuwen awa kiyala gannawa, naththam ara aththa bird handa athi una kiyala hitanawa.
eka waradi piliganimak.

kawadawath manase ekak bahirata danna ba.
 

2nd example : meka thawa akarakin dakin wa kiwwa

roopayak roopayak pasa balana wita sakas wena chakku wynaanaya wenas nisa, eya anithya yai lokaya pili gannawa 
onna fan eka baluwa , cupboard eka baluwa , biththiya baluwa,
api hithanawa cupboard eka balathdi fan eka nirudda wela kiyala 
e nisa fan eka anithyai kiyala api hithanawa
namuth e kramaya waradie.
(mekata hethuwa thamai , lokaye pawathina dewal isthirai kiyala gaththu nisa)(atha ho natha yana sankalpaya tibba nisa)atha/natha sankalpaya lokayata  aithi deyak
budun deshana kale lokoththara dahamak.
patichcha samuppada niyaaya anuwa 
atha ho natha kiyana antha walata giye na
kiwwe meya athi kalhi meya we. (hethu pala dahama)

enam hethuwai palayai dekama ekatama pawathie.
enam lokayata budun kiyana de hambu wela na , patichcha samuppadaye hulagawath wadila na.
enam kawadawath niwan dakinna ba.

enam me dharmaya dakinna puluwan prakyawa uppadda ganeemen pamanamai.
enam jaanatho passatho wenne prakyawen misak wynaanayen novei.


----------------------------------------------------------------------
ehema gaththama

asa, kana , nasaya, diwa ,shareeraya kiyana ayathana 5 gaththahama. manata starting point ekak .
mana eka parashawikai, eyata thaniyen sparshaya gattanaya karanna ba. enisa anith 5hen thamai start karanne.
e nisa manasa appattikai kiwwe e nisai. (thaniyen gattanaya kala nohaka)

roopa = sani+dassanai (penawa)
anith siyaluma dewal ani dassanai
(asa,kana, shabdaya, me siyalu de ani dassanai)
asa kana nasaya diwa shareeraya sathpatigai (gateem sahithai) enam
roopa, shabda ganda rasa pottabba sathpatigai

dhamma appatigai - gattema walin thorai
manath appatigai.
enam mana+dhamma dekama gaththath appatigai and ani dassanai. 
meka gaburata katha karanna oni.
