questions deka

1) adaraya kiyana eka aleemak da

adaraya kotas dekai
ragayen/thushnawen hata ganna adaraya (chanda ragaya)(akusalayak)
ragayen thorawa, mythreeyen , karunawa dayawen hata ganna adaraya. (kaththu kamyatha chandaya)(kusalayak) (this also taken as kaththu kamyatha kusalak chandaya)

ragika hageem ganata tiyena kamaththa - pancha kamaya lesath
darmayata tiyena kamaththa - eimukkthi kamai (keles walin midima)

dharmayen balapuwahama 
prathipadawa ismathu wenna oni. (margayakin yuktha weema thamai prathipadawa kiyanne)(sowan margaya ho, aryashtankin margayakin yuktha wenna oni) enam ethara weema sanda , nathara weema ho pawath weema novie.

lokaye thula upaya , upadanaya, abiniwesaya, wini-badda pawathi.

upaya -lanwenawa
upadanaya -allagannawa
abiniwesaya - padinchi wenawa
wini-badda - badda weema (badeema)

mese wenne abhinandathi kiyana gunaya handa.
abhinandathi - sathutu wenawa
abhiwadathi - kiya kiya sathutu wenawa.
ajjo saya sittathi - ethula baha gena innawa

me 3 nisa thamai uda dewal pawathi.
eken thamai sakkaya dittiya athi wenne
ethkota lokaye athi wenne sansaraya goda nagenne oka handa.

me chanda ragaya tiyenne ape manasa thula.

ammai daruwai athara tiyena senahasa (sasara pawathweema sanada karana kusalayak) (awidyawa mulika wela tiyenne)yahapathak sidu unath niwan awabodayak na
chanda ragaya athi wenne hithe.manase me gathiyata 
udaw karana isbawayak thamai roopa wala tiyenne. (sanyojaneeya dharma)

ex:
rathu kannadiyena balanakota, okkoma rathui. habai bahira paththa, habai aha paththa rathu unada?
bahin apita penne warnaya witharai, ehenam roopaye yatharthaya warnayai.
enam pudgalayek barin upadinna ba.
ewita pugala jathi sobawayak athi wela na.
 jathiyak naththam siyalu keles duru wenawane.
 jathi -> jara -> maranen duru wela.

 me warna satahana pilisida dakkoth( sakyen thorawa awabodayen dakkoth). meka hariyata dakkoth ewa keles nevi.
 warna satahana kiyana eka keles nevi.
 keles hadenne hithe.
 bahira pudgalayek kiyala athi wunu hageema
 eka penawada ? 
 namuth prathipalaya widihata eliyen pudgalayek penawa. ( mehema wenne yathaarthya gana nodanna nisa )
 sathwa pudgala bawaya manasata hambawenne , hagaweemak widihata 
 ethkota bahira pudgala sobawayak athiwenawa ( nodanna kama hinda)
 sathwa pudagala nowana dathuwa prakata weemen, methek kal tibba ape huruwa gewila, aththa danagena waradi purudda ain karala/niwala danawa.
 
 
 duka pilisida dakeema = roopaya pilisinda dakeema
 roopaya pilisinda dakeemenma niwana awaboda karanna puluwan.
 
meka awaboda karaganna 
warna satahana keles nevi kiyana waga dakinna oni. (meka pudgalayek kiyala gaththoth ahuwela)
bahira sathwa pudgala kiyana hageema penne na.
habai
prathipalaya bahirin penawa.

e wage bahira roopayak arabaya prapancha yedunahama roopaya --> sathwa pudgalayek kiyala hamuwenawa.

keles ipadunata (waradi hageem) passe, 
bahira already tiyenawa kiyala hageema ipadila.

 
ex:
tv tiyennema warna satahan witharai, namuth api kochchara pudgala sathwa lesa gannawada.
me warna satahan warna sahan widihata dakinna puluwan nam, api roopaya thulin nirodaya awaboda karala wiwarai.
methana sanskara ismathu wenawa. ( yamak nevei,namuth yamak bawa ismathu weemak)

duka pilisinda dakkinna
roopaya pilisinda dakinna 



2) asangya thalaya roopa witharak pawathinne kohomada

jeewtiha indriye kotas dekai 
naama jeewitha indriya
roopa jeewitha indriya

ex:
gahak gaththaoth , roopa jeewitha indriyak pamanai,
wynaanayak na
ayu kalayak pawathinawa
ipedenawa marenawa
roopaye wahareema wenawa
sithak na

roopawachara dyanayedi , sithe dos dakala sitha nathuwa hitiyanam hodai kiyala aramunak gannawa. sitha kere kalakirila sitha nathi weema pinisa dynaya wadanawa.
ethkota thamai asanya thalaye upadinna.
eka abawya isthanayak. (guna darma wadiya nohaki, niya kes wawei( uthuja roopa)( kawruth buddhist methana yanne na)
mekata kiyanne upadinna hodama nathi thanak lesa. (ashta dushtakshanayen ekak)

dhanayak yanu, pancha neewarana balen yatapath karanawa. ethkota dhyana anga mathu wenawa ,
withakka
wichara
weethi
suka
ekaggatha
(1 dyanaya) yanu menna me kusala sith awasthawa, 



sitha misa kaya nathi bamba lowa 4ki
sitha nathi kaya pamanak athi ek thalayaki (asangya talaya,)
out of 31k thalaya remaining thala wala (26k) sitha and kaya dekama pawathi.

31k thalaya 
eka irak and eka handak pawathina loka 31. ehenam naththam sakwalak.

wokaara - iskanda
eka wokaara - 1 asanya thalaya
chathu wokaara - sitha misa kaya nathi loka 4
pancha wokaara - ithiri 26

roopawachara dyaana wadala sitha wiragi lesata bawana karanawa.
dyana shaktiye balayen asanya thala wala pahala wenawa.
sitha na kalpa 500 ayusha
kalpa 500 iwara unahama dyana shakthiye tiyena hakiyawa anuwa
roopawachara brahma lokeka nawatha pahala wenawa.

lokaye tiyena onima deyak thula tiyenawa prathya shakthiyak. ( pattana-prakaranaye thamai meka wisthara karanne)
sithakin anuthuruwa thawa sithak athiweeta - ananthara prathya shakthiya hethu wenawa
sithai chaithasikai athara tiyenne - sahajaatha prathya shakthiya (ekata ipadenawa kiyana eka) + samprayuktha prathya shakthiya (ekata mix wena )
onima ekak aramunu wenawa kota tiyenne - arambana prathya shakthiya
ekinekata udaw karana (rooya nisa asa athi weema) - anyamanya shakthiya
naamayai roopayai athara tiyenne  - wippayuktha prathya shakthiya 

me wage prathya shakthi 24k tiyenawa , wenama detail katha karanna oni subject ekak.


===================================================20-12-2020=========================================
chathurarya sathya simple lesa.
>dukka arya sathya 
>samudaya arya sathya
>niroda arya sathya
>niroda gamini patipada sathya.

arya sathya kiyanne ( marga pala labana uthuman / aryan wahanse kenek dakina widiha) - samma dittiya / pryaknawa awadi karaganeema.
habai meya mama dakina konawa nevei. ( sakkaya dittiya).
mama dakina widiha sasarata yana widihai.
aryan wahanese balana widiha  yanne sasaren eliyata.

oppu karanna yanne api :
Penena de thula nowa , nopenena de thula saba sathya pawathi. ( sammuthiye nowa , paramarthye ma sathya pawathi)


1) **dukka arya sathya** ( aryan wahanse kenek wisin duka dakina widiha)
meya kaikawa ho manasikawa danena dukak nevi.
example : pancha upadana iskndaye sadeema me wage dukak ( mind or body cant sense this)

jathi , jara, marana , soka , paridewa ( haiyen ka gaha gaha duk wenawata ) , dukka (kayata athi wena domnasa) , domanassa ( hithin athiwena domnasa)
upaayaasa ( sihi nathi weema / adika wehesa) -- me siyaluma de kayatai, mansatai danena dewal.

namuth 
"sakiththena pancha upadana iskanda dukka" - kayatai , manasastai nodanena dukak thamai me pancha upadana iskandaya kiyana eka.
meka thamai sasarata hethu wana duka.

kayatai , manasatai athiwana duka , sasara tibena kan pawathi.
sasara athi wena duka pancha upadana isknaya pawathinam pawathi
enam sasara nima kireema sanada pancha upadana isknaye, aththa athi satiyen dakinna oni.
yatharthaya dakinna oni.

 
වයලිනයයි,බෝ එකයි,දක්ෂ වාදන ශිල්පියයි එකට එකතු වෙලා තමයි සංගිතයේ රිදමි එක සකස් කලේ 
එතන රුපය සතර මහ භුතයි.සිතේ වින්දනය. වෙිදනාවයි ඒක හඳුනාගැනිම සංඟාවයි.ඒ ගැන කල්පනාකිරිම චෙිතනාව හෙවත් සංඛාරයි
දැනගැනිම විඤ්ඤාණයයි.මෙි ගොඩවල්  පහටමයි මම මගේ කියන්නෙ.ඇහුණා කිවෙත් ඒකටමයි.ඉතින් ඒ හඬට වයලින් හඬ කිවෙත් මමමයි.
ඇත්ත කථාව හඬ වයලිනයට අයිති නැහැ.
බෝ එකට අයිතිත් නැහැ.වාදකයාට අයිතිත් නැහැ. ඒ ශබිදය හේතු නිසා හටගත්තා හේතු නැතිවනවි ටනැතිවන අනිත්‍ය වුත් අනාත්මවුත් දහමක් පමණයි හේතුඵලයක්.මට අයිති නැහැ

e wagema thamai , pancha upadanaya iskndayath haduna kiyala apita therenne na , hethuwa kaaika and maanasika wedanawak nowana nisa. ( api me eka dukka arya sathya di katha kala)
mihirak lesa gaththu we sanyawa, widinna aasa kireema thamai thanhawa. (chanda ragaya)
e hadata alenawa, ehema naththam handa(sound) nikuth karapu deta alenawa.
namuth meka hethu nisa hatagaththu palayak.
api thamai mekata winawe hada kiyala aithiyak pavara dunne, e nisa handata asa unu nisa weenawata asa una.

ex: 

ballek e dannadak udin yanakota wathura diha balanawa.
ballek innawa kiyala penawa
wathure ballek hitiya kiyala dakina niyaaya hari da ?
balla dakinawa wathure ballek innawa kiyala 
api dakinawa wathurre ballek na kiyala , kokada hari ?

normally ape danuma anuwa apita hithenawa ballek hitiye na kiyala 
ethkota eka hari da ?

dan wathure ballek hitiye na kiyala gaththkoth ( ballek innawa kiyana eka kiyawenwa, api sapekshawa katha karana nisa) ( nathi wenna nam atha pawathinna oni)
enam
niwaradi uththaraya balla hitiye na kiyana eka nevi.
or wathure ballek hitiya kiyana ekath nevi.

baleema hinda prathibimbayak sakas una
niwaradiwa dakkoth prathibimbayak kiyala , balalla prathicharayak dakwanne na. ( ballage nodanuwath kama nisai, buranne, danuma madi kama)

ewagema minisath , prathibimbayak kiyala dana gaththu thanadi , api eyata abarana paladanna yanne na.
apita kawada hari awaboda karaganna puluwan unoth
asai+ wynyanayai + roopayai ekathu wechcha nisa api me lokaya dakke kiyala.
ara weenawe handa wage
ballage prathi bimbaya wage 
apita pene, roopa hariyata dakkoth , thamai api aththatama dakinawa kiyala kiyanne.
namuth normally hithenne
ahata pena roopa tibba kiyala 
weenawe handa aith weenawata kiyala
wathure ballek hitiya or na kiyala . ( me dakama waradie)
niwaradi karanaawa dakka nam aithiyak denne na.
e hata gaththu de 
mama ho
mata aithie kiyala ganne na
namuth
ahen roopa dakina wita, e sakas wechchi de api hithanawa mama kiyala.

ahen roopayak dakka kiyana thana hata ganne karana 5k
roopa,wedana, sanya , sankara , wynaana kiyala.

roopa = sathara maha dathun gen hata gaththu bawa.
wedana = hatagaththu bawa prakata wenawa windanayakuth ekka
sanya = haduna ganeema
sankara = e gana kalpana karanawa
wynaana = e anuwa dana ganeema.


me hata gaththu 5ta tiyenne,  mama thula kiyala, mama hithanawa.
e thula mama kiyala kenek innawa kiyala hithanawa
eka mage, mata aithie kiyala hithanawa.

namuth hata gaththu 5 hethu nathi unahama nathi wela yanawa
kawru hari hithuwoth meka tiyena deyak/ pugalayek/ thank kiyala waradi dushtriyakata yanawa.

melesa athi wana duka , awaboda karaganeema dukka arya sathyai. 



me widihata asa+roopaya+ wynaanaya ekathuweema 
nisa hata gaththu karanaa 5 (pancha upadana isknadaya) , mama, mage, mata aithi deyak lesa gannawa
namuth hata gaththu de nathi wela  yanawa, wenas wenawa mokada mewa okkoma hethu hisa hatagaththu palayak.

me wiparinamayata path wena nisa,
soka paridewa duk sowabawaya hata gannawa.

me duk hata ganna akaraya therum ganna nam, api dana ganna oni "siduwana akaaraya pilibada danuma"
meka dana ganeemen, 
duka hata ganeemata hethuwoo mamathwaya duru wenwa. mamathwaya duru wenakota 
athi weemata puluwan dukka domanassa upayasa heena wela duru wela yanwa (ek-los ginna duru wenawa)

me samma dittiyai. (hari dakma/ niwaradiwa dakina widiha)

duka pilibada awabodaya dukka arya sathya lesa api hadunwanawa.

   

ex: 
1) thoranak gaththoth , sathutu wenne thorane light paththu wenawa balala, namuth thorana randa pawathinne puwak kota sakille stability matha.
athathatama aloka rata saha katha mawa paama rada pawathinne , puwak kota sakille stability eka tiyenawa kan withrai.
namuth puwak sakilla thorana balana ayata nopene (adrushshya-manai). namuth thoranata sakilla prathyai. balannata e pathraya shakthiya nopene.
enema thorane sathya apita nopene.
enam 
Penena de thula nowa , nopenena de thula saba sathya pawathi. ( sammuthiye nowa , paramarthye ma sathya pawathi)

ex:
2) dethis kunupa walin mulma 5 thamai , thacha-panchakaya , enam 
kesa 
loma
nakaa ( niyapothu)
dantha
thacho ( hama/skin)
(hama mulika nisa thacha-panchakaya yai kiyai)

api photo ekak gaththuwahama labenne me tika, ramu karala tiyaganneth me tika
nopenena tika balanna x-ray ekak oh scan ekak ganna oni. namuth api eka ramu karala gedara ellannane na

thacha- panchakaya pawathinna nam nopenena shareeda dhathu pawathinna oni. sathya tiyenne ethana.
namuth aleema tiyenne dhrushyamaanaya (pena de) thula. eka pawathinne me adushyamana dewal nisa.
( mewa siyallama sankathai, patticha samupannai) - wenas wana sului.

mekata mulika hethuwa awidyawa (chathuraya sathya gana nodaneema) saha bawa thanhawai (athi, innawa, tiyenawa kiyana drushtiyata aleema)


manasika ho kaika nowana duka kumak da kiyala awaboda kirima - dukka arya sathya (innawa tiyenawa kenek deyak kiyala ganna bawa awaboda kireema)
esela anawabodaya nisa , gaththu deta alenawa / gatenawa (thanhawa) .
yali yalith duka hata ganne - me nisa  -- meya samudaya sathyai ( duka yali yali athi wena akaraya therum ganeema)

duka athi noweemata hethuwa haduna ganeema - niroda sathyai
duka nathi kirime margaya - niroda gamini patipada  sathya ( awidyawa duru kirima)

mata geyak tiyenawa <- dukka sathya
tiyena geta alenawa <- samudaya arya sathya
aasa kale naththam duka na <- noroda sathya
aasa nokarana margaya < - dukka niroda gamini patipada sathya




*** ahen roopa dakinakota api hithanawa , roopa tiyenawa mama dakinawa kiyala.

namuth
as deka aragena bara kalpanawaka inna welawaka as idiri pitin kenek giyoth, ohuwa nodakapu awastha tiyenawada ?
tiyenawa ne
based on science , asa+ roopa + alokaya tiyenawa nam definitly penna oni kiyala
namuth focus eka nathi nam penne nathi una.

prathibimbaya , ahe watunath penenne nathi une ahai+roopayai + wynyaanayai ekathu une nathi nisa. (sihiya na)
menna me dakeema athi wana wita 
hethu nisa dakeema athi wana bawa
enam hethu athi kalhi dakeema athiwana bawa,
nopenena nisa 
apita hagenne 
ahata tibena roopayak tibuna kiyala mai.
(hethu palaya dakala na , patticha sammupada dharma awabodaya na)

ahai+ roopayai+wynanayai ekathuwana kriyawaliya nisa roopaya athi wana bawa nodanna nisa 
hethu palaya ahuwela na.
e nisa hoda roopa nam alanewa
naraka roopa nam gatenawa.
ithin e anuwa 
therum ganne 
mama idala , mage asata roopa penawa , mage diwata rasa therenawa kyiala.


real world example:

usaawiye naduwak ahanawa
kenek car eke gihin aliyek happala.
driver kiyanawa aliya dakke na kiyala.
namuth dharamaya nodanna nadukaraya.
ahanawa kohomada mechchara loku aliyek dakke naththe kiyala. ( eya allpennithak da kiyala)

enam sammuththiye tiyena darmatha walin , me situation eka pahadili karanna ba
 
Penena de thula nowa , nopenena de thula saba sathya pawathi. ( sammuthiye nowa , paramarthye ma sathya pawathi)



---------------------------04/01/2021--------------------------------------------

drushti walata kotu weema,

podi kale onna babo billo enawa kiyathdi baya unu api, dan baya na
an e wage thamai ,
me siyalu drushti boru bawa therum giya data , wishesha nuwanak enawa ( prakshawa upadinawa)
eda niwana awaboda wela.
enam awiddyawa matha goda nagunu drushti tika galawunoth eya nidahas.
ethakota niwanata amuthuwen deyak karanna deyak na.

ewage purana karmayen apita api asa,kana,nasaya, diwa, shareeraya  mage karagena 
eka thulin karadara widinawa
eka sanasawanna hadanawa
eka thulin sathuta soyanawa

namuth me   aithi kara ganneema ain kaloth , alma nisa athi wana dewal adu karaganna puluwan
ex:
hariyata nikan thamata aithi idamak , kata hari liyala denawa wage. 

pudgala hageemak enna hethuwa thamai, methana tiyenne kriyakarithwayak pamanak bawa nothereema
ex: budun roopaya  deshana kale roppanaya kiyala. (deega nikaye maha nidana suthraya)
ruppanaya - masi maduruwekugen pawa jeewithaya wenas weeme isbawaya. ( pena pidak wage nesas wana swabawaya)
namuth api roopaya ganna gana isara lesa pawathi gana sanyawakin.
ex:
api hithanne jaathiya kiyanne uppaththiyak or prathi-sandiyak nisa athiwana kiyala ne. (dewa uppaththiya, manushya, thirisan uppaththi lesa thamai api haduna gaththe)
enam pudgala bawayen siyalu jara marana duka widinna puluwan lesa pahala weema jaathiya kiyala thamai api gaththe.
namuth budun deshanawata anuwa
pattichcha samupadaya anuwa budun kohomada jaathiya deshana kale
budun pudgalayekuge paminimak gana nevi katha karanne
sathwa pudgala panaweema nathi wenna oni 
enam anathma sobawayak pamanai budu dahama thula athiwenne
enam jaathiya athi kalhi jara marana wei.
jaathiya hethuwa bawayai

dan api bawaya , gaththe 'athi bawa' kiyala
athi kiyana hageema gaththu gaman ekata anuwa thamai karmaya sakas wenne 
athi kiyana swabawaya tiyena nisa pin paw dhyaana pawathina

me nisa atheethaya , anagathaya kiyana dewal aththatama pawathina eka lesatamai apita hagenne.
ehema isthira lesa pawathina hageema (mulu lokayak ma pawathina bawata tiyena hageema) thamai api mechcha kalayak bawaya kiyala gaththe.

e nisa widinna puluwan jaathiyak apita athi wela.
enam pudgala swabawayak hata ganeema sidu une menna me kiyala athi kiyana isawabawaye pawathma nisa . ( lokaya tiyenawa enisa api innawa)
e nisa pudgalayata sapekshawa athi/nathi dharashanayak api thula athi wela 
ekata anuwa thamai api jaathiya haduna ganne.
api gaththe e widihata

namuth bawaya , edap-pachchetha thawayen yukthai (enam pachchicha samuppadayata anukulai)
budun deshanawata anuwa 
upadanaya pawathina thek bawaya pawathi.
upadanaya naththam bawaya nohata ganie.

namuth api patticha samuppada dharmatha tika wena wenama dadiwa grahanaya kara gaththa.
dan apita penne patticha samuppadaya nevi penne.
pattichcha samuppadaya dakkoth thamai budun dakinne
namthuth api e dharmatha wena wenama dadiwa grahanaya kara gena. e nisa pachchicha sammupadaya niyayata apita miss wela.


pattichcha samuppadaya yanu hethuwa nisa palaya hata gani kiyana eka
pattichcha samuppada dharmayo kiyanne, hethuwa ho palaya lesa api ganna dharmathawayan. (ex: bawaya, upadanaya, jaathiya...etc)

e nisa apita patichcha samuppadaya penne na
namuth api hithanawa api patichcha samuppadaya niyaaya dannawa kiyala.
ekata hethuwa ,
ape concentration eka tiyenne patichcha samuppada dharmayo gana
namuth patichcha samuppada niyaaya kiyanne dharmayo nevie.
e kriyawaliya thamai pattichcha samuppada niyaya kiyanne.

ex:

3+5 = 8
ekathu kirima api podi kale igena gaththa
'+' naththam ekathu kirima kiyana niyaya 3 ho 5 ho novei.
enam pattichcha samuppada niyaya kiyanne,  hasirena  dharmayo nevi. (ex: sankara ,namaroopa, upadanaya, jaathiya...etc)

3 saha 5 hamuweema matha 8 hata noganie.
3 saha 5 ekathu kirima kiyana niyaya matha 8 hata ganie.
enam ekathu kirima kiyana prathya nisa 8 hi pawathmak atha.

maths wala api niyaaya denawa wage.
ex: agili walin wadikirima karana widiha podi ekukata kiyala denawa.

e wage 
sasara dukin ethawenna apita niyayak dunna.
namuth api niyaaya saha prathya dharmathawayan wena wenama dakinne na.

abidharamaye di
siyum widihata me niyaya pennannwa.
namuth suthra pitakaye di , meka samastha siduweem rashiyak widihata pennanawa.

ex:
pancha upadana iskandaya sama witama athiwenawa nathi wenawa, enam samawitama ikshanika maranayata pathwei.
e maranaya upan da sitama pawathina maranayak.
abhidharmayen pennuwe anna e tharam sium thathweta gihin.

me arthayama denna 
sammuthi maranayak pennuwa suthra pitakaya thulin.
enam me siyaluth pancha upadana isknadayan ge hata ganeema saha nathiweema, enam samastha siduweema rashiya
pennuwa ekak widihata
eni sa,
wipaka sith 
kriya sith
karma sith
 gana katha kala menna me rashiyak widihata aran.
 
hodin wemaseemak karanna nam, (siyum lesa dakinna nam)
abhidarmaya thulin balanna oni

namuth , udin ( bird view) ganna nam 
suthara pitakayen dharmaya awaboda kara ganna puluwan.

 
api hithanne ,
bawaya athi une jeewath weema sahada ekathu karapu dewal thadin upadana kara gaththoth thamai kiyala.
namuth upadanaya nithya novie.
eka pattichcha summuppada niyayata anuwa 
thanhawa nisa hata ganie.
upadanayata hethuwa thanhawai. (roopa,shaba,pottabba, ganda, rasa , dhamma nisa hata ganna thanha) ( me thanha mulu thun loketama podui) (kama,roopa,aroopa loka, 31 thalaya)
namuth jeewatha pawathmata ekathu gaththu ( badumuttu, relationship) nevei.
api thanaha kala kiyanne 
ekathu karagaththu wasthu kerehi athi thanhawa.

budun katha karana thanhawa eka nevi
me thun lokayatama podui
thanhawak gana thamai katha karanne.

thun lokayatama podu thanhawa ta kiyanne ni-kanthi thanha kiyala. (ni-kanthi kiyanne ithaa sulu washayen ho didulana swabawaya nathi, enam nopenena thanha, apita kelin danne na)
enam ikanda wala pawathmata athi kamaththa. anithya gana nodaneema hewath awidyawa.


ex:
kenek apayata giyath , ethana jeewath wenna thamai kamathi
ethanin marenne kamathi na
pattichcha samuppadaya deela tiyenne ethara wenna, sansara gamanen ethera wenna
namuth ekata kamathi novi
sasara gamanata kamathi weema ni-kanthi thanhawai.

idap-pachchathawayata anuwa.
meka athi une wedana nisa

ethakota kohomada wedana hata ganne.
passa pachchaya wedana

patticha samuppadayata anuwa
isparshaya nisa wedana hata ganne

ex:
ahata roopayak gateemedi e wedanawa upeksha sahagathai (sapa duk kathandara na)
habai 
chakku sampassaya nisa hata gaththu wedanawa (chakku sampassa ja wedana kiyala kiyanne ), sapa duka upeksha dharma wenawa.
enam roopa iparshaya weema nisa mano mattamen sakas karapu wedanawak habuwenawa.

menna me mano mattamen hadunu wedana thamai sapa duka upeka create karanne.
enam
bahira roopaya + manomaya roopaya (abyanthara)+ ethana wynanaya apuwahama , isparshaya hata gannawa.

ekama wedanawa nisa 
dakeema + dana ganeema dekama siduwe, namuth e deka wen wen washayen dakinne na.

wen wen washayen dakimata nam wena nuwanak, ehema naththam ehema wena bawata danumak apita tiyenna oni ( wishesha wu danumak)


ex:

lanakawe tiyenawa , 6,4 wath nodanna kenek kiyala.

meke 6 4 kiyanne mokadda ?
normal people will say apaya 4 diwya loka 6 i kiyala.
enam hoda naraka kiyala thamai meka gaththe. ( api katha karana mattama)

namuth dharmanukulawa me kathawa meetawada ehata yanawa
menatha 4 kiyanne kriyakareethwayan
ditta (dakeema) , suta (aseema) , mutha (daneema) , wynyatha (dana ganeema)
6 kiyala kiyanne , ayathana
asa , kana, nasaya , diwa , shareeraya , mana

asa -ditta
kana - sutha
nasaya,diwa,shareeraya - mutha
mana - wynyaatha

meken thamai abhidharmaya goda nageegena yanne.

ex:

nasaya saha husma ralla aithi moketada uda 4ren ?

api kiyana ashwasa prashwasa kiyana eka aithi wenne mutata

ana-pana-sathiyedi,

deeganwa assa santho
deegan assa saameethi pajanaathi.

methana pajanaathi kiyanne (prakshawen dakimata)
methana praknyawa kiyanne nuwanin dakinawa kiyana eka
namuth api dakinawa kiyanne ahen
hulan ralla ahata penne na, (penawa nam ditta wenna epai)
meka mutha ne.

namuth budun deshana karanne meka dakinna kiyala 
dakinna ahak oni ne.
budun kiyana me dakmata kiyanawa 
prakna chakchusaya kiyala. (samawitama kriyawaliyak thamai dakinne)
enam me prakna chakchusayen me kriyawaliya dana ganna eka thamai 
praknawena dakinawa kiyanne.

e kiyanne api me kriyawaliya thamai awaboda kara ganne.
namuth me dakma wynanayen karana dana ganeema nevei. ( wyn-yaanaya kiyanne dana ganeema nam, dana ganna kenek inna oni, enam sakkaya dittiya poshanaya weema pamanai wenne, wnyanaya thulin)

budun deshan karana 'dakeema' menna me sihi nuwanin dakeemai.
eya wynawata gochara nevei.

enam
wedana pachachya thanha wenna oni namuth 
api karan tiyenne roopa pachahya thanha thamai wela tiyenne 

api kamathi wela tiyenne wedanawata novei, ekata padanama lesa api hithana bahira athi wasthuwa anuwa labuna kiyala. namuth eka waradie.
mekata hethuwa , api pili ganne 
ape hithata therena de pamanamai
namuth eka nevi budun deshana kal dharmaya.

-----------------------------24/01/2021
 
bahira deyak anuwa sathutu wenne kiyala hithanne.
enam api wedaanwa athi une isparshaya nisa nevi eliye tiyena roopaya kiyala thamai api hithala tiyenne.
namuth wedanawa athi wenne sparshaya nisa kiyana eka api danne na.
bahira wasthu nisa sapa duka athi wenawa kiyala hitha gena innawa.



me sasare pawathmai, ape pawathmai dekama pawathila tiyenne menna me kiyala waradi hageema handa.
thanhawa nisa upadana nisa bawaya. (sasara gena yana bawa) - (watta mulika thanha)
ewagema
me jeewithaye pawathma sanda athi wena thanhawa ( sumudachaara thanha)

ex:
roopa passe api panna panna yanawa 
sindu ahanna asai
roopa balanna asai
kama kanna asai
pancha induran pinawanna tiyena asawa, poshanaya karanne me jeewithaya.

api hamatissema aran tiyenne bahira roopa walata tiyena thanawa

me akarayata thanhawa aaakara dekakata pawathinawa.
ekak sasarata ,ekak mage pawathmata.

budun deshana kale,
chakku sammassaja wedana
(like other 5)
enam roopaya nevi isparshaya nisa wedanawa athi wenawa kiyala.
pachchichcha samuppadaya anuwa wedanawata tiyenna idam pachchatha hethuwa thamai isparshaya

me kiyana isparshaya kotas dekai.

patiga sammassaya (ayathayan ta aramunu gateema)(ahai roopai gateema)
adhiwachana sampassaya (nama naama gateema) (manase dharmatha gateema)

me isparsha kotas deka wen karanna ba
namaya aduna ganne sanyawakin
roopaya aduna ganne namayakin

patigaya saha adiwachanaya ekenekata prathyai.
e nisa 
api connection eka pennanawa.
roopa kayee adhiwachana sammapassaya lesath
naama kayee patiga sammassa lesath 
hadunwanawa.

dan api pudgalayai, prakyawai compare karamu me deka matha idan.

pudgalayata thamai yoniso manasi karaya athi wenne 
eya pancha upadana iskandaya suwakeeyathen (mama lesa athma) gaththa.
ehema unahama galawenna bane
eken galawenna oni nisa 
meka sallatho (ulak wage), gannathoo (age ena gedi wage),roogathoo (rogayak widihata) (40 akarayak lesa pennala tiyenawa) 
widihata ganna kiyanawa.
mehema karana kota (widarshana), eyata upadinawa prakyawak.
e prakyawa thamai ethara weema karanne.
enam roopaye yatha bootha isabawaya hambuwenna eyage prakyawata.

ethara wenna hamatissema wenne prakyawen ( marga shyanayen)
namuth yoniso manisakaraya karanna puluwan pudgalayakuta.
yoniso manasikaraya karala prakyawa wadawa gena thamai samma dittiya yanna puluwan.

pancha upadana iskndayak hadenna nam monawada tiyenna oni ?

pancha upadana iskandaya hadenne me ayathana 6 haraha roopa aramunu weemen.

ayathana 6 bawitha kireemama , pancha upadana iskandaya upadeemata hethuwai.
ehi mulikama  awasthawa , apita hithata ho kayata dukak nevi. (roopaya chakkuwe gatena awasthawa)(me awasthawa galawanna ba adhiwachana sampassayen)
mokada api eka gana thama danne na. 

ex:
ada ipadichcha lamayek, hadawatha , wakugaduwa , panahali dannawada ? nane
namuth hodata jeewath wenawane

eyata wada api sanya lokayak api ekathu karan.

budu hamuduruwo deshana karanawa ,
pancha upadana iskanda dukka kiyala.


==================31/01/2021========================= (dharmaya haduna ganeema)

dharmaya gaththahama api katha karanne ape me jeewana chakraya saha apa awata athi siyalla gana.
me tiyena siyalu dathun wala muula swabawaya ( bedagena bedagena yamen) abhi darmayedi  wishthara karanawa.

dharmaya haduna ganna nam ape jeewithaya wada karana widiha gana api igena gannaoni.
gas kola jeewin hadila tiyenne kohomada kiyala balanna oni
mewa wisthara karanne abhidharmayen.
pin paw , sathwayan ge wisthara , me siyalu de.
nirwana dathuwa, lokoththara iswabawaya wisthara karanne abhi dharmayen.

mathu ipadeemak athi bawa piliganne naththam kanek
karmayata anuwa sathwaya sapa duka labana bawa piliganne naththam
apaya dwya loka athi bawa piliganne naththam
ekata hethuwa dharmaya nodanna kamai

pruthakjana lesa me aya dakwanna puluwan.
ape sithata danena , saha asu wena dharmathawayanta api arthaya lesa hadunwanawa.
artha nowana kisiwak me loke na. (sama dekama apita arthayak ganeeme hakiyawak pawathinawa.)

athi lesa hithata danena dewal athata. mewa habawata athi saha nomathi dewal tiyenawa. wadihariyakma tiyenne sathya washayen nathi dewal.

ex:
kaluware inna kenek gini pellek karakawanawa
dura sita balana kenekuta atha gini walalallak penawa
namuth tibbe gini pelellak
athi hatiyata penuna gini walallak naha
gini pellelle wegawath kama nisa tiyenawa kiyala hithuna deyak penune.

api athi widihata salakana, siyalu de.
mesaya , koppaya , balla, athaa, siyalu de gini walallu.
me onima deka muula swabawaya dathuwa (patan gaththu sobahawaya) lesa kiyanawa.
me dathuwala wegawath chalana sobawaya nisa gini walalla wage gannawa.
ewa sathya washayen nathi namuth athi kiyana hageem maathrayen athi bawata salakena dewal walata kiyanawa prakyapthi.

enam arthaya (hithata watahena de / hageema) kotas dekai 
sathya washayen naththa wu arthaya (sithata danena de)
sathya washayen aththa wu arthaya lesa

anna ehema sathya washayen athi bawa hi athi watinakama nisa , ekata api kiyanawa paramarthaya lesa ( parama arthaya)

summary :
hithata asuwana de = arthaya
arthaya kotas dekai
1) sathya washayen nathi namuth athi lesa hageem mathrayak (ikanaya thula athiwana swabawaya) athi artha - prakyapthiya (sammuthiya)
2) sathya washayen athi saha hageem mathrayak athi artha - paramarthaya.

problem 1:
 kohomada me deka wen kota haduna ganne ? 
kotas walata wen karala baliya yuthui.
wen karala balana kota nathi wenawa nam sathya washyen tiyena ekak nevi ( prakyapthiyak)
mese beda gena yanakota ithuru wana bedanna bari de (paramarthaya)

paramartha 4
chiththa 
chithasika
roopa 
nibbaana.

me muula swabawayan pilibanda satananak denna ba.
satahanak yanu ( diga, kota , kuda mahath , hada satahanak nathi bawa)
mehe satahanakin pennanna bari dewal api energy ( balawegayak / dharmathawayak lesa) hadunwanawa

ethkota 
chiththa  -> paramrtha dharmayak -> arthayak -> hithata asuwana de ehema naththam hithata danena de -> enam daneema kiyanne hithata kiyana namak -> 
hitha yanu daneemai,
daneema yanu hithai

hithata nam 10k atha - chiththan,mano, maanasaan(manasa),hadayaan (hadawatha), pandaran,mano manaayathanan,manendriyan,wynyaanam,wynyaanak kando, mano wynyaana dhathu. 

ex: 
kuburu kotana wita manussayata kiyanwa - goviya
eyama school eke ugannnanawa nam - teacher kiyanawa

ekama pudgalaya karana karya anuwa wiwida nam tiyenawa , e wagema hithatath ehemai.

hithata danena de - arthya
arthaya daneemata hethu wechchi de - aramuna kiyala kiyanawa 
aramunen thorawa arthyak pahala nove, enam sithak pahala nove.

ex:
berayakata gahana kota , bera handa athi wenawa wage
indriyan hi aramunu gatena kota wena wena sith ithaa wegayen athi wenawa.

e daneem siyallatama - api kriyawoo kiyala kiyanwa.

kriyawa penawada ? 
ex: bus eka yanwa , eka apita penne na. warnaya wenas weemak witharai, 
sammathuyedi me warnaya wenas weeme sobawaya  kriyawa lesa hadunwanawa.
paramarthayedi , indriyanhi aramunu gatena kota ewain wena wenama sith athi wei. indrayanhi aramunak gatunahama api daneemak kiyana nisa
e daneem siyallama kriyawak lesa hadunwanawa. 

ex: bera hada,
ahena wita,
ahe, kane, manase adiye aramunu gatena wita , wena wenama sith athi wenawa.
ahe sitha wenai kane sithata.
ahe kriyawaliya wenai kane kriyawaliya
me kriyawaliya api kriwak lesa hadunwanawa.

ethkota paramarthayedi , mese sithak hewath aramunu daneemak athi wana kota, e daneem kriyawa ha mishra wela athi wena anith (anya) kriya, chithasika lesa hadun wanawa. (chithasika 52 pawathi) 

ex:
cooking a curry
pirisidu wathura - sitha
daana ingrediants - chithasika

chaithasika :

sitha samaga upadinawa 
sitha samagama nathi wenawa 
sitha ganna aramuna mai ganne.
sithata udaw wechchi wasthuwa (prasadayama nishraya karagenai tiyenne)

me chaithasika wala lakshana 4ta kiyanawa sathara samprayoga lakshana (samprayoga yanu ekata mishra wela pawathi kiyana eka)

chaithasika sithata prathyai. sitha chaithasika walata prathyai.
sithakin thorawa chaithasika hata noganie.
eka sithak thula mulu chaitasika 52ma na. (it can be any combination)
awama washayen chaithasika 7k pawathi. (sabba chiththa sadarana chaithasika)

me 7 thamai,
passa,wedana,sanyaa, chethana, ekakgratha, jeewitha indriya , mansikaraya


dharmaya haduna ganna nam:

1) raga , idvesha , moha duru wenna oni
2) arya ashtangika margayata ekaga wenna oni
3) chathuarya sathyata ekata wenna oni.
4) pattichcha samuppanna wenna oni.

me hatharatama galapena deshanaya aithi katada ? budurajanan wahanseta.
enam asiya yuththe bhudda wachanaya witharai.
siyalu wenath matha saha mage mathaya iwath wiya yuthui, mishra noviya yuthui.

mehidi mata labiya yuththak natha. (enam mama sitiya nohakie, mamen etheta wiya yuthui. nathara weemata novei.)

nathara weemata hethuwa thamai, api sakkaya dittiya poshana weemai.
sakkaya dittiya tiyebena thana
wichikichchawath tiyenawa 
seelabbatha paramasayath pawathie
e nisa marga pala nomatha.
enam sasara yai.

okai gataluwa.

niwaradiwa anithya dakima thula,
ihatha haduna ganna siyalu darmayo pawathi.

me anithya dakina thana kothanada ?
ethana akaalika thana.
daham guna 6ma tibiya yuthui.
-> suwakkatho bagawatha dammo (budun hodatama deshakarala tiyenawa)
-> sandittiko (me bawayema dakinna puluwan)
-> akaaliko (kaalayata ahu novei.) (pachchupannaye pawathi, kriyawalik/sakas weemak pawathie.)
-> ehi passiko ( enna balanna)
-> opanaiko ( thama thulin balanna puluwan)
-> wynoheethi ( for people with wisdom)

me thana kothanada ?
niwana.
yan kinchi samudaya dhamman, sabbanthan nirodha dhammanthi (me lokaye athiwana samudayo , e mohothema nirodha wenawa)
nacha kinchi loke, upaadiyathi. (me lokaya thula upadanaya karanna kisiwak na, echchara wegayen nirodhaya wenawa)


ex:
budun lankawe wada siti bawa.

thanak, kenek innawa kiyana hageema ismathu wela.
enam sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wela
shraddawata hodai namuth ethera weema pramadai.
e nisa e bana padayath ikmawa yanna oni. 
e nam e iwabawaya ikmawa yanna oni niwana awaboda karaganna.

ex:
budunge wachana , thripitakaye tiyenawa , namuth arthya sithata anukulai, wena wena aya therum gath arthyan wenas. 
e nisa margapala ipadeemata badawak wiya haka.
api me kiyapu ekak mathak noviya yuthui.

wiya haki ekama de ethara weema pamani. nathara wanne nam sakkaya dittiya poshanaya kirimaki.

1) mata wada danna ayage matha walata aleema, (compare kireema) -> eya dannawa kiyana eka mage mathayak. onna ahu wela. sakkaya dittiya poshana wela.
2) eta waradie kiyana ekath mage mathak, nawatha nathara wei.

me nisa ethara weema yanu, enlightment ( awabodhayama pamanaki).awabodaya yanu budda swabawayai.
enam pachchupanna mohothe, awabodaya tibiya yuthui.

ex: 
onima kaleka thrikonayakata pada thunai. thrikonaya kiyanne sakas weemak. prakyapthiyak
e kiyanne sankarayai.
sabbe sankara anichchathi
anithya swabawaya haduna gaththu kramaya waradie.
anithya swawaya pramartha dharmayak.
budda wachanaya anuwa anithya balanna oni  " yankinchi samudhaya dhamman sabbaththan nirodha dammanthi" kiyana widihata
enam siyalu de athiwana thana nirudda wena bawa.

athi deyaka nathi weemak - budda deshana novei.
athi wana iswabawyama nathi weemai - budda deshanaya.

ex:
motor bycle eken yanne , tibbichcha petrol or pawichcha karapu petrol walin nevi
pichchena petrol walin.
eka pennannada ba. kriyawak pamani.
sithath, chaithasikath kriyawak / balawegayak /energy ekak pamani.
me awabodayata kiyanwa buddha kiyala.

pichchena petrol walin yana moto bycle eka wage eye hitapu mama ho heta inna mama ho dan pawathina mamek natha.
aththe sakas weema kiyana kriyawak pamani.
sankara duka iwarai.


--------------------------------08/02/2021--------------------------------------------
anichcha vs anithya

ඉචඡා (හෙවත් ඉචඡාබද්ධ) සූත්‍රය

‘‘ඉච්ඡාය බජ්ඣතී ලොකො, ඉච්ඡාවිනයාය මුච්චති;
ඉච්ඡාය විප්පහානෙන, සබ්බං ඡින්දති බන්ධන’’න්ති.
(භාග්‍යවතුන් වහන්සේ මෙසේ වදාළසේක.) “ලෝ වැසි තෙම ආශායෙන් බැඳේ. ආශාව දුරැලීමෙන් මිදේ. ආශාව විශේෂයෙන් පහකර දැමීමෙන් සියලු බැමි සිඳේ. “

අනිත්‍ය සූත්‍රය

‘‘රූපං, භික්ඛවෙ, අනිච්චං, වෙදනා අනිච්චා, සඤ්ඤා අනිච්චා, සඞ්ඛාරා අනිච්චා, විඤ්ඤාණං අනිච්චං. එවං පස්සං, භික්ඛවෙ, සුතවා අරියසාවකො රූපස්මිම්පි නිබ්බින්දති, වෙදනායපි නිබ්බින්දති, සඤ්ඤායපි නිබ්බින්දති, සඞ්ඛාරෙසුපි නිබ්බින්දති, විඤ්ඤාණස්මිම්පි නිබ්බින්දති. නිබ්බින්දං විරජ්ජති ; විරාගා විමුච්චති. විමුත්තස්මිං විමුත්තමිති ඤාණං හොති. ‘ඛීණා ජාති, වුසිතං බ්‍රහ්මචරියං, කතං කරණීයං, නාපරං ඉත්ථත්තායා’ති පජානාතී’’ති. පඨමං.

“මහණෙනි, රූපය අනිත්‍යයි, වේදනාව අනිත්‍යයි, සඤ්ඤාව අනිත්‍යයි, සංස්කාර අනිත්‍යයි, විඤ්ඤාණය අනිත්‍යයි, මහණෙනි, මෙසේ දක්නාවූ බොහෝ ඇසූපිරූ තැන් ඇති ආර්‍ය්‍යශ්‍රාවකතෙමේ රූපයෙහිද කළකිරෙයි. වේදනාවෙහිද කළකිරෙයි. සඤ්ඤාවෙහිද කළකිරෙයි. සංස්කාරයන්හිද කළකිරෙයි. විඤ්ඤාණයෙහිද කළකිරෙයි. කළකිරීමෙන් නො ඇලෙයි. නොඇලීමෙන් මිදෙයි. මිදුනුකල්හි මිදුනේය යන ඥානය ඇතිවෙයි. ජාතිය ක්ෂය විය. බ්‍රහ්මචර්‍ය්‍යාවෙහි වැස නිමවන ලදී. කළයුත්ත කරණලදී. මේ ආත්මභාවය පිණිස කළයුතු අනිකක් නැතැයි දැනගනියි.”

anithya and anichcha liyana widiha dekak, dekata tiyenne therum dekak. e nisa artha dekak.

labena siyaluma de walin sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wenawa.
niwana labenna deyak nevi, etharaweemak.

budun ge siyaluma deshana tiyenne sakkaya dittiya kadanna.
ehenam labenna , hambenna puluwan dharmayak nevi.
sansara dukata wisadumak wenne ethara unoth witharai.


--------------------------------------08/02/2021--------------------------------------------

apita aththa kiyala hithena lokayai tiyenawane 
ekat apita hithata danena hageemak ne
me hageema 
habaawatama tiyeanwa ,
habaawatama na kiyala kotas dekakin katha karanna puluwan.

mama nathi wethdi lokayak tiyenawa kiyana eka aththa nam
api balanna oni
aththatama tiyena ewa monawada
naththam aththatama nathi ewa monawa kiyala.

ex:
gini pellellak karakawathdi , walallak penawa.
aththa wage penawa but eka aththata na. kriyawaka prathipalayak.

ex2:
kos gediyak kaduwa , eka tibba galak uda.
dan meka awrudu ganak gihin balana kota ,
kos gediyak widihata aduna ganna geyak tiyei da.
me widihata 
ethakota kos gediya iswaroopaya tiken tika wenas wela neda ?
ehenam kos gediya nithya washayen tiyenawada ?
kos gediya anithya nam
kos gediya prakyapthiyak da paramartha dharmayak da ? [this is a seperate session]

ex:
pudgalayek, deyak, thanak, tiyenawa , innawa, -> kiyana hama dema athma sankalpayen ganna ewa, enam prakyapthiyaka kotasak.
mewa okkoma apita therenne hageemak lesai.

sithata athi hatiyata pena ewa kotas dekak tiyenawa.
1) aththatama tiyenawa ewain
2) aththatama nathi ewai.

prakyapthiyen eha giya deyak thamai paramartha dharma,
meka abhidharmayen hodata wisthara karanawa.

ex:
gas gal, gewal dorawal tiyenawa kiyala hageemak enawa
sithata danenawa mewa tiyenwa kiyala .
sithata asu wenawa ( dakinawa, kalpana karanawa, danenawa) (asu wena widihata arthaya kiyala kiyanne)

lokaya kiyala deyak tiyenawa mama kiyala kenekuta sanyawak enawa - meka miriguwak lesa thamai dharmaye sadahan wenne.

prakyapthi awabodayata eha giya awabodayak thamai, paramartha dharma kiyanne.
meka thamai pilisinda dakinawa kiyanne.
roopaya pilisinda dakinawa. ( roopaye iswabawaya (wynyaanayen hadapu) ikmawa dakeema ( prakyawen )  )

ex:
dharmayo dharmayata galapanna oni. ethana kenekuta ida tiyala na. (satipattane asurin)
api dharmayo dharmayen allanna oni , kenekugen alluwoth api aye mohayata ahuwela, (idwithawayata ahuwela)

ex:

api redi mahana machine ekak gamu.
hamotama me machine eka panawa . 
habai mechanis danna kenekuta , methana tiyena mechanisam eka dannawa. habai penne na.
e wage machine eke uda noola penawa. yatin duwana noola penne na.
uda noolen mahanawa widihata thamai penne.
namuth gate gahanne yata noolen.
yata noola naththan mahanna ba

ewage thamai thanhawath.
thanhawa kotas dekak tiyenawa
1)uda noola thamai bahira wathsu walata tiyena thanhawa.
2)yata noola tiyena iskanda walata tiyena thanhawa. (nikanthi thanhawa)(meka sitha paththen hadenne , meka penne na)

nikanthi thanhawa ex:
loku mountain ekak uda idala oya watenne yanawa, 
ethana tiyenawa asuchi walak.
watena kota kohoma hari galawenna asuchi wala allagannawa neda ?
e asuchi walata kamathi nisada ?
eka alluwe jeewithayata athi kamaththa nisa. <- meka thamai nikanthi thanhawa kiwwe.
iskanda wlata tiyena thanhawa kiyala mekata kiyanne
iskanda ( wedana, sanya, sankara, wynaana) saha me satharen osawapu roopaya (pancha iskandaya)
tiyena aleema.

machine athule wena kriyawaliya ( mahuma gata gahena kriyawaliya)
uda noolai , yata noolai ekathu wela , redi kalikota ekinekata amineemata api kiyanawa sibbanee kiyala.
enam thanhawe kriyakarithwaya thamai sibbanee kiyala hadunwanne.

e nisa eka sithak thawa sithak ekka nonawathwama gatagahenne me sibbaniya nisai.
e nisa, 
aththatama irak pawathinawa 
gas gal, sathwayo pawathinawa , innawa, tiyenawa kiyana prakyapthi haduna gannawa.

athi de lesa penunata, 
aththatama athi saha 
aththatama nathi lesa 
de akarayakin pawathinawa

me wyaanaye mayawa igena ganeemedi, nawatha nathwath api me kiyana mayawatama ahu wenawa
pudgala sanyawata ida labenawa
athma drushtiya poshanaya wenawa
sakkaya dishtiya gedi pitin enawa
anthya daka watahenne nathi wenawa. mulawe kotu wenawa
atha ho natha lesa tharkayata ahuwenawa. (iwthawayata asu wenawa)
mohaya enam awidyawe gilenawa.

budun, me athma sanyawen ahapu prashna , tapaneeya dharma ( wisikarapu problems)
uththara nodun prashna kiyala.

dharmaya samawitama , nissaththwa, nijeewa, shunyoo we.

me nisa thamai,
budu rajanan wahanse ge deshana prathharaya athi wishishtai kiyala kiyanne.
kisima drushtiyakata nowatena se, 
dharmaya deshana karanna puluwan hakiyawa tiyenne budu kenekuta pamanai.

e nisa budda wachanayama asiya yuthui,
ewita prathyakshaya awaboda wei.


sankatha - hethu prathyen sakas wu wak. meya samawitama sapekshai
asankatha - awabodayak pamanai. dharmayak pamanai ( me awaboda karaganna kenek nathi bawa prathyaksha weema). asanakatha dharmaya pudgala sobawayen ganna ba.(nirapekshai)

maranaya - sankathai. (sakas wechchi deyak, yali sakas wenna ida kada tiyenawa )
asankatha - parinirwanaya (yali sakas weemak natha)(nirapekshai)

atha saha natha kiyana eka pudagala iswabayen ganna wita athi wena deyak.
namuth dharmaya dharmayata galapala ( pudgala sobawayata ida nothaba) awabodha kala yuthui.
nissatho nisjeewo shunyoo..

mehidi
athi bawa nathiweema nowa.
athi wana bawa nathi weemai wataha gatha yuththe.

athiwana thanama nathi wana iswabaya prathyaksha karaganna udaya waya nyanaya hada ganeema sanda thamai.

nagina godanagillata usa nodana inimaga hadala wadak na.

ex:
onna koppayak ganna 
dharmaya haduna nogath kena , methana koppayak tiyenawa kiyala eyage haduna ganeemata purudu widihata gannawa
dharmaya asa dana gath kena, koppaya prakyapthiyak kiyala dana gannawa, ethana koppayak aththata nathi bawa gannawa.
dan me denna athara koppaya tiyenawada nadda kiyala logically argue karala wadak na.
mokada 
ekama koppaya awabodaya anuwa pawathinawa , nopawathinawa
enam pawathina saha nopawathina sobawaya ekatama pawathinnak
eya awabodaya thulin hata gannak. (hethu prathyai)

enam koppaya athi bawa nathi weema nevi budu dahame katha karanne.
koppaya athi wana bawa nathi weemai.
enam koppaya athi weeme kriyawaliya ( pancha upadana iskandaya thulin upadanaya weeme kriyawaliya) awaboda kara ganeemai.
ethkota 
prakshawa morapu nathi kenekuta koppaya pawathina bawath
prakshawen baluwahama nathibawath
me dekama ekata pawathi.
enam awabodayata anuwa athi wita atha
nathi wita natha.
awabodaya hethuwen lokaya pawathi
awabodaya hethuwen loyaka nopawathi
lokaya pawathina ho nopawathina lesa tharkayata yomu karanna nam atha ko natha kiyana kotasa niyojana karanna kenek
sitiya yuthui.
ese tharka kirimen nawath awidyawe ale.
dharmaya dharmayen gatha yuthui.


ex:
kenek kiyanawa thripitakaye methana meaning eka mekai, mewidiha hari , me widiha waradie kiyala.
onna hari ho waradi pathi deken ekak allagaththa.
ethkota hari ho waradi kiyala depaththak thripitakaye tiyenawa da ?
eka wenne api eka pudgala sobawayen alla gaththa handa. (mage danumata hari/waradie)
allana kenage danuma anuwa, eka hari ho waradi wenna puluwan.
hari ho waradi weema pawathinne ekata, athi wenne awabodaya handa (hethu prathya)
enam sapekshayai, sapeksha nam (idwithawayen alla tiyenne)
ehenam hari ho waradi kiyala tharka karala wadak na.
tharkaya apiwa thawa duratath mohaye gilwanawa.


-----------------------------14/02/2021--------------------------------------------


siddartha kumaraya , mahallek ahata penila , matath me sobawaya ikmawanna ba kiyala , 
kochchara salli tibunath e sobawayen midenne ba kiyala.

namuth apita ehema hithenne nane. mahallek dakkata , e drushti konaya apita enne na.
apita laga kenek marunath ,maximum 1 year ,2 year walin passe e okkoma hageema diyawela adu wela gihin.

ehema wenne mokada ?

api awaboda karagaththu duka mokadda ?
leda wenawa jara wenawa 
api kiyana me dukada budu rajanan wahanse awaboda kara ganna kiwwe ?

budu rajanan wahanse awaboda karaganna keewa duka mokadda ?
budun pennuwe pachchupanna bawai.

me inna pudgala sobawaya thula mokadda pawathina duka ? 
eken galaweenna patan ganne kothaninda ?

apita duka,
samatha bawanakin ,ho widarshana bawanakin ho duka kelawara karanna kamaththa apita tiyenawa.

ex:
pilikawak haduna ledek ge pilikawa ain kalath , podi hari kotasak miss unoth ,
egaye sanasilla tiyenne tika kalayai neda ?
aye ara ithuru mulen udu duwapu gaman duka nawatha paminenawa.

nuwana nathi kena, hamatissema duka ain karanna try karanne dura diga giyata passe. ( symptom ekata thamai solution)
namuth
nuwanaththa, roga nidanaya gana thamai focus karanne.(eka awaboda karaganna thamai daksha wenna try karanne)


e wage thamai,
ape dukath.

ex: 
api idaganna putuwak ganne sapak balaporoththuwen neda ?
habai hugak welawak indagena innakota meka epa wenawa neda 

wenas weema sapak sapak/dukak kayala gannawa ?
me duka haduna gaththe mokak nisa da ?

sammathaye api suwayata hurui, eka wenas unahama suwayata athi kamaththa nisa api inna akaraya wenas karala aye suwaya hoyanawa.
me duka haduna gaththe apita athiuna wedanawa handa.

ethkota wedanawa hata gaththe mokak nisada ?
api ida gena innakota putuwa agata sambannda wela tibba , ehenam 
mulinma e sparshaya sapak kiyala theruna, eeta passe e sparshama dukak una.

dan onna apita as panapitama 
putuwata tibba sparshaya handa thamai wedana athi wela tiyenne . ( me wedanawa eka witaka sapa lesath, duka lesath , madyatha lesai api aragena)

ethkota apita hagena widihata,
duka hata aran tiyenne 
api putuwe wadi wela hitapu handa ( bahira tiyena putuwa nisa (roopyak nisa)
ehenam ithin bahira roopaya ain karanna epai , api me dukin midenna nam
onna putuwa kadala danawa.

dan kaduwe mokadda , api poddak putuwa wishleshanaya karamu.
putuwa apita danune ,
dharmatha 5k nisa , ayathana walata gatena ayurin 
roopa, shabda , rasa ,ganda, isparsha lesa
api dan putuwa replace karamu 
me dharmatha 5n (putuwa bahira deyak nisa danata sithuwilla poddak paththakin tiyamu, putuwa allanna ehata 5 onima nisa eka gana mulin focus karamu)

ehema nam , me kiyana duken midenna nam 
ekko apen putuwa aath karala tiyanna oni ehema naththam
api putuwen aath wela inna oni.

dan ethkota putuwen nidahas wenna nam , 
api roopa,shaba,rasa ,ganda ,isparsha kiyana 5n midenna oni . 

dan api putuwa kaduwath, ehema naththam ain unath, eka aramunu wenneth me pahen mai.
ehenam me 5n api midila na.
dan api putuwen ain unama e duka nathi wenawa kiyala hithuwata,
me pahen midila na. 
api karala tiyenne me 5n wena aramunak aran. ( onna dan hitan innawa)
eka sapai kiyala gaththata inna ba wadi wela , onna aye wenin ekakata yanawa.

duka aapu dewal walin ain weema , me lokaya thula nam saarthakai kiyala thamai therenne.
enam
idan hitapu duka nathi wenna , api hitagena inna patan gaththa.
dan puduwe duka 100% ma nathi wela, aluth dukak aramunu kala (sapa,duka, madyathsa lesa)

duke sobawaya aduna gaththu widiha wenas unata, duka ain wela na.
duka ain karanna ba.

onna dan putuwa puchcharala , alu karala , gange paa karala yawanawa.
dan onna gange pawela , putuwe alu tika giya kiyala gaththeth,
me iskanda panchakayenma thamai.
tibbichcha putuwa na kiwweth me 5n mai.
methana nathi bawa kiyala kiwwe hiss bawata nevei neda ?
nathi putuwa gana adahasak tiyenawa.
eka tiyenneth me 5n ma thamai.

athi bawata sapekshawa nathi bawa sahalluwak.
namuth parama sahalluwak nevei.
me nathi bawath tiyena deyak wela.
me puchchapu putuwa thama hithe pawathinawa.

ehenam athi bawa ho nathi bawa kiwweth kisiyam wu deyak athi bawak. 
athi bawin nathi bawata yanwa kiyanne , atha saha natha kiyanne antha dekak.
anthayaka innawa kiyala eya hira wela innawa kiyana ekai.
simawakata kotu wela.
eunata api gannawa me athi -> nathi ho nathi -> athi sobawaya sahalluwak kiyala.
eth api aththatama hira wela inne.

api hithanawa apita nathi una bawa therila kiyala.
nathi deyak wishthara karanna kiwwoth. e de allala balanna oni neda ? (previous sparshayak tiyenne oni)(bahirin ho sithiwali walin)
api prathipadawen ahuwenna onna othanata.
api mechchara kal try kale duka nathi karanna, 
dan putuwa nathi karala api hithanawa duka athi wana de nathi kala kiyala.
namthu duka nathi wela na
nathi unahama tiyena duka therila na.
wachana sobawayen nathi bawa withara karanne athi bawama thamai.

ex:
kalu pata gana kiyanna puluwan sudu pata dannawanam witharai.
araya tikak kalui, meya sudui. (relative)
ehenam sudu bawa dannawa nam thamai kalu gana katha karanna puluwan wenne.
ekinekata prathyai.

ex:
mal pochchiyak atha,
ain kaloth natha. 
ehema kiyanne nathi bawa tiyena nisai.
api ayeth katha karala tiyenne tiyena bawak.

duka tiyenne bahirin kiyala hithala , bahirin(pancha kamayen) ain unata

sithata definion ekak denna try karamu. ( isella api sithuwilla park kalane , eka gana thamai me balanna hadanne)

me sithuwilla wisthara karanna balanna ?
me mohothe danena de wisthara karanna kiyalane api me kiyanne.

ex: 
dan onna apita kurulu hadak danenawa. wisthara karanna kiwwoth
apita hithata dannenne mokadda ?
hithara danune shabdayak ne. ehenam ayeth api wisthara karala tiyenne 
me roopa,shabda,ganda, isparsha tika neda ?
hama tissema sithuwilla wisthara karanna kiwwata , api wisthara karaanne
sithuwilla nowena ithuru 5n thamai api wishthara karanne.
hama tissema ayathana walata ahu una dewal walin thamai withara karala tiyenne.
ayeth me pancha kamaya thamai wishthara wela tiyenne.

sithuwilla withara wela naneda ?
sithuwili mattama ahuwela na thawamath.

sithuwilla thamai wisthara karaganna oni.
langa, dura,solid,suwada, lassana, katha kiyala nanathwayak lokaye hamu une ai ?
eka aththatama ayathana 5ta gochara wu wak nevi.
me wenas gathiya hamu wenne,
me ayathana walin aramunu wena gathi wala wenasa nisa.
isparshaye sobawaya nisa.

ex:
gal,wali,simenthi, tiruwana, api sakman maluwaka asuranawa.
oyata wiwidathwayak hambuwenawa neda.

e tika aduna gaththeth ara 5nma thamai. ude nagitta welawe idan 5n pahata pana pana innawa.
ude nagitta mohothe,
idala
monawa hari sobawayak danenawane.
nagitta mohothema, thama asdeka hariyata arilath na.

anna e andunkun sobawaya thula, roopa shabda kiyala bedeemak naneda ?
namuth ehema nathi sobawayak pawathina bawak hambawela.

jeewitha indriya tiyena kenekuta , menna me ara 5n aramunu novu awasthawak pawathina bawa therenewa.
eka thamai sithiwili apita therena mattama.

onna dan api sithuwillak wisthara karanna kiwwahama ,
hamatissema wishtara kale pancha kamaya gana witharai.
onna sithuwilla aramunu sobawayen thorawa pawatina bawa pennanna thamai uda example eka gaththe.
e sithawillata aramunu una de ara pancha kama aramunu walin wechcha deyak nevi.
eka handa thamai me andunkundun sobawayak apita therenne.

meka thamai apita hambuwena sithiwili mattama,
me sithuwili mattama pawathina nisai
apita ara pancha kamaya aramunu wiya hakke.

kalin api katha kala ekata meka sampurnayen prathi wiruddai.
mulin katha kale
putuwa eliye tiyenwa , e bahira isparshaya nisa (indriya 5he aramunu wunu gathi sobawayak gana) wedanawa hata ganna bawa.
namuth methana,
eeta sampurnayenma prathi wirudda kathawakta thamai goda nagenne,

dan kiyanne

aththatama dan wena wenama hithuwoth 
aththatama hithe pawathma hata gaththu sobawaya , ikmawala na ( overtake karala na).
bahira sparshaya nisa wedanawa hata ganna sobawayath meka thulama thamai tiyenne.
ehema me pawathina bawak therena sobawayen thamai meka paran aran tiyenne.
enam bahira isparshaya siduweemata pera , sitha pawathiya yuthui.
(sabbachiththa sadarana cythasika 7)(wathura sobawaya enam muula sobawaya nathuwa ingredeants add karanna ba)
enam muula sobawaya wedanawa thulin hata gaththu ekak nevi.
muula sobawaya thula pudgala sobawayak na, anathma sobawayak mai.
muula sobawaya thula sapa or duka labila na, wedanawa saduna deyak nevi.
menna methana upekshawayai. (upekshawa 11 akarayak pawathi, me api kathara karana upekshawa wedanawen sakas wana ekak nevi, passa pachchaya wedana gana nevi me katha karanne) 
(upekshawe 11 akara pilibanda abhidarmaye wenama sakachcha karanawa)

ex:

issara tiyenawa bell ekak.

on welamai tiyenne.

obapu gaman ring wenaw.

menna me hakiyawa wishthara karanna ba.
ara sithiwilla wage, me ability ekata definion ekak denna ba ara roopa shabda ganda rasa isparsha nathuwa.

ex:

me nodanna kama thamai dukata hethuwa. (awidyaawa)

awidyawa thoranna awdiyawenma puluwan weida ?
ehema ba, awdiyawa therenne na namuth wataha ganna (awaboda karaganna puluwan)
nodanna kama awaboda weema (meya theruna nevi, mokada hithakata therenne roopa,ganda,shabda,rasa,isparsha witharane)


hakiyawa kiyana eka penne na,
eka wisthara karannath ba.
hakiyawa tiyenawa nam chithrayak adinna puluwan.
namuth adapu chithrayen hakiyawa wistahra karanna ba.

ethkota mamathwaya kiyana eka nirwachanaya une roopa,shabada ,ganda,isparasha,rasa thulin.
namuth aththatama une

ex:

apita me me hakiyawa miss wela mama kiwwahama allaganne deyak.

ex: bell example

thula (lokoththara awabodayata anuwa)

ewage

e wage keles gala wenne na

-------------------21/02/2021--------------------------------------------
niwana gana dana gamu.

iskandayagen nathiweemen niwana panawanna ba. ( me lokaye pawathina dewal walin)
ewagema ayathana 6 nathi weemen niwana panawannath ba.

ehenam me sankatha kiyala kiwwwe mokadda,
dana ganna mulin bumi gana dana gamu
bumi 4k tiyenawa
kamaa wachara bumi( wachara - kiyanne hasirenawa kiyana eka, wanachara - wanaye hasirena)
(eke loka 11k tiyenawa) (sathara apayai, sadev lokaya / divyaloka 6 , manussa lokayai)
-roopawachara bumi
(eke loka 16k tiyenawa) ( synyaawa nathi eka loka 1, synyaawa athi 15i)(dyaana walin thamai yanna puluwan)
(pancha neewarana yatapath karapuwaha, dyaana upadawa ganna puluwan, ewa pirihen nathuwa maloth me loka walata thamai uppaththiya)
-aroowachara bumi
(eke loka 4k) ( dyaana anga samanai aramunu wenas)
qualification eka roopawachara awasan dyaana deka labal tiyenna oni, kamaththa anuwa synaawa tiyena or nathi thanata 
yanan puluwan.
-apariya panna bumi
ihatha thun bumiyata athulath wela nathi kotasa thamai apariya panna bumi
me awastha bumiyak, sithama thamai bumiya lesa ganne.
methana upadanaya nowana thanak. iskanda witharak pawathinne.
methana kriya sith na.

 
 sankatha kiyala kiyanne menna me 4 bumiye tiyena kusal,akusal, wipaka saha thun bumiyata aithi kriya athulu siyaluma roopa walata. ( sankatha - sakaskeruna, pryathen hata gaththa, hethuwen hatagaththa kiyana adahasa)
 ethakota sankatha kisima dathuwe deyak na, hethuwen hatagaththa kiyana adahasa thamai tiyenne.
 
 ex:
 tea ekak loke kohewath na. tea eka nowana kali tikak ekathu wela sakas wechcha praknyapthiyak ehenam naththam sankathayak.
 sammuthiya thula katha karana bashawena dapu nam walata api prakyapthiya kiyala kiwwa. ( aththatama tiyenawa wage penunawata aththatama na)
 praknaptiya kiyana eka type of asankathayak lokaya thula pawathina.
 sankathaya kiyanne prathyen hata gaththa kiyana adahasata.
 niwana kiyanneth type of asankathayak habai lokaya thula hamuwenne na.
 
 
 hadila tiyenne yam dharmatha tikakin nam
 e hatagaththata de tai api badenne.
 dharmatha tika lehena kota palaya nathi wenawa.
 ehema unata api kiyanne api kamathi de nathi una kiyala.
 wechcha de danne na.
 e kiyanne athi wena hati ho nathi wena hati api danne na.
 prathyen hata gaththa dewal prathya nathi wenakota nathi wana sobawayen yuktha nam eka dukai.
 mama mage kiyanna sudusu na , eka anathmai.
 e kiyanne ,
 
 3 bumiya pawathinawa nam pancha upadanaya pawathinawa, enam dukka sathya pawathinawa kiyala kiwwath me katha karanne
 sakas wechcha ekak gana.
 enam sankathyak gana.
 
 enam sankathayak igena ganna prathya 24k oni.
 mekata thamai, su-wusi pattanaya kiyala kiyanne ( pannam prakaranaya thula)
 -> hethu prathya
 -> arammana ( starting) prathya
 -> adhipathi 
 -> ananthara
 -> samananthara
 -> saha jaatha
 -> anya manya 
 -> nissaya
 -> upanisssaya
 -> pure jaatha
 -> passa jatha
 -> aasewana  
 -- ohoma thawa tiyenawa pic eka balala updated karanna.
 
 ai api meka igena ganne ?
 pattichcha samuppadaya anuwa pachchupanna kiyanne prathyen upan kiyana adahasa.
 me lokaye pawathi sobawayan sankathai.
 pattichcha samuppadaya, me mokaye athi sankatha dathu walata apply karanna , api parathya kiyana eka hariyata aduna ganna oni.
 sankatha gana igena ganna api prathya 24 gana balanna oni.
 
 ex:
 jeewithe kawadawath no asunu, nodakapu dekata chanda raagayak tiyei da ?
 no asunu nodakapu, nosithapu  deyak wisthara karanna puluwanda ?
mata wisthata karanna ba kiyala kiyana kotama , e nodanna de gana wisthara karala iwarai neda
enam ehema deyak pawathinna puluwan namthu wisthara karaganna ba.
ehema deyak tiyenna puluwan kiyana hageema wishwasa karala thamai me deyak wisthara karanna ba kiyala kiwwe.

pahanai , tirayai, thelui athi thula thanaka alokaya pawathinna puluwan.
enam pahanai, tirayai thelui tiyenna oni kiyala adahasak enawane.

laukika jeewithaya thula hethu tika nirwachanaya kale palaya thulin.
palaya thulin hethuwa dakima thamai api karala tiyenne.

ex:
kaluwara kamarayak inna kenek lagata,
kiwwtu karala pahanak dalluwoth
e alokaya tulin neda pahana, thel tika, kena, me okkoma dakke ?
pahan alokaya thamai palaya.
namuth palaya thulin thamai hethu tika dakala tiyenne.
enam
aha tiyenawa kiyana eka tiyenawa kiyala therenne roopaya tiyenawa kiyala therunoth neda .
peneema harata wechcha prathyakshayak lesai asa, and roopaya hambu wenne.
aththa kathawa habai
asa , roopa prathya wela thamai wynaanaya hadenne oni.
namuth 
ehema wela na, pancha upadana iskandaye hulaga wath wadila na apita .
roopaya tiyena nisa , aha tiyenawa kiyala mathaye thamai idala tiyenne.
pala walin hethuwa
budun deshana kale 
hethu walin palaya
 
 dan methana,
 kriyawakin hata gaththu palayak me pahan dalla. 
 ethkota me dalla namathi palaya thulin hetu seweemak api karanne. 
 apita aha hambu wenneth e widihata ( penima roopayak haraha, indriya gana adahasak apita awilla na)
 indriya hariyata dakkoth, apita hethuwen palaya wigraha karanna oni.
 enam roopaya hambenna nam asa namathi indriya hamu wiya yuththe,
 ehi kriya karithwayai hambenna oni.

api mulin hithapu karamaya , pattichcha sammupaada dharmaya gawila wath na.
hithannawath ba.

indriya gana nodanna kama nisa thamai duka enne.
arya sathya lokayata watahenne naththe e nisai.
ape nodanuwath kama thamai therum ganna oni.

passa pachchaya wedana kiyala kiwwahama  ekath me pahan dalle kathawamai.
passaya thulin thamai wedana dana gena tiyenne ( isparsha une naththam me mukuth na kiyala ne hithanne)
namuth awidyawata passe neda passaya define karala tiyenne.
namuth apita awidyawa allagena tiyenneth passaya haraha.
ehenam patticha samuppadaya hariyata ahu wela na.

hama witama , api daraa gena inna eka thulin thamai hithanne.
hethu pala waadaya aniwa awidyawena thamai mulkota patan ganne.
nodanuwath kama pamanai awaboda karanna tiyenne.

awidyaa we nirodhayama thamai kara ganna oni.
me nirodhaya awabodayak pamanai.

ex:
mama kiyna palaya apita hambune ayathana walin.
mama kiyana ageema apita aththa wela.
e nisa mama thulin me lokaya allanna patan aran.
pattichcha samuppadaya apply wela na.
api palayen hethuwa hoyala.

ayathana 6 nisa hata gaththu mama kiyala palaya  -> mulin dakiya yuthui.
namuth 
me sparsha ayathana 6 nathi kala kiyala mama kiyana sobawaya nathi unata.
niawana panawanne ethanata nevi.
mokada 
ayathana 6 nathi una kiyana kota , ayathana 6 nathi bawa apita hamu wela.
ayathana nathi unata , nawatha ayathana hadanna tiyena hakiyawa nathi wela na.

hakiyawa me nisa mamathwaya thawamath pawathi.

sanyojana kiyana badeema kadenne , awidyawa hariyata awaboda unahama.
awidyawa nisa sanyojana dharma wala badeema aduna gaththahama,
sasara duk hadana ayoniso manikaraya lokuwata yodanne nathuwa ,
sasaren midena budda wachanaya aseemata pelabena budda wachanaya yedeemen
sasara jaya gatha haki,
vimukkthi dhana darshanaya laba ganeemata ida lasalevi.

practically apita karanna tiyenne,
yahapath kriya thamunta saha anunta karamin atalo dahamata nosali sitima.
 
--------------------------------07/03/2021------------------------------

chiththa vithi igena ganna nam,

1) sith athi wana mula hethu gana dana ganna oni ( below secton)
2) sith ha roopa wala ayusha dana ganna oni. ( upadina , pawathina, nasena)(uthpaada, titi, banga)
3) roopa athi wena widi
4) roopa pravurthi

---------------------------28/02/2021 (sith athi wana mula hethu)--------------------------------------------

hitha gana igena ganna giyahama apita mula hethu kiyala deyak hambenawa.
sitha aramunak allaganna gihayama , e kriyawaliya wenna hethu wana hethu mula hethu kiyala kiyanawa.
gahaka polowata ahuwe wana mul wage , me hethu.
mula hethu 6k - awedesha , amoha, aloba, - kusala paththata
				loba moha, dwesha - akusala paththa.

eka hithaka, akusala paththa gaththahama ekko e hethu 3n labenne ekak ho dekak witharamai pihitanne. thunama ekata athi wenne na. 
eka hethuwak nisa -eeka hethuka sith 				
dekak nam - idwi hethuka sith
akusalayata athi wenawa, akusalayata thri hethuka sith athi wenne na.

akusalaya bohoma lesiyen sakas karaganeemata lesie.

kusal warga tiyenne dekai
iwihethuka 
thri he thuka
kusal wala eka hethuka sith na.

kusal and akusal nowana , awyakrutha ( wyakrutha kiyanne , wachanayen kiyanna puluwan kiyana eka)( me kiyanne kusal akusal washayen kiyanna ba kiyana eka)

ex: roopa. 
siyaluma roopa awyakruthai.
roopayaka sith na.
almariya kiyanne kusalayak, pansala kiyanne akusalayak kiyala kiyanne nane.
e wage me roopa kusal washayen ko akusal washayen nokiyana , sith atha.
mewa awyakrutha hethu sahitha sith.

sitha aramunak thadin allaganna hethuwana mula hethu 7 thamai api katha kale.

sasankarika - bahira balawegayakiyan upan. ( support ekak sahitha)
asankarika - bahira support ekak nathiwa , sithnma upan 

ex:
yaluwek awith me wage wadak karamu - (para anugraha sahitha) oyata athi wenne sasankarika sith thamai athi wenne.
matama hithenawa meka puja karanna oni kiyala - iwsyan siddai - mewa asankarika sith.

samprayukka - ekathu wela.
vippa-yuktha - dittiyen thorai.

ex:
kaleawata yaluwo 4k yanwa, badapu daramiti tikak gambenawa
yaluwo thun denek meka horen aran yanna hadanawa , namuth ekkenek kamathi na
namuth yaluwo handa e kattiyath ekka wadeta yanawa.
yaluwo 3n denata awe - ditti gatha samprayuktha sith
kamathi nathi yaluwata awe - ditti gatha vippa-yuktha sith
