----------------------(sith ha roopa wala ayusha dana ganna oni)(chiththa weethi)--------------------

 sith ha roopa ayusha awastha 3k tiyenawa . ( upadina , pawathina, nasena)(uthpaada, titi, banga)
 
 ahi pillamak gahana wegayen lakshayen panguwakatath adu kalayak api ikshanaya kiyala hadunawa.
 me ikshanaya athule katha kara ganeeme pahasuwa sadaha api kuda ikshana 3k let hadunwanawa. 
 
 sithaka kalaya ( chiththayaka kalaya) api chiththa+ikshana 1k lesa hadunwanawa. 
 sithakata ayusha awastha 3k tiyenawa (uthpaada, titi, banga)
 sithak pawathinne 1 chiththakshayai.
 1 chiththakshanayak = kuda chiththakshana 3i

 roopayakata ayusha chththakshana 17k tiyenawa. ( 1m aduna gena api dura meter walin maninawa wage )
 roopaye upatha, hamawitama , palamu chiththakshanaye, palamu kuda chiththakshanayen patan gannawa
 mekata uthpaada ikshanaya 
 melasa aga ikshanaya , banga ikshanaya kiyala hadunwanawa.
 
 me widihata titi ikshanaya = 49 kuda ikshanayak pawathinawa ( 3x17-2)
 roopayakata sampurna ayusha kuda chiththakshana 51.
 me anuwa roopayage titi ikshanaya sahenna dihai.
 
 chiththakshana 17 tiyena roopa thamai wishala washayen pawathinne. ( pradana roopa)
 chiththakshana 17 wada adu roopa athalossak pawathinawa , ( apradhana roopa)

 roopayaka ayusha chiththakshana 17k kiwwata eka piliganna ba neda.
ex: koppak gaththahama digatama tiyenawa neda ?

onna aatha wali godak penawa, eeka eka deyak nevi neda 
wali kata godak tiyenawa.
e wage punchi wasthu godak ekathuwela thamai apita me goda penne.

onna api aba atayak gamu. mekath wali gode wali kata wage godak roopa kalaapa godak me aba ate tiyenawa.
roopa kalapa laksha ganak tiyenawa eka aba ateka.
ethakota , me aba ataye tiyena laksha ganaka roopa kala me eka eka ayusha mattan wala tiyenne 
(samahara ewa ayusha chiththakshana 51 sampurna wechcha, samahata palaweni eke , samaharak mada )
e widihata roopa kalaapa me kuda chiththakshana 51 eke cycle eka eka thana pawathinawa.
51k weni ikshanayata pamini roopa bidena wita, 2->49 ikshanayata pamini roopa pawathinawa.

apita wasthuwala roopa bidena iswabawaya apita penne na. koppaya chiththakshana 17 wada pawathina deyak lesa 
apita therenawa. enam wasthuwe wenasak penne na. mokada 51 chiththakshaye tibena roopa witharai banga wenne. anith siyaluwa roopa koti ganak pawathinawa.

ethkota me roopa kalaapa aluthen ipadenawada ?
roopa jathi 4k pawathi.
1) karmaja roopa (karmayen hatagath)
2) chiththaja roopa ( chiththayen janitha woo roopa)
3) uthuja roopa (irthuwen hatagath)
4) aharaja roopa ( aharayen hatagath)

eka wasthuwaka pawathina, wayasin noyek pramana wala roopa kalaapa siyallama,
> me hathara akarayen hata gaththu ewa.
> eka wara chiththa weethi hata ganna upakari wenne na.
> chiththa weethi athi wanne , eka wasthuwaka aththawuu wayasin samana wu roopa samuhayak aramunu karagena.
(same age kattiyata witharai, eka chiththa weethiyak start karanna aramunu wenne)

roopaya thulin aramunu wena chiththa weethi , athi wena karama keepayak tiyenawa.

aramunu sama witama roopayak nisa hata ganna handa,
aramunu athi wena aakara anuwa meka wisthara karanawa.

mulin api balanne pancha idwarayata ahuwena aramunu.
me aramunu athi wena aakara 4k tiyenawa.

1) aramune wishalathwaya ho, alokaya hodin wati athi nisa ho, ithaa sameepaye tibima nisa ho prakata wena aramuna
mekata api kiyanawa = athi-mahan-thaarambana aramuna
2) athi-mahan-thaarambanaya tharam prakata naththam, athi kalla halanawa, so mahan-thaarambana aramuna kiyala kiyanawa.
3) mahan-thaarambana tharam prakata naththam , pariththaa-rambana aramuna (kalpana karala pennala dagalala thamai meka aduna ganna oni)
4)pariththaa-rambana wath penne nathi ewa, athi-pariththaa-rambana aramuna lesa hadunwanawa ( pennema na)

mano-iwarayata goduru wana aramunu kotas dekai. ( meka pasuwa wisthara karannam)

1) wibuu-thaa-rambana 
2) awi-buu-thaa-rambana 

mese aramunu 6 akaarayak we.

me aramunu 6 , wada karana widi kipayak tiyenawa. mewa chithta niyamayan lesa hadunawanawa. 

1) roopaya , ehi udpaada ikshanaye di idwaarayen hi no-gate.
2) idwarayen hi gatenne titiyata pamani roopa witharai.
3) ipadila, 1 chiththakshanayak ( kuda chiththakshana 3k)ikma ikma-gihin , dewani chiththakshanayen idwaraye gatena aramunu
athi-mahan-thaa-rambanaya. (chiththa withi 1)
4) 2,3 chiththakshana ikmawa giya ewa , mahan-thaa-rambanaya (chiththa withi 2)
5) chiththakshana 4,5,6,7,8,9 ikma giya ewa , pariththaa-rambana (chiththa withi 6)
6) chiththakshana 10,11,12,13,14,15 ikma giya ewa , athi-pariththaa-rambana (chiththa withi 6)

ethkota,
aramune wishalathwaya, alokaya, dura anuwa
apita chiththaweethi, pancha idwarayatama 75k liyanna puluwan. (mono idwaraya excluded)

chakku idwaraye,
athi-mahan-thaa-rambanaya weethi 1  
mahan-thaa-rambanaya weethi 2
pariththaa-rambana weethi 6
athi-pariththaa-rambana weethi 6
total is 15
ethkota pancha idwarayata 15x5 (sotha,gaana,jiwha,kaaya,chakku) = 75
pancha idwara weethi 75.

ethkota chiththa weethiyak kiyanne?
yam aramunak gena , e aramune aayu kalaya awasan wana thek, chiththa niyamaya anuwa
sitha hasirena rataawa. chiththa weethiya nam wei.

meke kathak a , aramune aayu kalaya ( eka gana katha kala)
chiththa niyamaya (katha kala)
aramunu wena aakara nam kala, 
saha athi wiya haki weethi nam kala.

dan api balamu kenek maranaya thulin aye upadina widiha, (palewani sitha, muula chiththaya wisthara kara ganna thamai hadanne)

marana aasannayedi , sithata watahunu deyak aramunu kota, eelaga bawaye palaweni sitha pahala wenawa.
api ekata namak denawa,
prathi sandi chiththaya. ( nawatha sandi una nisa - prathi sandi)
eka aapu gaman eka nirudda wenawa.
eka nirudda woo pasu, ema aramunama gena eeta samana wuu sithak, 
jeewitha maranaya thek ma nawatha nawatha athi wenewa.

ethkota,
maranasanna mohothe athiwana anthima maranaasanna chiththa weethiye aramuna anuwa,
prathisandi sitha nirmanaya wenne.(aluth bawaye)
ethkota parana bawaye bawanga sithe kriyawaliye awasaana sitha api chuthi sitha kiyala nam karanawa. 

me bawanga sith kriyawaliya nikan pulse diagram ekak wage.
bawanga sith paramparawe, aluth aramunu ganeema nisa aluth chiththa weethi hataganee.
eka nikan pulse eka wage.
pulse dekak athara , bawanga sith prakoti ganank tiyenawa.
e sith wala quality wenas wela na.

ex:
light walak ganna , current eka tiyena kam first bulb eka paththu wenawa, dewani bulb eka paththu wenneth 
ara current ekenma thamai. e current eke quality eka wenas wela na.
chithta weethi nikan me bulb wage.
current eka bawanga sitha wage
bulb dekak athara dura bawanga sitha kotiyak wage tiyenna puluwan. 
bawanga sithaka awasanaye thamai chiththa withiyak athi wenna puluwan. ( eka api atheetha bawangak lesa kiyanwa)
dan onna eka chiththakshanayak gewichcha roopalambanayak awith chakkuwe wadiddama, ema mohothema ,
bawanga sitheth wadinawa.
roopaya ipaduna mohothe mai atheetha bawangath ipadune, me mohothe roopaya bawanga sithe wadinna ba. ( atheetha bawanga chiththaye wadinna ba)
ehenam wadinna puluwan wenne eeta passe eka bawanga sithe, api mekata bawanga chalanaya kiyala
dan bawanga sitha helawenakota , bawanga sitha galawenawa, eka api bawanga upachcheda kiyala hadunwanawa.

thii, atheetha bawanga 
naa, bawanga chalana
dha, bawanga upachcheda  

bawanga upachcheda wenne , aluth aramunak awith waduna nisa.
upachaheda wechcha gaman, sitha aluth aramunata hataweema sadaha, kenek innawa(bus eke driver wage wade karana kena)
eyata kiyanawa, pancha-idwara wajjana sitha (pancha idawa gana sihi kiri kirime gunaya, eyata tiyenawa)

ethkota methana chiththakshana 4k gihin.
(1)atheetha bawanga -> (2)bawanga chalana -> (3)bawanga upachcheda -> (4) pancha-idwara wajjana sitha

apu aramuna awe mokenda kiyala dana gena meya chiththa weethiya hari chakkuwata yomu karawanawa ( ahen awa nam ahe chakkuwata)
(4)pancha-idwara wajjana sitha -> (5)chakku winyaanaya (relavent ekata)

pancha idawaren dena aramuna me chakku wynaanaya resistance ekekin thorawa bara gannawa, (higannata kama ekak dunna wage)(hoda naraka balanne na)

5)chakku winyaanaya -> (6)san pattichjana sitha

san pattichajana sithe wade bara ganeema witharai, ena onima kunu godak eelaga sithata bara denawa
eka santheerana sitha

(6)san pattichjana sitha -> (7)santheerana sitha

santheerana sithen sudden judement ekak karanne. 
ex: mango ekak hambunaha , api obala balanawa idilada nadda kiyala e wage, loku judment ekak kale na.

(7)santheerana sitha -> (8) woththapana sitha

meya thamai hariyata theeranaya karanne,  ( meka mano idawara awajjana sithakmai) methana nam karanna woththapana kiyala.
yoniso ho ayoniso manasikaraya yedenne menna me point eke di
ex: dan ruwanwali saya dakkahama, wadinawada , galak gahanawada kiyala kiyanne meya.
kusalayata hari akusalayata hari action eka decide karanne methanadi.

(8) woththapana sitha -> (9) jawan sitha ( ekama quality ekak tiyena sitha methana 7 parak wada karanawa)
jawaya kiyanne shakthiyak neda,
jawana pitiya kiyanne duwana pitiya
kriyakaari sith tiyenne methana.
karma athi karanawa sith 
(9)J->(10)J->...->(14)J->(15)J-> (16)(17) thadaa-aarambana sitha

thadaa rambana , kiyanne arambaye awasanaya.
methana sitha dekak pawathinawa.
ekasithakin awasanaya da anith sithin , bawangayata alla deemada (bawanga gatha weema) siduwei.


ethkota chiththa withi life cycle eka gaththu hama

thi->na->da->pa->cha->sa->n->wo->jjjjjjj->tha,tha->nawatha bawangayata

dan me ekaka kuda chiththakshana 3 gane tiyenawa
ethkota 
roopage ayusha chiththakshana 17i
kuda chiththakshana nam 51i

ethkota palamu 3ma bawanga sith ( thi,na,dha)
ethkota palamu bawanga sith 3, roopayak aramunu karanne na.


 
prasadaye gatenna niyamitha roopaya upadichcha mohothe tibena bawanga sitha api kiyanawa atheetha bawanga sitha kiyala
bawangasithe kriyakarithwara itha wegayen gana nisa,

prasadaye gatena roopaya,
pera pasu novee, heart (hardaya wasthuwe) pawathna bawanga chiththaye ha gate.(meka atheetha bawanga sitha nevi, me next bawangaya, mekata api kiyana bawanga chalanaya kiyala)
me nisa eelaga chiththakshanayedi sitha galawei. (dan route eka wenas wela) (meka bawanga upachchedaya kiyala adunwanawa)

ipida eka chiththakshanayak ikma giyata pasuwa , roopalambanaya
chakku prasaadeye gatenne deweni chiththakshanayedi. 

roopaya aramunu karala athi wena palamu chiththaya ( upachchedaya pasuwa)
pancha-idwara chiththaya kiyala hadunawanwa.
ethan patan dewani thada-arambanaya dakwa athi sith 14 ( thunak iwarai ne)
parasadaye gatunu roopaya aramunu kota ipadunu sith wei.

Next session
karamaya,karma nimithi, gathi nimithi ( maranasanna chiththa withiye aramuna athiwana hethu thamai me)
chiththa withi athara paratharaya
mono idwarika 4 


------------------pancha iskanda saha pancha upadana iskanda -----------20/03.2021-------------

me deka dekak, saha e awabodaya aniwarayen oni niwan awabodaya pinisa.

me deka nikan twinsla wage , eliyen balala hoyanna ba.
hoya ganna puluwan wenne, ekata prathya wena dharmatha walin.

tiyenawa , karanawa , balanwa ... wage hithata hithena hama deyak ma tiyenne pancha upadana isknadayata.

pancha upadana iskandaya - wadakayek ehema naththam pasa-mithurek ( mithuru wesin inna hathurek) let thamai dakwala tiyenne.
pancha upadana iskandaya ta dena nam 40k dharmaye dakwenawa.
ex: gaduwak,ulak..etc
ehema kiyanna hethuwa eka e tharam wisak

wenasa hoya ganna puluwan wenna prathya walin handa
dan prathya balamu deke

thanhawa -> pancha upadana iskandaya 

panchaskandaya adyathmika ekak nevi, katawath aithiyak kiyanna ba.
  
panchaskandaya kiwwata ethana tiyenne ( skanda 5k), ithin e wala prathya balamu
- roopa iskandaya (sathara maha dathu saha (4k) ewa asuru karagena ena upadaya roopa(asuru kara gena ena mewa 21 tiyenawa)
---- ahaara prathya
- wedana iskandaya ( wedanawa yanu weemak danaweemai, methana athi unu roopaya aramunu karan athi unu wedanawa)
---- isparya prathya
-sanya iskandaya ( haduna ganeema hadayen warnayen e roopaya haduna ganeema)
---- isparya prathya
-sankara iskandaya ( gatena aheema,  pahala weema )
---- isparya prathya
wynana iskandaya (dana ganeema)
---- nama roopa prathya

methana nama ( wedana, sanya , sankara walata ) roopa (roopa iskandayata)

ikanda kiyana de wigraha karanne , kalaya ha awakashaya matha
e nisa 11 aakarayata bedenawa, roopaya gaththoth
> atheetha roopa
> warthamana roopa
> anagatha roopa
> olarika roopa ( asa, kana, nasaya, diwa,shareeraya)saha ewagata gochara wena roopa (gorosu mattame ewa)
> sukuma roopa ( chiththa samuttaana roopa)(hitha nisa hata ganna roopa)
> heena roopa
> praneetha roopa
> dura roopa 
> laga roopa
> adyathmika roopa
> bahira roopa

me widihata wedana,sanya ,sankara and wynyana lesa pawathinawa
11 akaara 5 e nisa =  iskanda 55

dan balann methana thahawena hadichcha kisiwak na.

api paramartha dharma katha karathi meke pawathina 4k katha kala 
chiththa , chithasika, roopa, nibbana kiylaa.
owa withrai me loke tiyenne.

methana 

chiththa kiyanne wynanam iskandayata
chithasika gode tiyenawa wedana,sanya, sankara
roopa gode tiyenwa roopa iskandaya

methana me thune api aithiyak , pudgala bawayen thamai katha karanne 
habai methana pudgala sobawaya ganna kenek na

me katha karana mattame iskandawala athma drushtiyak na ( aithiyak gana katha karanna ba)
kisi panaweemak ( sathwa pudgala washayen, ehema naththam kama loka aroopa loka lesa ) tiyenna ba.

me iskanda tika ehema panawannam hithe keles tiyenna oni
ehema panawanne e e mattame tiyena keles walin. ( thanha -> upadana -> bawa)

me keles mattamen me iskanda asuru karana kota
api roopa walata wena namak kiyanawa saasaawa upaadaniyaa kiyala ( aasrawa walata saha upaadana walata hithathi kiyana arthya)
ethkota 
pancha iskandaya niyojanaya wenne paramartha dharma walin
eka asuru karanna gihin upadana iskandayak hada ganna wa.
( meka hada ganna nisa thamai apita niwan dakinna puluwan, upadana iskandaya hadila handa dana gena galawanna puluwan handa)

pariya panna boomiya ( thun lokayata athulath, kama,roopa,aroopa loka) prathya wenna keles.
apariya panna boomiya ( lokoththara boomiya) prathya wenne nuwanai / praknawai
niwanaya kiyana eka iskanda walata aithi na, e kiyanne apariya panna boomiyath ikmawa yanna oni.
eka kaalaya saha awakashayata aithi na.

ex:
gehan ge niwana , sarath ge niwana ehema ekak na  ( aithiyak panawanne na)
atheetha niwana, warthamana niwa ehema ekak na ( kalayak pawathinne na)
niwana kisiyam idak ganne ho, pawathina thanak  ehema ekak na. ( awakashayak ganne na)

e nisa iskanda walata aithi na.

aashrawa kiyanne boho kal asuru karapu gathi.
ex:
gahak tiyenawa 
geyak tiyenawa 
gehan innawa 
gehan ge gedara . e widihata pudgalayek thanak deyak kiyala asurak tiyenawa 
anna ekata thamai asrawa kiyala kiyanne.

namuth
roopayan ge lakshana
anaathmai, roppanaya wei ( samawitama wenas wei, anithyai), dukai ( asuru kirima handa thamai meka athi wenne)

aashrawa handa meka mata oni widihata tiya ganna puluwan kiyala gannawa 
enam aasrawa nisa roopaya nithya lesa gannawa 
ehi anathma swaroopaya balanne na.

ex:
onna mata puluwan pol gas naginna kiyala kiyanwa 
namuth kakula kadunoth pol gas naginna puluwan da ?

kakula kadenne nathuwa isthiya lesa tiya ganna mata puluwan da ? ehema ba
enam roopawa mata oni widihata pawathwanna ba
namuth pol gas nagala tiyena hakiyawa handa 
api kakule kadime sobawaya amathaka karala thamai katha karanne 

ehema naththam  roopaye anathma sobawaya maga harala .
e nisa athma lesa gannawa.

anathma kiyala kiyanne thamunge wasagaye pawathwanna bari bawa.
shareeraya aithi roopaiskanyatama thamai.
roopaskandaya yata prathya wenne aahara. ( jathi 4k tiyenne ein kabalinka ahara gamu)

kabalinka ahara wala tiyenneth sathara maha dathuwen hadichcha, ewa anaathmai.
anaathma dewal kala athma wu shareerayak hadei da ?

roopaya asuru kirimama dukak.aasawaa upaadaaniyaa ( asuru kirimama dukak) duka athi wenne me aasawa walata athi purudda nisa.
 ehenam me roopaya anathmai, . 
 e wagema eka anithyai , samawitama wenas wei (nithya na)(rooppanaya wei)
 e wagema me roopa ani-miththai ( nimithi na, raga, idwesha, moha gathi roopaye na)
 e wagema me roopa wala prarthana karanna puluwan kisiwak na. enam appani-hithai kiyala ( mata sapa labewa, duka labewa kiyala , ehema ewa roopa wala na neda?)
 e wagema sathwa pudgala gathiyakuth na e nisa roopa shunyai.
 
 e nisa
 roopa samawithama, hihatha lakshana 6n yukthai. ( aniyai,dukkai, anathmai. animiththai, appani hithai, shunyai)
 
 ex:
 dan oyata yamak sihi karanna puluwan hakiyawa niyojanaya wenne pancha upadana iskanyakin mai
 aththatama e sihi wana roopaya ,
 me mohothe tibena saba roopaya nevi.
 e wage ma roopayak mai ( twin wage)
 
 mata onna office kola pata mesaya sihi wenawa.
 eka mathakaye tibila thamai sihiyata awe.
 habawata me mohethe eka penne na.
 namuth eka ha samaana roopayak thamai athi une.
 sihi kirime hakiyawa me roopa walata tiyenawa.
 enam roopa upadana iskandaya sihi kirimata puluwan.
 namuth roopa skandaya sihi karanna ba.
 
 mama  diha kannadiyen balapuwahama mata penne warna satahanak nada.
 habai hithe hadenne mama me wage kiyana iwaroopaya.

 aawe warna satahana witharai. namuth hadunu roopaya aththa roopaya nevi eka upadana iskandayak.
 e nisa roopa upadana iskandayen sathya hoya ganna ba.
 e nisa api bahira tiyena iskanda panchakaya wisthara kara gaththa.
 
 saasawa upaadaniya kiyala  updana iskandayata aithi roopaya bahirin haduna gaththa
 namuth api methana withara kale eka nevi.
 methana wisthara kale pancha iskandaya gana. ethana aashawa dharma na.

summary:
api methek dakapu roopawa athule twin sobawaya thamai api aduna gaththe.
e twin kenek 
sathara ma butha dathun gen saduna, paramartha dharma asuru karagath pancha isknadaya 
anith ekathamai
me pancha iskandaya asuru karagena sadaa gath upadana roopa. 

ethkota hithe hadena roopa -> pancha upadana roopa

ex:
danna hoda lagama kenek mathak karaganna 
eyawa hamba wenna , call ganna , katha karanna oya yanawa.
oyata eya innakota , eya gana sihi wenawa, eyawa balanna yanawa.
dan onna eya marenawa.
dan liyum, katha karana ewa karanna ba.
habai eyawa sihi wenawa ( atheetha roopaya sihi enawa)
oya ganu denu karapu roopaya thamai sihi wenne.
oyata mathaka iwaroopaya thamai sihi wenne.
e roopa iskandaya aththatama nathi unath, sihi weema pawathinawa.
sihi karala adannath puluwan.
e roopa upadana isknadayai.

roopa upadana isknadaya thamai duka genawe.
e wagema roopa upaaana iskandaya thanahawa nisa athi wena handa.
eka eka marana sidda unath athi wena duka wiwidai. 
thama thaman ge thanhawa anuwa , sonyojana ( badeem) walata anuwa duka wiwida mattam walin pawathinawa.
habai kuka kelawara wela na.
e unata roopaskandaye me mukuthma na.

e nisa panada upadana iskandayama dukak bawa budun deshana kala

me anuwa niwanta yana para saha sasarata yana paara thoraganna wenawa.

ex:
eka nika kochchi rail para wage.
eka welawakata kochchi para open, anith welawata bus para open.
e wagethamai 
niwan para clear wenawkota sasara para close
sasara para clear wenakota niwana para close.

ex:
nilpata sunglass ekak da ganna .
dan eliye paththen manussayek enawa thanikara sudu ada gena.
athule kenata eliya kena penne nil patata.
awata tiyena deyak aramunu karala baluwath penne nil patata.

kannadiya nikan awidyawa wage.
athule inna ape hitha
bahira tiyenne roopa.
penuna nil pata roopaya upadanayai.
enam bahira penneth upadanayak widihatamai.
namuth api hithanawa roopaiskanda mai dakke kiyala .
kannadiye awidyawa handa.
 
bahira roopaya tibuna ho notibuna ho.
upadanaya nisa athi unu duka wenas wenne na.

ehema naththam,
dukta hethu unu upadanaya, bari pawathina roopaya samaga galapau nisa , bahira roopa athi n nathi wenas weemen.
duka pawathina bawa awidyawa nisa api gannawa.
namuth. 
me upadanaya ye sobawaya nisa ma thamai me duka.

pera karapu karmayaka palayak widihata ,
apita asa kana nasaya labila tiyenawa.

e nisa atheetha hethu 5k thamai.
- awidya  
- sankara
- thanhawa
- upadana
- bawa

e nisa apita labena pala 5k tiyenawa. (jeewithaya)

- wynaana
- nama roopa
- salayathana
- passa 
- wedana

labena pala nisa api nawatha athi weeme hethu 5k hadanawa
e hethu 5 nisa apahu jiwithayak labenawa.

- thanha
- upadana
- bawa
- awidya
- sankara 

 e nisa mathu bawaye jeewithaya nawatha labanawa.
 meka thamai ( hethu->pala, pala->hethu, hethu->pala)
 
 
 ethkota niwan dakinna
 wipaakaya wipaakayak lesa dakima
 ehi keles , anusaya natha, enam nawa karma sakas weemak natha
 
 penawa kiyala kiyanne mokadda ?
 wipaka mattame peneemak, eka apata nawathwanna ba.
 sitha yeduna handa upadana iskanadayak kiyala kiyanawa 
 namuth meme upadana iskandaya upadana wela na ( pera karapu karmayaka prathipalaya apita nawathwanna ba)
 
 ex;
 kandak udata naggoth wate penawa.
 bahithdi wate penne na. enam e roopa wala peneema iwarai.
 
 ethkota kanda udata giya nisa thamai aatha penune.
 enam kanda udata yama, sitha yedeema nisa penuna.
 kanden bahinakota hethu wenas.
 
penieema athiwana hethu dewidihakata wishtharakala
1) karmaya anuwa , wipaka mattamen
2) anya wu hethu nesas

hethu waya wela peneemai. ekama mohothaka wela tiyenne.
meya athi kal meya wei.

ex:
wathure diyasulak tiyenawa
meka ekak da dekak da ?
meka ekak kiwwath ho dekak kiwwath waradie.
methanata patticha samuppadaya niyaaya galapenawa.
hethu prathyayen athi wu wak.
meka withara karanna ba.

atheethaya sihi weemama nathara wenna oni (chetho - wimukthi)
wimukthi nyana darshana ( marga pala nyana)
ekai rahath sobawaya. 
eya pudgalayek nevi.

sanyuktha nikaye , 3 wana kanda suthraya.

questions
thirokunda suthraya - kalpa anu ganaka pera relations pin deema gana kiyanawa.
mathakaya wada karanne kohomada

--------------------pancha upadana iskandaya udaya waya gamburin part 2 ---------------

meka igena ganeeme tiyena bararum kama mulin balamu.

ex: card sellamak gamu
pinthura paththa eliyata hitina widihata 
backside eka mage paththata tiyala yaluwanta penawana kiyala hithanna
apita penne na satahana.
api yaluwo set ekath ekka parashna kara kara meke tiyenne mokadda kiyala dana ganna try karanawa.

eka karanne ape tiyena danum mattam walin, ape dan tiyena danum mattamata thawa aluthe deyak ekathu kara ganna widihata.
mokada apita eka purudu wela tiyenne ehema.

methana karalath tiyenne asharawa wadi karaganna eka witharai.
api mamathwaya hewweth me widihatamai.
mamathwaye tiyena lakshana walin thamai haduna gaththe. namuth mamathwaya dakala na.

e wage pancha upadana isknadaya me card eka pinthura paththe tibba nam.
api eka hoyannthen me danum mattam sansandanayen, naththam me purudu walin.

me karamayata kawadawath adyathmika wigrayak therum ganna ba.
api sama witama bahira deyin mai alla ganna try karanne.

ex:

mama thulin thamai dharmaya dakinna hadanne.
namuth dharmaya thulin mama thamai dakiya yuththe.

api pancha upadana iskandaya hoyanneth oni dharmaya thulin. eka bahira danumen allaganna ba.  mage danumen nevi.

pancha upadana isknadaya gana katha karapuwahama , sama witama api hithanne eka bahira roopa ashrawa karagena.
namuth eka thanhawen hata ganna nisa, melesa kaama loka indriyan gen gochcara kara ganna ba.
eka adhyathmika wigrahayak.
eka bahirin ena deyak lesa haduna ganna ba.

api ehema dewal mechcha kalayak igena gena na.
api me igena ganna system eken adyathmika wigrayan ismathu wenne na.

ex:
chanda ragaya kiwwahama apata hithenne mata tiyena kamaththa kiyala.
api ehema hithala e wage prathipadawakin thamai thanhawa duru karanna yanne.
ethkota chanda ragaya mul wela thamai duka enne.
ehema misak yam deyakata athi kamaththa mul karagena nevi.

kamaththa and chanda ragaya athara wenasa mokadda ?
budun deshana karanne.
thanhawa duru karana widiha nevi,
arya ashtangika margaye widihata, 
thanawaha pilisida dakina kota , awidyawa duru kirimen thanha nirodayai pennuwe. (samma dittiya)

api dan margaya hoyannna yanne ,

mage thanahawa duru karanna kiyana nam , mage weemata mame athi bawa sanatha wela. 
enam awidyawata asuru sanen ahu wela.

thanhawa pihitana thana nathi kirimai wenne. (ehenam thanhawa hatagaththu hethu nirodaya krimai sidu kale)
me subject eka nodaneema ,nisa upakalpana matha based weema.

ex: hithanne oya train stations ekaka innawa kiyala underground tunnel ekak tiyenawa.
oyata ena train eka paththa wenas kiyala hithala baluwoth e paththata thamai yanne.

ethkota me balana konaya ( angle eka ) anuwa pena de wenas wenawa.
laukika dema laukika ho lokoththara washayena baleema siduwanne me koonaya mathai.
koonaya namathi awidyawa duru kara, arya konayen baliya yuthui.

laukika paththatatha tiyenne danuma, ( anu sothagami) ( danumen balana handa ashrawa pawathi)
lokoththara paththata tiyenne prakshyawa / awabodaya (pati sothagami) ( awabodaya nisa asharawa sadeemak natha)
  

last session eke di , 
adyathmika paththe asa gana misak bahira pena de gana nevi explain kare. ( i repeated this several times but i think you missed it)

hithana bawa wenas wenne konaya mathai. ehema naththam sakas weema sidu wanne balana widiha anuwai.


hamuwenne deyak. ( kiwwa gaman hithanne deya tiyenne bahira kiyalane)
hamuwenawa kiwwe deyak hamu weema nevi.

adyathmika wa hamuwenne , mechchara kal karapu waradda, ehena naththam awidyawa
meme deyak hamu weeme waradi sobawaya awaboda weema , prakyawe awadiyai, ehenam samma dittiyai.


api dan udaya waya gana balamu...

ahata warnya gocharai
kanata shabdaya gocharai

ex:

camerawa athi prasada roopaya ( nikan photo nogahapu reel ekawage), asa kiyanneth tirayak witharai.
aloka kiranaya watena witama, eka pichchenawa.
eka nawatha use karanna ba.
use karanna nam, prasadaya aluthen hadenna oni. 
eelaga mohothe ena alokaya nisa eka pichchenawa.

melesa , saama prasa roopayak ma athiwana thanama nathi wei.
digatama pawathina swabawayak naha. enam eka digata pawatina asakuth na, roopayakuth na.
(anuppada nirodhaya)

menna methana thamai udaya waya tiyenne.

menna me process eka hariyata dakkoth, pancha upadana iskandaya athi wenne ba neda ?
enam me athi wena thana nirodaya , dakina vidyawa pahala unahama ( praknyawa )
pancha upadana isknaya sakas wenna ba neda.

e hinda thamai me prasada roopaye udaya waya dakima ma paramanawath kiyanne .
mokada awidyawa wada karana sobawaya , enam ape upan gei waradda ismathu kara ganna puluwan.

budda wachanaya wenne
athi wechcha deka nathi weema nowa.
athi wana bawa nathi weemai. ( anuppada nirodaya)

e nisa 

api magen sewwoth lokayen ma thamai ahuwenne.
api mage lokaya soyana widiha hoyanna oni.

enam , card eken tiyena eka hoyanawata wada , card eka hoyana kenage hoyana widihata sewiya yuthui.

adyath ma - mama
bahira - mage

ex:
mage duwa
mage gedara
mage pansala
me ahu wenne barima thamai.

mama - mage kiyana eke himikaruwa kawda ?
anathma dharshana thula mehema kenek nathi bawa thamai awabodaya wenna oni.

meka dana gaththahama, yana enamak nathuwa yanawa... eka normal.
mokada niwanata yana enamak, ena yana kenek, pin paw, sathara iriyaw na.

thanhawata wahal bawayen nidas weemata puluwan.


enam maa thulin dharmaya dakka nevi.
dharmaya thulin maa nathi bawa dakimai.

maa naththm pancha upadana sadenne na.

athi wana bawa nathi weemen thamai meka dakke.
athi bawa nathi weemen novei.
thanahawa pihitimata thanak nathi weemai.

chulla wedalla suthraye, dhamma dinna rahath theraniya ha wisaaka athara athi discussion eka balanna.



ex:

bahira roopaya saha adhyathmika roopaya ekama nevi kiyana eka me vidihata oppu karanna puluwan.

eka ahak wahala , anith ahen bahira bulb eka balanna
wahapu aha ehema tiyena kota aragena tiyena ahe awata mussle eka ehata mehata kranna.
dan pena bulb eka helawenawa neda.

e helaune eliye tibba bulb ekada.
eliye tibba bulb eka helaune na.
ehenam ahen dakke eliye tiyena bulb eka nevi.
ehenam e deka dekak.


manese hadena 31 weni roopaya mokadda ?
meka wenne mathakayen. meka hadenne manomaya washayen.

mathakaya kiyanne awidyawe kotasak.
mathakaya kiyanne aroopi dharmathawak ne.
hithe sobawaya sithana ekamai. sithimama sithak, 
mathakaya lesa ahu wenne awidyawa thula athi nithya sanyawamai.
meka manase hakiyawak.
eka kenek ge nirmanayakin soyanna ba apita.


udaya -waya ganna danna dakina kenata thamai budun wahanse ashrawa ikya kirimak gana katha kale.
udaya-waya prakthasha wela tiyenna oni.


---------------------------------18/04/2021-----------------
udaya waya part 3 , pattichcha samuppadaya apply karana wena pariyayak ( thawa widihak/ thawa angle ekak)
------------------------------------------------------------

me pariya walhugak tiyenawa. e nisa ( kenek hithapu ekata wada wenas deyak kiwwahama hari de thoranna yanawa)
api piligaththa method ekata anuwa wena ewa match wenne naththam api ewa discard karanawa.

hariyata nikan wahana thada badayaka, mata galapena widihata yanna handawa.
apita galapena widihata, therena widihata, ahala tiyena widihata, ape knowledge ekata 
gala pune naththam api eka piliganne na.
(mama first theory)
apita me dharamya absorb nowana hethuwa menna mekai.
budun kiyapu de apita madi wela.
scientist and other relative concepts walata galapannath api hadanawa.
enam e thulin apu mathayannta galapanna hadala.

enam me hama mathayak thulama mama innawa.
mamathwaya tiyneawa.
mata galapena dharmaya misak, budun deshana kala dharmayata ahunkam denne na.

buddha wachanaya api sentence ekata dammoth,

pera nothibimenma athi wela, sheshayak wath nathuwa nirudda wechcha dharmathawayak.

budun pennuwe anna ehema deyak.
meka api ape jeewithayata galapanna , 4 akarayakin wisthara karagannawa.
>ahenawa
>penenawa
>danenawa 
>dana gannawa

enam , ditta,sutha,mutha,wynyatha lesa gannawa. (ayathana 6 me karunu hatharen pennanna puluwan mutha ta 3k tiyenawa(diwa, nasaya, body))

api ekak balamu, ( hamadama ganne penewa handa ada ahenawa)
> ahenawa gamu.

kana , shabbada mulika karagana ahenawa kiyana eka wisthara kale.
e deka tiyenawa kiyala assumption eka uda idan thamai me okkoma katha karala tiyenne.
enam kana, shabbadaya nithya lesa aran neda me katha karala tiyenne.
api nithya sanyawen neda meka allanna hadala tiyenne.
me base knowlege apply karapu widiha harida ?

nithya sanyawen thamai api anithya sanyawa hoyanna hadala tiyenne.
api kakul deka comfetability tiya gena inne nithya sanyawemai.

starting point ekama waradila neda ?
budu dahama anithya wu dharshanayak.
meka nithya sobawayen allagena hoyanna puluwan da ?
ese seweema waradi neda ?

ahenawa kiyana eka kiya padayak da naama padayak da ?
bus ekak yanawa kiwwahama eka kriyawak neda
kriywak naama padayakin wisthara karanna puluwan da .

namuth kanak, shabdayak kiyanne naama pada.
ehenam aheema kiyana kriya padaya naamak una kanak, shabdayak lesa wisthara karala.
eka hari da.
kanath , shabdayath nisa aheema kiyana eka waradie.

ethkota aheemak nadda ?

nahai kiyala kiyanna bane, mokada ehenam e gana katha karanna deyak nane.
tiyenawa kiyala gaththoth nithyai kiyala aran neda.
ekakota aheema kiyana nithya sanyawak tiyenawa da ?

nithya wu aheemak , na neda ? ( digatama ahena ekak na)
meka isthiwa tiyena ekak nevi ehenam pera nothibimen athi wechcha ekak ( enam pathrayan gen hata gaththu ekak)

ekata wachanayak denna epai, mekata api kiyana sumdaya kiyala ( pera nothibimen hatagaththu, sakas unu/ sanskaranaya/ sankaara)
pera notibeemen hata ganna sobawayata api udaya kiyala kiyanawa.

udaya nam nikan tikak therenawa, 
namuth waya kiyana eka kohomada dana ganna.

kanai shabdayak kiyana base eka waradi handa , apita waya gana katha karanna points na.
kanak , shabbayak nathi thana aheemak nathi bawa kiyanna ba.

ehenam meka apita kagen hari ahanna wenawa.
danna kenek gena ahanna wenawa.
budun gen ma thamai me gana ahanna wenne.

ex:
kukkusathi kiyana raja kenek, budun hamu wenne gawa polaka hitiya.
budun wadiyata passe , machang level eken katha kale , ayushmathun wahansa kiyala.
dan budun eya dakalada ?
budun dharmaya deshana kalata pasuwa thamai , ane mata waradeemak kiyala. samawa illuwe.
budun dakinna puluwan ekama widiya thamai dharmaya thulin.

e kiyanne asen dakina dharmaya dakeema nevei. dharmaya thulin oni budun dakinna.

api mechchara kal kiwwe,
kanai , sabbdaya nisa aseema athi una kiyala ( eya athi kal hi meya wei)
namuth 
pattichcha samuppada niyaya ta anuwa  ( meya athi kalhi meya wei)
meka symultaniously wena ekak.
meka pattichcha samuppada siddiyak, 
kana, shabbdaya saha aseema kiyana thunama ekama mohothaka vidya mana wana siddiyak.

meya athi kalhi meya kiyana kota - meya, meya kiyana dekama ekama bawa thamai methana therum ganna oni.
imasmin sathi idan hothi. 

ex:
alokaya athi wita adura nathi weema, 
 ( eya athi kal hi meya wei) - apita therenne , alokaya apu handa adura nathi wela kiyala
 ( meya athi kalhi meya wei) - alokaya , adurai ekama kasiyaka depaththa, adura nathuwa alokaya pawathinna ba. ehenam alokaya wadi wana wita adura aduwenawa  or vice versa.coin eka gaththath, apita penne eka paththai , habai depaththak samawitama tiyenawa. me dekama ekata hata ganna wu , pattichcha samuppanna siddiyak.
 ethkota meya saha meya wenne ekama kasiya nisa, ekakata pasuwa anekak sidu weema nevi, eka wara sidu weema.
 me ekinekata link wunu sobawaya thamai api dakinna oni.
 
 
dan apita udaya kiyana eka therenawa
samudaya kiyana eka therenawa.

ethkota waya haduna ganne kohomada,
meka gana kiyanna api laga words na. ( nithya sanyawen gaththu eka waradie kiwwane)
ehenam mata ekata uththarak denna ba.
budun kiyala dunnu de soyanna oni.

budun deshana kale,
pera nothibimenma athi wee sheshayak wath nathuwa nirudda wei.

me budda wachcanaya thula nirodaya pawathinawa.
meka apita lokaya thula wigraha karanna ba.
e nisa budun ge wachanayak lesi shardrawen piliganna wenawa.
meya lokaya thula nathara weemata nevi, ethara weema dunnu wachanayak.

ethkota,
mama kiyana concept eka methanta danna ba, mokada nithya sanyawa nathi nisa.
enam mama alu wela gihin.

enam 
mamek innawa epai, paw pin karanna
mamek innawa epai , sansare yanna.
mamake naththam siyalu duk nimawai neda

enam meka therum giyahama api pruthak jana konayen arya konayata maru wenawa.
enam marga pala gyanaya ipadenawa.
nuwana pahala wenawa.
 
 
 ex:
 
beejayak hoda polowaka pala karapuwahama palayak hambuwenawa.
pala weema kiyana kriyawa hamu une nane da ?
kalin beejaya hambuna dan palaya hambuna.
pala weema kiyanneth me  sanskarana wage , 
sansakaraya hamu wenne na. 

ex 2:
oyata rathu pata karayak yanawa penawa
dan yanawa kiyana eka panewada
oyata pata wenas weemak penawa.
namuth oya yanawa kiyala hithanawa.
eka imagination ekak.
enam kriyawa kawadawath penne na.
enam sanskaranaya penne na.
ekama thamai duka.

menna me duka gana misak wedanawen ena duka gana nevi budun focus karanna kiyanne.
sankara duka thamai deshana kale.

waya kiyana ekata wachana naththam, lokaya thula katha karanna bari nam, 
lokayen eliya dakapu kenekgen margaya asa dana ganna oni.
budda wachanaya mokadda  ?
yan kinchi samudaya dhamman
sabbanthan nirodha dammanthi

enam me penne nathi samudaya , awaboda karagath wita nirodaya ethanama athi bawa sakshath wenawa.
 
yankinchi samudaya dhamman < - yamak sumudaya wunada , e siyallama ethanama nirodai.

ex:
rathu pata car eka yana kota , car eka tiyenawa kiyala gaththa handa thamai api yanawa kiyana eka hambune.
yanne mokadda car eka.
e nisa penune car eka
car eka hadune manase enam, nithya washayen gaththu  e manomaya car eka dan 
yanawa, warna satahan wenasa, car eke gamanaya lesa api gannawa.
warna wenasa api haduna gena inne me manomaya car eka thulin.

warna wenasa api dakala tiyenna sada gath manomaya upadanaya thulin.
enam awidyawa nisa hata gath manomaya upadanaya thulin.
warna wenasa upadanaya nokara gath wita.
warna wenasa hatagath thanama niroda wena bawa therum yanawa.

enam , car eka giya kiyana eka ahu une sanskaranaya hariyata ahu nowuna nisa.
sanskaranaya ahu una nam ithuru nathuwa ma niruddai. meka thamai prakyawen dakinawa kiyanne.
ethana thamai anithya. ethana thamai "waya"
samudaya wana thanama "waya"
samudaya dakka kiyanne "waya" dakala.
eka mama dakka nevi, budda bashithaya thulin dakke.

budun deshana kala widihata
sabbanthan nirodha dhamman -> siyalu de nirodha wenna oni . namuth apita car eka ithuru wela.

ehenam mechchara kalayak api nirodhaya hoyala tiyenne 
pancha upadana iskandaya thulin
ithin car eka ethana nathi bawa kiwwata , ehema therum yanne na
mokada car eka penena nisa.

namuth warna wenasa athi thana niroda wana bawa dakkahama , siyalu de nirodha wana bawa dakinna puluwan.
"waya" kiyana eka awaboda kara ganna puluwan.

udaya waya kiyanne onna othanata.

"udaya waya" mage knowledge eken ganna ba. ehema baleema dharmayen baleema novie.
dharmayen "udaya waya" dhakinna oni.

ex:
"mama" kiwwoth niwanak na 
mata gehan kiwwoth niwene hulagath na.

dakinakotama , meya sudath, meka almariya kiyapu gaman api ahu wela iwarai. pramaadai
indriya dharma hodata wadila tiyenne oni, meka welasana haduna ganna.
(shardha,veerya,sathi,samadhi,prakyna)
e thathwayata tune wenna oni,
maraya ekata ida denneth na, kohen hari alla gannawa.

menna me tika dana gaththahama api kiyanawa  " dhamman saranam gachchami kiyala"

isipiso gathawa <- me point eka eli karapu thanaththa 
swakkatho bagawatho dhammo <- me point eka gana dharmaya.
supatipanno <- me arya sangaya wahanselage guna.

ex:
awidinawa kiyala explain karanna kiwwahama,
kattiya kiyanne, onna left kakula tibba dan right kakula tibba
namuth mehema kiyala tiyenne oya hithalane.
ethkota me wisthara karala tiyenne oya hithana ekane. 

awidinawa kiyana eka wisthara karanna kiwwahama hithana eka wistharka karala hari yanawada ?
sanyaa dekak kawadath overlap wenne na. ( ekata hamuwenne na)
(methana hatiyata , awidinawa kiyana kriyawai, hithanawa kiyana kriyawai ekata yedenne na)
awdinawa kiyanne shareerayata daneemak danenawa witharai. (mutha sanyawak)
hithata aithi winyatha kiyana kotasa.

awidinawa kiwwahama api wisthara karanne hithin hithapu de.
api keriya dekak ekak kiyala sambanda karla.

alawwe anomadassi hamuduruwange deshana balanna.
chulla wedalla suthraya balanna.

--------------------------pattichcha samuppadaya gamburata--------02/05/2021--

imasmin sathi, idan hothi
imasmin asathi, idan nahothi
(meya athi kal hi meya wei) its not (eya athi kal hi meya wei)

update: alokaya & adura gana use karapu coin example eka needs some correction.

uda haranayak kiyanne dharmaya nevi.
eka upamawak witharai, upamawak denne loka-dharma tha walin.
ekai eka logical, ekai apita eka wadipura therenne.
habai upamawa kiyanne dharmaya nevie.
adahasa/ hageema ismathu wena hangeema witharai apita ganna tiyenne.
ehema nathuwa upamawa dharmaya lesa nogatha-uthui.
ehema gaththoth, api eka allanne lokaya thulai, aye api antha thamai poshanaya karanne.
ayeth api mula,mada aga kiyana antha walata yanawa.
e hinda hageema aragena (upamawen thorawa) dharmaya awaboda karagatha uthui.

ex: wathure hadena diya suliya.
wathura saha diya suliya ekak da dekak da ?
me sobawaya, dekakuth nevi ekakuth nevi.
lokaya thula meya dekak ho ekak lesa dakiya hakie.
dekak nam ekak wen karagatha haki wiya yuthui.
ekak nam , haduna ganeem dekak noviya yuthui.

mema siduweemaya , lokaya thula wachanayak denna puluwan kamak na.
lokayen ikmawoo dharmathawayak penweemata thamai hethu pala niyaaya, hewath imasmin sathi idan hothi kiyana pattichcha samuppada niyaya budun deshana kale.

api lokaya thula sama witama wigraha kara ganne palayen palaya dakina widihai.

ex: kaudnu putuwai gana kiyanne hoda putuwak oluwe tiya gena.
putuwak tiyenawa kiyanne putuwak nathu sobawayata sapekshawa.
putuwak aththema na kiwwoth eth putuwata saapekshai.
mese athi bawa ho nathi bawa kiyanne lokaya thula hamu wena deyak.
budun wahanse wadale nathi weema gana nowa.
nirodaya ganai.

e nisa "eya nisa meya" hata ganna bawa tiyenne lokaya thulai, enam eka pattichcha samuppadaya nowe.
pattichcha samuppadayen ethara weemak/nirodayak wiya yuthui.
ehenam pattichcha samuppada dharma niyayen anuppada nirodaya ismathu karai.

enam imasmin sathi, idan hothi.
meya athi kal hi meya wei.

wathurai, diyasuliyai example ekata dammoth.
lokaya thula -> wathura wenamai diya suliya wenamai. ( issella wathura dan diya suliya wela , api katha karala tiyenne palayan dekaka wenasak gana) ( wenasa pennanne hamatissema kalayak peradari karagena)
patticha samuppadaya thulin baluwoth meya dakkinna oni -> akalikawai, ( kalayata anuwa nowei.)   enam kalayak nathuwa wenasak pennanna ba. ( apita kalaya lokaya thula isthira wela)
akalikawa ehema balanna ba.
ekata kiyanne pachchupanna kiyala . ( ennam prathyen upan bawa)
wathurai , diyasuliyai, patticha samupada dharmaya thulin. meya athi kal hi meya wei lesa baliya yuthui.
enam, wathura ta prathya wu deyak pawathina thek wathura pawathi.
suliyata prathyawu deya pawathina thek suliya pawathie.

enam sapekshawa balannath ba , kalayen balannath ba.
e nisa me dharmathawaya harima siyum and gaburui.
lokayathulin wisthra kirima harima aseerui.

e nisa , me sobawaya awaboda kara gatha yuthui.
ese kala hakke nyanayak ipadaweemen pamanai.
e nyanaya sandaha yoniso manasikara kala yuthui. mama hithen karana manasikaraya ( mata sapaksha nisa eya prathya wekshayak) 
enam prathyakshaya sanada budun wahanse ge dharmaya wena yomu weemata weerya gatha yuthui.
meya yoniso manasikarayai.
e nisa yoniso manasikaraya thulinmai praknyawa upadinne. (annuppada nirodhaya dakeeme praknawa upadinne)

enam sapenkshawa balannath ba , kalayen balannath ba, 
kohomada "meya" awaboda karaganne.

(lokaya thula udaharanayakin wisthara karaganna balamu.)
ex: onna beejayak polawe hitawanawa.
prathipalaya palayak wenawa. ( anith prathya pahasukam dunnata passe , wathura, pohora)
palaye wardanaya, hewath wenas weema,
kiyala kiyanne sapekshwa baleemak, palayakin palayak.
palaya gana wistharak. meka wadak na.
budun wahanse deshana karanne hethuwa gana hoyanna kiyala.
beejaye pala weeme shakthiya apita penne na.
e hethu apita hambuwenne na. (e shakthiyata hethuwu prathya pahasu kam apita ahuwenne na, mokada api kiyathdi mama thulin baleema nisa)
meme parohana shakthi kriyawaliya apita penne na, e nisa katha karenne na. (penne na , danne na . katha karanne na)
ehema katha karana hama thanakama sitheema nisa athi wechcha palayak pamanai. (mano dwarika palayak)
hitheeme kriyawaliya thulath apita me parohana shakthi kriyawaliya hamuwela na.

muula pariyaya suthraye di ( majjima nikaye palaweni padama)
budun deshana karanawa lokaya thula sama pariyaa yakma mannyanawak ( hithaluwak, hithin sada gath deyak)
pamanai.

beejaya thula, api katha karana parohana shakthiya kiyana hakiyawa hewath sobawaya hamu nowanawa wagemai,
mamathwaya apita hamu noweema.
parohana shakthiya hamu noweema nisa pala athara sambanadaya katha karai.
maththwaya kiyana hakiyawa hamu noweema nisa pala athara sambandayak manomaya washayen api sada ganaie.
mema  mamathwaya kiyana sobawaya lokaya thula, hithaluwak misa sathyak novie. (hithaluwata anuwa mamek sada gena poshanaya karai)
sathya nopene.
eyai awidyawa.  
meya thula hewath hithaluwa thula sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wei.

enam,
meya athi kal hi meya athi wei. ( imasmin sathi idan hothi)
hithaluwak nisa hithaluwakma athi wei.
meyath drushtiyak.

onna ada dakwa ape gamane hatiyata,
1)mulin api bahirin tiyena sambandayen miduna, ( eliye tiyena de thamai api me dakkinne kiyana state eka waradi drushtiyak, kiyala haduna gaththa)(bahira ain kala)
2)hithen karana siyalu dewal hitheema nisa karana hithaluwak bawa awaboda karagaththa ( hitheeme palayak pamanai)
ehenam thamai api palaya thamai atha gala tiyenne, hethu hambu wela na. (abyanthaya ain kala)
3)kalaya tiyenne lokaya thulai, wenasa dakinne kalaye wenasin. hiss kiyala hithan inneth nathi bawak. (lokaya ain kala)

methanin idiriyata yanna,
budun kerehi achala shraddawen, budda wachanayata ahunkan denna oni. achala shraddawa athi wenne marga nyanayatai.

mama, mage kiyana hageema (manyyanawa/manyyathi)duru karapu wita karunak hamu novi niroda wenna oni. meme sobawaya (^na-manyyathi)kiyala hadunwanawa. (me niroda sobawaya tiyenne rahathan wahansetai) 
^ma-manyyathi - sathwa bawayakin thorawa, upan marga nyanaya 
 
manyyathi ->  ^ma-manyyathi -> ^na-manyyathi 
(mamathwaya)-> (mamathwaye)niroda margaya -> (mamathwaye)nirodaya

ma-manyyathi weema sanada sowan palayata laba ganna oni.

ex:
api pudgala sobawayen katha karapuhama, kesaa, loma, nakaa , dathaa, thacho kiyala
me penena dewal, api patavi kiyala aduna gannawa.
mama allagaththe , pancha indrangen ma thamai meka alla gaththe.
mama kiyala hitha gena hitapu hithaluwe penena widiha wisthara kirimak pamanai api karan tiyenne.
ehema hithana eka margaya nevi.
eka sammuthiye panaweemak witharai. ( sammuthiyata prakata weemak pamanai) ( prakata weema yanu nahai kiyala piliganna kamathi na, echcharakata apita eka prakata wela.)(echcharata api mamathwayata ahuwela)

meme "panaweema" gana budun deshana kale,
"nethan mama nesoo hamasmi"
"^na measo aththa"
mage nevi,man evi, mage athmaya nevi.

me widihata hithana eka marga nyanaye arambayai.   

(^ma-manyyathi) kiyana niroda margaya , marga praknyawata aithie.
sowan margaye sobawaya manyyana nokara dharshana nyanaya praguna kirimai. 
( udin kiyapu tika yoniso manasikarayen sihipath karana ekai)
summary : 
mechchara kalayak, api palayen palaya hoyala tiyenawa kalath ekka.
lokayen danuma labagena, danuma use karala palayak hoyagena.
me okkoma manyyana. meya pruthakjana sobawayai.

saeka pudgalaya kiyanne sowan margaye sita arihath margaya dakwa sitina pudgalayan. ( arya pudgalayan 7k)
1)sowan margaye in thanaththa
2)sowan palaya in thanaththa
3)sakurda gami margaya
4)sakurdagami palaya
5)anagami margaya
6)anagami palaya
7)arihath margaya.

saeka kiyala kiyanne hikmenawa kiyala eka. ( arya margayen hikmila, pruthakjana sobawayen thorai)

pruthakjana sobawaya haduna ganna mulin try karamu.

mechchara kalayak upadanaya sathwa pudgala sobawayen haduna gaththa.

upadanaya kara gaththa kiyanne manyyanawak kiyala dan therenawa.
menna me upadanaya kara ganeemata api kiyanawa upadaya kiyala.
kawda upadanaya kale mamathwayai, e nisa ethna manyyanawak thamai pawathinne.

upadana pachchaya bawo kiyala tiyenawa pattichcha samuppadaye.
methana katha karanne  marga wigrahayama thula.
ehenam sathwa pudgala sobawayen meka balanna ba
enam 
sathwa pudgala sobawaya ikmawa gaththu marga nirwachanayak thamai upadanayata tiyenne.
upadanaye haiyen thamai bawaya hadila tiyenne.

sathwa pudgala sobawaya ikama upadanaye swaroopaya haduna gatha hakke saeka pudgalayanta pamanai.
(habai meya manyyana karana kenek na)

ex:
api ekinekata labunu , ayathana athishain ekinekata awenikai.
api apema indriyan thamai pawichchi karanne.
allapu gedara wahanaya mage nowana bawa , bara ganne magemai wana indriyan thulin mai.
mage kiyana sobawaya already bara gaththu nisa thamai anunge kiyana sobawaya pawathune.
mage kiyana sobawaya bara gaththeth magemai kiyana indriyan thulinma thamai.
awidyawa athi kalhi,
-> salayathana kiyala  kiwweth me point ekata.
ayathana apita hamuwenneth lokaya thulama thamai.
ayathana thulin lokaya ikmawoo deyak allanna ba.
ayathana nirodayen lokaya nirudda wenawa.

methana nirodaya kiyanne nathi wenawa nevi, nathi wenna deyak tiyenna oni
nirodaya kiyana hata noganeemai.
enam uthum nirwanayai.


awidayawa athi kalhi salayathana wei.
bahin wath, (lokayen)
abyantharayen wath, ( manyyanawen)
kalayakin, 
sapekshawa bawakin wath

awidyawa ahuna ganna ba, ese haduna gaththu awdiya danumata gochara wu manyyanawak pamanai. 

awidyawa nathi kalhi loyaka/salayathanaya/kalaya nirodai.(hata noganie)

ex:
awiddyawa thaththa lesa ganna 
thanhawa amma lesa ganna
athi wana lamai mona widiha unath
amma thaththage jaana wenas karanna ba.

pin paw kala kiyala awiddyawa ho thanhawa wenas wenne na.
meya karanna puluwan marga nyanaya thulin witharai.
e sanaha budu wadanata kikaru wiya yuthui.

api nitharama inne awidyawa karagaha gaththu thanhawen poshanaya wechchi sithuwili thulai.
e nisa dugathi gami bawa prakatai.

ema nisa in midima sanda , pin kala yuthu mai.pinata biya wiya yu na.
tempary fix ekak witharai.

pin/ paw walin awiddyawa ho thanahawa nirodaya kala nohakie.

awabodaya samaga , nathara weemak nathi ethara weemak sidda wei.
asa kana nasaya diwa shareenaya saha manasa, kiyana siyalla salayathana lesa hadunnawa athara.
metha wisheshayen balanna oni , manasath laukika deyak bawa.
enam salayathanayan giniganna sului. ( adithya pariyaya suthraya)

salayathanyan gena ganna siyalude awidyawa thulin mai hambenne.
api kiyana kota athi wana e hamuweema , apita kawadawath hamuwenne na.
e nisa api kiyanakotama awidyawe badila.

ex: lokaye gathiya
hodawada karana aya wate kattiya ekathu wenawa wagema
naraka wada karana aya wateth ekathu wenawa.
kalaye awamen, ekathu weeme wishwasa niyojanaya karanna 
roopayak sakaskaraganna , ( symbolic reference)
ita pasu kalayaka awamen, menissu me symbolic reference wandana mana karanna patan gannawa.
sathya wahenawa, soyannata idiripath wenneth na.
mama gana seweema gilihenawa.
bahirin mawa sowan kirimata , enam maa thulin sowan margaya upawanna balanawa.
api hari asaranai.
apita kagewath pihitak na.
deiyowath man diha nobalana bawa pawasanawa
meka mage pera karapu karumak
oka ithin loke hati
ehema kiyala asarana bawama sarana kara gannawa.
habai 
budun, dhaham, sagun sarana yanne na.
ithin kohenda niwana.
matamai wenne kiya kiya innawa :)

duka awboda kara ganeemen niwana namathi sapayata path wenawa.
marga nyanaya kiyana awabodaya nisa ,
awidya sobawaye awabodaya samma dittiyai.

awidyawe sobawaya hariyata dakkama, me kriyawaliya gana kala kirenawa
kala kirenawa kiyanne duk wenawa kiyana nevi
kalakirenawa kiyanne eken nidahas wenna balanawa kiyana eka.
awidya dharmathawaya gana kalakiri in midi nidas wenawa
enam
salayathana sadeemata athi kamaththata pihita sitimata thanak nathi wenawa.
salayathana nirodaya nisa jeewthaye pawathma niroda wenawa.
piriniwan pana thek, 
pawathina salayathanayan athulu anekuth iskandayan pariharanaya karanawa upadanayata asu novi.

ex:
karama karanne sithin, kayen, wachanayen
chethanawa mul welai karanne.
chethanawa kiyanne drushtiyak

ex: pare kenek yanawa ( karmayak karanne, kayen karana karmayak)
ehema yanakota parawal dekak hambenawa.
kumana ho parak decide kara gatha yuthui.
decide kiyanne theeranayak
eka hithana eke prathipalayak. hithaluwak
enam drushtiyak
enam gaman karana karmaya sahayogaya denawa
parawal deken ekak samma dittiya , aneka mithya dittiya wei
drushtiya auwa karmaya sahayogaya dei.

samma ditti pare yathdi onna aye junction ekak
aye thoranawa,
decision ekak,
eka anuwa gaman karanawa
ekak niwanata ekak sasarata
lokoththara sammadittiya niwanata , laukika samma dittiya sasarata
decision ekak ganna pera karama sidu une na.
"mano pubban gama damma"
pera gamankaru drushtiyai. 
"mano setta manomaya"
manasa thamai mul wela tiyenne
"manasa che paduttena" / "manasane pasan nena"
manasa dushta unoth / prasadaya upadawana yahapath kriya karoth
"bashathiwa karothiwa"
bashawa saha kriyawa
"thatho nam dukka man wethi" / "thatho nam sukka man wethi"
duka athi karai / sapa athi karai
"chakkanwa wahatho padan" / "chayawa anapaini"
chakrayak se pasu pasa enawa. / chayawa se pasu pasa enawa

decisiom eka ganna thak kal , chakraya ho chayawa pasu pasa enawa.
decision eka ganne dittiya anwua
dittiya tiyena kan dicision eka gannawa, sasara yanawa.
ema pruthakjana konaya wenas kara
manyyanawen thora hewath, ma-manyyathi weemen
saeka bawatath, mulumaninma iwath weemen na-manyyathi hewath uthum arihath palaya 
shakshath kirimen nirwana awabodaya sakshath wei.

nohata ganeema hewath arihath pala nyanaye sobawaya "punya paapa paheenassa" hewath anuppada nirodayai.
me nisa 
lokoththara sobawaya laukika wachanayen wisthara karanna ba.
wena kenek  dharma sakachchawa kochchara washayen awaboda gaththada kiyana eka , wena katawath therum yanne na.
eyage pera karma anuwa awabodaya pamana sakas wei.
