(https://youtu.be/0aDoqaf9xis)
නාම රූප අන්තවලිනන් මිදිමට උපකර දේශනය - Ven Gothatuwe Rewatha Thero
(https://youtu.be/jsoR8mknRh8)

--------------------- awidyawa pawathinna saha duru weemata hethu -------------------05/09/2021

api awidyawa allanne , hama patan ganna lesa, awidyawa tiyenawa silayuma dharmatha pawathina lesa.
e kiyanne awidyawa thamai ekama hethuwa kiyala api hitha gannawa.
enam pattichcha samuppadaye arambaya wana awidyawa isthira sanyyawak lesa ara gena.

awidyawa pawathinnaath duruwennath hethu pawathinna oni pattichcha samuppadaya anuwa. 
ehenam awidyawath isthira sanyyawen allanna ba.
budu dahame anithya sobawaya samathanama dakiya yuthui

ehenam awidyawa pawatheemata saha duru weemata hethu pawathinna oni, budun pennala deela tiyenawa.
ada api eka balamu.

meka api katha karanne wisheshayenma etharaweeme margayath ekka
awidyawata hethuwa pancha nee-warana ( niwana awaranaya karana dharma)

kama-chanda
wyapaada
theena midda
uddachcha kukkuchcha
wichikichcha

me dharmathawo samawitama niwana awaranaya karanawa.

kama-chandaya - pancha indriyan pinaweema. kama lokaye api inne me kamaththa hinda.
wyapaada - tharaha.
theena midda - chichtha chithasikayan ge mali kama.
uddachcha kukkuchcha - no sansun kama, sitha wisirila, eka eka aramunu walata yana sobawaya.
wichikichcha - sakaya , buddadi 8 thana kerehi sakaya.(budda,dhamma,sanga,sikshapada,patichcha samupadda dharmaya, patichcha samupadda dharmaya kerehi atheetha , warthamana, anagatha lesa sakaya)

mema pancha neewaranya tiyena thek,
niwana awaboda karana widyawa wahila pawathi.

pancha neewarna athi wenne ai :
ekata hethuwa,
thriwida dushcharitha, 
kaika
manasika
wachasika

enam sithin kayen wachanayen sidda wena waradi katayuthu

ethkota thriwida dushcharitha athi weemata hethu,
indiya asanwaraya.
enam
me ayathana 6 sanwara na.asanwarai

ethkota indriya asanwarayata hethu monawada ?
"asathi asampajanya"
e kiyanne 
sihiyath na nuwanath na kiyana sobawaya.

ethkota sihi nuwana nathi wennath hethu tiyenawa?
ayoniso manasikaraya
ehema kenata kawadawath sathya awaboda wenne na.

ayoniso manasikaraya hethuwa mokadda ?
budun wahanse ge dharmayata yomu noweema, 
laukika washayen ho lokoththara washayen 
desu dharmaya aseemata / pilipadieemata athi akamaththa.
a-shardawa nathi wenna nam budda wachanaya ahanna oni garu karanna oni.
shardawa nathi kena sath dharmayata kamathi na, discussion walata enne na,
sath dharmaya/ budda wachanaya ahanawa wada wena wada walata priority.

sharddawa nathi bawa.->ayoniso manasikaraya-> sihi nuwana nathi wenawa -> indriya asanwara wenawa
-> sithin kayen wachanayen akusal karanawa -> awidyawata hethu wenawa.

sharddawa nathi wenne ai,
meka wenne asath dhamma shrawanayen
dan balanna dharmaya ahanna kana kochchara wadagath da kiyala.
kana kochchara hodata tibbath , api dharmaya ahanna pelabila nane.

asath dhamma sharawanayata hethuwa,
thamai
asath purusha sansewanaya, aashshraya

ayeth mathak karanna 
pancha ne warnaya gana budda deshanawe than dekaka kathakaranawa
margaya samaga (pancha neewara samuchchedath prahaanaya)
dyaanaa samaga (pancha neewara yatapath karala thamai meka karanne)

margaya samaga gaththahama lokoththara paththata gamana karanawa
dhayaana smaha laukia roopawachara , aroopawachara pawath mata yanawa

margaya nathmatai, dhaayana pawathmatai.
pancha neewarna yatapath weema nisa dhaayana mattamak margayye mula hamuunata, roopawachara aroopawachara uppaththi sanada awashaya laukika wipaka sakas wanne na.
e hinda margaya saha dhayanwa depaththakata bedenne.
e nisa wipaka mattam waduwoth , laukika roopa aroopa loka uppathiya siduwenawa
margaya waduwoth nirodaya sakshath wenawa.

api me katha kale awidyawa athi weema hethu ne.

dan widyawata hethu balamu.
widyawata athi weemata saptha bojjanga wadiya yuthui.

enam
sathi sambojjangaya (bodiyata angayak woo. bodiya yanu awabodayai) ( enam bodiyak wadena lesa athi sathiya)
dhamma wijaya sambojjangaya (bodiyak wadena lesa dhaham karunu wimarshana kirima)
viriya sambojjangaya (bodiyak wadena lesa virya kirima/ unanduwa uthsahaya)
prithi sambojjangaya (bodiyak wadena lesa athi wana prithiya, dharmaya dana ganeema nisa athi wana sathuta)
passadhi sambojjangaya (bodiyak wadena lesa athi sahalluwa, neewarna nisa tibba badawa adu wimen athi wana sahalluwa)
samadhi sambojjangaya (bodiyak wadena lesa sithe ekagathwaya/ ekagrathawaya, sitha ehata mehata adinne na)
upeka sambojjangaya ( bodiyak wadena lesa kisima aleemakin / gateemakin thorawa sitima)


widyawa wadeemata saptha bojjanga wadiya yuthui kiyala kiwwa
api neewarna pahadili karanne,
bojjanga dharma wala sapekshawa.

enam neewarna nathi, bojjangaya wadimen thamai, widya wimukthiya pahala wenne.
e kiyanne
neewarna duru unata , awiddyawa duru una kiyala kiwwe na.
api katha kale saptha bojjanga pahala una kiyala thamai kiwwe.

saptha bojjanga athi wenna hethu wenne 
sathipattanaya.

sathipattanaya waya weemen thamai margaya wadenne. ( mewa bawana enam bawithawaya/ wadeema)

sathipattanaya ( sihiya + pihitana than)
sihiya pihitana than 4k gana budun deshan karanawa
kaya nupassana (kaya anuwa sihi kirima)
wedena nupassana (wedanawa anuwa sihi kirima)
chitta nupassana (sitha anuwa sihi kirima)
dhamma nupassana (sithuwili anuwa sihi kirma)

meka broad subject ekak, api issarahata indetail katha karamu.
sathipattanaya - piyage boomiya lesa hadunwanawa, marayata ahu wennema na, hoyaganna ba



sathipattanaya wadena paridi sucharithayen inna oni.
api sucharitha une naththam sathipattanaya pinisa
widyawa wimukthiya hambenne na.


sucharitha bawayata hethu monawada,
indriya sanwaraya

indirya sanwaraya ta hethu
"sathi sampajanya" bawa
sihi nuwana athi kama

sihi nuwa athi kamata hethuwa thamai
yoniso manasikaraya.

ethkota samma dittiya tiyena purwa nimiththa ( palaweni milestone eka ) thamai yoniso manasikaraya

ethkota yoniso manasikaraya hethu monawada
sharddawa athi bawa.

sharddawata hethuwa mokadda 
sath dharmaya shrawanaya wenna oni

ekata hethuwa mokadda 
sath purusha sewanaya (kalyana mithra asura)

e nisa 

sath purusha sewanaya 
yoniso manasikaraya
sath dharmak shrawanaya
dhammanu dhamma prathi patipadawa ( dharmaye hasirena prathipadawa)

wadeemen sothapaththiya laba ganna puluwan.
e nisa me piyawara 4, sothapaththi anga 4 lesa hadunwanawa.

dharma shrawanaya weemata nam sharddawa prathyai. ( ape palaweni padama)

dharma margayata athula weemata sharddawa prakata wenna oni.
methana sharddawa use karanna oni yoniso manasikaraya upadawa ganna.
ehema nathuwa witharka kirimata nevi ( logical sense)
ehenam thamunge ramuwa ikmawanna oni.
thamata hariyana yoniso manasikaraya wadak na.
thamunge ramuwa ikmawana prathipadawa pawasuwe 
budu rajanan wahanse pamanai.

budun thamai widyawa thaniyen upadawa gena
nuwannaththanta maha karunawen and maha praknyawenui
deshana karanwa dharma awabodaya pinisa

saralawa denna puluwan hodama widiha thamai budu rajanan wahanse deshana kale
ethanin eheta katawath yanna ba.

sunitha sopakath marga pala upadawa gaththe e widihatamai. (budun wahanse pennapu karamayata sharddawen yomu wela, witharaka nokara)
methana thamai mularambaya.

buddhist dharshanaya , buddagamen differenciate karana ekath menna me point eke thamai tiyenne.

agamaka mularambayath sharddawai, mema sharddawa bakthiya lesa thamai sasana wala pennanne. 
bahira pudgala sobawayak / deviyan kerehi wishwasaya , thama thulin baleemak sidu wenne na.

"sath purushaanam adassaavi  (sath purushayo dakinne na, value karanne na)
sath purusha dhamme akoowidoo (sath dharmaya awaboda karaganna daksha na)
sath purusha dhamme awineetho (dharmaya hasirimata wineetha bawak shikshanayak na, oni papayak karanawa bayak nathuwa)
ariya dhamman adassaavi (arya dharmathawayan ganan ganne na)
ariya dhamme akoowidoo (awaboda karaganna daksha na)
ariya dhamme awineetho"  (arya dharmayan thulin wineetha lesa hasirimak na)

menna me ayata thamai pruthakjanayan lesa withara karanne. buddagama, naththam siyalu agam padanam wenne menna me 
pruthakjana sobawaya matha.

dharshanaya kiyanne ariya dharshanaya enam sathya gaweshanaya.
meka api karanne sothapaththi anga 4 thulin. (kusala chandaya athi wenna oni meka karanna)
enam yoniso manasikaraya + shardhdha marthya thamaa thula upadawa ganeema thulin. ( dharmaya thulin budun dakeema)
budun guruwaraya karagaththe dharmayai. ( pera kala siti budungen dharmaya asa danagena niyatha wiwarana laba, thama thulin viryaye soyagena )(swan boo nyanaya upadawagen) awaboda kale.

budu rajan wahanseth gaman kale dharmaya guru kota gena,
e wasi giya dharmaya nawatha swan boo nyanayen soya idipath kota ,
sharawayan ethula gaman kirimata awasha awabodaya pinisa dharmaya saralawa deshana kala.
pera kala siti budun gana mathak karanneth me sobawaya nisama thamai.

dan balanna nikleshi budun gen , keleshi sahitha prarthana illanawa ( bodi pujawak tiyela, prarthana itu karaganna hadanawa )
balanna dharshana sobawaya nothereeme gabura.

seela sampaththiya athi kena 
pancha upadana iskandaye sathya dakimen sothapanna wanne.

ehenam dharma awabodaya pinisa 
api thula wada ganna oni gunaanga gana wataheemak tiyenna oni.

summary :
awidyawata hethu 
widyawata hethu
margaya, dhanya samaga dhayana  pancha newarana wigraya
margaya thulin saptha bojjanga  walata sapekshawa thamai neewarna gana katha kale.
enam 
neewarna duru weema thulin awidyawa duru una kiyala kiwwe na. 
saptha bojjangayan athi weema ganai katha kale.
saptha bojjangayan athi weeme hethuwa thamai sathipattanaya ( nuwana pihitawa ganeema)
e nuwanath ekka thamai margaya wadenne.

enam sucharithawa sitinna oni koi widihatada sathara sathipattanaya wadena widihata.
ex:
sucharithaya kiwwahama kayen,wachanayen,sithin paw nokara sitimane kiyala ne apita hithenne.

sathara sathi pattanaya wadena widihata sucharithaya inne kohomada ?
dasa kusal pilipadinna oni
ehema pirisidu wechcha kena nikan idala hari yanne na.
sathara sathi pattanaya wadanna oni.


Dasa kusal
> pranagathayen walakeema
> nodun ge ganeemen walakeema
> waradi lesa pancha kamaye noaleema 
> boru nokeema
> kelam nokeema
> parusha wachana nokeema
> his wachana nokirima
> dadi lobayen aathweema
> tharaha noganeemai
> waradi drushtiyen ath weema
   
sathara sathipattanaya wadanne kohomada ? eka bawana karamayak eka wenama katha karanna oni subject ekak.
mulin dasa kusal wadala e sucharithaya sathara satipattana wadima pinisa yomu wiya yuthuya.
dan api dannawa bawana karanne ai kiyala.
budun deshana kale bana bawana da bawana banada ?
awabodaya thulin thamai bawanawa.
enam bawitha kirimai/ prayogikawa bawitha kirimai.

budun deshana kale,
wimukthi margaya samaga yomu wanawita 
awidyawa duru weema dawas 7 kin.
ehema naththam awrudu 6 panama gatha karanawa kiyala.

budun pudgalayo kotas 4ta bedanawa 
udhgati thanyya ( sariyuth thero wage , tak gala awaboda karagannawa)
wipachi thanyya ( thawa tikak wisthara karapuwahama awaboda karagannawa)
neyya thanyya ( detail washayen wisthra karanna oni)
pada parama ( awaboda kara gannama ba) ( padaya parama karagena inna aya , namuth adahasa ismathu karaganne nathi aya)

budunge dharmaya mul,mada,aga washayen kotas thunai
udhgati thanyya -  mula kiyathdima awaboda kara gannawa  ( palaweni pada peliyen sowan wela)
wipachi thanyya - mula saha mada dekama kiwwahama awaboda kara gannawa ( peli 4ma kiyanna oni)
neyya thannya - mula mada aga thunama kiyanna oni ( peli 4i arthayai wisthara karanna oni) ( api wage)
pada parama - aya awaboda karaganne na. kiyapu de saha kiyapu kena allan innawa.
 

dasa punya kriya
dana
seela 
bawana
apachaayana (piya yuththan pidiama)
weiya wachcha ( wath piliweth karanawa)
patti daana ( pin denawa)
paththanu modana ( anun dena pin anumodam wenawa/ sathutu wenawa)
dhamma sawana ( bana asanawa)
dhamma deshana ( bana deseema)
dittiya riju kara ganeema ( waradi drushtiya iwath karagannawa)

dan dasa kusal and dasa punyak kriya wala wenasa dakinna.

------------------------- dharma Dhanaya therum ganeema ------------16/05/2021-------------

api ahala tiyena indriyan wardanaya karanna puluwan kiyala.
sadda ,wirya,sathi,samadi - indriya lesa haduwannne , mennam dharma margya wadanakota ibe mewa diyunu wena handa.
meya indriya dharma diunu wenawa. meka mama talented handa karana deyak nevi, mokada mamen thorawai meya siduwanne
meka dharma sobawayak, mata lakunu daganeemak sidu wenne na.
ehema unoth aye sakkaya dittiya wadi wenawa.
enam me dharma margaye awabodaya saha practically kirima magin , onima kenekuta mema indriya wardanaya siduwenawa.
hari awabodaya saha seweema pamanai awashaya.

giya sare questions : avidyawata hethuwa ekama hethuwak nevi thawath hethu tiyenawada ? avidyawata hethuwa ashrawa noveida ?

ashrawa kiyanne monawada ? ape experiance , mama gathuthu tikak neda ? mage huru purudu thamai api me ashrawa widihata 
haduna ganne.
asathpurasha sewanaya , asath dharma shrawanaya, ayoniso manasikaraya , ashaddawa...aadhi washayen wisthara kale 
ekamai. me gathi okkotama thamai aasharawa kiyanne.
awidyawata hethuwa ashrawa kiyala nawaththowath, eya api allaganne lokaya thulin.
e nisa thamai , isthira sanyaawen thorawa, awidyawata hethu dharamaya thulin wigraha kale.
awabodaya lokaya thula , nam apita awidyawata hethu lesa ashrawa  kiyala kiyanna pulwuan. me dekama ekai
ehema kiwwoth apita galawena athak hoyaganna ba. ashrawa walin nathawara wenna wennawa.

ashrawa duru karanne kohomada ?
e nisa ashrawa mamathwayata tiyena relationship eka thamai pennuwe.
ashrawa nisa awidyawa hata ganna kiyana eka (meka hari saralai, kiyanna lesie), api hethu prathya thulin giya sare katha kale.
ehema nokaloth 
asharawa nisa awidyawa hata gannawa kiyana eka , thawath sylabus ekaka wachana mathrayak witharai.
meka mathaka tiya ganimen , marga nyanaya upaddawa ganna ba
awabodayai wadagath.

api eda katha karapu , danaya  gana tikak detail balamu.

dharma dhanaya kiyala kiyanne kenek ge shardawa mathu karala dena ekane. eka thamai dharma margaye piwisuma doratuwa.
me dorata yana margaya penweema saha unanduwa athi kirima thamai , kenekuta dharamya kiya deemen api karanne.

dhanaya deeme uthkrushta thana, kisima balaporoththuwak nathi wai wenna oni.

e nisa mekata kiyanawa , "dunnoth danaya labei nidanaya"

eka kohomada eka wenne kiyala balamu.

ape hitha thula adahasak tiyenawa , yamak ahanakota e de therenne oni kiyala. ehema neda ?
enam yamak laba ganeema pinisa api ahukan deema karala. ( ahun kan deema, deemak tiyenawa thereemak balaporoththuwen)
api danayak denne kelewara ama maha niwana balaporoththu wen nam. balaporoththuwa mama nithya karala neda. 
ehenam niwana balaporoththuwen dan denna puluwan da ? ba neda ?

ex:
gahak pala weyan, pala weyan kiyala kiwwata gaha pala wei da ?
eketa awashaya watapitawa sakas karana eka witharai neda karanna puluwan.
ehenam labenawa kiyala hithana dekata prarthana karala wadak na neda ?

"mama nidahase dharmaya hoyanawa kiyala" , therum yama pinisa awashya wedikawa wiryayen sakas karana ekirima witharai neda kala hakke.

giye sare api sakachchawe di mathak kala , monawa kalath mulin hikmeema , sheelaya tiyenna oni kiyala kiwwa.
e seelaye awasana kelawara, "mama dan hikwenawane kiyala" adahasak enna ba. awoth mama innawa.
ethkota onna labeemak. balaporoththuwak. dan seelayak tiyenawada ? 
menna me sobawayata kiyanawa seelabbatha paramasayak kiyala.
mama sil gaththa kiyanne seelabbatha paramasak ( mamathwayen ganeema)
mama hikmila, mama dana sil aran inne.
me sobawaya thula mama isthira wela.
sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wela , 

api adura ganna oni methana kiyanne, sil ganna hoda na kiyana eka nevi,
mama sil gaththa ho mama dan ashtanga seelaya samapath wela hikmila inne kiyana 
sobawwaye tiyena drushi poshanaya saha ehi waradda ekai. ( seelabbatha paramasayai)

dan balanna api sil ganna giyahama,
ape lokaye , rate lokaye wada mathak wenawa
menna me kunugoda tiyena kan bana dhara ganna ida tiyenawada.
me kunu goda ain karanna uthsaha karana kota , bana deshanawe yam kalayak gihin.
kunu gode pramanaya anuwa , kalaya apathe yanwa.

e nisa kalamana karithwaya api hada ganna oni.
bawanath ehemai, ewelawe sudanam wela ba.
pera sudanamai wadagath.
awasana prathipala pinisa , kunu goda ain karagena inna oni.

ex:
dura gamanak yanakota ,
api kakaa innawakota ,
api mahansi wela innakota,
apita bana ahanna puluwan da ? 
dharmayata sitha pawathwanan puluwan da ?
bane.

api samawitama hithanawa , "api hithan innawa dharmaya ahena thanakata giyahama apita dharmaya labei kiyala"
habai dharmaya labena widihata watapitawa sakas karala na.
lokaya nithya lesa aran, e thula tiyena wiwida ashrawa pramuka wela.
mokada labena deta hethuwa lokaya thula pawathina lesa ganna handa ? ( palayen palayata yaama)

ex;
job eka karahama salli hambenawa. job eka handada apita salli hambenne ?
lokaya thula hithana mattama thamai job eka nisa salli. meka poddak api gaburata baluwoth.
salli hambaweemata wata pitawa sakas karapu eka witharai api karala tiyenne.
namuth api meka ganne job eka nisa salli hambenawa kiyala.
enam api anithya dakala na ,
noolpotak wath nathi minissu, sahenna ras karanwa , habai dalayana dawasata dukai.
ras kirima thula duka pawathinawa.
me ras kirime sakas kirima thamai api aduna ganna oni.

ex:
upadina kota tibuna nidahas manasata jeewath weema sadaha api dagaththu karadara walta api kotu wela.
me boru walawal walta watila , eken galawenna thamai ape try eka.
budun deshana kale me palayen palayata gaman karana eka gana nevi.

ipadena ekama prashnayak kiyana ekathamai deshana kala.
ipadeemen passe hada gaththu problems gana nevi
hada gaththu problems wisada ganna karana wirya thula ( palayen palaya pamanai hamuwenne)
hethuwa hamu novi, nirodayak nopawathi.

budu himi deshana kala ipadeemama dukak bawa.

dharma dhanayak ho onima dhanayak  yedenna kalin 
 api,
gochara saha agochara sobawaya gana api dana ganna oni. ( hoda ho naraka, hari ho waradi, kusalaya ho akusalaya
gana dana gena mama kumak kala yuthuda kiyala prashnaya enna oni)
ethkota me gocharaya
bala karala karawanna ba, iswyan chinthanayak awadi wenna oni.

me gocharaya thulath

"mama kumak kala yuthuda kiyala " kiyana chinthanayata eha giya chinthanayak tibedai soyanna oni.
namuth,
methek kal , mata oni widihata dewal purudu karapu apita ,
mata oni widihata wada eha giya giya chinthanayak kiyana eka aluth karamayak / event ekak une
e huruwa nathi nisa.
mawa lokka karapu thal kal, lokkage ana witharai.

hurupuru kama nathi nam sanweedi kamath adui.
athisha-yin bahutharayak , mata therune nathi nam eka atharala danawa.
meka loku aparadayak.

ex:
onna podi lamayek ge athe manik kala tiyenawa , 
oka ganna oni nam.
mokada karanna oni ?
lamayata watinakam therena deyak denna oni.
onna lamaya kamathi deyak ( gochara-yak) dennawa.
hithanna ko losinjarayak kiyala.
api kiyanwa losinjaraya mara rahai, me gala raha na.
lamaya thamange gocharayata harima lesiyen ahu wenawa.
manike watinakama danne na.

e wagema dharmaye watinakama therila naththam.
dharmayen galawanna harima lesie.
podi losinjarayakin , (chuti kam sapayakin) galawanna puluwan.

lokaye sobawaya , adharmayata ammai thaththai wage, kawadawath dharmaya denne na.
e deshaye innakan hambenne adharamaya thamai.

me deshayen galawenna budu piyanan bodi mulaye wadi wenne.
e weeryaye tharama kochchara shreshtada ?
apita hitha gannwath puluwan da ?
budu rajan wahanseta , deepankara budu rajanan wahanseta niwan dakinna tibuna.
ehema nokara api kerehi , athi maha anukampawen,
buddathwak laba ganeema pinisa , sara sanka kalpa lakshayak perum piruwe me ada api me katha krana dharmaya denna.
kopamana weeryayak da ?
sara sanka kalpa lakshayak. 
( ayusha awrudu 10x^1 (aw10yak) idala -> awrudu asankeiya 10x^140 gihin aye adu -> 10x^1)- anthak kalpa 1i.
anthak kalpa 20k tiyenawa kalpayakata.
kalpa 4 maha kalpayak wenne.
(aggannya suthraye meka withara wenawa)

api ada katha kale, dharmaya giliheema kochchara lesiyen ikmanata wenawada kiyala.
ithin hithanna echchara wegayen iwathwana dharmaye yedima kochchara amaruda.
dharmaye jeewithaya pawathwa ganeema kotharam apahasuda .

e nisa thamai budun wahanse, meka karanna karapamak hadunawala dunne.
api meka kalin kala,
sutha, datha , wachasa parichitha.
manasa upekithaa.
dittiya suppati widyaa

me kiyanne arthya therenawa kiyala nevi, meka marga nyanawa upadawa nageemata athyawasha wena yoniso manasikaraya
upadawa ganeemata penawa athi karama wedayai.

pada wiyanjana nisa sadunu prathiroopayakin niyama arthaya wahila.
e nisa yoniso manasi karaya updinne na.

pada wiyanjana kiyala kiyanne : padaya / saha wisthara karanna hethuwu anekuth wynajana alla sitima nisa niyama arthya gilihila ( agocharayak wela)(padaya allan idala)

ehenam pada wiyanjana walata asu novi thamai dharamaye yedeema kala yuththe.
arthaya wahila nam yoniso manasikaraya upadinne na.

yoniso manasikaraya upadinne naththam, budun desu dharmaya ahenne na.
me sath dharmaya ahune naththam marga pala nyanaya upadinne na.
margapala nuwanin thorawa nirwanaya shakshaath karanna ba.

ex:
"chukkuncha pattichcha roopecha upathjjathi chakku winyanan tinnan sangathi passo" 
asath roopath, winyanayath ipadaweemen thamai isparshaya hamu wenne.

ethkota hamuwenna katada ?
mata kiwwoth sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wenawa.
mama nevi , mage nevi kiyala kiyanneth manasenma nisa (manyyanawak thulin) ayeth sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wela
dan meka ibe da une ? na ide hata gaththu deyak nevi.
hethu pala dahamakin athi une kiyala api wigraha kara gannawa.
dan kawda wigraha karaganne ? api , onna aye ahuwela. 

eka manase karyayak ( manasi karayak) - eka man karapu ekak nevi manase karyayak.
ehenam ekata hethu hoyanna oni.

yamak desa balala, 
eelagata wenath nama+ roopayak hamuwena wita wynanayata mokada wenne ?
issella ekamada ? na neda . ehenam mul eka nirudda wela.
mul eka nirudda wela nam ekkama manasikarayath nirudda wela neda ?
ethkota api kohomada ilaga hamuweema wela tiyenne.
mula eka niruddanam, manasikaraya nirudda wela nam
eya niwan dakinna epai.
namuth eelaga roopaya dakinnawane ,
mekata hethuwa mokadda ?

mekata hethuwa mokadda awidyawa.
awidya pachchaya sankara...
melesa lokaya thula niyojanaya wana 
siwaluma pancha upadana isknadayan awidyawa matha padanam wee ath nam
e siyalla sathya nowiya yuthui neda ?
upadana iskandayan thula sathya na neda ?
eka mohothaka di api niwan dakina. thawa mohothakadi sasarata yanawa.
mehema wenna puluwanda ?
ehenam meka sathya nowiya yuthui.
 
 
ehenam , mema pancha upadana iskandaya mage ho wena kenekuge nowei nam
meya dakiya yuththe keseda ?

me sanda , apa budu piyanan desu akaraya anugatha wiya yuthui.
thama danumata ho , wena ayekuge matha walata nowa.
iswan boo nyanyen awaboda kala 
budu rajanan wahanse ge wigrahaya aseemata hodin awadanaya kala yuthui.
ehenam attention eka yanna oni budun wigraha kala widihata.

roopa, wedana, sanya, sankara , wynana pilibanada wa budu rajanan wahanse pennu upama thulin
wataha gatha yuthui.
roopaya pena pidak
wedanawa - diya bubulak (... etc penapindupama suthra , pera api katha kala)

mese kala wigrahaya thulin deshana karana lada dharmayan ge arthya ismathu kara gatha yuthui.

pena pidak , gedara gihin showcase eke dala tiya ganna puluwan da ?
 e wage me pahema gatha yuththak na neda ?
 labiya yuththak na neda ?
 monawa labennada ?
 
 me hama ekakinma kiyala tiyenne ma e tika.
 mese ape awadanayath, budun wahanse dehana kala arthayata yomu weema thulin yoniso manasikaraya upadeemata 
 base ekak wenawa. ( wata pitawa sakas gena)
 
 isella kiyapu wihata , api dakke eka welawaka niwana , ekawelawaka sasara.
 namuth
 budun deshana kale
 sakkaya dittiya prahanaya wana widihai.
 asa, roopaya, chakku wynanaya, chakku sammpassaya, sammpasaja wedana ( duka sapa upeksha)
 duka washayen ehema naththam dukka arthayen ( pancha upadana iskandayo dukka)
 dana , daka gannakota ( janatho passatho)
 sakkaya dittiya prahanaya wei.
 
 
 thawa point ekak balamu.
 sammpasaja wenada kiyapu siyaluma de duka lesa api haduna gaththa. enam pancha upadana iskandayo dukka
 gaththahama,
 
 ase uppaththiyen hadunu suka wedanawa dukai kiyala kiwwahama parasparai neda ?
 pancha neewarna yatapath karal gaththu palaweni dharnaya dukai da sapai da ?
 sapai.
 budu rajanan wahanse duk jathi thunak deshana kala
 dukka dukkaya
 wiparinama dukkaya
 sankara dukkaya

ai ehema duk thunak deshana kale ? mata ehema wenne mama hitapu nisa ( api echcharata sakkaya dittiya gedi ahuwela)
thunak washayen deshana kala , sakkaya dittiye gabura wisthra karanna.
mata dukak labune mama hisapu nisa
mama duk une mage pawathma nisa

hethu prathya dharmayen  deshan kale mama kiyana eka galawila yanna 
ehenam mata epa/oni kiyana eka hethu prathya dharmayata galapenne na.
ehenam dharmata anuwa mama pramuka unu siyalu de gala penne na.
ehenam pudgala , athma washayen ganeeme waradda, hethu prathya dharmaya thulin ahu wenawa.

"mama kiyala hambena eka" waradi nam,
duka epa wena gathiyak hamu wenne na. ( duka epa wena gathiya pihita sitimata thanak nathi wenawa)

ex :
mama samadimath wela inna eka dukak da ? mata samadhiya dukak da ?
na , hena sapak kiyala neda therenne.

onima aramunak enne patticha sammupadawa nam.
pancha upadana skanda dukka. siyaluwama de dukai
memea iskandayan ge anthiya bawa danna kota dakina kota thamai, 
pancha upadanayama duka bawa therenne.

mata epa wechchi nisa wath , mama awaboda karapu nisa wath nevi me duka hamuwela tiyenne.
mama kiyana ekama galewenna oni.
sakkaya dittiyen thorawa thamai menna me duka hamuwela tiyenne. 
api me wisthara kale mata ena feelings nevi
pancha upadana iskanda dukka kiyala kiwwe me anithya bawa danna kota  dakina kotai.


ex:
budun deshan kale , hithala therum ganna deyak da ? dana dakina deyak da ?

dan dakina sobawayak. pudgalathwaya waradi bawa dakkahama "asa thulin" dakkahama
anith ewa gana katha karanna oni da wadak tiyei da ?
ewath gala wila yanwa neda 
mama gala wila giyahama ewath okkoma galawenawa neda ? oni na neda ?

me widihata anithya dukka anathma kiyana thrilakshanaya dakkoth.

anithya - pancha upadana iskandaye anithya sobawaya
dukka - anithya bawama duka wu sobawaya (isthira lesa pawathwa ganeeme nohakiyawa)
anathma - mama pramuka karala ganna bari sobawaya 

ethkota mulika wenna oni 

obe vimukthiya nevi ( mama niwan dakinawa nevi)
budun desu dharmaya mulika wiya yuthui. ( onna api dhamman saranam gachchami lesa hari lesa sarana yanwa)
api karanne (kamman saranam gachchami, mathu wipaka pinisa karma ras karapu eka withrai karala tiyenne)
dharmaya kageda budu rajanan wahansege 
ehenam dharmaya thulin dakinna oni.

   

dhana mattame kusalathawayak karanakota , kisima balaporoththuwak nathuwa ne eka karanna oni.


-------------------------Roopa roopa thula anathma sobawaya ---23/05/2021--------------

ada kathawa namaroopa pachchaya salayathana ( 6 ayathanaya)

mulu wishwayema tiyenne namaroopa withrai ne.
naama dharma  sitha thula pawathina ehema naththam sithata sambanada dharmatha ( sitha saha chithasika)
naama kotasa, enam sitha saha chithasika  sathara samprayoga lakshana walin yukthai.
ewa thamai,
1) ekatamai upadinne
2) ekatamai nirudda wenne
3) ekama wasthuwaka pihitanne. (ase patan gaththoth ase thamai pawathinne, diwe patan gaththoth diwe)
4) ekama aramuna thamai ganne.

waasthu kiyana wachane theruma dannawada ? 
waasthu wydyawa kiyanne mokadda ? gewal hadana widiha ne, gewal hadanne padinchi wennane.
waasthu -> apu wachanayak thamai wasthu kiyanne.
eken kiyanne sitha pihitana thang.(isthana)
e sthaana tiyenawa 6k
e 6ta kiyanawa ayathana kiyala.

podi deyak wistha karagena yan, manasa koheda tiyenne kiyala,
manasa kiyala photo ekak kohewath na,
eka shakthiyak. ( energy ekak hakiyawak)
manasath ayathanayak, ekata kiyanawa manayathanaya.

meka pawatinne kohomada,
me shakthiya , heart eke le dathuwa asuru karagena pawathina shakthiyak.
leth ekka gaman karanne na,
ethakota
heart eke athule tiyena le dathuwa asuru karagena tiyenawa thamai meka pawathinne
habai meka shakthiyak, meka le wath heart ekawath nevi.

ex: wathura walak tiyenawa kota current wire ekak eka thanakata gaunoth. wathure onima thanakin current eka 
wadinawa neda, e wage le dathuwa pawathina sama thanama me shakthiye sobawayan dana ganna puluwan. namuth shaktiya pihita tiyenne heart eka athule tiyebena ledathuwa samaga.
hariyata nikan circit ekaka power eka dena  battry eka wage.
meka malli withara kala last time as wathure pawena kola tikak kiyala.

e nisa sitha padinchi wela inna than 6k ( ehema naththam wasthu 6k) gana dharmaye sadahan wenawa ,
mewata ayathana kiyala kiyanawa.

e ayathana tiyenawa 6k. 
ewa thamai, 
chakkayathanaya ( asa)
sothayathanaya ( kana)
ghanayathanaya ( nasaya)
jiwhayathanaya (diwa)
kayayathanaya (body)
manayathana (sitha)

dan chaithasika danna ayathanyak nane eka hadenneth sitha athi kal hi ne, e nisa eka danawa 
dammayathanaya ( chaithasika walata)
e wage
sithata gocharai chaithasika kiyana eka
manayathana walata gocharayai dammayathanaya
e wage
chakkayathanaya gocharai  warnayathanaya
sothayathanaya gocharai shabdayathanaya 
ghanayathanaya gocharai gandayathanaya
jiwhayathanaya gocharai rasayathanaya
kayathanaya gocharai poddabayathanaya 

me pancha ayathanyata gochara roopa walata api kiyanawa roopayathanaya 
methana pancha indriyan ta gochcara wana roopa walata api kiyana gorosu roopa ( olarika roopa)(gorosu roopa(olarika/rough))
pancha indriyanta gochara ayathana 10 api katha kala , ekata adala gorosu roopa 12. (poddabbayata 3k niyojanawa wana handa)

namuth sukuma roopa (siyum roopa) kiyala jathiyak tiyenawa, eka me pancha indriyata danna ba
enema eka danne kohatada (sukuma roopa therenne sithata)
enenam me pancha indriyata gochara nathi roopa tika api dhammayathanatama danawa.

ethkota dan dhammayayathanaya athule chaithasikai, sukuma roopai dekama tiyenawa.

methana thawa deyak dana ganna oni,
dashaka kalaapayak athule , prasada roopaya kiyala kiyanne maha bootha wala opawath gathiyak.
maha bootha pawathina asuru karagena tiyena , maha bootha nowana roopa walata api kiyanawa upadaya roopa kiyala.

sitha nathuwa katha karana kota, pancha indriyan athule , api olarika roopa gana katha karanawa.
ethkota olarika roopa jathi dekak tiyenawa ,
1) ekak hodata danewa,
2) anith eka hodata danne na ( ithaa sium)

hodata danena ewa tiyenne shareeraye witharai. enam kayayathanaye witharai.

dan , paramaartha dharma 4n, 
chiththa, chithasika, roopa kiyana kotas thunama api katha kala,
dan ethkota anithama eka nibbana kiyana dharmaya kohatada danne ? 
dan nirwanaya kiyanne hithada ? na, ehenam manayathanaya danna ba.
nirwanaya kiyanne roopayak nevi neda ? ehenam roopayathana dannath ba.
e nisa nirwanayath apita pennanna wenne dhammayathana use karala. ( wena danna sudusu thanak na)

ethkota dan dhammayathanaya tiyenawa (chaithasika,sukuma roopa, nirwanaya)
dhammayathanaya athule chaithasika 52, sukuma roopa 16, nirwanayai gana api katha karanawa.

dan me katha karapu ayathana 12n, iskanda 5 hadena widiha balamu

wynanaya kiyanne sith tikata, api sith (chiththa) tika damme manayathanayata 
e hinda 
iskandaya kiyanne godak kiyana ekata. ehenam me manayathanyata aithi sith okkotoma (enam sith 89 tiyenawa, dirga washayen kiyanawanam 121) (89 hadenne- laukika81,lokoththara sith 8)(me ata wenuwata dyaana bedeyen 40k karala pennawa, dyaana 5 eka lokoththara sithakata, enisa laukika sith 81+ lokoththara sith 40 = 121)
kiyanawa wynanaskandaya kiyala.  

roopaskandaya kiyala kiyanne , me roopa siyallatama ( olarika roopa 12i, sukuma roopa 16i)

wedana isknadaya kiyala kiyanne, dhammayathanaye tiyena chaithasika 52n, ekak api wenama gannawa , mokada sith 89 athulema me wedana chaithasikaya pawathina handa 
e okkoma wedana chaithasika 89ta api kiyanawa wedana iskandaya kiyala. ( meka 121 katha karannath puluwan)

e wagema 
hama sithakama sanyawath tibiya yuthui, ekath api elesa sanyyaiskandayak lesa wenama pennanawa.
sannayaiskandaya athule (89/121 sanya chaithasika pawatinawa)

dan apita paramaartha dharma walin 

chiththa giya wyaanaiskandaya kiyala 
roopa giya roopa iskandaya kiyala
eeta amatharawa chaithasika walin api wedana isknada saha sanya iskandaya ganath katha kala

dan ithuru wela tiyenne ,  sanskarayai , nirwanayai

dan e deka balamu,

dan niawana iskanda bedayen winir mukthai( thorai)(e iskandayak lesa katha kara karanna ba) ( enisa api ehema katha karanne na)

dan sankara kiyanne mokadda ?
dhammayathanaye tiyena chaithasika 52n (api dekak gana already katha kala , wedanawai ,sanyyawai)
ehenam me ithuru siyallama tiyenne sanskara iskandaye.

methana sathwa pudgala , athma bedayak na
anathama sobawayak mai tiyenne, dharmathawayak witharai.
 
dan api roopaya poddak balamu
 
roopa kiyanakota roopa upaththi wena krama 4k tiyenawa
1) karmayen upadina roopa karmaja
2) chiththaja roopa , hitha nisa athi wena
3) uthuja roopaya, irthuwa wenasak nisa
4) aharaja roopa, aharaya nisa ( ja kiyanne janitha wana, ahara nisa janitha wana)


roopa kiyana wachanaya , me wiwida lesa bawitha karanawa
isawaroopa ( enam e akaraya, e widiha) kiyana eka roopaskandayata aithi kathawak nevi.
roopa kiyana eka sammuthiya athule eka eka widihata bawitha kalata 
me roopaskandayata adala na.

ex:
eyage penuma mata alluwe na nikan rawagena hitiye kiwwahama,
methana katha karana penuma kiyana roopaya , sammuthi bawithayak,
paramartha dharama wigrahaye kotasak nevi.
e wenasa api dan ganna oni.
sammuthiye roopa wigrayan ekka paramartha wigrahaya palawa ganna epa.

summary 

ayathana 12 wenama kathakala,
eken ayathana 10k pancha indrayanta gocharai. 
me ayathana 10ta gochara roopa gorosu ehema naththam olarika roopa kiyala katha kala
olarika roopa 12k pancha indraiyata gocharai. ( e mokada poddabba ayathanyata maha bootha )
thunak aithi nisa,
ayathana 10 olarika roopa 12kin pennuwa.(enam adyathmika 5i bahira 7i)

indriyak kiyala kiyanne pradanathwayak ganna awasthawakatayai,
ayathana 10 athule , api indriya sobawayak denne me promukasthanaya ganna kenata.
ehenam,
asa saha warnaya athurin wadath wadagath kumakda ? (balawatha)
balawatha yamak karanna puluwan hakiyawa tiyena kenek, prasada roopayak pawathina kenek.
ehenam meke balawath kawda asa,
e nisa 
indriya dharathawaya soyanna oni bahrin nova adyathmika paththen.

e nisa adyathmika ayathana 5ta indirya lesa hadunwanawa.
me nisa 
pancha indriyanta sitha yomu weemen, isparsha ayathana labei.
roopa roopa hamuweemen isparsha ayathanak nolabena bawath,
sitha yomu weemen isparsha ayathanaya pahala wana bawath dan therenawa.
passa pachchaya wedana kiyala , sapa, duka, upeka kiyana thuna pennanne isparsha ayathanayak (passa ayathanaya) athule.
sitha ekathu une naththam, isparsha wachanaya apita bawitha karanna ba.
sithai , adyathmika roopai, bahira roopai walata ekathuwa passa lesa kiyanawa
"thinnan sangathi passo" kiyala kiyanneth menna methanata.
sitha ekathu unahama thamai api me wedana chaithasikaya ( sapa ,duka , upeka) kiyana eka gana katha karanne
wedanawa enne naama paththen , ehenam sitha paththen.
"pass pachchaya wedana" kiyana eka apita awaboda karaganna puluwan.

mechchara wela katha kale roopa roopa mulika karagena hata ganna isparsha gana 
api manayathanaya gana katha kale na.
me widihatama 
manayathanayai saha dhammayathanaya hamu weemath wedanawata hethu wenawa.

e gana poddak balamu.

api mechchara wela katha kale manayathanayai , dhammayathanaya nathuwa
sitha yomu unahama wedanawa hata gaththe roopa roopa awasthawata anathuruwa.

bahira roopayak dakina wita pothak dakka kiyala kiyanne.
aththeetha wedanawak mul kara genai.
me nisa, 
manasa mul kara gena sidu wena me kriyawaliya,
aththeetha wedanawa kiyala ekak mul karan thamai patan aran tiyenne.

wedana, sanya, chethana, passa , manasikara wei. yana dharmatha mul wela.
ethana isparshaya atheetha wedanawak.
weemak danaweema thamai "wedanawak" lesa hadun wanne

dan warnayak penakota methanata pothak kiyala kiwwe ai ?
methana mokak hari atheetha danumak mul karagena neda ? 
wedanawak ehema naththam weemak danaweemak mul karagena ( mathakayak awadi weemen)
eka thamai manasaikarayen karapu wade , menehi karala dunna tak gala.
e nisa 
wedanawa mul kotagena manase kriyakarithwaya wana bawin,
wedana->sanya->chethana->passa->manasikara lesa kriyathmaka wei.
methana passa tiyenne mulin nevi.

ahata warnaya hamuwanathana (roopa roopa awasthawa) api ekata kiyanne na isparsha ayathanayak kiyala, pothak lesai dakke sitha yamu wechcha thanai. ethkota thamai isparsha ayathanayak wenne.
enam isparsha ayathanaya sitha pradana kotagena thamai athi wenne.

e nisa bahira roopayata (enam sitha thula hatagaththa / dhammayathanaye sobawayata) ehema naththam sitha thula hata gath
manomaya pothata/roopayata , kamaththa akamaththa, upekshawa athi wanne.

namuth e bawa nodanna nisa,
bahira roopaya pothak lesa gana, pothata athi kamathi / akamathi/ madyastha bawa awidyawen allagannawa.

methana atheetha wedanawa kiyanne mokadda ?

atheetha huru purudu walata api kiyanne keles kiyala.
me keles thula thamai okkoma raga,dwesha moha tiyenne  
manasikarayen atheetha wedana sanya mathu weemen chethana passaya siduwei.

meka wenne kohomada ?
sithe kriyakarithwaya mokadda ? 
mana hi karyya menehi kirimai.

ex: 
redi walak gamu, eka kelawarak eka kanuwaka anith paththa anek kanuwa gata gahala tiyenawa
ethakota thamai walak wenne.
dan meka walak bawata path wenne me awastha dekama tiyenne oni.
meke eka thanak galaunoth wala iwarai neda.
e nisa eka kanuwakata kiyamuko manasa paththa
anek kanuwata kiyamuko roopa paththa kiyala.
dan manasa kiyanne naama paththane 
naama kanuwai roopa kanuwai. wala tiyenne nam meka api ekaneka gata gahanna oni.
naama kiyanne chaithasika ne
chaithasika athara gateema harima siyum, ( adi wachana sampassaya)(wachana wala gateema)
ehenam e adi wachana sampassaya genalla gata gahanna oni roopa paththe.
e nisa roopa kanuwe gata hapu wachana wala gateema , enam
roopaskandaye adi wachana sampassaya.
dan roopa kanuwe , roopa roopa gateema nisa athi wana patiga sampassaya nama kanuwe gata gasiya yuthui.

methana chaithasika dekak gateema , enam aroopi dharmayan ge gateemak.
enam aroopi dharmayan ge gateema adhi wachana sampassaya ehema naththam  naama paththen wachana wala gateema lesa hadunwanawa.

e wagema roopa roopa dharmayan ge gateema , nama walata wadiya gorosu nisa (olarika sobawaya nisa)
patiga sammpassaya kiyala hadunwanawa.

naama roopa wala hadanna nam
me passayan deka kanu dekata huwamaru wenna oni.

enam 
naama iskandayen apu adi wachana sammapaya roopa iskandayen dakiya yuthui.
e wagema roopaiskandyen apu patiga sammpasse , naama iskandayen dakiya yuthui.

e nisa me kriyadamaya sidu weemata ,
roopas iskandaye adhi wachana sampassayath
naamas iskandayen patiga sammpassayath 
hamuwiya yuthui.
ethkota thamai naama roopa sambandaya sidu wenne.

menna me isparsha deka ekathu weema thamai isparsha ayathanaye hata ganeema.
dan roopayata pothak keeme hakiyawa , menna me wala pawathina thak pawathie.

mehi aththa sobawaya dakeema nyaanaya hewath praknawata api kiyanwa 
"naama roopa parichcheda nyaanaya"  

-----------------wipaka mattama saha ehi wedanawa p1-------------

wipaka mattame kriyawalia gana awabodayak ganna oni 
naththam api  me sanskara ugulata ahuwenawa.
wipaka mattama kiyala kiyanne kalin karapu deka prathipalayak.
eken thawa duratath yamak karanna ba.

me anuwa wipaka mattame chakku wynaanaya upeka sahagathai.
(api katha karanne roopa anuwe athule wena de gana, kanuwe sobawaya)
esema sotha,jiwha,gaana wynaanaya upeka sahagathai.
pancha indriyangen 4k weemak danaweema upesha sahagathai.

namuth kaya wynaanaya , suka sahagatha ho dukka sahagatha wei.
eya kayata awenika sobawayak. (pottabba roopaye maha bootha thunaka sobawaya nisa)

meka detail katha karanna oni.

wedanawa karama dekakata katha karanawa,
1) indriya bedayen (indirya 6n pramuka wela hata ganna wedanawa)
2) anubawana bedayen ( anubawa kiyanne aharayata gaththa/ prayojana gaththa)(widinawa kiyana arthayen)

ex: kamak anubawa karana kota rasa wideemak wenawa, menna me sobawaya anubawana bedaya kiyala.
mekath wedanawa katha karana eka widihak.
mema widaweeme sobawaya anubawana arthayen sapa , duka , upekka kiyala gannawa.
meka sithatath kayatath yodanna puluwan.

ex: oluwe kakkuma - deparak widinawa 
ekak kayen wedanawa widinawa
sithin wedanawa widinawa.
oluwe kakkuma double wela.
paya ganak meka tibba kiyala sithin widinawa.
tibbe kayata. namuth sithinuth e duka anubawa wenawa.
e nisa kayatath , sithatath duka anubawa wenawa.

(dan therenawa kohomada dewiyan sathuta anubawa karala )

ehenam sapa duka upekka kiyana eka kayata yodannath puluwan 
sithata yodannath puluwan kiyana eka dan therenawa.

ex:
kushtayak kasana kota saneepai kiyala kiyanwa.
kushtaya parenawa, eka dukak, eka kayata danena wedanwa.
kasana kota saneepai kiyanawa, hithata danena wedanawa.



anubawana bedayen gathdi sithata saha kayata , dekatama suka , duka upeksha kiyala katha karanawa
namuth indiriya bedayen kathanakota ehema karanne na. 
 sithata katha karanne , somanassa ,domanassa , upeka lesai.
 kayata suka , duka lesai.

 indriya bedayen katha karana wita 
 wedanawa kotas 5kin katha karanawa
 
 eka thamai, 
 suka 
 somanassa 
 duka 
 domanassa 
 upeksha
 
 melesa kotas dekakata kadala wedanawa detail balanne naththam enam poduwe sitha kaya ta wedanawa  suka,duka, upeksha 
 lesa gannawa.
 mehedi mathaka tiyaganna oni wadagathma de thamai, kaya sambandayen somassa domanassa kiyanne na.
 anubawana bedayen kotas 3i, indriya bedayen kotas 5i.
 
 me 5n ,
 somanassa saha domanassa , upeka
 yana thuna kayata nodane.
 eya sithata awenika gathiyaki.
 (eka nisa somanassa/domanassa/upeka sahagatha nyana samprayuktha kiyala sitha jathi katha karanwa )
 e hinda 
 suka saha gatha kaya wynaanaya 
 duka saha gatha kaya wynaanaya kiyala katha kalata 
 kawadawath upeka sahagatha kaya wynanaya kiyala katha karanne na.
 
 suka saha somanassa athara wenasa mokadda ?
 ekama sobawaya hata ganna thana anuwa nam dekak denawa, e anuwa thamai sith bedanne.


e wage ayathanaya kiyanne yamak hadana thanak.
me anuwa asa kiyanne warnayata sambanda ayathanaya
kana kiyanne shabbadaya sadana ayathanaya.

e nisa 
adyathmika ayathanaya saha bariya ayathanya ekinekata prathyai.
menisa 
ayathana sakas weema sanda hethu sakas yu wita,
bahira saha adyathmika dekama hata gannawa.

enam bahira saha adyathmika dharmatha dekama, ekama hethu walin sakas wena bawa awaboda kala gatha yuthui.

adyathmika ayathana hadena hethu monawada ?

1) karmaya
2) thanhawa
3) aahara
4) awidyawa
5) nibaththi lakshanaya  (ipadeemata athi anekuth saadaka)

enam me hethu 5 sakas woo wita asak upadie.
asak upadimen ekata prathya wu, bahira roopaya upadi.

enam bahira lokayak pawathinna ba adyathmika ayathana nathuwa.
e nisa bahira lokayath me hethuma thamai pennanne, me deka hamu wena thana me siddiya sidu wena nisa
ex:
bahira athi roopayakata hethuth me tikakmai kiyala kiyapu eka gana thawa tikak balamu?
bahira athi wasthu dakkine kawada ? mama ma thamai.
bahira wasthu ehema tiyenawa ho naha kiyala hithanne kawda ? mama thamai.
mamen thorawa lokaya tiyenna puluwan da ? bane.

ex: london wala bombayak pipuruna,
me welawe e shabdaya grahanaya wenne nane
api kisiwak danne na.
habai eka haduna ganne tv eken hari radio ekan hari nam
e shabdaya manasin menehi karala , arthayak therum gannawa.
mekata kiyanwa ( saadukam manasikarootha)
budda wachanayak tiyenawa (than sunaatha saadukam manasikarootha)
eke theruma , kane shabbayak ahanakota eke arthya manasin ganna welawe,
ithuru ayathana okkoma wada kaloth. pawathinne eka manasak nam wada karaganna bari wenawa.
eka wara eka sanyyawai ganna puluwan kiyala kiyanne.
e nisa 
ekama sithaka ( enam manayathanaye) daneem lakshana 6 thamai wigraha karagaththe.
ekama sithaka daneema lakshana 6ka wenasa thamai api kathale. (giya padama)


dan ayathana 6ta wena wenama nam kalata. ekama sithaka sobawayak thamai pawathinne
ex:
thel ginna, gas ginna, dara ginna....etc
me hama ekenma wela tiyenne thapayai, alokayai hata gaththu eka neda
awasanaye gindara kiyana eka podu wela neda 
onna e gindara wage thamai sitha kiyana sobawaya
ginna athi weemata athi hethu thamai ayathana sobawaya

ginnak wiwida hethun ge ekathuwa nisa hata gannawa wage ma thamai
sithak wiwida indrayan ashaya karagena pahala weema.

dan hitha hitna nisa athi wana gattanaya kohomada ?

sitha tiyena thak kal sitha kiyana sobawaya mathu wenawa ( manayathanayai dammayathanai athara gateema)

ex:
gindarak athi danaka , gindarak pathireeme hakiyawa tiyenawa wage.

nindedi heena dakinawa,
ayathana pahama wada nokara welawe.
manayathanaya wada ( manayathanayai dammayathanai athara gateema)
ethkota chiththaja roopa mathu wela enawa.

roopayathanayai + manayathanyai gatunahama chiththaja roopa hatagannawa
ewagema
manayathanayai dammayathanai gatunahamath chiththaja roopa hatagannawa

hariyata nikan 
kri gahakata kothanin ketuwath , kiri enawa wage.

ehenam 
ahen dakkath , kanen ahuwath manasinma hithuwath,
hitha athule athi wana hethu dakala awasan karanna puluwan.
ehenam 
hitha athule hethu dakala meka awasan karanna puluwan.
mehema apita enne atheetha hethun hatagath wedana sanyya.
ehenam me mohothe hethu sakas kara nogaththoth 
atheethath, anagathayath iwarai.
enam tiyena atheethayak awilla iwara wenawa.

ex:
hariyata nikan awidinawa wage.
awidina kota pada maru wenawa , idiriyata tibba paya, saha pitipasse tibbichcha paya
humaruwa thulai awideema pawathinne.
dekama eka laga tiyenakota awideemak na neda.
enam awidinawa kiwwe sasara
nawatheema kiwwe niwana.
enam sasara gamana nathara karana ekata thamai niwana kiyala kiwwe.

lokaya thula minissun, me thanhawata dasiyek wela , kawadawath thrupthimath wenne na.
hariyata nikan thirisana , thirisan bawa danne na wage.
pawathina sathwa sobawaye dur gunaya hadunanne na,
hinsa peeda widina bawa danne na.

ex: covid tiyethddith jeewithaya pawathwa ganna yanna hama dema karanwa.
work arounds hada gannawa.
covid thula life style ekata huru wenawa.
eeta passe eka norm eka wenwa, eke honda dakinawa.

me wage wimukththiyatath unanduwak athi kara gaththoth
me siyalleema athi yathaa  ababodaya dana gena sasarin goda yanawa.

arya margaya wadana kenek me hakiyawa thamai wardanaya karaganna oni.
e nisa budun himi deshana karanawa,
iswoyan jeewithaya wada sasanaye athi yatharthaya  gana awaboda karaganeema.
sath dharmaye me gunayata, api sadhu sadhu washayen wandana karanawa. 

ex:
thaththa kiyana eka kiyanna puluwan da thol deka happen nathi widihata ?
puluwan da kiyala balanna hithuna neda ?
amma kiyana kota puluwan da ?
ekath balanna hithuna neda ?
api hitan inna prashnath menna me wage thamai,
thol deka wadinawa danne na kiyana sobawaya wage mai,
ape hithe ena mano wikara tika.
danna widihata karala balala thamai answer eka ganna handanne.
e wage thamai
jeewithaye tiyenawa prashna tikath me wage thamai,
eka ekkenata awenikai, lokaya thulin hithala remedy ekak hoya ganna try karanawa.

ex:
oya ledak nathuwa doctor kenek gawata gihin kiyannakota aga athapaya ridenawa kiyala.
balanna ko, doctorta answer ekak nadda kiyala.
e anwer eka oyatada sambanda , doctor ge lokayatada sambanda ?
prashanaya oyata awenikai,
uththarai doctorge lokayen laba gath danumata awenikai.
e wage thamai
10 denek gen ahuwoth tiyena duka mokadda kiyala ?
eka eka uththara thamai hambenne.
e uththara sama witama sapekshai. 
sansandanayak pamanamai.
eeta passe , apith e sansandanaya , ape jeewithayata sanandanaya kara gannawa.
balanna kochchara mono wikarayak da kiyala ?

chiththaja roopa kiyanne sitha mul karagena ena shakthiyak.
sitha mul karagena athi wana shakthi prabeda dekak tiyenawa. (chiththaja roopa jathi dekak)
1. kaaya wynapthi roopa
2. wachi wynapthi roopa

ex:
mama hithe apu chithtaja roopa hageemak widihata kayen hagawenawa.
kayen hagawanawa ( katha karanakota atha paya selaweeema)
wachanayen haganawa ( hithana eka katha kirima, sadde , tone eka wenas kirima)

ex:
biththiyakata gini pellellakin gahuwahama gini pupuru wisi wenawa wage.
e wage wachanayak katha karanakota , chiththaja roopa wishala pramanayak hata gannawa.

enam dan shabdaya athi wana widi dekak api katha kala
1. chiththaja roopa nisa (me dan katha karapu sobawaya)
2. uthuja roopa nisa ( issella session eke katha karapu sobawaya) (gahak watenakota saddayak enawa, hulaga hamana kota ena sadde..etc)

sadde kiyana eka chiththaja roopak kiyala katha kalane.
hande mihiri bawa athi wenne kohomada ?
meka waag kusalayaka palayak. ( waag - wachana )
oya pera karapu wachanayen sidu karapu kusal sithaka palayak widihata thamai eka hambenne.
wachanayen sidu kala kusalayan nisa. ( apriya wachana, his wachana , kelam,boru  katheemen walakeesitima nisa )
10 kusal wala wachanayen sidda wena kusal gana balanna.

ethkota instrument play karanakota , eka mihiri wenne kohomada ?
insturment ekak kiyanne roopak, 
roopa wala wedena tiyenawa da ?
wedanawa athi une sithe, ehenam mihiri sobawaya hithe athi wena dharmathawayak.
instrument eken apu handa uthuja roopak eka prasadaye wadunahama,habdaya grahana una, e shabdaya
adura aran na ethkota , grahanaya weemak pamanai. 
e grahanaya weema manasen menehi karapu handa thamai
manasa paththe wedanawa hata ganne. eeta passe haduna ganeema dakwa yanne.
kanata ahune 20hz patigayak nam, e patigaya manasin menehi karala
eeta samana atheetha athdakeem anuwa arthayak therum gaththa.
e wedanawa mulika karagena , wedana ,sanyya, chethana dakwa giya.
me athi wechcha adi wachana sammassaye kanata sambanda karapu handa thamai.
kanen ahuna shabbdayak kiyana eka haduna gaththe, volin shabbdayak lesa gaththa ( awidyawa nisa) 

nama roopa parichcheda kiyanne ma me wen kerimatai.
me naama roopa sambandaya me widhata dana gaththahama 
me deka wena wenama dakanna nyaanayak upadawa ganna puluwan. (praknaywa)
e nisa 
hitha athule hethu dakala awasan karanna puluwan kiyala kiwwe oka handa .


Question answer :
neranjan aiya kiwwa , kaya ,wachi, chiththa sankara witharai ahala tiyenne kiyala.
sitha kayen wachanayen raga idwesha moha mulika wela kriya karanawa kiyana eka thamai sankara kiyala kiyanne


methana awidya pachchaya sankara kiwwe, abhi sankara thunakata saha kaya wachi chiththa sankara walata
abhi sankara kiyanne mathu wipaka pinisa yedena karma walata.  
 abi sankara dharmatha thunakata
punyabi sanskara, apunyabi sanskara, aanenjaabi(dhyana sith) sansakara
ehenam kusal, akusal, dyana sith walata.
e nisa sithime hakiyawa, katha kirime hakiyawa, kaya pawathime sankara unata. 
ehi wipaka sakas weemak na.

katha kirime hakiyawa wipaka mattmak pamanai. katha karana wachana anuwa 
punyabi sanskara, apunyabi sanskara, aanenjaabi(dhyana sith) sansakara ras wenne.
ethana katha kirime di raga,dwesha moha mul weela thulin wachi sankara (mano sankara kaaya sanakara) athi wenwa
කාය සංකාර කියන්නෙ ආශ්වාස ප්‍රශ්වාස දෙකට
චිත්ත සංකාර කියන්නෙ වෙිදනා සඤ්ඤා  දෙකට
වචි සංකාර කියන්නෙ විතක්ක විචාර දෙකට
මෙිවාට රාග දොස මොහ මුලික උනාම තමයි කුදල් අකුසල් ආනෙඤ්ඤාභි ඇති වන්නෙ
e nisa thamai budun, rahan wahanselata kaya , wachanaya sitha use karanna puluwan une.
රාග දොස මොහ මුලික nowena kota abhi sankarayan hata ganne na.
e thulin wipaka pinisa karama sakas wenne na.
ehema no-una nam nirwanaya awaboda karagaththu kenekuta awidinna , katha karanna bari wenwawa.
awidina ekath, katha karana ekai hama sarema karma abhi-sankara  sakas wanawa nam kawadawath apita nirwana laga karaganna bari wenawa.

dharmaya athule sankara jathi hugak pawathinawa. ( punabhi, apunyabhi,anenjabhi, kusalabhi,akusalabhi,jeewitha,bawa, kaya, wachi,chiththa) sankara, eeta amatharawa 
sasaren galaweemata thawa payoga sankara (pragoya kiyalath kiyanwa).

e sankara walin abhi sankara tiyenne thunai.
e thuna thamai api me awijja pachchaya sankara kiwwahama salakanne.
mathu karma wipaka pinisa sakas wana abhi sanskara 3 thamai awadanaya yomu karanne.
eke tiyena dosaya thamai api dakinna oni.


Prmuditha ge question : 
mama siyum kiyala adahas karapu eka poddak misguided una wage hithan eka aye poddak balamu.

api katha kala,
roopa upadawana widi 4k gana
1) chiththaja
2) uthuja
3) aharaja
4) karmaja

roopa 28n, 16k ma tiyenne dhammayathanye (sukuma roopa widihata/ mekatama thamai sukshama roopa kiyanneth)
dhammayathana tiyenne manayathanaya tibboth witharai
e kiyanne marichcha minussanata me tika na , enam ( sukuma roopa na)

me roopa 28 api thawa deakarayakin aduna gannawa
 1)ekaantha roopa ( ekama hethuwak handa)
 2) anekantha roopa ( anith hethuwalin puluwan/ ekama hethuwak nowana ewa)

chiththaja roopa kiyanne sitha nisa hata ganna roopa, ekema eka hethuwak nisa hata ganna roopa
me roopa hadena widi walin ekak witharak nisa hata gannawa nam ewa ekantha roopa kiyala kiyannawa
e nisa ekaantha chithtaja roopa ehema naththam ekantha karmaja roopa 


ekantha chiththaja roopa jathi dekak tiyenawa
ewa api giya sare katha kala
kaaya wynnapthi (kayen hagawanawa kiyana ekai)
wachi wynnapthi (wachanayen hagawanawa kiyana ekai)

dan sukuma roopa 16n dekak thamai me, e nisa 
ekantha chiththaja roopa 2k sukuma roopa wenawa.
anekantha roopa kiyanne wena wena hethu nisa hataganna puluwan ( roopa hadena hethu 4n)  
ekama palayata wiwida hethu tiyenna puluwan kiyana eka thamai me kiyanne. nathuwa combination ekak nevie.
ex:
lahutha (sahallu bawaya), mudutha (mrudu bawa), kammanyatha(kriyakari bawa) kiyana roopa 
chithtja,uthuja,aharaja,karmaja nisa hata gannath puluwan
ex: thel handa ginna hata ganna puluwan e wagema dara handath ginna athi wenawa.

pancha indiryan saha gochara roopa siyallama olarika roopa wei ethana 12 tiyenawa.
e kiyanne maha bootha 4i, upadaya roopa 8i
methana me upadaya roopa 8i maha bootha tharam gorosu na.
habai me roopa sukuma roopa nevie. ( giya sare sium kiyala wachanaya use krapu handa thamai poddak patalune)
me upadaya roopa 8i maha bootha tharam prakata nathi handa thamai 
warna ase gateema prakata naththe.
namuth me roopa olarika roopa ma thamai.
olarika roopa 12ta aithi upadaya roopa 8.


Q 3 : kayata , sapa, duka thamai therenne methana upesha mattama kiyanne sapa ho duka kiyana dema nathi awasthawa.
 

----------------------- wipaka mattama p2 (dhathu sobawayan)-------------------------14/06/2021 


dhathu kiyala kiyanne mokadda ? eka mulika sobawayak, arambaka awasthawa.
sathwa pudgala nowana.
api athma sankalpaya hada gaththen manasen,
eka drushtiyak. ( mano wikarayak)
ewa ikmawala giyahama saba sobawaya katha karanne dhaathu kiyana wachanaya use karala.
dhaathu kiyala sammuthiye wena wena dewal gana katha karana 
namuth methana katha karanne eka nevi.
e nisa dhathu kyiala katha karanakota 
sathwa pudgala bawayak ennama ba.
e nisa sathya wu mulika sobawawya lesa hadunwanna puluwan.


dan balamu monawada me dhathu 6.

1)patavi
2)apo
3)thejo
4)wayo
5)akasa (shuddashtaka dekak athara hidasa)
6)wynyaana.

siyallama hadila tiyenne me dhathu 6n.

meken 5k ajeewai, ekak sajeewai. (wynaanaya)

methana ajeewee saha sajeewee kiyana sobawaya gana tikak katha karala imu.

paramparaa washayen pawathinna puluwan wenne sajeewe dharamatha walata.
e kiyanne 
pawathma sakas karaganeeme hakiyawa thamai api me pramparawa washayen haduna ganne.
enam sajeewi kiyala kiyanne pawathma sakas karaganeeme hakiyawai.

sajeewi dhathu tiyenne ekai, eka thamai wynaana dathuwa.
api jeewitha indriya kiyala katha karanne bawanga sitha tama thamai.
bawangaya kiyanne bawaye angayak, enam bawangaya pathina thak kal bawaya pawathinawa. 
jeewitha indriya pawathinne menna me bawangaya kiyana sitha enam wynaana dathuwa samagai.


ex:
ahala tiyenawa da law ginnak gana. eka kawruwath karapu ekak da ?
sathwa pudgala sambandayak na neda ?
ginna athi weemata awashaya hethu sakas weeme palaya thamai law ginna.
ginnata awashaya amudrawya laga patha pawathina thak kal, ginna automatically 
pathireema sidu wenawa.
ginna nawaththanna oni nam, gini barrier apita hadanna puluwan.
ginna wate area ekak sudda karala ginnata awasha hethu tika ain karanna puluwan.
dan ginna nimenawa,
e wage thamai me palamu dathu 5he sobawaya, hethu naththam pawathmak na. ajeewie. pawathma sakas karaganna ba.
barrier ekedi nawathinawa.
api me ginna, wynanaya ehema naththam sitha namathi sajeewi dhathuwa lesa gaththama.
ginnata awashaya indana unu lee kali, saha anekuth amudrawya wage,
wynaanaye pawathmata awasha indana thamai raga, devesha, moha kiyala dharamatha.
wynaanaya sajeewi lesa hadunwanne , me ginnata eha paththata paninna puluwan kama hadenna nam
ekata awasha athu gas kabali pawathinna oni,
e nisa wynaanaya raga, dvesha, moha sakas kara ganeema sanda (awidya, thrushna) kiyana dharmatha deka enam
sathwa sobawya mawa panawa, methan sathwa kiyala kiyanne sasare pawathmata alunu kiyana sobawaya.
me sathwaya raga ,dewesha , moha kiyala hethu awidaya thrushna padanam karan sakas karanwa.

onna dan ginna menna me barrier eka paneemata awashaya hethu pawathina , 
ginna warrier eka panala pawathma digatama sakas karagannawa.
me sathwaya hata raga, dewesha , moha sakas kara ganeemata wynaaya anekuth dhathu sobawayan use karaganna
awidyawa thulin , me dhathu sowabaye sathya wasan kota, thushnawen allala denawa.
hewath upadanaya kawarawanawa.
upadanaya pawathina thek ginna pathirenawa

raga dewesha moha kiyana hethu sakas weemata
me dhathu 6 namathi sanyogaya (punjaya) waradi lesa dana ganeemata awasha nisa 
dathu hadunaganeemata salayathana bihi wenawa.
salayathana thulin dhathu isparshaya sakas wenawa
upadanaya thula thun bawaya sakas kerenwa ( kama bawaya, roopa bawaya, aroopa bawaya)
e nisa 
salayathana pachchaya bawo lesa me sobawaya hadunawa.

"sabbee dhamma passa sambawo" ehema naththam sparshaya siyallata hethuwa bawa buru rajan wahanse deshana karanawa.

ehenam me deshna kale ekama chathurarya sathyayai.
sparshaya nisa duka athi wana bawath
duka matha siyalla pawathina bawath 
dukata hethu (awidya saha thanha gana) namathi sathwa sobawaya gana pulul awabodayen
ginna saha pathieeme sobawaya, athi wana bawa nathi weema sakshath kala haka

meya athiwana bawa nathi weema hewath , anuppada nirodayai

me gana gaburen balanna 
lowthuru arana channel eka karana suseela hamuduro ekka karana
discussion eka refer karanna. its 9 hour session
https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4rupW9dlCnw
'Sinhala Dhamma Talk with a Real Monk - 555.5 Minutes' - Ancient Dhamma

pachchicha samuppada niyaya ehema naththam 
dharma niyamaya wu 
"imasmin sathi idan hothi" - 
"imassa uthpada idan udpajjathi"
"imasmin asathi idan nahothi"
"imassa nirudda idan nirujjathi"

meya athi kal hi meya wei
meya upadina kal hi meya upadi
meya nathi kalhi meya hata nogani
meya nupadunu kalhi meya nohata gani

meya meya kiwwe ekama siddanthayak
enam eya nisa meya nowana bawa 
hethu pala kriyawakinma meya pawathina bawa. dana gatha yuthui  

meya gaburin awaboda kale nam 
anuppada nirodaya hewath, nohata ganeema sakshath wiya yuthui. 
ehi dee samudaya thula nirodaya nowa.
samudayama niroda bawa. (sakas weemama niroda wela)
e nisa palayakin thorai.
sakas weemak naththam 
palaya nopawathi, 
enam niwanai.

me anuwa athiwechcha deka nathi weema nowa,
athi wana bawa nathi weema hewath nuppada nirodaya sakshath kara yuthuya.

ex:
switch eka dammoth fan eka karakenawa
fan eka athin karakara kuwata ehema karakenne na
switch eka danna ayasayakin.
fan eka karakeema nirayasayen wena ekak

ayasaya laukika samma dittiyai.
nirayasaya lokoththara samma dittiyai.
me anuwa 
ayasaya pawathinne lokaya thulai
nirayasaya pawathinne lokoththra thulai.
fan eke switch eka damme naththam fan eka karakenne na.
enem
ayasen api karann tiyenne monawada 
sucharithaye yedimai, ( enam sitha kaya wachanaya sanwara kara ganeemai)
enam raga , dewesha , moha duru karaganeemai.
fan eke switch eka damma nam 
fan karakaweema 

ehema naththam sucharithaye yedeema thulin nirayasayen nirwanaya awabodayata padama wei.

e nisa lokaya sankathyak lesath ( hethu pala dahamak)
niwana asankathayak lesath ( hethu palayak novuu)
awaboda karagannawa. 

e nisa chathuraya sathye anupiliwelak gana katha karanawa
lokaya thula : ( hethu pala lesa katha karanwa)
dukka sathya ( duka kiyanne palayak)
samudaya sathya ( duka hata ganna hethuwa samudayai)

lokoththra sobawaya thula:
dukka niroda sathya ( niwana pilibanda awabodaya)(inimaga badinna pera building eke usa dana ganna oni ne)
dukka niroda gamini patipada sathya ( marga sathya)(awaboda karagath niwana sakshath karaganeema sadaha wadiya yuthu prathipadawa)

me marga sathya thamai api arya ashtangika margaya lesa kotas 8kin katha karanne.
ehi arambaya lokoththara samma dittiyai. 
enam dukka sathya saha sumudaya sathya gana athi niwaradi 
awabodayai. ( enam fan eka karakeemata awashaya aayasayai)

e nisa 
gihi geya hewath gini geya thula aayasaya pamanamai kala hakke,
me sanda sathi sampajanya (praknayawa), enam sathiyai praknaywai awasha wenne.
enam praknawen thorawa sathiya pawathmen wadak na.

 ex:
 bombayak hadaddi pin eka hariyata set karanna oni naththam athe pupuranawa.
 e wage sathiya tibbe naththam wade karanna ba. sathiya pawathwanna nam awashya deta pamanak focus karanna oni
 wada wadi unoth sathiya pihitanna ba. e nisa pin eka nam tiyann eka gana focus karanna oni.
 namuth bombayen wena aadinawaya maha winasayak. ehenam praknaywa yedila na
 ewani sathi (mutta sathi) hadin wenawa. raga,dwesha,moha wadi weemak pamanai, enam sasarata hethuwai.
 

enam sakman karana kota sathiyen karanna oni kiyala kiyanne me nisai.
sakman karanne raga dwesha moha adu wena widihata nam , ethana sathi sappajanya ( ehema naththam sithiyai, praknawai) 
tibiya yuthui.
ehenam sathi sampajanya thamai api purudu kala yuththe.


mechchara wela api katha kale wynana dhathuwa ganai.

dan balamu ajeewi dathu set eka gana .

thejo dathuwa balamu.

ex:
kanna puluwan appayak hadanna nam, thejo dathuwa kohomada tiyenna oni?
thejo  kiyanne unusuma saha seethala kiyana sobawaya.
ehenam kanna puluwan appayak hadanna ,
sudusu mattame thejo dathuwa pawathinna oni. ( mekata api kiyanawa prasastha mattama kiyala)
eeta adu una ho wadi una kiyala kanna puluwan appayak hadanna ba.
ehenam thejo dathuwata hakiyawa tiyenawa 
deyak athi karannath deyak nathi karannath puluwan.

thejo dathuwa shuddashtakayen ekak.
 
api katha kala shudda+asshtaka roopa kalapa kiyanne ( sathara ba boothyai, e asuru kota pawathina upadaya roopa 4i)
(warna ganda rasa oja) , me 8 kawadawath wen karanna ba .
e nisa ekata kiyanawa avinip-booga kiyala. (wen karanna ba)
ebadu roopa kalapa, athara tiyena hidasa , akasa dathuwa kiyala hadunwanawa.

ex:
loriyaka alagoni tikak patwan yanwa.
ala goniya helawena wita , ala eheta meheta move wenna puluwan une 
ala athara tiyena hidasa nisa.
ala goniyak kiyanne shuddashtaka kalapayak.
ala kiyanne shuddashtaka nam 
helaweemata athara tiyena ida akaasa dathuwai.

me okkoma ajeewee dhaathu. ( patavi,apo,thejo wayo, akasa) 

api thejo dathuwa thulin hata ganeema ho winasa weema sidda wenna puluwan kiyana eka api aduna gaththa.

ex:
ape body eke temp wadi unoth apita una,
adu unoth eth ledak, 
prashastha mattame tibiya yuthui.

patavi dhathuwa  ralu/ gorosu / mrudu /thada bawa
ex: maluwa ebenawa , welapu karolaya ehema na. ekama maluwa, enam dekama patavi.

wayo kiyanne selewena sobawaya (pimbena hakilena sobawaya)
ex: suli sulak gamuwoth wena winasaya balanna.
wathaye tiyena patavi dathuwa gas, gewal wala gatunu nisa thamai ewa galawila giye.
wathaye tiyena selewena sobawaya nisa thamai eka gaman karanne.

mewage 
wathureth patwiya tiyenawa.

api katha kale patavi, thejo,wayo 
me thuna ekata bandala tiyenne apo kiyana sobawayen

ex: hal piti karala kudutika wathura dala anapuwahama 
giluyak hadanna pulwuan.
wathure tiyena thethamanaya ehema naththam apo gathiya nisa thamai
me kudu tika guliyak washayen ekata pawathwanna puluwan une.

apo gathiya naththam me lokaye tiyena 
eka eka wasthu ekata ekathu wela tiyenne apo dathuwa handa
apo dathuwa adu wenakota eka wisirenawa hulaga wage
wadi wenakota watery sobawayak gannawa
hugak wadi wethdi solid wenawa.

gana, drawa, wayu kiyala api bedanne menna me apo dathuwe hakiyawa matha.

apo dathuwa indriya 5ta gochara na. eka gochara manayathanayata. enisa api eka damme dammayathanya.

ex:
apo dathuwe tiyena bond kirime hakiyawa . dana ganeemak pamanai neda .
piti tikak anuwahama, guliya apita therenne eke tiyena pataviya handa.
eke tiyena rasnaya/heethalaya apita therum ganna puluwan thejo handa.
eke tiyena pipena sobawaya  apita therum ganna puluwan wayo widihata.
roti thatiyata dala thuni karanna puluwan wenne me wayo dathuwa handane.
namuth meke anshu athara tiyena sambandaya pawathwanne apo dathuwen.
eka apita me pancha indriyanta therum ganna ba.
eka manasen thamai gochara karaganna puluwan.
e nisa apo dathuwa api sukuma roopayak lesa dammayathanayedi katha karanawa.

ex:
pani tikak plate ekata dapuwahama ,
eka thallu karanna puluwan neda.
eka issarahata yanwane.
e alena wagirena sobawaya. apo dathuwe sobawayak.
pani tika athe dawateema sobawaya / e gattanaya athi wenne wadirena sobawaya handa nevi neda 
gattanaya patavi sobawayai.
ehenam apita danune gattanaya misak wadirena sobawaya nevi.
ahata penuna warnaye wenasa thulin wagirena sobawaya haduna gaththe.
namuth ahata penune warnaya witharai, e nisa wagirena sobawaya pawathune manasa thulai.

e nisa ape sobawaya manasata pamanai haduna gatha hakke.
e nisa apo sobawaya dhammayathanaya danawa sukuma roopak nisa.


ex:
pita dige dadiya binduwak yanwa kiyannako,
e danenne apo gathiya nevi , eka patavi gathiya.
apo gathiya sukumai nam ehema dannenna bane.
dadiya  binduwa danenne kohatada kayata.
enam pottabayata,
pottabbaya haduwanne maha bootha thunakin ( patavi,thejo, wayo)
ehenam api hithan inna me wagirena sobawaya  apoo dhathuwa kiyala hithuwana eka dharmayata anukula na.
enam 
pottabbayak thula dana gatha haki wenne patavi, thejo, wayo witharai.
pita dige dadiaya gala yamedi 
thejo - unusume variation ekane
wayo gathiya kiyanne selewena /hamana gathiya.

dadiya binduwe prakata wenne patavi gathiyai.(ralu ho sumata sobawaya thamai prakata wenne)

ex:
rasnaya danenawa neda ? rasnaya danenne kohata da kayata
rasnaya danenawa kiyanne api eka haduna ganne pottabba roopaya lesa , enam kayata.

ex:
hulagak hamagena yanakota dannenne ai
eke tiyena wayo sobawaya nisa mekath poddabbayak, kayata danenne.

ex:

poddabbaya kiyanne kayata gochcarayane.

oyata ahata penna pirisudu widuru dekak 
eka mattmakata wathura purawala tiyenawa oyata penawa.
dan oyata puluwan da ?
oyata puluwan da ekaka unu wathura tiyenawa ekaka al wathuwa tiyenawa 
kiyanna.
ehenam kayen thamai dana puluwan.
eka kayata awenika lakshanayak.
enam pottabbaya hamatissema 
kayata witharai  gochara.

ex:
dan tea ekak unui. kohatada danune ?
ara thel pallamata danune na , enam giwha prasadaya unusuma danaganna ba.
namuth tea eke unusama danune kaya prasadayata.

asa kana ,nasaya diwa nikan kada dasiye tiyena thel binduwa wage.
ape shareeraye pihitala tiyena indriya 5k thamai enam wishesha hadunaganeemak kara gatha gaki than.

kaaya , kotas 32 gana katha karanwa. 
(sotha, jivha ,gana, chakku ) ewath api ethana katha karanwa.

e nisa thamai
ahata annoth kaya prsadayata thamai e pottabbaya therenne.
thel pallama wage thamai chakku prasadaya.

ex:
bath kanakota diwa hapenawa,
rasayak da danune. ?
kaya prasadayata ahu unu handa thamai wedanawa.

olarika roopa 12hen 
1)ahata 2)roopayata
3)kanata 4)shabdaya
5)nasayata 6)suwada
7)diwata 8)rasaya
9)kayata 10,11,12)poddabbaya ( maha butha thunai / patavi,thejo, wayo)


ethkota kayata thamai maha butha gateemak danenne
enam poddabaya.

ex: 
wathura jump karanakota 
wathura wadina gathiya ( patavi gathiya)
wathure unusuma dakina eka thejo gathiya
wathura athule peenanna puluwan wenne wayo gathiya nisa 

me thuna witharai kayata dana ganna puluwan,
olarika roopa witahrai apita prakata wenne
sukuma roopaya prakata na, eka pottabbaya thula athi wana ekak nevi eka sitha thula hada ganna ekak.
enam kayen sukuma roopaya danne na.

namuth 
wathure yana wita wathura age gawena sobawaya therenawa.
eka patavi gathiyak. me sobawaya apo gathiya nevi
apo gathiya  mano wynanayenmai dana ganna puluwan.
enema kayen dana ganna ba.
gawena sobawaaya pamanai kayata danenne
wathura thamai gawune kiyana sobawaya kaya thula hamuwela na.


ehenam kayata thamai sapa/duka danenne

ex:
amma oluwa pirimadinawa,
duka da sapada ?
pataviye lakshana monawada 
ralu sumata
bara sahallu
thada mrudu

oluwa atha ganakota mrudu/sumudu gathiyak neda danne.
ehenam eka patavi neda

wedanawa ( weemak daneema ) kotas thunai ne ( pancha indriya  thula)
sapa 
duka 
upeksha

manasata danena "sapa/duka kiyana danena hageemata" api kiyanawa somanassa/domanassa kiyala.

e nisa wedanawa dan kotas pahai ( indiya 6th ekka gaththuwahama)

sapa, 
somanassa,
duka, 
domanassa
upeksha

dan me indiya 5 thula sapa duka athi wenne koheda kiyala balamu

roopa 28, maha bootha monawada 
patavi, apo, thejo ,wayo 
ethkota me 4 arunahama , ithuru 24ma upadaya roopa (maha bootha roopa nowana roopa )
me upadaya goden,
warna, ganda rasa oja kiyana 4 hamatissema sathara maha bootha asuremai pawathinne.
ekai mekata shuddashtakak kiyala kiwwe, e 8 kadanna ba.

shareeraye kotasak neda asa,kana,nasaya,diwa kiyanne
shareera hadila tiyenne mokenda 
shuddashtaka godaka ekathuwak
enam asa thula 
apo thejo wayo patavi asuru karagath  upadaya roopa 4k saha parasa roopayai, jeewitha indriyai ekathu wela dashaka 
kalapak hadenawa , eka thamai thamai asa kiyala ganne 
e wage 
kana, nasaya , shareeraya diwath me widihamai
ethkota upadaya roopayak wu warnaya , upadaya roopayak wu asa samaga hamu weemak thamai sidu wenne.
ehnam upadaya roopayak samaga thawa upadaya roopayak hamuweema thamai asa thula wenne.
meka apita danenna tharam prakata na.
enam potabbaya tharam prakata na
api katha kranne hamu weemak gana.

dan shareenaya upadaya roopayak unata 
eke gocharaya pottabba ekak. ( maha butha thunai patavi,thejo,wayo )
shareeya gaththahama,
e dhashaka kalayapa athule palamu 8i, jeewitha indiryai, prasada roopai.
me pradaya poddabbaya danime hakiyawai.
asata warna upadaya roopaya danime hakiyawa wage.
shareeraye prasada roopaya samawitama maha bootha rupa 3na katai, enam pottabba roopayai.

asa,nasaya,diwata sama wita gochara wanne upadaya roopayai.
asa -> gochara wenne warnaya ( upadaya upadaya hamuweemai)
nasaya -> gochara wenne gandaya ( upadaya upadaya hamuweemai) 
diwata -> gochara wenne rasa  ( upadaya upadaya hamuweemai)

kana -> gochara wenne shabdaya ( upada upadaya gateemak da ?) (meka pasuwata balamu)
shareeraya -> gochara wenne poddabbaya (patavi ,thejo,wayo ) shareeyaya dhasha kalapayak unata 
ekata hambena gocharaya upadaya roopa nevi, eka maha butha thunen yuth poddaba roopaya pamanai.

ex:
as deka wahala torch ekak allanawa agata 
danei da ? ( kawruth kiwwe naththan therenne nane)
rasne dananewa neda ?
eka poddabbayak neda (thejo)
hulagak nam wayo gathiya therenewane
gateemak therenawa neda ( patavi gathiya)
methanata sitha yomu unoth witharai, 
roopaya kiyala dana ganne. ( sitha yomu unoth withrai dana ganne)
sitha thamai prathibimbaya pilibada dana ganne.

ex:
sitha yomu wiya yuthui roopaya gana dan ganna.
e dana ganna roopaya bahirata paththa kaloth , mama kiyana kena hadenawa.
mama innakena thamai meka balanne.
elagata shabbadaya ahunahama
ara roopaya dakapu mamama ara shabddaya asuwe kiyala mama hithanawa.
melesa wiparitha ayathana 6n widinnekuth nirmanaya wela.

anna e thiyena athma drushtiyata 
"roopan athththatho samanu passaththi"  <- aththanu dittiya ( sakkaya dittiye 20n ekak)
enam athma drushtiyata ida kada laba deela nawatha nathwa asuru karanawa.
mehema athmai kiyana gathi witharak ain karanna ba.
ain karanawa nam
yam thanakada pihitiye , e pihiti thanath yain karanna wenawa
enam warnaya ain karanawa nam ahath ain karanna oni.

nawatha lokaya kiyala panawanna thanak nathi wiya yuthui.

mese anathma sankalpanaya pilibada budun deshanawa mokadda ?

hethu nisa sakas wana warnaya hethu nathi wenakota nathi wenawa.
anathma weeme hethuwa ethana pawathinawa.
roopaya pilibadawa kisiwak thama wasagaye pawathwanna ba.
prasadaye akaraya wenas wenakota gocharaya wenas wenawa.

mee massekuge ahatai, deviyek ge asatai, manussayek ge ahatai penena widiha wenas
prasadaya wenas nisa.
isella katha karapu hethu pahe wenasa nisa (  awidyawa, thanhawa , karmaya, ahara, nibbaththi lakshana )

roopa 10 ( manasai dhammai harunokota ithuru set eka)
budu himi anathmai kiyana dharmaya penwa dunne , topics dekak yatathe
1) wasagaye pawathwanna nohaki bawa
2) "thuchcha sankaara samanu passana" washayen (pahath , hiss bawa, asara bawa) 

e nisa 
"athma sara" washayen asarai. 
"nithya sara" washayen asarai.
"suka sara" washayen asarai.

e nisa thamai api anathmai kiyanne.
athma ho athamaneeya gathiyak athnam asara novie.

ex:
 athmaneeya kiyanne athmayata hitha kiyana eka 
 adaneeya amma kiyanne , adarayata hitha woo amma
 ehema tiyenawai kiyala ganna sobawaya.

ex:
 sara wenna nam athma ho athmaneeya gathiyak tiyenna oni
 prathya bawayen hata gaththu ewa pathara nathi wana wita nathi wenawa 
 enam 
 athma saara lesa anshumathrak wath na
 roopa 10ma na.
 
 yamak athma sara wasahyen asarai nam
 e dema thamai asarai kiyanne.
 
 "asaa-rattena anaththa" lesa budun ge dharmaya wydyamana wenne.
 meka apita danichcha ekak nevi.
 
 nithya roopa lesa panawanna puluwan kisiwak me lokaye naha.
 "sabban roopan anichchan"
 
 e nisa ayathanen thorawa lokayak gana katha karanne ma na.
 ehema katha karanawa nam 
 ewa sithaluwak witharai.
 mayyanawak witharai.
 mama kiyana eka ayathanak nevi. eka mayynawak pamanamai.
 
 
 praknappthi/ sammuthi waradi drushtiya nisa.
 ayathana wala aththa sobawaya danne nathi handa
 lokaya kiyala kiwwe nirodaya gana nodanna moda kama nisa.
 
 
 
 ara shabbadaya gana tikak balamu.
 
 shabbada hadena karama dekak tiyenawa 
 1) sithin upan roopaya ( chiththaja roopaya, sithin hithala katharanawa, sitha nisa hata gath)
 2) uthuja roopayak widihata ( erthuwa wenas weema nisa, ewa wenas wenakota shabbadaya hata gannawa)
 ex:
 yakada dekak ekata gatimedi 
 pera nothibu shabbadayak hata gannawa 
 bahira roopa dekak gatila
 ethana sobawaya wenas weema nisa (erthuwa wenas weema nisa hata gaththu deyak)
 meka karamaya kin nevi
 sithakin karapu ekak nevi
 parisaraye yam wenasak nisa hata gaththu ekak
 
 e nisa koi loke kohoma ipadunath shabbda roopaya na hata ganna mohothe na
 
 kanata -> gocharaya shabbadaya
 mahabootha nowannawu roopa upadaya roopa kiyala kiwwa
 shabbadaya kiyana eka mahabootha da ?
 sithin hata ganna or uthuja lesa hadanne updaya roopak.
 kanath upadaya roopayak. ehenam ethana tiyenneth 
 upadaya upadaya gateemak pamanai pawatiyenne.
 
 ex:
 adata katuwakin annoth, wedanawa athi une warnaya nisada poddabbaya nisa da  ?
 enam poddabbaya thulin neda wenadawa hata aran tiyenne
 e wedanawa anuwa thamai sapa ho duka athi wela tiyenne.
 
 ex:
 kadasiye thel pallamak tiyenwa kiyala ganna. ( kadadasiya kaya, thel pallama prasada roopaya)
 thel pallama ta katten annoth hil wenne kadadasiya neda
 ehenam danenenne kadasiyata 
 kada dasiya kaya nam
 danenne kayata 
 warnaya danenne thel pallamata. 
 eha paththa penne thel pallama thulin
 kadadasiya thulin nevi
 
 warnaya penne thel pallama thulin. (upadaya roopayak)(ase prsada roopaya, wedanawe awasthawak)
 wedanwa danenne kadadasiya thulin. (olarika roopayak) (kaye prasada roopaya, wedanawa thawa awasthawak)
 
 wedana than dekama hadenawa,
ase prasada roopayata  gatenne warnayak nisa eken athi wena wedanawa harima siyum. upadaya roopak handa prakata na
kaye prasada roopayata gatenne pottabbayak nisa ekan athi wana wedanawa prakatai. ralui/ gorosui

ex:
ahen roopa peneema  sapada ? dukada ?
kanata shabbadaya aseema sapada ? dukada ?
nasayata diwata  daneema sapada ? dukada ?

me mulika awasthawa , wipaka mattmai
ewa upksha sahagathai

namuth kayata 
mulika mattama prakatai, enam e wipaka mattama dukka sahagatha ho sukka sahagatha wedanawaki.
mechchara wela api katha kale roopa roopa mattmai.
methana sitha ekathu unoth thamai "passa" kiyala kiyanne



ada api katha kale wipaka mattama.


-------------------------keles duru karana ayuru-----20/06/2020-------------------

keles kiyanne raga idwesha moha walata 
mewata keles kiyanne sitha kilutu karana handa 
sitha pirisudu karanna  yanakota api keles pilibanda dan ganna oni.
enam keles kiyanne akusalayata hethu wana dharma.

mulin balamu keles pawathina widiha,

pruthakjana yeku nitharama inna / keles pawathina sobawaya  pari-uttanaya mattama kiyala hadun wanawa.
ehenam me uttanaya nowu mattama mokadda kiyala balanna oni.
anusaya mattamak kiyala kiyanne keles nidan inna mattak, keles tiyenawa kiyala therenne na.
pruthakjanaya inne hamatissema pariuttana mattame tiyenne , keles hama tissema nakitala ena mattama ( upadana sanyojana mattama) (onima welawaka sanyojana hadeeme hakiyawa tiyenawa)

ex: watura wage hama tissema galagena yana sobawaya eke tiyenawa. gala yamata prushtak hamu unoth gala yanawama thamai.
(engadge wenna balagena inne , ever ready position. hotblood)

involment eka weethik-kama mattama kiyala hadunnawa. ( atha paya, wachana wisi karala engadge wenne me mattamedi)
me widihata tiyena keles walin
hitha pirisidu kara ganna nam , keles prahanaya karanna oni.
keles prahanaya karana krama 5k tiyenawa . (method)

1) ikshanika samaadiya ( sabba chiththa sadarana chithasikayak thamai, ekagrathawaya, eka onima sithaka tiyenawa,
e nisa ekagrathawaya thulin ikshanika samaadiyak athi kara ganna puluwan. e nisa raga,idwesha, moho athi weema, e mohothe thula kriyathmaka wena eka palanaya kara ganna puluwan)( anusaya mattame idala pariuttana thamai ikshanika samaadiya pawathinne , weethik-kama mattamata yanna ida denne na)

ex: onna kenek pare yanawa. hitha gaththu kenek dakinawa.
eyawa allanna , lagata gihin katha karanna , eyata hirihara karanna, asaawa sansidawa ganna  
lasthi wenne na. namuth keles mathu wela tiyenawa. action eka aran na.
ethkota methana e mohothe keles sansideema karala tiyenne. ikshanika samaadiya athi karagena , weethik-kama mattamata yanna ida deela na. mema keles prahanaya , thadanga prahanaya lesa hadunwanawa.
pruthakjana onima kenekuta me sobawaya tiyenne. 

2) thawakalikawa, dirga kalayak keles yatapath kireema. api mekata kiyanawa wishkambhana prahanaya

ex: dahan walata sama wadeema. (me prathipalaya allan inna puluwan kalaya, kalpa 80 haradahak tharam deergai.)
brahma thala wala ayu kalayath mekama thamai. thawakalika dahan thulin wishkambana prahana mattame pawathinna puluwan.

ex: gedarata wada pansalasedi sitha damanaya kara gena sitina sobawaya wadie.
athul wenakota tiyenne thadanga prahanaya, bana ahanakota wishkambana prahanaya.
enam raga idesha moha mathu novi inna puluwan sobawaya.

me sobayan dekama pruthakjanai.
Arya shawakayage mattama anusaya mattama lesa hadin wenawa.
anusaya mattama kiyanne agata nodanena tharamata pawathinawa kiyana ekane
keles nidagena inna sobawaya. ethkota arya shawakayata keles sampurnayen nasa ganna bari unata.
anusaya mattame wadi kalayak radawa ganna hakiyawa pawathinawa.

3) samuchcheda parahanaya

anusaya mattame naturally inna puluwan gathiya. eka sampurnayen nasa ganna bari wenna puluwan.
namuth anusaya mattme boho durata pawathinna puluwan. idala hitala kama tikak deela boho kalayak
ninde tiya ganna puluwan.
samuchcheda kiyanakota sampurnayen sindalapu kiyana arthya apita enna puluwan.
namuth me awastahwe anusaya (raga idesha moha ) sampurnayen nasala na.

4) patipassaddi prahanaya

samuchcheda mattamen passe nawatha nawatha ahaara denne na
puluwan tharam kalayak ahara nodi innawa.
pati passaddi - kiyanne nawatha nawatha sansunwenawa kiyala/ enam mohothak mohothak pasa sanwara wenawa.

5) nissarana prahanaya

keles mukuth ma na, e kiyanne anusaya mattamen ethera wela. nissarana wela.
me sobawaya marga pala mattamak.
enam sowan mattamedi  sanyojana 3 sadahatama prahanaya wela iwarai.(sakkaya ditti, whichikichcha, seelabatha paramasa iwarai)
thada nindewath sowan palaya nathi wenne na.


dhayana jathi dekak pawathinawa 
1) arya dhyana
2) anarya dhyana

anarya dhyana pawathinne wishkambana prahanaya thula. ( roopa / aroopi dhyaana mattam)(mewa lukika dyana)
arya dhyana pawathinne nissarana prahanaya thulai. (marga pala, sowan mattamen patan ganna)

hari dan  pruthakjana sobawaya ganna poddak balala imu.

gihiyan wisin nadaththuwa sanada danaya soya gatha yuthui ne.
budun deshana kala
gihi apita noraka yuthu job 5k 

1) wahal/slaves weladama ( sathwa wanijja - padiyakin thorawa gaha gaha wada gannawata )(niwahal chithanayak tiya ganna denne na)
