2) ayuda weladama (saththa wanijja - kenek ge parapana nasumata upkari wana tools nishpadanaya saha weladama)(prathipalaya naraka nam nuwana yedila na, sathi sampajanya na)
3) wisa weladama ( wisa wanijja)
4) mas weladama (mansa wanijja) 
5) math pan ha math drawya weladama ( majja wanijja) ( bothalayak yaluwekuta denna salli deela ganeema gana nevei methana katha karanne, business ekak widihata karanna epa kiyana sobawaya)
 
me pahatama aithi nathi rassawak hoda rassawak lesa hadunwanawa.
rassawe yedeema raga, idwesha, moho aduwena widihata karanna oni.
gihiyek washayen rassawak karanakota niwan dakeema pramada karanna hethu wana job 5k thamai sadahan kale.

ex:
ra walin pani hadannath puluwan math wennath puluwan.
wikunana kena pani hadanna witharak nam wikunuwe. ending point eka waradak na
namuth ganna kena gaththe math wenna nam eka waradie.
wikunapu kena math weema sanda ha nam wikunuwe , ekath nokala yuthu job ekata thamai aithi wenne.
sama witama chethanawa saha ein athi wena prathipalaya matha rada pawathi.

budun pudgalayan kotas 4ta bedanawa.
prathipadawa saha abinyyawa anuwa

prathipadawa ( karanna oni de / pawathina pasubima matha danuma wardanaya karanna karana de ) matha saha abinyyawa matha ( abinyaa kiyanne danuma/awabodaya)

abinyyawa matha 
1) dandaa (bohoma himin thamai enne)
2) kippaa (bohoma ikmanin/ wegayen awaboda wenawa )

prathipadawa anuwa
1) duka
2) sapa

e anuwa pudgalayan kotas 4i,
1) dukka patipada dandaa abinyya
2) dukka patipada kippa abinyya
3) sukaa patipada danda abinyya
4) sukaa patipada kippa abinyya

(dukka patipada dandaa abinyya)
 dushkara prathpadawak ( prathya pahasukam, gilapasa senasana ) saha awabodaya harima semin.
 pera karapu pinpaw anuwa
(dukka patipada kippa abinyya)
 dushkara prathipadawak habai ikmanata awaboda wenawa
(suka patipada danda abinyya) 
 prathya pahasukam ithaama hodai, namuth awabodaya ithaa semin
(sukaa patipada kippa abinyya) 
prathya pahasukam ithaama hodai,awabodaya ithaa wegayen.


budun saha sariyuth thero inne 4 weni awasthawe.
mugalan thero inne 3wana awasthawe.

ada api dharmaya sakachcha karana kota ihatha 4n palamu thuna thamai wadipura hambenne.
ekenuth 3 wana sobawya etha durlabai.

dharmaya sakachcha karna kota , me pudgalayan 3 akarama hambenna puluwan.
palamu saha dewani sobawaya thamai boho wadi.

godak sapa tiyenawa nam dharmaya soyanne na.
budun kalayen , raja kama athaharala giya aya hitiya
namut hada kale yai da ?


e nisa dharamaya sakachcha karanna yedunoth. api kala yuththe

ex:
geyak gini gannawa nam , eya niwana adahasin wathura thothak hari e desata wisi karana ekai.
eken ginna niwenne nathi wenna puluwan. namuth ape yuthukama ignore nokireemai.
dharmayen dothak wisi karanne , ginna athi una thama pera karapu kusalayan awadi weeme sobawaya mathu kara ganna
hethu sakas kirimak widihata.
enam raga,iwdesha, moha ginna niwa ganeemata sudusu parisarak athi wena widihata stimulate karanna.

me sobawaya handa thamai,
maha karunawa, maha praknyawa tibu budu rajananwahanse mulu india wama rahas karanna haduwe na.
me dharmayaye therum ganeema thama thulin wenna oni kiyala therum yanna oni.

sawan palayata wath path weemata , me dakwa apita bari une eka etharam dushkara handa.
dharma awabodaya awrudu 35kata passe hamu unath, eelaga bawayedi nawatha mula idala igena ganeemata awasha wenawa.
mekata hethuwa raga,iwesha.boha chaithasika thulin bawa sakasma wena handa.
kenek sowan mattamata paminunahama, eyage athi wana chiththa weethi raga, dewesha moha thulin aramunu weema athi weeme hakiyawa adu wela tiyenne ( sampurnayen duru wela na)
e nisa praknaya chaithasikayen chiththa weethi hata ganeeme hakiyawa digatama pawathinawa.
e nisa me bawayen eelaga bawayata yathdith sowan sobawaya pawathinawa.
sowan novi sakwithi raja kenek wenawata wadiya
sowan wela higannek unath kamak na.
etharam watinakamak pawathinawa.


---------------------------anithya sanyyawa--------27/06/2021-----

giya sare kalaye anithya sobawaya gana katha karapu eka tikak theruna madi kiyala hithuna 
e hinda 
dan balamu, anithya sanyyawa gana tikak gaburin balamu.

thun kalayaka sanyya , hithnma athi unu sammuthi/praknyapthi neda ?
atheetha , warthamana , anagatha yanu hithnma athi karagaththu sammuthi hewath praknapthi witharai neda?

ex: oyata oyage punchi kale siddi mathak karanna puluwan.
habai mathak karanne me mohethe.
anagatha plan ekak gana hithanneth me mohethe manasin.
habai, asa, kana, nasaya, diwa, shareerayata. ta aramunu wenne warthamanaye aramunu witharai.
ewata thun kalayak gana katha karanna ba.
eka manasata pamanai thun kalaya yedenne.

ehenam indriya 5 gana katha karanakota , warthamanaya pamanai.
ehenam me warthamana mohotha kiyana kiyana eka tharum kara ganna oni , atheetha , anagatha , warthamana gana katha karanna.
eka mohothakadi chiththa weethi koti lakshayak withara yanawa.
enam api me katha karana warthamana mohothai me wage. chiththa weethi wishala ganaka ekathuwak.

dan api katha kala atheetha, anagatha, warthamana dana dana ganna puluwan hithata kiyala.
ayathana 5ta eka dana ganna ba kiyala.
ehenam sitha gana balanna oni.
sitha kiyanne mokadda chiththa+chithasika godaka ekathuwak.
sitha hasireema sidu wenne chiththa niyamayata anuwa.
chiththa niyamaya mathakada ? eka mohothaka eka sithak pamanai athi wenna puluwan, athiwana mohothema nirudda wenawa
chiththaya pawathinawa nam chithasika pawathinawa..

ehenam api pancha indriyan saha sitha thula athi wena chiththa weethi gana thawa poddak idiriyata balanna oni

giya sare katha karamu chiththa vithi padame danuma apita tikak ada oni.
e hinda liya gena yamu.

pancha indriyan pramuka chiththa vithi gana api igena gaththa.

(atheetha bawanga -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda -> panchadiwaaraa warjjana sitha ->sotha wynanaya  -> sampatijjana sitha ->
santheerana sitha -> woththapana -> jawan 7 -> thadarambana 2 -> bawanga)(marena mohothe tiyena awasan bawangaya thamai chuthi sitha)

api e chiththa veethi walata kiyana pancha idawarika chiththa weethi kiyala.  

mano idwarika chiththa weethi , me widhata nevi pawathinne.


mano idwarika chiththa weethi warga dekak tiyenawa.
1)chiththakshana 17 pawathina wibutharambana 5k saha awibootharambana 2k lesa chiththa weethi kadanna puluwan.
2)chiththakshana 17 nathi widihata gaththahama wibutharambana 1k saha awibootharambana 1k

wibutharambana(thadarambana 2k tiyenawa )pawathinawa nam 
awibootharambana 1k ( thadarambana na) (methana atheetha bawanga kiyala katha karanne na.)

chiththakshana 17 pawathina chiththa weethi wibutharambana 5k saha awibootharambana 2k kadanna puluwan
chiththakshana 17 nathi chiththa weethi wibutharambana 1k saha awibootharambana 1k

17 tiyena eka balamu

1) wibutharambana chiththa weethi

(atheetha bawanga -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 4k)
(atheetha bawanga 2k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 3k)
(atheetha bawanga 3k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 2k)
(atheetha bawanga 4k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 1k)
(atheetha bawanga 5k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 0k)

rooparambanaya , manoidwaraye gatenna kalin iwathwa giya chiththakshana gana thamai me atheetha bawanga walin pennuwe.
 sith walata aramunu wena roopaye pawathina kalaya thadarambana 2k ta passe tiyena bawanga sitha walin penwanawa.


chiththakshana 17 athi wibutharambana chiththa wethi 5k gana thamai api katha kale.
ehema naththam.
chiththakshana 17 athi warthamaana roopayak aramunu kota athiwana wibutharambana chiththa weethi 5 gana thamai api katha kale.

2) chiththakshana 17 athi awiboothaarambana chiththa weethi

 mewa dekak tiyenawa.
 1) atheetha bawanga 5kata wadiyen wena eka
 (atheetha bawanga 6k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 1k -> bawanga 0k) 
 
 chiththa niyamata anuwa minimum thadarambana sith 2k awama pawathinna oni , methana ehema tiyenna ba e nisa thadarambanaya hata ganne na, e nisa jawan 7k oasse bawanga 1k thamai hata ganne.
 
 (atheetha bawanga 7k -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda ->mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k -> thadarambana 0k -> bawanga 0k)
 meka jawan 7n iwarai.
 
 me dekema thadarambana sith nathi handa , api awibootharambana chiththa withi kiyala kiyanawa.


mechchara wela katha kale chiththakshana 17 tiyena ewa ne.

elagata thawa tiyenawa 
chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi ewa.

chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi wibutharambana 1k
chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi awibutharambana 1k
meken 
 chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi wibutharambana weethiya balamu
 
 bawanga sitha -> bawanga  chalana-> bawanga upchcheda  -> mano idwaaranaa warjjana sitha -> jawan 7k ->
thadarambana 2k -> bawanga 1k. (okkoma tiyenne 14)
 
 poddak balamu monawada me chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi wibutharambana walata examples kiyala
 ex: 
 1)thun kalayaka athi kamaa wachara chiththa chithasika yo ( eka wara eka kalayak, thunkalayen aramunu wena ewa)
 2)wynnappthi roopa deka ( kaya wynnapthi , wachi wynnapthi) ( mewatath 17k na)
 3)lakshana roopa 4. (upachaya,santhathi,jarathaa, anichchathaa)(onima roopayaka tiyena lakshana 4, ipadenwa,pawathinawa,jarwata path wenawa , nathi wenawa)
 4)atheetha,anagatha witharak tiyena chiththakshana 17 pawathina roopa 22 tiyenawa.
  
menna me 4 yam kisi ekak mano iwarayata hamuweemen.(aramunu weemen)
hamawitama athi wanne chiththakshana 17 ayusha nathi wibutharambana chittha weethiyak
( roopaye ayusha 14 enam 17k nathi)


meeta amatharawa chiththakshana 17 nathi awibootharabana chiththa withikuth tiyenawa.

ekata aramunu wenawa.
atheetha,anagatha,warthamana lesa ganna sith 89,chithasika 52, wynpthi roopa 2, lakshana roopa 4

atheetha anagatha pamanak pawathina roopa 22 pawathinawa. anna e roopa aramunu wenneth, chiththakshana 17 nathi awibootharabana chiththa withiyenma thamai.

e wagema 
eta amathara lesa 
kaala wimuktha nirwanaya 
praknapthi 
kiyana dekath aramunu wenneth awibootharabana chiththa withi widihatama thamai.

(methanath thadarambana na)
bawanga -> chalana -> uppachcheda -> mano idwaraa wajjana sitha -> jawan 7 -> bawanga 1k (methana 12k pawathinawa 17 na)

mechchara wela api chiththakshana 17 athi saha nathi chiththa withi 2k igena gaththa.
eka api categorise kala,
wibootharambana saha awibootharambana lesa.

chiththakshana 17 nathi awibotharambana chiththa vithi walata 
chiththakshana17 nathi wibotharambana chiththa vithi walata wada dekak gochara wenawa / aramunu wenawa
nirwanayai 
praknapthi

me withi deken wibotharambana chiththa withiyata aramunu madi wenne thadarambanaya pawathina nisa.
thadarambanaya dubala sithak. (duwala duwala, nawathinna hadanakota tiyana step eka wage)
eyata kamawachara dharma pamanai aramunu karanna.
kamawachara dharma kiyala kiyanne kama sith 54 ewata yedena chithasikayan (52n tikak), roopa (28n ekak).
enam
thadarambana athi hama chiththa withiyakama ,
kamawachara dharma hara anek ewa aramunu wiya nohakie.

chiththakshana 17 nathi awibotharambana chiththa vithi walata ,
pawathina jawan sitha walata , kamawachara dharma saha nirwanayai , praknapthi aramunu karanna puluwan.

methana api thama dyana gana katha karala na.

dan dyana kiyana ewa ase hadenna puluwan da ? ba 
ewa manase witharai. enam manoidwaraye pamanai.

e nisa manoidwara chiththawithi warga dekakata benawa.
1) kaama jawana widi (kama loko sith)
2) arpanaa jawana widi (roopa aroopa sith (mahaggatha sith), lokoththara jawan sith)

api katha karapu roopa 28n,(atheetha,warthamana, anagatha lesa )
chiththakshana 17k bagin ayusha tiyena roopa 22 tiyenawa. (atheetha,warthamana, anagatha lesa )
anek roopa 6ta echchara ayusha na. (atheetha,warthamana, anagatha lesa )

me roopa set eken, 
chiththakshana 17k bagin ayusha tiyena, wathamana roopa awasthawa aramunu kara ganne.
wibootharambana 5n saha awibootharambana 2 ken. (chiththa weethi 7kin)
chiththakshana 17k bagin ayusha tiyena, atheetha saha anagatha awastha aramunu karanne,
wibootharambana 1k saha awibootharambana 1 ken. (chiththa weethi 2kin)

me widihata kamawachara jawana manoidwarana chiththa weethi 9k atha.(7+2)

aramuna kiyanne ekak, chiththa withiya kiyanne thawa ekak.
aramuna ayusha pennanne chiththakshana walin.
chiththakshana 17k tiyena aramunuth tiyenawa , 17k nathi ewath tiyenawa.
chiththa withi tiyenwa , panchaidwarika saha mano idawarika kiyala.
panchaidwarika chiththa weethi types, 
athi mahantharambana chiththa weethi 1 (atheetha bawanga 1i).(roopaye ayusha mulumaninma gewila)
mahantharambana chiththa weethi 2i (atheetha bawanga 2k ho 3k tiyena awasthawa) 
pariththa rambana chiththa weethi 6i(atheetha bawanga 4k,5k,6k,7k,8k,9k  tiyena awasthawa) 
athi pariththarambana chiththa weethi 6i (atheetha bawanga 10,11,12,13,14,15k tiyena) ()

whidihata eka idwarayatakata 15k pawathinawa.
idwara 5ta 75k.


roopayak chakku prasadaye gatee, chakshu idwara weethiyak athi wu pamanin.
ohuta mokak hari dakka kiyana daneema athi wenne na.
eka wipaka awasthawa witharai.
daneema athi weemata, me weethiyen pasu.
mano idwara weethi gananak wiya yuthui.
chakku prasadaye gatune paata pamanai. (pahaya pamanai)
pachnda iwara withi walata amatharawa 
e withi walin gath aramuna sambandayen
athiwana manoidwara weethi walata
anubandaka mano idwara withiya yai kiyala ( e anuwa badunu kiyana adahata, ekama aramuna pawathinne)
anu bandaka mano idwara lesa athi wanneth chiththakshana 17k nathi wibutharambana /awibootharambana chiththa withi 

pancha idwara withiyak nirudda unahama , eka nisa  hata gaththu atheetha roopaya aramunu karamin
mano idwarika weethiyak athi wenawa.(anubandaka kiyala)(hadaya / sanyyawa )
eetapasu e roopayata kiyana nama aramunu karana mano idwarika weethiyak athi wenawa.
eeta passe eka niruddawu pasu
e namin   hadunwana deya mokadda kiyala , e wachanaye arthaya ganna thawath mano idawarika chiththa weethiyak wenwa.

dan therenawa , mama asawal de ditimu kiyana sobawaya athi wanne ,
menna me 3n weni mano idwaraya athi weemen passe.

enam pancha idawaria wethi 1i, mano idawarika chiththa weethi 3k kin anathuruwa , mama dakka kiyala haduna ganeema athi wenawa. 

ex:
shabdayak kane gatunahama mulinma 
shotha wynanaya pramuka chiththa weethiyak hata gannawa.
ee pase atheetha wu shabdaya nawatha ganna manoidwara chiththa weethiyak athi wenawa
eka nirudda unata passe , eke namaya arthya mathu kara ganna thawa chiththa weethiyak hata gannawa

daneema kiyana eka pudgalata athi wenne 3 weni mano idawarika weethiya athi weemen passe.

me anuwa jawan sith 35ka prathipalayak thamai me combination eka athule tiyenne.
pancha idawarika chiththa weethiyen jawan sith 7k enawa . (7k)
anubandaka chiththa weethi walin ekakin 7 gane 3k enawa. (21k)

eelaga chiththa withiyen me dakka kiyana ahuna ganeema hambela. (7k++21k+7k) - total of jawan sith 35 oni minimum lesa haduna ganna.

 ex:
ahata roopayak penena kota,
mulin pancharwarika chiththa weethiyak yanwa.
ethkota athiwana bawa prakatai.
namuth eeta passe athi wana mano idwarika chiththa aprakatai. eka hinda apita ewa therenne na.
atheetha aramuna eka gaththa kiyana eka wath apita therenne na.

ahen roopaya danagannawa kiyanakota , panchaidwarika chiththa withi 1kui, manoidawarika chiththa withi 4k  thulin 
thamai api dana ganne.

api mechchara wela katha kale warthamana roopa haduna ganna widiha.

ex:
ruwanwali saya lagata giyahama. chakku iwara widiyak athi wena.
gedarata giyahama dakka ruwanwali saya sihi una.
sihi wunu eka mano idwarikai.
kalin dakka ruwanwali saya sihi karana manoidawarika roopayak athi una.
kalin dakka ruwanwali saya chakku idawayen hata aran nirudda wela iwarai.
ewa dan na.
dakka ruwanwali saya sihi kirima nisa hata ganna mano idarika chiththa withiyata arumu wenne 
anthimata dakapu roopayak.
enam dan nathi atheetha roopa samuhayak.
enam 
atheetha roopa aramunu karana , mano idwara vithi dekak tibba mathakada chithakshana 17 nathi.
enema me athi wechchara mano idwara roopaya anna e deken ekak.


ex:
dan oya gedara innawa.
oyata ahata penne nathi ruwan wali saya dihata harila wadinawa.
dan me wadinne kalin dakka ruwan wali saya nevi.
dan wadinne , wadina mohothe manomaya washayen pawathina  ruwanwali sayata.
chiththakshana 17 pawathina warthamana roopa asuru karagena kiyala eka hadenne (wibootharambana saha awibootharambana chiththa weethi 7k) walin.
e nisa api gedara idala ruwan wali saya wadinakota 
ruwan wali saya washayen api salakana warthamana roopayama witharai.
ruwanwali maha saaya kiyana 
praknapthiya mano idwarayata yomu weemen. chiththakshana 17k nathi praknapthiya aramunu karana
mano idwarika chiththa withi thamai athi wenne.

ex:   
 ruwanwali saya dutu bawa mathak wenwa.
 chukku idwara kiyana weethiya aramunu karana mano idawara weethiyak thamai ethna tiyenne.
 nikan sihi karnawa kiwwoth eka thawa ekak
 ethenadi wenne 
 mano idara weethiyak athi wenwa warthamana roopayak ekka.

ex: ruwanwali saya dakeema nisa athi wechcha prithiya mathak wenawa nam
prithi chithasikaya aramunu kara gath mano idawara weediyak.

ex: kawru kambul paharak gahapu ekak mathak karanawa nam
ethana athi wenne wedana chithasikayak aramunu karana mano idawara weediyak.

-------------------------Mathakaya saha maranaya ---------

ada session eka lokoththara nirwana margayata echcharamawadagath kamak na, namuth loka sobawaya aduna ganna oni handa 
thamai katha karanne. 

giya sare kalaya gana katha karapu eka 
kohomada mata sambanda wenne kohomada kiyana eka poddak balamu?

sitha athiwana mohothemai chaithasika athi wanne (sathara samprayoga lakshana)
ethna kalayak na. pera pasu novi athi wana sobawayak tiyenne.

api katha karapu atheetha roopaya katha karanne warthamanayata sapekshawa.
e mohothe athi wana mano idawaraya katha kale sankalpamaya mamathwayak thulin.
naththam lokaya thula wachana bawithayen katha karanakota ( kaya wynpthi, wachi wynpthi) sidu wenakoa mamek inna bawa hagenawa , mata mano idawarayen chiththa weethi athi wenawa. e nisa mama thula kalaya pawathinawa.
 e nisa niwanata pera hamuwana siyaluma de akalika nevi, enam lokaya thulai.
lokaya thula nam mamek pawathi, enam thun kalaya pawathi.

e nisa praknapthi thulin hata gaththu siyalla pawathinne sitha thulai, e praknapthi gana katha karathdi
ewa bahira tiyenawa kiyala hithenawa.
menna me hitheema nisa kala ha awakashaya pawathinawa.
kalaya saha awakashaya kiwwath e dekath praknapthima thamai.
siyalu praknapthi pawathinna nam
sankalpamaya mamek pawathiya yuthui. mama pawathina thek kalaya saha awakashaya pawathie.
e nisa lokaya thula mama athi kalhi mamata sapekshawa siddeen api kalaya saha awakashaya thulin wigraha kara gannawa.

ex:
town ekata yanawa.
town eka praknapthiya sithuwillak
mata bahirin town eka pawathi yai sitheema nisa 
mama saha town eka athara awakaashayak pawathina bawa hithanawa.
mata eliye town eka tiyenawa bawa hithapu nisa ethanata yanna , kalayak awasha bawa hithenawa.
town eka saha mama , nithya wuu nisa kalaya saha awakashaya nithya lesa gannawa.
lokaya thimanawa baluwoth praknapthi dekak athara kalaya saha awakashaya pawathinawa.
lokaya thula eka sathyak. mewa sammuthi sathya lesa hadunwanawa.
e nisa praknapthi dekak gana katha karanakota kalayen ho awakashayen sambanda kara gannawa.
lokoththara sathya thula dee , kalaya saha awakashaya thawath ekak mulawak praknapthiyak pamanai.

ex:
anun kiyapu de ahenawa 
anun wisin prashna ahanawa , mama kalpana karanawa
shareera wedanak denenawa
hathurek ehema naththam mithurak hambenawa 

mewa okkoma mano idawarika  chiththa weethi athi wenna puluwan hethu.

ex:
gaantarayak warak gasu kalhi 
maha hadak athi wela 
eta passe gaseemak nathiwa , mulin athi wu handa 
karamayen sihin wemin
naada paramparawak athi wenawa.

e wage chakku idawara weediya aramba wela awasan unata
e roopalambanaya nisa mano idawara weethi dasas ganan athi wenna puluwan.
pas doren ganna aramunu nisa mano idwarika chiththa weethi hugak hata ganna puluwan.
 

pas doren gaththu roopaya nisa athi wena dahas ganan chiththa withi, parana eka wage kiyala hithenne ai?

pas doren ganna aramunu nisa mano idwarika chiththa weethiya nirudda unata passe
mano idwarika chiththa weethi godak thamai athi wenne.
shabdaalambanaya aramunu kara ganna nisa thamai parana eka wage kiyala hithenne.

meka tikak igena ganna apita theory tikak oni e tika poddak balala imu
---
roopa  jathi 4 ( chiththaja ,karma, uthuja, aharaja)
hardaya roopayai, indriya roopa tikai - karamayen withrai hataganne
wynpthi roopa - sithin hata ganna ewa
shabda roopaya - chiththa , irithu dekenma hata gannawa ( katha karanakota hithin, hulan hamathdi irithu)
wikaara roopa  - lahutha,mrudutha , kammanyatha ( iruthuwai, chiththa, ahara) 
 
 ex: 
 hitha aul unahama , kriyathmaka karanna puluwan sudusu mattamakata na 
 car eke ac eka noda yathdi danena apahasuwa - lahutha , mrudutha , kammanyatha roopaw walata balapawa parisara iruwa
 ekathakota ac eka dammoth roopa thuna hoda mattame tiyenawa.
 e roopa kalapa hoda naththam, shareeraye bara gathiya, kammali sobawaya, kriya kirimata hoda nathi thathwayak enawa.
 
shuddashtaka saha akasa dathuwa me prathya 4ma nisa hata gannawa
kisima prathyakin hata noganna roopath tiyenawa. (lakshana roopa 4 wage)
 mewa roopayaka lakshana mathayak. ( upachaya ,santhathi, jaratha, anichchatha)
 
methana santhathiya kiyala katha karanne roopa paramparawa pawathwagena yama.
roopaye kuda chithakshana 51n, 49kma aithi jaratha lakshanayata.
anith thunatama aithi eka eka. (upachaya saha santhathiya kiyanne upadeemata thamai, chiththakshana 17passe upadina ewa santhathi), upachaya kiyanne chiththanashana 17 adu awasthawe hata ganeema.
full 17k giyata passe athi wana eka santhathi.

upachaya,jaratha,anichchatha thamai wenne eka wage roopa paramparawak pawatheema santhathiyai.

jeewitha indriya kiyanne - thama ha bandee upadina roopayan param para washayen yam kalayak pawathina widihata
araksha karana / jeewath karawana indriyata api kiyanawa jeewitha indriya kiyala.

jeewitha indriya hama tissema karmaja roopa thamai pawathwa gena yanna hadanne. mokada ewa prathisandi sithen hata aran
prathisandi sitha dan nirudda wela. eeta passe ithuru wena bawanga tika pawathwagena yanne.
me jeewitha indriyen.
e nisa karamaja roopa walata thamai jeewitha indriya wadagath wenne.
anith thune di roopaya palanaya karanne amuthu deyak oni na
(irthuwai, aharayai, chiththayai) pawathina nisa ewata hakiyawa tiyenawa pawathinna.

karmaja roopayak hata ganne , e awasthawe nathi atheethaye athi una karmaja rooyakin neda ?
e nisa ewa araksha karanna thawa ekak tiyenna oni, ekathamai jeewitha indriya

ex:
kenek upadithdi, karmaja roopayak hadenawa
e hadena prathi sandi sitha , ethanama nirudda wenwa
karamayenma athi una roopayak thamai me jeewitha indriya.
jeewitha indriya anubawayen roopa paramparawa. warsha siya ganan , dahas ganan mululle
nosidi pawathie.
me roopa paramparawa uga kalayak pawathwanna, shakthimath karanna ooja roopaya upakari wenawa
ojaa roopaya hama aharayakama pawathinawa.
namuth ojaawen shareeraya rakenne
sudusu aharaya gaththoth pamanai.
ganna aharaya matha ojaawa wenas wenawa.
------
 
dan question eka aye balamu,
pas doren gaththu roopaya nisa athi wena dahas ganan chiththa withi, parana eka wage kiyala hithenne ai?

atheetha warthamana anagatha thunama ganna puluwan mano idwarayata.
panacha idwara chiththa weethiyakin hata gath roopaya chiththakshana 17 passe iwarai. warthamanaye pamanai pawathune.
e iwara wechcha ewa atheetha roopa kiyala kiyanawa.
e atheetha roopa pancha indriyen nawatha ganna ba.
namuth manasata me hakiyawa tiyenawa.
enam
api katha kala
pancha idwara 1ta passe mano idawara 4k athi wenawa kiyala .
anthima ekata kiyanawa wishesha namak ( karma sadaka chiththa weethiya kiyla)
meken sithata pauluwan 
aramunata upakari uu mano idawarika chiththa weethi nawatha athi karanna puluwan.
(chiththakshana 17 nathi wibutha saha awibootharambana kiwwe mewata)

ex:
ruwan wali saya dakapu mohothe- pancha idawara chiththa weethiya saha anubandana mano diwara weethi 3 saha karma sadaka chiththa weethiya.
ruwan wali saya mathak karana mohothe - chakku parasadaye gateemak na , pancha iwdarika chiththa weethi na
api dutu ruwan wali saha dan sihi wenawa. - methana mano iwarika chiththa weethiyata aramunu wenne 
chithakshana 17 nathi atheetha roopa aramunu karana mano idwara withi deken ekak.

pera athi wu mano idawarika chiththa weethi nawatha athi kirime hakiyawa , mano idawarayata pawathinawa.
e nisa thamai atheetha gadayan haduna ganeem karaganna puluwan.
mekata thamai sihi weema, ehema naththam mathakaya kiyala api kiyanne.

meka mano idaraye hakiyawak. namuth eya isthirayen pawathina deyak nevi.
gabada kirimak na. e mohothe athi kirime hariyawak thamai pawathinne.
sithata kalpa 91k thorathuru ganna puluwan kiyala sadahan karala tiyenawa.
sihi kirime hakiyawa diunu karanna puluwan.
eya itha hodin wardanaya kara wita , pera wisu kanda piliwela sihi karanna puluwan.
meke uparima awasthawa , pubbe niwasaa nusmathi nyaanaya lesa hadunawanawa.

ex:
gedara idala ruwan wali saya paththata harila wadinawa
dan wadinne oya atheethaye dakka ekak da ? na
dan wadinne dutu ruwan wali saya nevi.
dan wadinne me welawa ethana athi kiyala hithena warthamana roopayata.
ekata chiththakshana 17k athi wibootharambana ho awibootharambana 7n ekak.
e 7 hata ganna sobawaya matha, oyata eka hodatama mathakai, ho yanthamanata mathakai kiyana sobawya mathu wenawa.

ex:
ruwan wali maha saya kiyana nama ahenawa.
me praknapthiya mathak wenawa.
ethkota wenne chiththakshana 17 nathi e praknapthiya aramunu karana
mano idawrika weethi 2ken ekak hata gannawa . (mathaka nam nirwanayai, pranapthiyai aramunu wenne awibootharambana ekata e nisa methana hata ganna awibootharambana weethiya)

ex:
ruwan wali saya dutu bawa mathak wenawa.
ethkota dutu bawai sihi wenne, enam pancha idarika chiththa weethiyak athi una bawa. enam chakku idwaara chiththa weethiya ho chakku wynyanaya wennath puluwan.
 chakku idwaara chiththa weethiya kiwwath 
 chakku wynanaya kiwwath ewa sith. praknaypthi nevei.
 enam sitha aramunu karagath mano idawarika chiththa weethi
 meka wibootharambana weethiyak chaththakshana 17 nathi ( 17 nathi deken anek eka)
 
 e nisa ruwan wali saya sihi weema saha
 ruwan wali saha dutu bawa sihi weema akara dekak.
 e akara dekedi athi wena weethi deka dekak.
 
 
ex:
e wagema thamai
prithi chithasikaya athi weema saha prithi chithasiyaka sihi weema me wagema thamai.
wedana chaithasikayath me wagemai.
mewa praknapthi newei, ehenam chiththakshana 17 nathi wibootharambana chiththa weethiyak thamai athi wenne.

adaraya, kopaya, karunawa , mythreeya , irisiyawa, okkoma chithasika
enam chithasika aramunu karana mano idawarika weethi walin thamai ewa enne.


sihi weema sah,a sihi unu bawa seihi weema wadi karaganna nam
pancha idarika chiththa weethi athi wana bawa adu kara ganna oni.
ethkota mano idarika chiththa weethi 
athi wenna puluwan chakku wynnanaya ho mano idaraka chiththa weethi aramunu karala witharai.
menna me hakiyawa wardanaya kara ganeemen
praknpthi saha nirwanaya awaboda karanna puluwan chiththakshana 17 nathi 
awoobootharambana chiththa withi hada ganna puluwan.
meya marga nayanayai.
meya bawitha mahuleekatha wa thulin , nirwanaya waboboda kara ganna puluwan.

enam praknapthi ikmawa yana sobawaya marga nyanayen ismathu karai.


dan api prathi sandi mohotha gana poddak balamu.

sitha hama witama athi wela nathi wenawa,
meken prathi sandiyata pasuwa athi wana sith okkoma bawanga sith
jeewitha awasanayedi athi wena bawanga sithata api namak denawa chuthi sitha kiyala.
marana sanna mohothedi athi wana chithta withiya ( chuthiyata pera athiwana awasana chiththa weethiya)
maranasanna chiththa weethiya kiyala.
e wage athi wana maranasanna chiththa weethi types 24k tiyenawa .
1 ayathanayakata 4 bagin.

(manussa sithaka)prathi sandi mohothe roopa dasaka kalapa 3k athi wenawa.
1) kaaya dasaka ( shuddashakayai + jeewitha indriyai + prasada roopayai)
2) bawa dasaka ( shuddashakayai + jeewitha indriyai + isthi/purusha roopayai)(meka nathuwath athi wena awastha tiyenawa, eka thamai napunsaka)
3) wasthu dasaka ( shuddashakayai + jeewitha indriyai + hardaya wasthu roopayai)

purna manussayek gana katha karathdi
30he set ekak , kalapa thunak. athi wenne.

sithaka kuda chiththakshana 3k pawathinawa
uthpada , thithi, banga kiyala thunak
eken 
uthpada iskanayata thamai me kalaapa thuna awe.
sama ikshanayak pasama aluthen 3 gane enawa.
uthpada awasthawe dashaka kalapa 3
titi awasthawe dashaka kalapa 3
banga awasthawe dashaka kalapa 3

ethkota banga wethdi 9k hata aran.

ethakota prathisandi sitha iwara wethdi kalapa 9k pawathuna.
eka iwara unu gaman,
palamu bawangaya athi wenawa.
palamu bawangaya.uthapada wethdi 12
palamu bawangaya.titi wethdi 15
palamu bawangaya.banga wethdi 18 
 
chiththakshana 17 eehema naththam , kuda chithakshana 51 thula , (roopa kalapa 153 hata gannawa. 3x50 + 1x3)
roopyaka ayusha, kuda chiththakshana 51, naththam roopa kalapa 153.

maw kusata , pilisida gena sathi 11kin enam dina 77kin (7dina x 11sathi), thawa roopa kalapa 4k ekathu wenawa
chakku dasaka
sotha dasaka
gana dasaka 
jiwha dasaka

prathi sandi sitha thula me dasaka kalapa 4 tibbe na
ewa pasuwa athi unu dasaka kalapa. ( mekata kiyana pravurthi kalaye pahala weemak kiyala)

enam 77wana dinaye sita athiwana bawangaye, palapa 3 nevi 7 bagin athiwenawa.
alapa ayusha tiyena sathwayo maw kula thula echchara kal inne na.
deerga ayusha tiyena sathwayo wadi kalayak wesenawa.

alpa ayusha tiynea sathwayange dina 77 yanna pera me 4 dashakayan pahala wenawa.
manusasyakuta thamai dina 77 kathawak kiwwe.

me widaya 77 dinayen passe. uthpada 7, titi 7, bangayedi 7
dina 77n passe idan , chithakshana 17 thula kuda chithakshana 51 x7 = roopa kalapa 357. athi wenawa.
 uthpada 7 nathi wethdi , titi 7 upadinawa
 eka nathi wethdi banga 7 upadinawa
 roopa kalapa 357 digatama pawathinawa.
 
 ehenam manussayek marena kam pawathinne roopa kalapa 357 pamani.
mewa karmaja roopa.
methanadi , chiththaja, uthuja ho aharaja gana katha kale na.


palamu sithe chiththakshana 17, palamu eka, prathisandiya (1)
ithiri ewa bawanga ( 16)
awasaana bawanga sithe bangakshanaya di - kalapa 153 athi wela. ( mul dawas 77 yanakan)

prathisandiya (1)
passe ena ithiri ewa bawanga ( 16) wala palamu sithe bawanga uthpadaye di pamanak, chiththaja roopa kalapayak upadinawa
enam chiththaja roopye ayusha maha chiththakshanayak pamanai.
karmaja roopa hama kuda chiththakshanayakama pahala una 
chuththaja roopa pahala une bawangayage uthpada kuda chitthakshanaye pamanai.
ehi ayusha kuda thuthakshana 3 iwarawethdi iwarai.

enam chiththaja roopa kalapa upadinne prathisandiye di nova, eeta anathurawa athi wana palamu bawangaye sitai.

ewagema 
hama titi awasthawakadeema uthuja kalapa upadinawa. prathi sandi sitheth  titi awasthwe uthuja roopa kalapa pawathinawa.
habai chiththaja roopa prathisandiye na.

mother anubawa karana araha wala tiyena ojaa roopaya maw kusa sitina ladaruwata 
hamuwenwa aharaja roopa widihata.

-----
majjima nikaye tiyenawa seeha naada suthraya, balanna
lichchawee raja daruwaku mahana wela siyuru ariya.
eyage hithata ena sankalpayak ma thamai kiyanne 
logically eka kiyanna puluwan hakiyawa tiyenawa
ekath hithaluwak witharai.

kiyala dos kiya kiya giyaaa.

eeta passe sariyuth hamuduruwo megana ahanna hambuwela.
budunta megana pawasanawa.
ethkota pawasanawa 
bosath kale karapu bosath gaweshanaya thula soya gaththu dewal ( uppathi / maranaya gana )
budda wachanaya , mewa gana focus nokara
lokoththara sobawaya gana focus karanna oni.
------

maranasanna kalayedi,
chuthi sitha kiyanne anthima kuda chiththakshanaya
chuthi sitha sidda wenna kalin chiththakshana 17 gana hithuwoth.
e 17, palamu
e sithe tithi ikshanaye idala karmaja roopa ipadeema nawathinawa.
pera sith wala upan siyalu karamaja roopa chuthi sithe hataganeemata pera niroda wela iwarai.
e nisa chuthi sitha thula karamaja roopa na.
karamaja roopa ipadeema nawatheemen pasu,chiththakshana 17 yanwa , anthima chuthi sitha
karmaja roopayak 7n, pawathwagena yame hakiyawa tibunu wasthu roopaya. ( hardaya roopaya saha jeewitha indriya )
nathi weemen, 
chuthi sithen pasu shareeraye sith upadinna ba.
harda roopaya nathi nisa chiththaja roopath na
jeewitha indriya nathi handa aharaja roopath na.
enam karmaja, chiththaja , aharaja roopa ipadeemak na
namuth uthuja roopa parampawa pamanak pawathinawa.
me awasthawata api mala miniya kiyala kiyanawa.
methana uthuja roopa aulthen hadenna ba, enisa hadunu tika winasa wenakan.
body eka pawathinawa.
bonesuth tika kalayak yathdi wiparinama wela yanawa 

ahara warga 4k tiyenawa ( yamak gena enu labanawa kiyana arthya)
- wynaana ahaara  ( nama roopa)
- mano sanchethana ahara ( kusal akusal)
- isparsha ahara ( wedana, sanyya, chethana)
- kabalinka ahara ( roopa kalapa - oja roopaya)(jiwitha indriya tiyena kota thamai meka ganna puluwan)

api bath, paan kawpi walata kabalinka ahara kiyala hithuwata 
shareerayata ekathu wena kota eka ekathu wenne ojaa roopak widihata.
eka jeewitha indriya pawathinawa nam pamanai ojaa roopayak bawata path kara gatha hakke. ( pawatheemata awasha shakthik lesa)
e nisa me ojaa roopaya ta path karaganeeme hakiyawa nathi una wita 
enam marunu shareerayata kabalinka ahara wala prayojanayak na.

me widihata ta 
summarize karapuwahama 

roopa kalapa 21 pawathinawa.

karamaja kalapa 9 ( prasada kalapa 5 (chukku dasakaya...etc), isthri kalapa 1, purusha kalapaya 1,wasthu dashaka kalapa 1,jeewitha roopaya 1) ( me anthima ekata api kiyanawa jeewitha nawaka kalapaya kiyala (shuddashakaya+jeewitha roopya))

asanyya thalaya pawathinne menna me jeewitha nawakaya pamanai. awanibboga roopa 8i + jeewitha roopayai.

chiththaja kalapa 6k tiyenawa.

suddashtaka kalapaya (awanipboga 8 witharai)
kaya wynyapthi nawaka kalapaya (suddashtakaya + kaya wynyapthi )
wachi wynapthi dashaka kalapaya (suddashtakaya + wachi wynyapthi + shabda roopaya)
eka dashaka kalapa ( 11k, lahutha/mutha/kammanyatha 3i + suddashtakaya)
dwa dashaka kalapa ( eka dashaka kalapa + kaaya wynapthi)
therasaka dashaka kalapa (eka dashaka kalapa + wachi wynappthi + shabda roopaya)

uthuja kalapa 4k

suddashtakaya
shabda nawaka kalapaya  (shuddashakaya+shabdaya) 
eka dashaka kalapa ( 11k, lahutha/mutha/kammanyatha 3i + suddashtakaya) 
dwa dashaka kalapa ( eka dashaka kalapa + shabdaya)

aharaja kalapa 2k tiyenawa

suddashtakaya
eka dashaka kalapa ( 11k, lahutha/mutha/kammanyatha 3i + suddashtakaya)---> eka dashaka kalapa, ehenam chiththaja saha uthuja,aharaja thunama nisa athi wenawa.

me katha karapu roopa kalapa 21 uthuja kalapa 4n 
palamu deka , (suddashtakaya, shabda nawaka kalapaya )
sathwa shareerayen pita tiyenna puluwan.
ithuru 19 shareerayan thula misak pita nove.

ex:
ira gaththahama
eka shuddashtaka witharai, ethanata maha bootha 4i , warna prakatai.



-----------------widarshanawa thulin pancha upadana iskandaye anithya praktically baleema ---------11/07/2007


dharmaya wenath konayakin balanne dharmaya hodata haduna ganeema sanda.

api mulin tharaha gana katha karamu.

tharaha / gateema thula sathutak tiyenawada ?
ex:
principle kenek school ekata lamaiwa hasurawanna , tharaha mode ekak gannawa.
ethkota palanaya kara ganna lesie. 
ehema palanaya karagena lamai hoda unahama , 
lamai inna thana balala, sathutak /ashwadayak athi kara gannawa 
mama saren lamai hadapu handa thamai , ada hodin inne kiyala.

enam gateeme saha aleeme sathuta dakinawa.
sansaraya purama , windanayak/sathutak tiyena nisa thamai lokaye pawathmak tiyenanne.


gatena eka dukak wenna kochchara kalayak yai da ?
mona awasthawe da duka lesa haduna ganne ?

ex:
gedara kunu tiyena bawa haduna gaththahama athu ganawa.
kunu penna naththam athu ganne na.
habai duwili kiyanneth kunu, ethkota kochcharak kunu ekathu unahamada athu ganna / action ekak ganna hithenne ?

allapu gedara minihek beela awith , badu polawe gahanawa, sadda karanawa.
apita hithenawa , maranayak unath wenna puluwan me widihata giyoth kiyala.
eeta passe hithanawa, ape gedara nam ehema na kiyala podi sathutak upaddawa gannawa.
ehema karala , allapu gedara kerehi anukampawak athi kara gannawa.

e unata api danne na ape hithath gatila thamai, me anukampawa pennanne kiyala ?
ara kunu goda karadarayak uneth , me wage hithe gateemakata passe.

ape hithe hata gaththu sium gateema prakata na, ehema une , athiwechcha anukampawa namathi wanchanika dharmayen 
me gateema awaranaya unu nisai.

ai api anukampawata wanchanika dharmayak kiwwe ?

ekaparata allapugedarin bana gannawa ahunahama,
mulinma hithenne , apoo onna adatha patan aran.
katin nokiwwata hithen gatila , eeta passe lokuwata e gedara aya gana anukampawen katha karanawa.
anukampawen , me hithe athi wechcha gateema wahagena.
e nisa api apita marks deemak kara gena. ( api hodai, e nisa apita palleha ayata anukampawa lak karala)

e nisa anukampawa thulin, ape hithe gateemen nidahas wenna ba.
e hinda thamai ekata wanchanika dharmayak kiyanne.

thawa ex:

issara tharam, mata dan loku loku asawan dan na. issara wage winoda wenna 
badu goda gaha ganna , 
me hama thanama , api katha karanne issaraha saha dan kiyala sapeksha sobawayakin.
enam dan sobawaya , issara sobawaya tharam prakata na.
e hinda api kiyanawa mata issara tharam tharaha yanne na kiyala.

athi wana sobawaya nathi wela na, athi unu de aduwak lesin dakala sathutu wenawa.

aleemai gateemai kiyana ewa kriyathmaka wana sobawaya danne nathi handa 
sapekshawa aduwak diha balala duru wenawa kiyala hithanwa.
namuth ehema duru wela na.

apita lakunu deema thula pawathinnema sakkaya dittiyai. 
budu wadan pela gasenne sakka dittiya sampurnayen duru karanna mai.

ehenam budda wachanayama soya yanawa nam,
sama witama hamu wena dharamaya sakkaya dittiya duru wenna ma thamai pawathinne.

namuth api atharinne , aleema nevi alena dewal.
habai e alena de thula mai gatena de tiyenneth.
ekama dathuwakin thamai mewwa hata ganne. wen karanna ba.

mokadda me ekama dathuwa aleema gateema athi wena , hitha.
aleema saha gateema hithe athi unata , alena/gatena dewal bahiraya thula na
meka awaboda kara gaththoth, 
ese alenne gattenne nathi handa athi wana sahanaye uparima awasthawata 
api sanwara seelaya kiyala kiyanawa.

me aleema gateema wala adeenawa dakala 
sasarata baya wela daana denna unath puluwan.
me daana deeme prathipalaya hoda thanaka ipadeematai, 
mewani awastha hamu nowawa parisarayakata athi kamaththa.
enam sasarata baya wela hoda sasarak hada gannawa.

enam danayai , seelayai, budda sasanayen epitath tiyenawa.
wena agam walath me sobawaya gana katha karanawa.

ehenam api karanna oni mokadda ?

alena gatena dewal gana katha kara karala wadak na.
hithena hitha , wadakarana widiha awaboda kala yuthumai.
methana tiyena anithya bawa 
wenas wana bawa
ehema naththam
pancha upadana isknadama anithya bawa dakkoth 
alenna gatenna deyak tiyei da ?
enam 
roopa -> wedana -> sanyya -> chathana -> wynaana kiyana kriyawalima anithya bawa 
awaboda unahama 
e nisa hata ganna palaya samaga aleemai/ gateemak athi wena eka nawaththaganna puluwan.


e nisa , me anawabodayen athi wana rawateema , hari lesa dakkoth 
siyalla awaboda wenawa.

eka poddak balamu gaburin

ex:
obata mawa penawa kiyana thana.

penne mokadda ? mage roopaya.
e penena roopaya pramanawath kale kopamanakinda ?
oya dakke eka roopayak da godak da ? 
aha, as pallama, nahaya, kata, konde, nahaye sidura kiyanne roopayak
mama kiyala dakke me walin ekak da godak da ?
mama kiyala kiwwe kochchara paramanayakatada ?
aha kiyannetha roopayak , as bami kiyanne thawa ekak ?
ahi pillama thawa ekak, 
mewa eka hithakina balanna puluwan da ?
wynnanaya wenas wenna oni neda ? 
chakku wynnayen eka mohothakata aramunu wenne eka nimiththai, ( asa, nahaya, nikata ...etc)
ehenam wynnanaya wenas wenna oni.

wynnanaya wenas wenne ai ?
wedanawa wenas unu handa 
wedanawa wenas une sparshaya wenas unu nisa
enam 
wideema wenas unu hinda thamai haduna ganeema wenas une.
e hinda chathanawa wena wenawa 
dan wynyanawa wenas wenawa.

me anuwa ,
oyata mawa penawa kiwwe , 
me siddi walin koi kallada ?

methana hama nimiththak ma pancha upadana iskanayak.
athi wechcha pancha upadana iskanayan anithya une naththam
obata mawa dakinna puluwanda ?

ape hithata aramunu wana siyalla , pancha upadana iskanadayak
ehenam 
oba dakina maa da pancah upadana iskandak ma thamai.

ehenam 
api hama witama dakinne / ahenne / agrahana karanne  ,
pancha upadna iskandaye anithya sobawayamai.

enam 
 melowa thula dakina wenasa, 
 athi wennema 
 pancaha upadana iskandaye anithya sobawaya handamai.
 

ex 2:

ahenawa ahenawa kiyana sadde oyata aththatama ahenawada ?
ahena ewa godak.
methana mokada wenne ?

"a"he"na"wa" - eka eka wynaana pahala wenne 
palamu akura ahu wena wynaanayata puluwan da dewani akura allanna? ba
ehenam wynanawaya wenas wela 
anithya wela

ehenam 
ahenawa kiyana eka sakas une pancha upadana iskandaya anithya una nisai.

ahenawa kiyana wachanayak, 
api katha karanne e wachanaya nevi sansiddiya gana.
e wachanaya sansiddiya nisa panawa gaththu praknapthiyak. ( eka nisa thamai english walin ekata hearing kiyala kiyanne)

ehenam 
pancha upadana iskanaye anithya sobawaya nisama thamai.
aleema / gateema widyamana wenne.

ethkota 
sithe gathiya thamai
sapa pennala dukata adala dana eka .
eka hithata awenika gathiyak.
eka karanna puluwan pancah upadana iskanadaya anithya unu nisai.

tharaha giyath eketh aswadayak tiyenawa   
hoda balaporoththuwak deela , eke wenuwen amaruwe wattannawa duka athi karanawa.
jeewitha suwa pahasu kara ganeema sathutak kiyala pennala,
e wenuwen, awasha sama dema upaya ganna duk athi kara gannawa.
jeewitha mattama ihala da ganna , duk wideemak athi kara gannawa.

ehenam me jeewithaya namathi mage game eka, mage hithata sakas kara ganna puluwan
wenne pancha upadana iskanadaye anithya nisamai.

meka hari wela awaboda unoth , kochchara wegayen api niwila yai da ?

e nisa 
api 
roopayak athi bawa ho nathi bawa  gana katha kale na.
eka drushtiyak.
pancha upadana iskandaye anithya dakina kota 
duken nidawas wenawa kiyala.

enam budda wachanaya 
"pancha upadana iskanada dukka "

api mehchchara kal , eka eka adum hodai kiyala ada gaththa, ewa galawa galawa 
nidahas wenna baluwa.
dan kochchara salara adumak da ? aluth awruddaa aluth adumak
namuth parana ewa adina, galawana eke amaruwa danne naththam
sarala adume watinakama therenne na.
namuth podi lamayekuta unath sarala aduma ada ganna lesie.
e nisa marga pala awabodayath pahasui.

enam 
pera thalu mara mara study karapu / logics walin tharaka karapu.
tika naththam, sarala adume watinakama therenne na.

pubbetha katha punya thawaya  ( pera kala pin kala bawa / yam mattamakata paramitha purnaya kala bawa)
indriya dharma(sadda,wirya, sathi, samadi, praknaa) dharmabodayata sudusu mattamata tiyenna oni.


chanda ragaya kiyanne mokadda ? kamaththa
me kamaththata alenawa ? me aleema theeranaya wenna awidyawa matha.
awidyawa kiyanne mokadda ? danne nathi kama.
mokadda danne naththe ? apiwa rawattanawa kiyala , naththam mula karanawa kiyala danne na.
kawda meka karanne ? karna kenek na, sitha thula pawathina awidyawe sobawaya

mehema hithanna hithanna, athi wenne yoniso manasikaraya
yoniso manasikaraya kiyanne budda wachanayata ahunkan deemai.
yoniso manasikaraya athi une naththam.
awidyawa thulin upadanaya hata gannawa.

enam 
chanda ragaya mathai duka upadinne kiyala dakkoth awabodaya nisa
kala kirinewa.
hitha sathuten piliganne na.
enam 
pancha upadana iskanaye pawathma tiyenne hithaka
e hitha thamai me api sathuten piligaththe naththe, 
e kiyanne api abhi nandanaya kale na (sathutu wena eka)
e nisa adbhi wadhathi kale na (wadan walin wisthara kaleth na)
ajjo saaya tittathi uneth na ( baha gena hitiyeth na)

me mattamedi , 
pancha upadna iskanda dukka kiyana e sobawaya thamai wisthara kale.
sapak kiyala ganna eka nathara wenawa.
pancha upadna iskanda dukka kiyana e sobawaya awboda unahama,
dukin sadahatama nidahas.

ex:
priya wippayogo dukko,
priyan wen weema dukak
e kiyanne 
priyan ge wen weema athi wenne
priyan hada gaththu handa 
priyan gen wen weeme duka niroda wenna nam
priyan athi karana eka nawaththa ganna oni
ehenam
priyan athi wenne ai kiyana eka awboda kara ganna oni 
meka pancha upadana iskanda nisa athi wana dukak bawa wataha ganna oni
priyan hata noganeemen
panchan updana iskanda duken api nidahas wenawa.

madyama prathipadawa kiyala kiyanne 
ath hareema nevi.
ath hareema siduweemata awashaya wana awabodayata path weemai.
mulaa karana bawa dakeema samma dittiyai.
madyama prathipadawa kiyanneth  arya ashtangika margaya kiyana thawath namak. ( mokada arya shatangika margaya patan ganneth samma dittiyen)

ethkota me 
sithe mulawa nisa thamai,
31 thalayak gana katha karanneth , ehi upadinneth.
mokada 31 thalayema upadinne thawath prathi sandi sithak pamanai.

mechchara kalayak api 
ada putu mesa , koppa, aran kuda kali walata kada kada 
alu duwili walata path wee 
shunya una kiyala kiwwata .
eken mage duka shunya wela na.

me siyalu de api katha kale, eda wedaye bamunu matha kandanayata awasha nisai.
e nisa paramartha dharshanaya oppu kara ganeema sanda.
e siyalu dewal api mechchara kalayak katha kale
api inna thana nirawul kara ganna.
api ewath drushti gatha kara gena

api ragaya , idweshaya atha hariyata,
upakalpana nigamana lesiyen atharinne na.
ewa igena gaththa kiyala ,
duka niwenne na. ( ewa matha kada dameema sanda hodai)

duka niweemata nam pancah upadana iskanadayen duka sobawaya aduna ganna oni.
e awabodaya thulin,
dukin sadahata nidahas weeme hakiyawa labenawa.
e nisa meya sath purusha dharmaya lesa hadunwanawa.

enam 
sath purusha dharmaye pihiteema, arya sobawayak.
marga nyanaya upadeema upatha sath purusha dharmaye pihiteema thula pawathinawa.

summary :

sapayak pennala , apita deela tiyennema duka.
duka dunne kawda hitha
sansare yanne me gana nodanna handa 
no danna nisa hataganne awidyawa namathi akusalaya
enam akusala nisa sanasara gamana pawathinawa.

me anuwa akusalaya upadina sobawaya gana dannawa.
ipadichcha akusalaya prahanaya weemen
nuupan kusalaya upadinawa
meka nithara nithara bawitha bahuleekatha kirimen
upan kusalaya wardanaya wardanaya wenawa. 

akusalaya upadina sobawaya gana daneema-> akusalaya prahanaye -> nuupan kusalaya upadeema  -> upadan kusalaya 
wadi diyunu kirima (bawitha bahuleekathawaya)

me 4ta api kiyanwa ( sathara samyak-padan weerya) ( hodata padamana watichcha weerya)

akusalayata wadiya kusala wipaka balawath.
kusalaya kiyanne dakshathawaya / hakiyawa.
itha katha karapu sathara samyak-padan kusal 4 nisa
karmaya ikshaya wenawa.

bahira sobawyama anithyai. enam dukai.
katha karala wadak na.

ex:
albariyak gaththa, awridu ganak tibba  dirala nathi wela giya .
meka gana katha karala therumak na
mokada katha kala kiyala 
ape duka niwenne na.

bahira sobawyama samada dukai,
lokaya duka matha pihitala tiyenawa kiwwe eka nisai.
bahira lokaye duka gana katha kala kiyala 
ape duka niwa ganna ba.
ehenam 
ape duka niwa ganna puluwan wenne 

pancha upadana iskanadaye athi anithya bawa awaboda weemen pamanai.
menna me point eka prathaksha unahama 
nidahask weemak pamanai.

ex:
daruwek miya giyahama , adika wedanawak athi wenawa hithata.
ehema wenne daruwata aluna hinda
ekata hethuwa eya jeewath uwa nam sapai kiyala hithapu nisa.
hitiyoth sapai kiwwe hitha.
sapai kiyala sobaawaya athi wenne 
onima welawaka sapa pennala dukata adala dapu hitha.
pennuwa sapa denne duka.
rawateema dukai.
e nisa ehi awabodaya sapathai.
daruwa nisa nevi duka 
ape armartha kaami nisai duka. 
daruwawa pawathwa gena yame duka sapa widihata dakapu nisa.
katawath ba 
thawa keneku wenuwen adanna.
adanne thamage badimata sapekshawai.
armartha kaami lesa gaththu aleema/ gateema nisa.

mama hithanne ,
mama kamathi widihata anek aya inna oni kiyala.
mage daruwa mama kamathi widhata inna oni.
mawa dukata damme daruwa nevi mage kamaththa.
e nisa 
me loke duka 
sama witama thamange kamaththa mul karagath chanda ragayai.
eka sankalpayak pamanai.

e sankalpaya thula apiwa sada kalika hira karuwek karala.

mulawa ehema naththam mohaye namathi hethuwe,
pala dekak dekak thamai aleema saha gateema

enam mohaya nisa aleema saha gateema pawathi.
enam mohaya prahanaya thulin aleema gateema nathi karaganna puluwan.

mohaye upatha awidyawa.

meya hariyatama dakkoth,
kadulai susumai sadahatama welila yanawa 
puduma sathutak athi wenawa me baren nidahas una kiyana ekata .
meya samma dittiyai.

enam samma dittiya laba ganeemata 
me sath dharmaya 
sutha, datha ,wachasa parichitha, mansa upekkitha, dittiya suppati wijja
lesa puhunu kireema pamanai karanana tiyenne.

me siyalu sasara gewanne ,
balaporoththu nisa. ( apekshawan)
e nisa apeksha thula upekshawak nopawathi.
e nisa 
balaporoththu hitha dakeemen , mulawe sobawya wataha ganna puluwan.
menna me point eka 
dittiya suppati widdya unu wita ,
sowan sobawaya laga kara gana puluwan.


ehenam 
atha natha kiyanne drushti dekak.
ekama mohothaka thamai dekama athi wenne
e mohotha duka apu gaman mathak karanna oni.
hitha wisin dukak/ sapak dekak pennapu nisa thamai duka une awe.
me double game eka matha thamai balaporoththu hariyaaama ho kada weema pawathinne.
me kriyawaliya dakkahama
lokaya thula duka sapa kiyala paththak ganne na 
kisiwek gana dos pawaranna ba. (pawarala palak na kiyala therenawa)

meka hariyata dakkoth 
satha brahma wiwarana wadenawa. ( meththa, karuna, muditha, upekitha)
demapiyek thama lamayata kelesada salakanne 
elesa siyalu sathwayata salakeema 
me thulin hamwenawa.
e nisa dharmaya 
sathwa pudgala bawaya nathi kirimata nevi yoda ganna oni
duka nathi kara ganna.

ex:
gedara ka biththi wahala tiyenne arakshawata.
araksha wenne baya handa 
baya kiyanne dukak
enam gedara kiyannema dukak.
baya athi wenne hithe

hitha tiyenne shareeraye handa 
shareeraya leda wei kiyalath bayai
shareeraya leda weemata baya une 
shareeraya sapai kiyala hithapu handa .
hitha apiwa rawattala .
hitha mawa rawattuwa kiyala dakkoth 
gedara biththi, wahala , shareeraya gana 
prashnayak na
bayen nidahas.
enam duken nidahas wenwa.

me tika karaganna, 
uniform ekak onida , ganu primi bawak oni da ?
diunu kara ganna puluwan sitheeme hakiyawak tibba nam athi.
ikshana sampaththiye watina kama wadagath wenne eka handa .
ikshana sampaththa proyojanayak karaganna puluwan wenne,
sath dharma shrawanayai,
kalyana mithra sewanayai,
yoniso manasikarayai,
dhammanu dhamma prathipadawai.
e hinda ,
sotha paththi anya 4 lesa hadunwanawa.

ein ganna puluwan uparima prayojanaya api ganna oni







 
-----------------------------------chakku samppasaya--------------
 

ex:
asata roopa gateemen chakku sampassaya (roopa roopa gatena thana neme, ethanata sithe pamineemath samaha thinnan sangathi passo - kiyana awathawa)(passa kiyana awasthawa)(wipaka mattamen ehata gihilla)

chakku sammappaja wedana ( chakkuwe isparshayen upan wedanawa)
wedanawa pachchaya thanhawa 

menna me set ekatama api kiyana chakku ayathanaya. 
e kiyanne asata roopa gateeme idala , wynnaya hata aragena, wedanawa nisa thanahawa hata ganna sampurna package ekama 
chakku ayathanaya kiyana kiyanawa.
enam dharmatha tikaka pawathma, saha kriyawaliya chakku ayathanaya kiyala haduna gannawa.
(naama, roopa dekama methana pawathinawa)

asai, roopayai, chakku winyaanayai kiyana dharmatha thune ekathuwa chakku samppasayai.
patichchasamuppadaya anuwa 
chakku sampassaja wedana.
enam 
chakku sammpasaya pawathinawa nam wedanawa janitha wenawa.
wedana pachchaya thanha.
enam wenadawa sapa nam aluna.
wena widihakata kiyanawa nam
raga sampassayen thamai thanhawa athi wela tiyenne.

menna me dharmatha tika ekathuwa thamai api ayathanaye pawathma kiyala ganne.

dan ethkota asa kiyana eka, iswaadeenawa idiripath wenna puluwan da ?
ehenam asa kiyala thaniyama ekak na, api me dharmatha tikakata thamai , me widihata bawitha karanne

atheethayen apu karma , thanha, awidya kiyana hethu dharma nisa
warthmanaye ahara prathya kota 
chakku prasadaya hata ganie.


chakku prasadaya kiyala kiyanne warna haduna ganeeme hakiyawa
meka nikan kadasiye thel sobawyak wage kiyala katha kala 
dan api katha kala 
meka athi wena hethu enam 
atheethayen api karmayi, thanaha awidya hethu dharmai,
warthamanaye ahara prahaya kota chakku prasadaya hata gannawa kiyala.

menna me kriyadamayata api kiyanawa , samudaa gathai kiyla. ( hugak ekathu wela kiyana arthya)

prasadaya hata gena eekata warthamanaya thula roopa wynanaya kiyana, upasthambaya ( udawwa) laba gena
thamai prasadaya dana ganne.

ehema nownoth prasadaya dana ganna ba.
prasadaya haduna me roopaya haduna ganeeme hakiyawa handai.
prasadaya kiyana sobawaya danne ne . mekata api dharmaye kiyanawa "aththa baawa pariyapannai"

meka dana ganna puluwan warna roopayathanen witharai. 
warna gaten handa thamai chakku prasadaya gana katha karanne.
ehema nowuna nam meka gana api katha karanne na.

ehenam asa naththam, sitha yedune naththam warnya dana ganna ba. ( samudaa gathai kiwwe ekata)
ehenam asa kiyathdi eka collection of dharmatha. e dharmatha siyalllema prathipalak lesa misak
warnaya hamuwe na ,
mama dakinawa , mata penawa kiyala waradi sanyya, sankalpana ganna eka dharmayata anukula na.

menna me sobawyata paaliyen api kiyanwa
"ahuthwaa samboothan, puthwaa na^-bawissathi"
"pera nothibeemen hata gena, warthamanayen anagathayak kara pawathmak nathiwama nirudda weemai"

menna me point eka awaboda weema  
"anithyaanu passana nyanaya" kiyala hadun wanawa.

warthamanayen anagathayata sambandayak pawathinne na.

e kiwwe mokadda ?
anagatha pawathmakin thorawa (anagathata no-pamina) nirudda wenawa.



ex:
maalayak kiyala kiyala api kiyanne , pabalu sahitha nosindee pawathina nulakata.
nula nosindi pawathina thak kala malaya pawathinawa.
eka pabaluwakin anek pabaluwata sambandayak tiyenawa.
malayak kiyala kiwwe me sambandaya tiyena thak kal.
malaya pawathinne nosindi pawathina noola handa.

atheetha, warthamana , anagatha sobawaya me malaye pabalu nam
ewa ekinekata yaa karana noolak nithya washayen pawathiya yuthui.
enam kalaya namathi noolen me pabalau thuna ekineka connect karana nisa malaya namathi jeewithaya pawathinawa.

kalaya namathi noole nithya lesa gaththu sobawaya handa thamai melesa awidyawen haduna ganne.

namuth asa gaththoth ,
asa hadila tiyena hethu thula mehema sambandayak naha.
warnaya gatunu parasadaya ethanama niruddai wenawa. 
hata ganna hethu walin ekak ho nathi unoth hataganeeme hakiyawa nathiwenawa.
atheetha prasadaya , warthamana prasdaya samaga sambandayakin thorai.
okkoma sadaka pawathina thak kal.

aluthma warnayak aluthma prasadayak samaga hatagannawa.
asa kiyana dharmathawayata roopa gateemen
chakku samppassaya pahala wenawa.

e nisa eka warakata gatha hakke eka sanyyawak pamani. hata ganna hethu tika eka prasadayak sadeema sanada hethu wela.
ekama hethu tika ayeth wena prasadayak hataganna e mohothe use karanna ba.

e kiyanne ayathana dekak ekata wada karanna ba.

e kiyanne 
eka ayathanyak duru karanna nam
thawa ayathanyak tibila wadak na ?

ayathanaya thulin thamai lokaya haduna ganne.
lokaya duru karanna nam ayathana duru karanna oni.
eka ayathanayak pawathina mohothe , thawa ayathanyak nopawathina bawin.
eka ayathanyak duru karanna thawa ayathanyaka yudaw ganna ba.

me sobawaya gana katha karanna ayathana dekak eka wara hata noganeeme hakiyawa gana awabodaya pawathiya yuthui. 

eka ayathanyaka pawatheeme hethu nirodaya wuu wita 
ayathana 6ma niroda wenawa.
enam 
loka norodaya , eka ayathanyaka nirodaya thulin laba ganna puluwan.

ayathanayaka nirodaya,
aasayen karanawanam eka lokaya thulamai ( meka api katha kala fan eke example eken giya sare)
nirayasayen wenawanam lokkoththarai 

enam ayathanayaka nirodaya nirayasayen karaganna widiha thamai balanna oni.

ethkota 
mama kiyana eka ain karaganna try kaloth eka lokaya thula.
mama kiyana eka automatically ain wenna oni.

enam mama pihita sitimata thanak nathi karanna oni.

Neewarna nomathi manasak hadanna , laukika prathipaththi siyalla awankawa riju wiya yuthi.
 
api kiwwa 
thul kalhi athi una sanyya samuththi sathya hewath praknyapthi pamanai.
ehenam paramartha dharma gana katha karanna ba.

prasada roopaya sadene hethu sakas nokirimen ayathana nirodaya laba agnna puluwan kiyala.

e nisa nuwana meheya wanna oni 
me penena thana ( enam prasada ayathanayaka) athi doshaya haduna ganna oni.

ex:
balana bawa hari nobawalana bawa kiyana deka hata ganna nam
peneema pawathinna oni.
e antha dekama pawathinne peneema pawathina kan pamanai.
eka anthiyaka baleema , eneke nobaleema 
mada tiyenawa paneema kiyana sobawaya.

hithe sobawya hithana eka
kane sobawaya ahena eka
diwe,shareenaye, nasaye sobawya danena eka

meka widinna yanawa nam dosayak.
peneema balen ain karannath bari nam
paneema tiyenne mada nam.

peneema kiyanne mokadda kiyala haduna ganna oni.
mese peneema kiyala sobawyata api kiyawa kaama thanha kiyala.
ehenam
kama thanhawe , eka paththak athi bawa 
anek paththa nathi bawa.

kama thanahawe  athi kiyana anthya anthaya bawa thanhawa lesath.
kama thanhawe nathi kiyana anthya wibawa thanaha lesath 
hadun wanawa.

kama thanhawen galawenna rahath wenna oni.
100% galawenna nam piriniwan panna oni. ( iskanda wala pawathma nisa)
enam jeewath wenakan peneema pawathina bawa.

pruthak jana api,
moho dewal athin athariyata , hithin atharala da ?

namuth hitha handama thamai iwara karannath puluwan. (praknyawen)
 
 e nisa 
 
 anichcha watha sankara  - yamak anithya nevi, yamama anithyai. (eke sakaseemama anithyai)
  yamak kiwwahama deyak pawathinawa kiyana hageema enawa,pawathina de ain karanna wenwa. enam pawathina deyak ain karanna wenne ayasayakin.
  ehenam ayasayakin ain karnawa kiyala karanne lokaya thula dewal.
  
pancah kamaye doshaya kiyala kiyanne,
me antha dekata ahu weema. saha ese antha deka pawatheema sadaha mada tiyena hethuwa / dosaya

mada athi dosaya , dakeema thulin thawakalikawa sitha niwa ganna puluwan.
eka thamai, api me raga,iwesha moha yatapath kara ganeema thulin karanna try karanne.
namuth yamak kirima yanu ayasak. enam lokaya thulai.
e nisa wishkambana prahanayak pamanai. e nisa dyaana mattam , laukikaya thula api katha karanawa.

duka therila, ( kaye athiwa duka wath , manasika wath nevi, dukka sathya kiwwe, yamak,kenek,deyak ,thanak kiyala adahas karaganeemai) ( eka mulika wela lokaya athi wenawa)
samudaya watahila, ( dukka athi weeme hethuwa watahila)
nirodaya penilai , ( athi wana bawama nathi weema dakala)
maga wadenne neda ? ( maga wadenne nirodaya dakkata passe, nirodaya dakapu kenek gen ahaganna oni)

ex:
sariyuth thero gihi kalaye nama upathissa,
eyage guruwaraya sanjaya bellatta puththa.
edawasak dakka, assaji maha rahathan wahanse
eya lagata gihin ahuwa
oba wahansege guruwaraya kawda , monawada ugawanne kiyala ?
ethkota assaji maharathan wahanse kiyawanawa
"ye dhamma hethuth pabawaa, thesan hethu thathagatho aaha"
" yam dharmayak hethu nisa hata gannawa da anna e hethu thathagathayan wahanse deshana karanawa"
meka ahala sariyuth hamuduro sowan una.

dan api ahanakota apita therune 
methana nirodayak gana katha kale na
samudaya gana witharai kiyala witharai apita therenne.

e unata me padaya ahala upathissa tharunaya sowan palayata paminuna.
eyata "sukaa patipada kippa wynaa" awasthawa tibba.

me tharunaya wataha gaththe 
sakas weema kiyana thana nevi.
sakas wenne baha kiyalai therum gaththe.

samudaya jathiya pramuka kota aththak.
nirodaya kiyanne samudaya duru wena sobawayak
nirodaya athi jathiya pawathinna ba.

deweni padaya kiyanna kalin eka therum gaththa.
deweni padayen meka kiyanwa 

"thesanchayo niroodoo, ewaan waadhi maha samanoo"
"ewaa nirodaya thamai budun deshan kale"


 
 


-------------------------sakkaya dittiya duru wena prathipadawa soya yaama 25/04/2021--------------------------------


ape me try eka iswakeeyathwaya, ikmawala ethara weema kiyana prathipadawa ismathu karanna. eka thamai me battle eka.
eka thamai ape motto eka , ape dharshanaya.
apiwa palanaya karanne ape sithiwili ne.
e hinda thamai iswakeeyathwaya ismathuwela tiyenne.
eka nisa apita niyama prathipadawata anugatha wenna hambenne na.
e nisa sakkaya dittiya wadi wena piliwelak mai tiyenne.
iswakeeyathwaya ismathu wela tiyena kan, apita ethara weema kiyana prathipadawa hambenne na.
ethara weema , tiyenne budun ge dharshanaya thula.
enam hambenne naththe budun ge dahamai. ( wena anam man dewal nam oni tharam hambei, apita hodai kiyana dewal/apita hari kiyana dewal hambuwela. apita hithena dewal
)
e unata , arthanwithawa, kalyana mitharayata (budun athulu arya shawaka) yomu wela na.
me nisa dharmaya hamu wenneth , lokaya thula hamuwana thawath deyak lesa. ( mata hamu wana bawa nisa)(hama tissema deyak wela). namuth meya labena deyak nemei wenna oni ethara weemak.
labena deyak pawathinawanam , ganna kenek inna oni, enam lokaya pawathinna oni.
e nisa e karamayata ethara weemak na.
budda wachanaya lokayen ethara weema sanadai. e nisa lokoththara dharmaya kiyala budda wachanayata kiyanawa.
deyak, kenek thanak, pudgalayek. onikamak, tiyena hama thanama
buddha gunaya ismathu kara gena naha.
budun ge deshanawa,
tan sunaa-tha, saadhukan manasi karoo-tha. ( budha aknyaawa)
(meya asaw, hodin sihipath karaw)
hodin asala, sajjayana (katha karanna).
ese karathdi 
budda gunaya ismathu wela
niweema kiyana prathi padawata yomu wenawa.
menna me wage mulambayak tiyenna oni.
dharmaye gabura dakinna.

iswakeeyathwaya thulin balana thek, buddha prathipadawata yomu wenne na.

ex:
durekshayaka arthaya mokadda ?
"aatha tiyena deyak laga kara baleema" kiyana gathiya tiyena object eka.
durekshayen balanakota , durekshaya penawada. ? na
durekshaya nodakkata, dureksh tiyena kriyakarithya tiyena kan thamai apita aatha deyak lakara balanna puluwan.
as deka lan karala balapu hama thamai ehema penne.
aatha idan balana kota ehema penne nane.

durekshayen atha balanakota durekshaya penne na. aatha penawa.
namuth durekshayen kerena karya neda api durekshaya kiyala wisthara karagena tiyenne .
ehenam  durekshaye tiyena plastic kali walin wath lence eken wath,durekshaye arthaya mathu wenne na.
durekshaya kiyala upakarana diha balapuwahama arthaya therum ganna ba.
arthya sakas wenne kriyawaliya thulin.
api durekshaya haduna ganne upakaranaye kriyawaliya thulin.
enam api durekshaya lesa arthyen haduna gaththe, upakarana yen kerena karya misak upakaranaya nevi.
parts nevei.

enam e durekshayen kerena karya karana oni ma upakarayak apita durekshayak.

ehenam api pruthakjana wasahyen ganna plastic and lenses tika durekshaya nevi neda ?

durekshaye arthya ismathu kara nogaththe nam, durekshaya apita upakaranak pamani.
eya lokaye hamuwana thawath deyak pamanai.

namuth arthya mathu wana se nyaanaya upadawa gatha yuthui.
budun penwa wadale,
lokayen ethara weemai. 

pancha upadana iskanadaya,
ayathana 12,
indriya 22,
dhaathu 18,
sathya 4,
patichcha samuppada anga 12
kiyana paramartha dharma
 
lesa hamuwana durekshaye kotas, ehema naththam  me durekshayata api kiyanawa widarshana boomiya kiyala.
me siyalu anga, widarshana boomiye kotas.
budun deshana karanna widarshana boomiye kotas gana dana gena / padanam karagena 
sitha , parknapthi walin galawala,
paramaartha dharmaye pawathweema  
ehenam naththam ,
dura baleemata nuwana upadawa ganeema (niwan awabodayata awasha praknawa upadawa ganeema) 
thamai weerya karanna oni.
methana  sitha praknapthiyen galawalaparamaarthye pawathweeme hakiyawa widarshana nyanaya kiyala adunwanawa.

enam boomiye kotas dana gaththa kiyanne niwan awaboda kala kiyana eka nevei.
durekshaye kotas gana dana gaththa kiyala ,
durekshaya use kale naththam dura penne na.
enam 
arthaya mathu kara gaththe naththam
widarshana nyaanye awadiweemak wenne na.

me aadi sama deyakinma pennum kale , lokayen ethara weemai.
dharmaya thamai durekshaya.
aatha penenawa wagethamai niweema hewath ethara weema.
ape watahima , hariyata durekshaya bahirin penawa wage mai.
eka sammathaye lebel ekak pamanai.
dharmaya asathdi dharaye arthya asanne na. ( durekshaya kiyanne plastic kali tikai, lenses tikai widihata)
durakshaye arthya haduna ganne dakina witai. ( aatha baluwe naththam penne na)
nathuwa as dekata pena dureskyen nevi.

aatha idan durekshaya diha balathdi , api durekshaya dakka kiyala hithuwa.
namuth dura penne na. ( arthya peni natha)
durekshayen aatha dakina wita durekshaya nopene. aatha penei
enam arthaya dakima wei. enam ethara wei.
enam sakkaya dittiyen ikma una wei. ( sakkaya dittiya kadeema sidu wei)


widarshana nyaanaya ta mulika washayen padanama, (foundation eke pradana anga)
-seela wishuddiya (sathara sanwara seelaya kiyalath hadunwanawa)
----prathimoksha sanwara seelaya (niwanata pamunuwana sanwara seelaya)
----indriya sanwara seelaya  (indriya sanwara karana seelaya)
----ajeewa parisudda seelaya (jeewath weemedi pilipadiya yuthu seelaya / nokalayuthu weladam gana api katha kale)
----prathya san-nishthritha seelaya (prathya weksha kireema) (ahara ganna kota , bada ginna niweema pinisa , dharmaye yedita pahasuwak pinisa misak, shareeya lassana kirimata nevi)

-chiththa wishuddiya (upachara samadiya sahitha ashta samapaththi yata) (kusala sithe uparima sobawaya thamai upachara samadiya kiyanne)(niyama samadiya nevie, samadiyata asannai) (niyama samadiyata kiyanne "arpana" kiyala)

(widarshana nyaanaya kiyala eka wenamama padamak, api ada nikan 
topic eka alluwa witharai, wishuddi margaya athule tiyena saptha wishuddi walin pradana dekak thamai api pennuwe,
thawa 5k tiyenawa) e pahama praknawa gana thamai katha karanne.
(ditti wishuddiya, (waradi dakmen ain weema ) 
kankaa witharana wishuddiya, (sakyen duru kireema) 
maggaa-magga nyana dassana wishuddiya, (maga nomaga dana ganeema)
patipada nyana dassana wishuddiya, (puranna oni wada piliwela dana ganeema)
nyana dassana wishuddiya, meya widarshana nyanayai.
)
enam widarshanawa wadana nam menna me wishuddi margaye thamai gaman karanna oni,
e gana api pasuwa , tikak gaburen katha karamu.

ada api katha kara kara hitiye, 
durekshaya use karagena widarshana boomiya wishthara kara gaththu eka.
widarshana boomiye anga dana ganna oni arthaya ismathu karaganna .
eeta passe 
eka prayogikawa kalyana mithrayan samaga sakachcha wen
hoda shuthamaya nyaanayak upadawa ganna oni. (sotha+awadhanaye pannyaa shuthamaya nyaanan)(ahunkam deema thulin laba ganna awaboda mattama.)

we need focus on this point very clearly.

dharmaya igena gannawa kiyanne sanyya goda gahagena innawa kiyana eka nevei.
shuthamaya nyaanaya upadawa ganeemak.
widarshanawa wadaweema sadaha athyaawasha woo angayak.
(eka handa buduhambuduwanta tiyenaa nyaana 73 kin pamalu nyaanaya , shuthahmaya nyaanayai)


ape wataheema hariyata durekshaya wage.
eka boruwata asu woo label ekak witharai. ( namuth eka oni shuthamaya nyaanaya upadawa ganeemata)
eka sanyya goda ekathu karaganeemak widihata ganna ba.

apita pancha upadana iskandaya , ayathana 12...etc ewa apita therenawa ne.
namuth api e dharmaya ahanakota, dharma arthya hambu wela na, apita hamwela tiyenne ara kacha tikai, plastic tikai witharai.
arthya ismathu wee natha.
arthya ismathu wenna nam durekshaya nopenee yanna oni.
enam arthya ismathu wena wita durekshaya nopenee, aatha penei.
enam
sakkaya dittiyen ethara wei.
nodanna kamen ena duka awaboda wela.

methana thamai api hodin awadanaya yomu karanna oni thana.
kachaya saha plastic kamabali tika durekshaya lesa allagena sitina thak kal me lokaya thulai, enam his purushayo lesa sasara yai.
api plastic kabali, widiru kiyana praknapthi ekka hira wela.
eken karagatha yuththa , ehema naththam
arthya mathu karagena na.


enam apita kranna puluwan mokadda ?
buddha wachanayata , awanatha weema, keekaru weema misak
ekata anugatha novi, apta awenika sithuwillak thulin dakeema novei.


me siyalu dharma kotas (eg: pancha upadana iskandaya...eetc) nikan durekshaya wage,
thama thulin dakina thek, meya syllabus eka pamanai api study karapu.
ehi arthya soya , buddha dharshaya ismathu kara gena eya thulin niweema shakshaath kara gatha yuthui.
(menna meya marga nyanaya kiyala hadun-wanawa).

marga sathya ehema naththam arya ashtangika margaya kiyala wadanne mekai. 

 
ex:
me loke tiyena dewal sakkaya dittiya thulin haduna ganeema nisa thawa deyak wela. jeewithai, dharmayai thawa lokaya thula ekthara deyak lesa aran. ( siyalu prapancha/praknapthi menna methenntai thamai hamu wenne.) 

me lokeye hamuwana dewal thulin arthya soyagena yaamen, marga nayaanaya upadawa ganna puluwan.
jeewithai dharmayai dekak wela thamai apita mechchara kal hambela tiyenne,
ehew apita,
me deka ekak washayen kenekuta hambenna puluwan da ? bane , mokada kenek innawane.
ayeth api sakkaya dittiya ahuwela.

jeewithai , dharamayai dekak washayen hambechcha apita , me deka ekak hatiyata kawadawath hambenna bane.( mokada pudgalayek innawane)
jeewathai, dharamayai ekak lesa labenawa kiyala hithuwoth.
ehenam naththam apita dharmaya labila kiyala hithuwoth , eka mano lokaye prapancha tikak witharai.
mokada mama ethana pawathina nisa.

dharama arthya ismathu unoth,
 "api dannawa" (jaanaami) kiyala kiyanna puluwan da  ? ehema yedenne naha neda ?
na^ jaanaathi wadeyya  ( dannawa kiyala kiyanna ba.) lesa thamai budun deshana karanne.
niwana kawadawath dana ganna ba, mokada laukika dharama walin wisthara karanna ba.
ethara weemak pamanai. ( asankathayak, prathya walin thorai)
methana api ajara, amara lesa hadunawanwa ( ajara - jaraweemak na, amara- maranayak na)

budun sathara pera nimithi daka, menna me nidahas weemai hewwe.
thaniyama hewwe. (swayan boo nyaanan)
e nisa samma sammbudda lesa hadunwana.
menna me soya ganeema , nisa budun kerehi athi wana achala shaddawata kiyanwa aakarawathi shaddawa kiyala.
aakarawathi shaddawata mulika piyawara wanne marga nyaanaya upadawa ganeemai.

marga nyaanaya upadawa ganeemata yomu weema, yoniso manasikarayai (budu wadan ahanna pelebenawa) 
marga nyaanaya upadawa ganeemata , arthya soya daka gatha uthui, enam danuma ikmawa praknyaawa ismathu karaganna oni.
enam lokaya ikmawiya yuthui. ( lokaththa wiya yuthui) ( menna meyata lokkoththara samma dittiya nam wei )

ethara weema , dakimama ethara weemai. dakima thula nathara weema nathi wei.
(anuppada nirodayai)
athi wana bawa nathi weemai. (athi wechcha deyak nathi weema nevei)

ex:
keekaru wenawa kiyala kiyanne,
budu wadanata adu ho wadiyen matha prakasha karanna ba.
kisima brahmayekuta, deviyekuta, brahmanayekuta, ho maryakuta ho katawath , kisiwekutawath dharmaya adu ho wadi bawak kiya nokayie.

ese kiyanne shardhaawa adu, sharawayek misaka, bhudda sharawakayek novi.
 

Summary 
 
ada session eka ahuwata passe? monawada duru une ?
mechchara kalayak arthya mamathwayen gaththa wu kriyawaliya prapanchayak lesa haduna gaththa. 
sakkaya dittiya hadena widiha haduna gaththa. 
e method eke tiyena waradda haduna gaththa.

me kriyawaliye, athi weema nathi kirima misa,
athi una deyak nathi kirimen sakkaya dittiya nathi nowana bawa awaboda karagaththa.

mama, mage kiyana drushtiya waradi bawa therum yanna patan gaththa.
lokaya samaga karana ganu denu waladi, arthya soya yama sadaha , marga nyaanaya upadawa ganna widiha igena gaththa.
eya apply kireema thulin prathyaksha kara ganna adishtana kara gaththa. 

nissatho , nijjeewo, shunyo lese hadiwu dharmaya (hethu pala dahama, dakinna patan gaththa)

budun e nisa,

naayan dhammo duppanyyassa
ayan dhammo panyawan-thassa

me dharmaya prayanwa upadawa gath ayatai. naththam prakyawa ismathu nokala ayata novei.

methana prayawanthaya kiyala kiyanne, ikmanata therum giya kenata nevei.
sakkaya dittiya duru karanna margaya wadana kenata.
mamathwayen ganeeme warada thamai awaboda wenne.
praknawa pawathinne mage awabodayata thula nevi.

onima shrawakayek thula samma dittiya upadawa ganeemata upakara karana
dharmatha 4k tiyenawa. (hethu prathya washayen)
1) paratho goshaya  (sath dharmaya danna kenek ge hadak, naththam maga pen weemak tiyenne oni, para tho goshaya)(wena kenekgen athi unu sath dharma hadak)(marga nyanaya upadawa gaththu kenek, ehema e sath dharma danuma bedana kenek)
2) yoniso manasikaraya ( meka upadawa ganna oni)
3) shuthamaya nyaanaya (meka thamai api mechchara wela katha kale)
4) chinthaamaya nyanaya (asuu sath dharmaya sihi kirime / menehi kirime hakiyawa)

prakyawa ismathu kara ganeemata , budu wadanata awanatha wiya yuthui.
shardawa tibiya yuthumai.

dharmaya tripitakaya thulin seweemen, yalith api durekshaya mai soyanne.
dharmaya arthya, enam maga nuwana ismathu kara ganna thamai uthsaha karanna oni.
(durekshaya wada karana widiha gana dana ganna oni shuthamaya nyaanaya upadawa ganeemata)
(nathuwa sanyya goda gaheemakata novei).
budda parinirwanayen pasuwa,
rahathan wahansela sangayana kala thripitakaya, thamai apita ada dharmaya guruwarayek kara ganeemata sadaha 
hamu wana muleeka adithalama.
rahathan wahanselage handa wachana lesa lekana gatha kireema thulin.
pusthakaye rahath weemak sidu wela na.
namuth 
dharmaye arthaya mathu kara ganeema sanda awasha wena siyaluma maga penweem ehi adangui.
ebawin 
padaye arthaya ikmawa giya , awabodaya sadaha
praknawa meheya weemai anugamanaya kala yuthu prathipakthiya wiya yuththe.

me pusthkaya dakkinna oni thawath durekshayak widihata.
arthaya mathu kara ganeemata nam
paratho goshaya saha yoniso manasikaraya etha wadagath.

kenek meme dharmaya waradiyata kiyala dunnoth,
paratho goshaya labilama na ( labila tiyenne mathayak, wena kenek ge drushtiyak)
enam yoniso manasikaraya mathu karaganna ba.

e nisa dharmaya thawath sannya gonnak pamanai wenawa.
e hinda ape thsahaya 

suthamaya nyaanayai
chinthamaya nyaanayai awadi-kara ganna.

e deke prathya thamai
paratho goshaya  -> suthamaya nyaanaya
yoniso manasikaraya  -> chinthamaya nyaanaya

enam paratho goshaya,yoniso manasikaraya athawashai me gamana yanna.
 

enam tripitaya thulin dharmaya gaweshanaya kala yuththe , me "maga nuwana ismathu wena aakarayatai".
arthya mathu weema hewath sakkaya dittiya duruwana se , mamathwayen thorawa dakeema aramba kala yuthui.

arthya mathu kara penwanne budu rajanan wahanse pamanamai.
e nisa dharamaya thulin budun daka gatha yuthui.
budun dakapu kala dharama arthya mathu wei.
dharamaya dutu kala budun hamuwei. ( yo dhamman passathi so man passathi)

kukkusathi raja themo, budun ruwa dakkath ,budun haduna gaththe na.
dharamaya aseemen pasuwa budun haduna gaththa.
ehenam roopaya budun lesa gaththu sakkaya dittiyen obbata gos.
dharmaya thulin badun bawa haduna ganeema sidu wenna oni.

enam sakkaya dittya thulin budun habuwenne na.
budun dakagatha hakke dharamaya thulinma pamanai.

dharmaya yanu sakkaya ditta duru wana awabodatha nyaanayai.
eya thulin sakkaya dittiya pihitana thana noroda karai.

meya prathyaksha kala wita , dharmaya thulin budun deshana kala nirodaya shakshsaath wei.

methek kal hithen sidu kale, prathya wekshawak ( prathyan nawatha nawatha sihi weema, being logical) misak
prathyakshak nevi. (prathyan ge ishaya weema)
yoniso manasi karaya thulin pamanai prathyakshayata giya hakke.

me siyalu sathwayan udesa kala deshanawak nisa, 
agam bedayakin thorawu, awabodha nyaanayaki. (jeewamana budun kalayedith niwan dakke anyaagamikayo, mokada budun dharmaya deshana karanna kalin hitiye ehema kattiyane)

eda indiyawe siti wikukkthi kamintath ,
sakkaya dittiya pilibada danuma tibuna, (durekshaya kiyanne lense and plastic tikak kiyana eka)
namuth arya konaya bawitha kale na. ( meya budun wahanse pamanamai ismathu kale)
arya konaya thulin budun dakimata weerya karamu.
(api ada dana gaththa , meya daka ganna nam
shardda, weerya sathi samadhi prayknaa yana indriya dharmayan diyunu kara gatha yuthui)
