alawwe anomadhassi thero discussion.
kinithulagala arnya deshana wala pattanaya gana katha karanawa ewa balanna patan ganna puluwan apita.
 

pitagala gunarathne thero
yamaka suthraya ahanna

 
 -------------------wipassanawa kirima sandaha awasha therawada siddantha 01/08/2021------------------
 
 api mechchara kalayak katha kale prakna gochara akarayata.
 e nisa sama witama awabodaya thulin thamai ape seelaya saha samadiya wadenne.
 
 praknawa diyunu kirime margayata api kiyawa widarshana ehema naththam wipassana kiyala.
 me wipassanawa gana thawa durath katha karanakota 
 apita awastha thunak igena ganna wenawa.
 
 1) uthpaadino dharma ( eelaga bawaye labena wipaka sith saha karmaja roopa )(kaya dasaka, bawa dasaka, wasthu dasaka mulikawa , dawas 77 giyahama chakku,shotha,jiwha,gaana dasaka)
 
 2) paramaththa jathika dharma ( paramartha saha praknapthi athara tiyena awasthawak) - meeta kalin ahala na.
 habai me kiyana awasthawa paramartha paththata barai habai, praknapthi nevie.
 
 praknapthi - sammuthi naama ( oni welawaka wenas wenna puluwan)(hithen hada ganna sankalpa)
 paramartha - samawitama sahajatha dharma samaga hata ganne. (thaniyama tiyenne na, chiththa, chithasika, roopa)
 roopa samawitama sathara maha boothyan ekka hadila tiyenne. ) thaniyen patawi na. aththa washayenma pawathinawa.
 
 me jathiye paramaththa jathika dharma kotas 5k tiyenawa.
 2.1) ajatakashaya = awakasayata= his bawak = space kiyala kiyanneth mekatama thamai (akasha dathuwa kiyala kiwwahama, roopa kalapa athara tiyena idata, me roopaya hadenakota , eka gaththe awakashaye idak. me roopa kalapa athule tiyena ida ta api akasha dathuwa (parichchada roopaya lesath hadunwanawa) kiyala.
ajatakashaya kiyanne  tiyena sampurna his ida. meka thamai space kiyala kiyanne.
 2.2) anuppanna roopa ( anishpanna roopa 10)(lahutha,mudutha,kammanyatha,kaya/wachi winappthi,lakkana roopa 4 (upachaya, santhathi, jaratha, anithyatha), akasa dathuwa) 
 me roopa wala hama witama katha karanne gathi lakshanayak gana. ( awenika lakshanayak),
 api paramartha dharma wala roopa kotase roopa 28 gana katha kalata , mema anishpanna roopa 10 wipassanawata use karanne na. mokada ewa gathi lakshana thamai pennum karanne. 
 e nisa me paramartha saha praknapthi athara pawathina paramaththa jathika dharma lesa thamai mewa ganne.
 2.3) thilakshanaya - anichcha,dukka ,anaththa , mewa aithi wenneth paramartha jathika dharmaya godata.
 mewath paramartha dharma wala lakshana 3k, e nisa meyath paramartha jathika dharma thamai.
 2.4) prathya shakthiya - sithen sithakata dena thalluwa. ( energy eka) (pattanayedi me pathya shakthin 24k gana wisthara atha, soowisi prathya lesath ahunwanawa. me gana pasuwata katha karamu)
 2.5) gathiya - gathi sobawaya, mannussayek marena kota napuru gathi yak awoth, e anuwa wipaka roopa sakas wenwa. ( gathi nimiththa kiyalath meka hadunnawa.) ballek wela ipadunoth, balu gathiya kiyana eka ikmawanna ba, eyata minis gathiya ganna ba. namuth minissu ekka hadunoth purudu anukaranaya karanna puluwan. eka gathi wenasak nevi.
eka awenikai. ballata kawadawath manussayek ekka hitiya kiyla manussayek wenne na. 
 ex: girawek manussoyo athara hadena kota, manussa bashawa anukaranaya kara hakie.
 kale inna giyawata eka ba. gira gathiya thula manussa gathi upadawa ganeeme hakiyawen thorai.
 
 
 3) anuppanna dharma - possibilities ( anagatha prathisandiyakadi labana naama roopa) (dharma kiyala methana damme naamaroopa dekama niyojanaya wana handa)
 karmanukulawa labena possibilities, 
 kusala karmayaka wipaka ho
 akusala karmayaka wipaaka ho
 dhyaana karmayaka wipaaka lesa sakas wana naama roopa paramparawa (naamaroopa parathisandi) ho naama only (aroopa prathisandi)/roopa only (roopa prathisandi/ asanyathalaya) paramparawa.
 
 31 thalaya gaththahama
 naamaroopa parathisandi - 26
 roopa prathisandi -1 
 aroopa prathisandi - 4
 
 summary ekak gaththahama 
 
 paramartha dharama kiyala kiyanne ipadena bidena dharama ( ahuthwaa samboothan uthwa na^-bawissathi)
 (pera nothibeemenma hata gena nathwa sheshayak wath ithuru nowana se nirudda wana dharmayan)
 
 paramaththa jathika dharma kiyanne , gathi sobawayak, shakthiya washayen bawayen bawayata pasu pasa enawa.
 meya sama witama karmaya matha padanam wei.
 karmayata dayaka wena dharmatha dekak thamai
 awidyawa saha thrushnawa.
 
 awidyawa karmaya ras weemata dayaka wenawa. ( awidya pachcha sankaraa)(punyabi,apunyabi,anenjabi sankaaraa)
 thushnawa karmaye prathisandi wipakaya digin digatama laba denawa. (thushnawata awashai, thawa thawa jeewitha laba deemata.)(me lokaye bawayen bawayata duka pawathwanna hethu wenawa)
 
 e nisa me lokaye pawathinne duka saha dukka nirodaya pamanai.
 
 anuppada duka kiyala kiwwe issarahata  paminennata tiyena duka. 
 niwan dakke naththam, paminennata tiyena duka , thama eka sakas wela na.
 paw/pin/dyana karapu handa hethuwa already sakas wela tiyenne.
 namuth palaya awilla na. namuth enna niyamithyai.
 ekai anuppada duka.
 
 kawada hari me anuppada duka ikshaya wena kota, marga awabodayath
 sampurnayen ikshaya unahama
 nirwanaya lesath hadunawanawa.
 meme athi wana bawa nathi weema
 anuppada nirodayai.
 
 api dan balamu,
 budu rajanan wahansege
 nyaana patha gana. (naanaya wisiriya haki ikeshthraya / field eka - pancha wida neiyya mandalaya.)
 menna me pancah wida neiyya mandalaya dana ganeeme nyanaya,
 sarwaknyatha nyanaya
 
 pancha wida neiyya mandalaya
 1) sanskaara (punya,apunya, anenjabi...)
 2) wikaara (lahutha, mudatha, kammayatha, kaya,wachi)
 3) lakkana ( upachaya, santhathi, jaratha, anichchatha)
 4) nirwanaya (sammuthi,thadanga,wishkambana, samujjeda, nissarana)(yam mattamaka niweemak)
 5) praknapthi 
 
 budurajanan wahanseta me kotas pahe 
 ithaa wishala awabodayak tibuna.
 
 dan api igena ganna yanna hadanne,
 yali uthpaththiya hata noganeema sahanda kala yuthu dewal.
 
 1) iklesha-prahanaya ( kleshayan yanu sitha kilitu karana dharma. ewa thamai awidyawai, thanhawai, ethkota eka duru deka karaganeemata marga nyanaya upadawa gannawa. api ekata kiyana wipassana nyanaya kiyala) ekata sathdharma danuma (parathogoshaya saha yoniso manasikaraya )awashayai.
 meka thulin shuthamaya nyanaya saha chinthaamaya nyanaya upadawa gena, sitha kiliti karana kleshayan prahanaya kara ganna puluwan. 

 2) karma shakthi-prahanaya  
 
 iklesha prahanaya thulin upadawa gath me ihatha nyana dharma 
 Bawanawa washayen  nawatha nawatha bawitha kirimen (bawanamaya nyanaya upadawa ganeemen) e nyana dharma upanishraya prathya wee ( lagin asuru wela)
 pasuwa pasuwa ena kusal diyunu tiyunu wee pahala wenawa.
 mema prabala kusal shakthiyen anagathaye naama roopa pahala weemata athi karma shaktiya duru kirime hakiyawa ipadenawa.
 wipassanawa lesin hadunwanne menna me karamayai.


methana api note karanna oni, nathi karanna puluwan mathu nama roopa paramparawa pahala weemata athi idakadai.
nathuwa danata wipaka awasthawe (pravurthi) pawathina karma shakthiya prahanaya karanna ba.
e nisa 
karmaya kotas dekai
1) pravurthi ( jeewath wana kalaya thula)
2) wipaka (yali ipadena wipaka prathisandi karma shakthiya)

e nisa mugalan maharahathan wahansetath pravurthi karma washayen wipaka dunna. 
 
kusalayak sidda kirimedi widi dekakin karanna puluwan 
1) uthkrushta kusalaya (thun sitha pahadawa karana kusalaya , purwa/munchana/apara awastha thunedima sitha pirisiduwa thaba ganeema) 
2) oomaka kusalaya ( purwa/munchana/apara thun awathawaka sitha kilitu unoth, eka bala ganaye kusalayak)

kusalayak karanakota loba idwesha moha walin thorai.
eheth 
kusalaya karana awasthawa saha pera pasu awasthawala 
sitha apirisidu weemen
eya oomaka kusalayak wenawa.

aloba,adwesha, amoha uthkrushta kusalayaka wipakayak thamai trihethuka prathisandiyak laba denne.

karmaya karma pala gana wishwasayak athiya yahapath deyak karanawa
1) uthkrushta (thunsitha pahadawa) -> wipakaya thrihethukai
2) oomaka -> wipakaya idwihethukai

karamaya saha karma pala gana wishwasayak nathuwa yahapath deyak karanawa
1) uthkrushta (thunsitha pahadawa) -> wipakaya idwihethukai
2) oomaka -> wipakaya ahethukai

meeta amatharawa,
akusal sitha 12k tiyenawa ewayen wipaka washayen labenne 
ahethuka sith. (uddachcha sitha harunu kota)
me ahethuka sith boho wita upaththiya jathi andayek ho beeri kenek,
goluwek.. habai manussa uppaththiyak.
sugathi ahethuka pudgalayek.
eyata manussa sobawayak hambenne kusala wipakayak handa namuth angawikalai.
enam akusal walain
ekka anga wikala naththam
sathara apayye. 


karmaya saha karama pala wishwasa nathi  oomaka wipaka,
dharmaya asanna nomathi , pathya pahasukam adu than wala uppaththi labanawa.
hoda dewal kala handa manussa paulaka upaththiya
namuth duken thamai jeewithaya gatha karanna wenne.

karmaya saha karama pala wishwasa athi  oomaka wipaka,
slums wala ipadunath, athi dakshayek.
eken aliyata yame hakiyawa tiyenawa.
ipadethdi prathya pahasukam adu unata 
thama wisin ewa ada ganna praknawa upaddawa ganna puluwan.


------akusala karmaya saha wipaka -----------------15/08/2021-------

abidharmaya igena ganna kota akusalya saha akusalaya moolayath 
kusalaya saha kusala moolayath haduna ganeema etha wadagath.
 wisheshayen me moolayan haduna ganeemama , samma dittiyata paminime eka margayak. (samma dittiyta enna akara 16 tiyenawa eken ekak. - patichchasamuppadaye anga 12 + athireka 4)
mokada 
kusalaya / akusalaya saha ehi moolaya haduna ganeema thulin dasa kusalaye pihitala, akusalayen bahara weema.
drushtiya riju kara ganeemak.

ada focus karanne akusalaya gana.

akusala karma 10k tiyenawa. mewata kiyanwa akusala karma-patha kiyala.
akusalyak sidda wenna piyawara wal keepayak sidda wenna oni
akusal tiyenawa 10k.
akusala karma sith washayen gaththoth akusala karma 12 hambenawa. 


sith washayen

-loba/raga moola sith 8
-idwesha mool sith 2 
-moha mula sith 2

mewa doratu 3nakin wenawa, meka karma-idwara kiyala hadunawana. ( kaya,wachi,mano) karma idawara.
karmaya sidda wena doratu.

kaya karma idawara kiyala kiyanne - kaya wynapthi roopayata. (ekantha chiththaja roopa mewwa, hithathdi kayen wena ewa)
wachi karma idawara kiyala kiyanne - wachi wynapthi roopayata. (ekantha chiththaja roopa mewwa, hithathdi kayen wena ewa)
mano karma idawara kiyala kiyanne - mano wynapthi roopayata.

ethkota kaya,wachi wynnapthi kiyala kiyanne ekantha chiththaja roopa dekak
mano karma idwaraya kiyanne sithatamai.

ehenam me igena ganne sitha gana.

pansil pada 5he mul 3 tuna gaththahama,
panathipatha, adinnadana, kame sumichchara - kaya karma (kaya wynpathi roopa)

ajeewa ashtamaka seelayedi 4
musawada,pisunawacha(kelam), sampraplalapa, parushawacha(raluwata baninawa) - wachanaya

ethkota ithuru wana 3 mano karma idawraya aithi wenne.
abiddyawa chethana- dadi lobaya
wyapadaya chethana- tharahawa/gateema
mytha drushtiya chethana

akusal 10kin wen wenawa kiyanne 10 kusala seelayak samadan wenna puluwan.
meka hariyata dana gaththata passe.
10 kusala seelaya gedaradima jeewithayata huru kara ganna puluwan.


api akusalaya gana katha karanakota , eke padanama poddak balanna oni.

akusalayata pradana washayen mul wenne mohayai. ( hethu darma thunak tiyenawa loba,idwasha,moha)
enam mohata thulin thamai me loba idwashaya athi wenne.
enam hama akusal sithakama mohaya aniwaryayen pawathinawa.


dan poddak akusala karma moola haduna ganna balamu.

1) prana gathaya, parushawachanaya, wyapadaya (tharaha yana eka) -- mula wenne idwashayai (mohaya thulin ipadunu)
ehenam akusal moola dekai -> idweshayai, mohayai
2) kama mithya charaya, abidyawai, mithya dittiyai -- muula wenne loba/raga +mohaya
enema akusal moola dekai -> lobayai(ragayai)+ mohayai

ethana mithya drushtiyedi, waradi adaheema, waradi matha dadiwa allagena innawa , loba moola sithak ekata mul wela tiyena handa.

3) ithuru karma 4, 
adinadana, pisunawacha (kelam), samprappalapa(his wachana),musawada - mulaya wenne mohaya + either (raga/loba or idweshaya)

ex:
horakamak kiyana eka 
meya gawa wadipura tiyenawa eka handa gaththata kamak na - idwesha + mohaya
meka man gawa na man ganna oni - loba + mohaya
me akara dekatama me akusalaya athi wenne puluwan.

4) wichikichchawai, uddachchaya - mohaya pamanai.

sith washayen gaththahama 

loba mulika sith -8
-kama mithya charaya, abidyawai, mithya dittiyai + adinadana, pisunawacha (kelam), samprappalapa(his wachana),musawada kiyana ewa athi wena sith akara 8k tiyenawa , hethu dekak mulika wena (lobayai, mohayai)
-sith 8 gana katha karanna puluwan
 -- sathutu sithin karanawa nam
 ---- somanasa sahagatha dittigatha samprayuktha asankarika /sasankarika sitha (dittigatha samprayuktha - dittiya ekathu wela)
 ---- somanasa sahagatha dittigatha vippayuktha asankarika /sasankarika sitha (vippayuktha- ekathu na)
 -- mathyastha sithin karana nam
 ---- upeksha sahagatha dittigatha samprayuktha asankarika /sasankarika sitha (asankarika- wena kenek ge meheya weemak na, thamanma thamai karanne)
 ---- upeksha sahagatha dittigatha vippayuktha asankarika /sasankarika sitha (sasankarika- wena kenek ge meheya weemak thulin)

iwdesha mulika sith -2
ara widihatama aye 7k athi wenawa idweshaya mulika karan, habai sith jathi dekak
--domanassa sahagatha  patiga samprayuktha asankarika /sasankarika sitha

ex: sport ekak widihata fun ekata saththu marana minissu gawa tiyenneth me sith dekama thamai, hina wela ka gahuwata
hitha athule domanassa sobawaya pawathinawa.

pranagathaya sidda wenna nam, dharmayata anuwa aniwarayen akusala sithak moolika, eka idwesha moolika sithak mai.
api rawatena idweshaya nevi kiyala, mokada hina wewi,asawen karana sobawaya handa , api bahira indriyen ne hina wenawa kiyana eka aduna ganne, habai adyathmika paththen kriyathmaka wana sitha, akusala sithak. idwesha + mohaya thamai mulika wenne. 

moha mulika sith -2
-- wichikichchawai (sakaya), uddachchaya (hithe nosansun kama) thula mohaya witharamai pawathinne.
---- upeka sahagatha wichikichcha samprayuktha sitha
---- upeka sahagatha uddachchaya samprayuktha sitha

moho mulika sith echchara prabala na.
eka hethuka dharmayak nisa prabalathawaya sapekshawa adui.

ex: hugak busy nam wada eka digata kara gena yanna ba.
ethkota athiwenne menna me uddachcha sitha, 
uddachcha sitha ithaa dubalai.

e nisa me akusal sithin dena wipakath itha dubalai.
maranayen pasu apaa gatha wana shakthiya uddachcha sithe na.
namuth anith 11 tiyenawa.

Summary ekak gaththoth.
katha kale akusal sith gana 
e sith walin monawa wenna puluwan kiyala katha kala.

sith 12k katha kala
eken somanassa ewa tiyenne 4i. (loba mulik sith walin)
upeka sahagatha 6k tiyenwa (loba mulika+ moha mulika)
domanassa sahagatha 2k. (idwesha mulika )

asankarika sith 7k (thaman hithala karaganna ewa ) (moha mulika sith -2 hamatissema asankarikai, ekai 2k wadi)
sasankarika sith 5k (wena kenekge udawwen)


dan api akusalaya sith washayen 12k katha kala 
e wala wipaka tika balamu. ( mewa katha karanne ahethuka sith 18)



-----------------------------akusalaya saha chathurayasathya athara athi sambanadaya------------------

meka katha karanna nam mulin akusal walata yedena chaithasika dana ganna oni.

siyaluma keles walata moolika padanama loba , idwesha, moha
suthra pitakaye thula 10 keles wisthara karanwa karanawa.
loba 
idwesha 
moha
maana
ditti
wichikichcha
theenamidda
uddachcha
ahirika
anuththabba

me keles 10ta yedena akusala chaithasika 14 tiyenawa (meka hambenawa abhidarmayedi)

1) moha chathuskaya (moha,ahirika,anuththabba,uddachcha)(mohaya tiyena hamathanama me 4 yedenawa)mohaya hama thanama tiyenawa. e nisa api mewata kiyanawa akusala sadarana chaithasika kiyala.
2) loba thrikaya (loba,ditti, maana). meka anithaya yogi, e kiyanne okkoma ekata yedenne na. ekko loba+ditti,loba+maana
namuth ditti+maana ekata hambenne na.
loba mulika sith wala,
ditti gatha samprayuktha (loba+ditti)
ditti gatha vippayuktha (dittiya yedila na, namuth manaya yedila)
3) dosa chathuskaya (dosa = idweshaya)(dosa,issaa,machchariya, kukuchcha). mekath aniyatha yogi. e kiyanne niyatha washayenma okkoma ekata yedenne na.
4) theenaya, middaya, wichikichchawa. (theenaya = sithe alasa bawa,chithasikayan ge alasa bawa = middaya, sitha saha chithasika ekatama pawathina nisa api meka ekak lesa hadunwanawa, theena middaya lesin. me nisa nidi matha gathiya
kammali kama mathu wenawa. samawitama ekata enawa.
enam yamkisi wadak karanakota kammali kamak enawanam- eka akusal sithak.
normal ninda nevi.
wadakata kammali kama , akarmanya bawa.

ex:
ane dan nam meka ba,
ada wada kala athi,
kala thawa tikak imu

api kammali wena hama thanama akusalayak thamai karaganne.
meka aithi wenne ,

loba moolika 4, idwesha moolika ewa 1 (sasakarika sith 5) - wala thamai theena middaya athi wenne.
enam theena middaya gaththuhama loba, idwesha pakshikai.
meka mohayata athi na. (mohaya uthpaththiyenma asankarikai)- mohayata athi upeka sahagatha sith dekai.
e deka udachcha saha wichikichchai.

ex: bahira balapamakin mohaya athi karanna ba.
thawa kenek ge mohaya wena kenekuta aussanna ba.

dharmaya nodanna nisa , api hithanawa api kiyana dewal walin kenek ge mohaya awussanna puluwan kiyala
e ape nodanuwath kamai. dharmaya thulin meka pahadili karala tiyena widihata api aragena na. 
me dharamayan ge haseerima gana api danne na.
e nisa thamai dharmaya igena ganne.
me nodanuwath kama nisa api wanchanika dharma walata ahu wenawa.
kusal kiyala hitha gena akusal karanawa.
e nisa akusala gana dana ganeema itha wadagath.

enam darmaya anuwa,
mohaya -> awiddawa/ danne nathi kama / moda kama

kenekuta widyawa kiyala dunna hama, eya thamai hithala eka awaboda karaganna oni.
naththam widyawa pahala wenne na. eka handa thamai hamotama meka kiwwata , eka mattame awabodayak hambenne naththe.
eka eyagema waraddak. 
eyama thamai hithin weerya karala meka kara ganna oni. (meka thamai hethu pala dahama api igena ganna hethuwa)
e nisa udachcha,wichikichcha naththam moho moolika sith samawitama asankarikai.
enam udachcha, wichikichcha moha pakshikai.

api katha kala ,
loba paakshika -> ditti + maana
moha paakshika -> udachcha + wichikichcha
loba,idwesha paakshika -> theena middaya


meeta amatharawa , loba,iwesha,moha thunatama paksha kattiyak innawa
e thamai
loba,idwesha,moha paakshika -> ahirika, anuththabba

ahirika - hiri eke wirudda eka  ( papaya pilikul nokarana sobawaya)(papayata lajja nowana sobawaya)
anuththappa - (papayata baya na kiyana eka)
akusalayata tiyena mahaa bala dekak thamai me deka. 

loba,idwesha,moha paakshika -> ahirika, anuththabba
(me deka thamai api wisheshayen dana ganna oni, mokada meka akusala pakshaye pradana bala dekak)
kusal paththedi meke wirudda adahasa ,
enam hiri / othappa - akusalayata tiyena lajja bawa / baya  (mewa dewa dharma lesa hadunwanawa )


ethkota api keles 10 (akusal sith 12), chaithasika washayen groups 4kin katha kala. (total 14 chaithasika)
meeta amatharawa,
loba,idwesha,moha wala thawa extensions tiyenawa ( gathi sobawayan)
sitha kilutu karana, chiththoopa-kelsha (upa klesha) (upa kiyanne laga kiyana adahasa, like upa sabahapathi)
 me wikaashayan 14 api padana washayen katha karanawa namuth.(1500 pamana tiyenawa, me akusala sobawayan okkoma allala, renukane chanda wimala hamuduruwo pothak gahala tiyenawa keles 1500 kiyala)

kroda upanaaha.(kroda - tharaha , upanaaha - badda wyrayata)
makka palaasa. (makka - gunamakukama, palaasa - thumun gawa aguna tiyenawa, namuth gunawathun samaga samana lesa hithanawa )
issa machchariya ( issa- irshiyawa, machchariya - masuru kama)
mayaa saateiya (mayaa - anunwa rawattanawa, sateiya - thamun laga nathi guna pennanawa)(sihalen kairaatika kiyanneth meka)
thamba saaramba (thamba - thada bawa/rough, saaramba - anun karapu de wadi karala kiyanawa)(athin dala)
maana athi maana ( maana - thama usas kiyala maninawa, athi maana - thama anek ayagena usas yai sithima)
mada pamaada (mada - math wenawa,(mada 21 tiyenawa, yawwanaya nisa math wena, sura madaya..etc), pamaada - pancha kamayata athi wena math gathiya.


ex:
dasa akusalaya thula surameraya wisheshayen sadahan nokale,
sura meraya nisa athi wana wikurthiya thulin 10 akusalayama siduwiya haki nisa.

surawa thula, prakurthi sihiya nathi nisa, pancha kamayata athi wana asaawa wadi karanawa.
enam pamaada kiyana sobawaya athi wenawa.

sitha wikurthi wechcha gaman, akusalayata automatically yata wenawa.
e nisa pancha seelayen di katha karana prada 5n ekak lesa salakanne e nisa.
e 5 kadima thulin dasa akusalayata yanna tiyena doratu margayan wiwurtha wenawa.

e nisa pradana doratuwa wahala tiyena kan, ara diguwa arenne na. enam akusalaya , thuna idwarayen 
sidu weemata awasha mulika prathipadana thamai pancha seelaya thulin wahala tiyenne.

pancha seelaye watinakama therenna , me danuma itha wadagath.
pancaha seelaya ada sita rakina kota , rakina dehi watinakama awaboda wenawa.
pawata athi lajja baya, naththam hiri othap, naththam dewa dharma wardanaya wenawa.

kenekwa baya / bala karala pancha seelaye pihituweema thulin hiri othap wardanaya wenne na.
eya me wadana seelaye watinakama danne na.
pancah seelaya saha akusalayan athara tiyena me sambandaya gana tiyenawa dharma
awabodaya thulinmai meka karaganna puluwan.
seelaye usas bawa haduna ganna wenne 
dharma awabodaya thulin mai.

ekai dharama awabodaye athi watinakama.


dan api katha karapu siyalu keles walata thamai ,
samudaya sathya kiyala api katha karanne. (thanhawa nisa ne duka hata ganne) (thanhawa kiyannema kelesayan. 
thanawa api katha karannema me akusal sith 12 thulin ma thamai)

enam samudaya sathya thamai, me 31 thalayaka , bawa gamanakata hethu wenne.
(sibbani-thanahawa, mahana kota yati noola), bawayen bawaye amunanne meken.

e nisa 
me thanhawa/ keles
- kama thanaha (pancha kamayata athi asawa )
- bawa thanaha (bawa gamanata athi kamaththa, roopi aroopi loka athi kamaththa)(sasrutha drushtiya)
- wibawa thanaha (me bawayata athi asawa, wena bawayak na) (uthcheda drushtiya)

me thanaha thunema base eka samawitama 10 akusalayai.

meka poddak wisthara kara gamu.

budun ge guna aratharin palamu eka 

arahan - siyalu keles walin duru woo seka, keles aratuwa sidalu seka, keles sathuran duru kala seka. aprakatawath keles pahala wenne na, e tharamata budun ge sitha ni-kleshi.

ex:
api kiyanawa , "arahan budu gunen ape siyalu apala duru wewaa" kiyala
dharma awabodaya nathi kenek,
mehe kiyala hari, 
budun ge guna gana pahadeema itha wadagath,
thaman ge apala duru wenna budun ge pihita pathanawa,
methana budun kerehi pahadeema pawathinawa
namuth awabodaya na , e nisa 
ekata amoolika shraddawa kiyala kiyanawa.

me wani kenek shaddawa thulin thamanta pihita patheema , sakkaya ditti poshanayak.
dharma, mema sobawaya ikmawa giyapu achala shaddawa (akarawathi shaddawa) matha thamai pihitanne.

e ahana kenata , amulika shaddawena -> akarawathi shaddawata yomu weemata nam 
dharma awabodaya sadaha udaw upakara kala yuthui.

apith mul awadiye pasu kale ewanima mattamak.

keles gana awabodaya tibimen , budun ge arahan gunaye athi usas bawa ismathu wenawa.
e nisa siyalu aamisa , prathipaththi pooja walata sudusu woo seka.


arahan gunaya ga katha karanakota , keles wala duru woo akaraya gana thamai katha karanne.
melesa dasa akulayen mideemen sidu wenneth menna me ,
arahan guna sobawaye wardanayak.

arahan gunayen kiyawenne chathurarya sathye awabodaye paniwidayai.

 
 samudaya sathya gana katha karanakota:
 
 damsak pawathum suthraye di deshana karanawa 
 
 "ye thassa ewa thanaha asesa wiraga nirodo" washayen sadan kara atha.
 eya samudaya sathye prahanayai.
 enam dukata hethuwa - samudaya sathyayai.
 dukata hethuwa nathi kirima niroda sathya yai. (yali mathu wenne nathi widihata nathi kirima)
 
 e nisa samudaya sathya dana ganna kena thamai,
 niroda sathyata path wenne.
 dukata hethuwa dana gena
 hethu sakas nowana lesa prahanaya karanawa.
 eka karanna margaya thulin.
 
 e nisa dukka sathiya -> samudaya sathya -> niroda sathya -> marga sathya 
 lesa piliwelin api katha karanne.
 
 api ada pennuwe 
 akusala prahanaya thulin chathurarya sathya wadaweeme athi hakiyawa.

enam akusalaya kerehi athi awabodaya
marga sathye kotasak.

samudaya ithiri nathiwa duru kirimata nam , uthsahayak tibiya yuthui.
me uthsahaye  focus eka 
seela,samadi (ekakgrathawaya), prakna wardanayata kala yuthui.

meka sidu wenne marga sathya yedi.
enam arya ashtangika maryayai.

arya ashtanagika margaye di 

samma ditti (prakna)(sitha)
samma sankappa (prakna)(sitha)
samma wacha (seelaya)(kaya/wachana sanwaraya)
samma kammantha (seelaya)(kaya/wachana sanwaraya)
samma ajeewa (seelaya)(kaya/wachana sanwaraya)
samma wayama (samadi)
samma sathi (samadi)
samma samadi (samadi)
 
dan me widhata balanakota 
praknawen -> seelaya -> samadi

namuth api igena gena tiyenne 
seela samadi prakna kiyala 

ehenam palamu widiha gaththama praknawa mulin pawathinawa 
devani ekedi praknawa agin iwara wenawa.

pulinuth praknawa , agatath praknawa ,
enam prakanwe wadeemak thamai katha karanne.
enam 
arambaya sanada daham awabodaya kara ganna prakanawa wadagath (shuthamaya lesin) 
seelaya haduna gena , seelaya niwaradiwa wadeema sandaha awasha mulika praknawa.

seelaye wardanaya samadiya pinisamai. samadhi sanwaththanika seelaya lesa hadunwanawa.
samadiya wardanaya kara ganna nam seelaya aniwaryayai.

samadhi thulin labenne chiththa ekagrathawaye theewra bawayai.
shuthamaya washen labuna woo praknawa , dharmaya thulin dana/daka awaboda karaganeema
ehema naththam prathyaksha kara ganeema.

enam 
prakna seela samadhi
seela samadhi prakna 

kiyana akara dekenma api katha karanne 
praknawe mulika mattame sita ethara weema (niwana) dakwa.
system eka thulin ma system eka dakala.

ex:
meka nikan , relay ekak wage
relay ekak start karanna batten ekak onimai, 
me relay batten ekath praknawa wagemai.
relay start karanna batten eka oni, ekathamai players athara maru karanne.
e batten ekama thamai relay eka iwara karanneth.
enam tharagaya iwara karanneth patten eka ma thamai.

enam jeewitha sasara duka kiyana relay eka iwara karanna nam
marga prakanawe awadiyak sidu wiya yuthui.
enam race eke niwaradi prathipada anugamanaya (batten eka aran yana kattiya, awasha diha thamai duwanne)(anik marga wala gihilla race eka iwara karanna ba).
batten eka wattaganne nathuwa gamana purna kirimata thamai awashya. 
me sanda puhunuwa aniwaryayai, wirya athyawashai. (wayaama pennanne samadi gode, sitha wena wena pathi wala duwala hariyanne na) (sitha wena pathi wala diwwoth, labenne apaya gaami ho sugathi gaami witharai, nirwana gaami nove)
batten eka athahariyoth eka relay ekak nevi.
prakna awadiya athya awashai.
batten eka ath nohara , me prathipadawa anugamanaya kirima thamai
race eka iwara kara ganna tiyena ekama widiha.
prakna awadiweema thamai api bodhi kiyala hadun wanne.
habai karapu kenek na.
enam praknawa awadi wethdi duwapu kena nathi wela.
eka dharamatha wala sowawayai.
enam duwapu kenada anithya, dukka, anathma kiyana sansakara dharmayan genma yukthai.
e awabodaya thulin thamai,
mamathwaya galawee, awabodayata pathwenne.



reference:

---------------------------sansara gamana haduna ganeema ------31/08/2021--------------------

api giya sare akusalaya aduna gaththa, akusalaya saha thanahawa athara sambandaya aduna gathatha
akusalayen ath weema thulin arya ashtangika marga wadeema sidu karana widiha api aduna gaththa.
ada 
lokoththara arya ashtangika margayata aithi  sathdharmaya nolabunoth,
me sansara gamana kiyana eka sidu wena widiha gana katha karamu.

giya sare katha kale akusal nisa, e hinda balamu kohomada akusalaya sathwaya sansarayata adala ,badala tiya ganne.

akusal kotas washayen katha karanakota. (akusala sangrahaya) kotas 9k katha karnawa.
e kiyanne me kotas okkoma akusal.

1) aashrawa (sinhala ayurwedaye, ashrawa hambenawa, beth jathi wathurata dala huga kalayak pal wenna arinawa, me pal wechcha wathurata thamai aasawa kiyanne, aasawa thamai arishta kiyala kiyanne. biwwahama math wenawa)(e wage thamai loba,idwesha,moha aaswath, sansarayak dige boho kalayak pasawa pawasa tiyena handa ewa biwwahamath minissu math wenwa. karana de therenne na.) aashsrawa bawaa-agraya (bawaye kelewata api namak denawa, katha kirime pahasuwata) dakwa pawathinawa. (lokaya yata kara gena gala gena yanawa ashrawa).

pruthak janaya sithak aasharawa walin galawenna , ehema naththam  lokoththara sithak bawata path wenna , gothara-bu sithak kiyana sith sobawaya  pahu karagena.meka wishesha thrihethuka 
kusal sithak . e nisa aashawa, bawa-agraye sita gothra-bu sitha wenawkanma pathira pawathinawa.
ashrwayan api anu kotas 4kin katha karanawa
	- kamashrawa ( pancha kamaya)( thuwalakin sarawa yanawa , aha namathi idwarayen loba/idwesha/moha namathi ashrawa dharmayo wagiyenawa. e nisa math wee alenawa/mula wenawa).
	- bawashrawa (roopa aroopa thala walata yamata athi kamaththa) (e e bawayan gana kamaththa)
	- dittashrawa (laukika samma dittiya athuluwa, ditti siyallama athi asawa)(lokaya niyojanaya karana siyalu ditti 62 kerehi athi aashawa)
	- awidyashrawa (saba thathwaya wahana , moha chaithasikaya nisa hata ganna aashrawa)
	
	chaithasika washayen gannakota,
	aasarawa niyojanaya karanne, lobaya,ditti,moha kiyana chaithasika thunen.
	lobaya kiyanne ragaya/asawa/kamaththa -> kamashrawa, bawashrawa 
	ditti chaithasika -> dittashrawa athi wenne.
	moha chaithasikayen -> awidyashrawa athi wenne.

2) oooga (sada paraharak, ahu unama gaha gena  yanwa nawaththwanna ba.)(sathwaya sansare gilwala danawa, galawenna dennema na). meka athi wana widiha kotas 4i. sansarayen goda wenna denne na gilwalama thamai tiyanne.
	-kamaooga
	-bawaooga
	-dittiooga
	-awidyaooga
3) yooga (nawatha nawatha yodawanawa). e kiyanne sansara chakraya athi wena lesa yodawanawa
	-kamayogaya
	-bawayogaya
	-dittiyogaya
	-awidyayogaya

	chathasika washayen, ooga,yoga, asharawa widihatamai wada karanne.
	
me tike summary eka gaththu hama. 
- math karana handa aasarawa kiwwa
- sathwayan sansara sagaye gilwana handa oogayak kiwwa
- sansara chakraye yodawana handa yoogaya kiwwa.


4) grantha (gantha kiyala thamai paliyen hamu wenne) - (gata gahanwa kiyana meaning eka)(grantha kiyanne gatayakara) (pothak kiyanne kola godak gata gahalane)me gataya nisa thamai potha pawathinne. e wage thamai warthamana bawaya anagatha bawaya sambanda karanawa 
e nisa grantha kiyala kiyanawa.
ewa kotas 4i.
	- abijja kaaya gantha (meth lobayama thamai)(kamaraga,rooparaga,aroopa raga, enam samastha lokayama aithi wenawa)
	- wyapada kaaya gantha (me idweshama thamai)(idweshayen sasara gata gahanawa)
	- seelabasa paramaasa kaaya gantha (sansara duka kelawa kirima walakwana, mithya drushti )(mewa thadin allan innawa, eka thamai hari kiyana eka thadin allagena innawa) 
	- idan sachcha-abi-niwesa kaaya gantha ("idan sachchabi niwesa" - meka thamai harima eka kiyala baha ganna prabala drushtiya, withakshana nyanayata awasara na, itha thadin allagena innawa) - e nisa meka dittiya nisa athi wenne

	chaithasika washayen,
	-lobaya -> abijja
	-idweshaya -> wyapada
	- ditti -> anith deka
	
	
5) upadana (lesiyen atharinne nathuwa thadin allagena innawa)
	- kama upadana
	- ditti upadana
	- seelabbatha upadana (niwan maga nowana mithra matha,seela niwan maga kiyala wardawa thadin allan innawa)
	- aththawada-upadana (aththawaadu-paadana) (athma washayen thadin gannawa)(mama,mage kiyala thadin allaganna eka)
	
	chathasika washayen gaththuhama,
	lobaya -> kama
	ditti -> anith thunama
	
	me asarawa,ooya,yoga,grantha,upadana ain karanna nam samudaya sathya dakinna oni, thanhawa duru karana margya, lokoththara aryashtangika margaya wadeemen thamai duru karaganna puluwan.

6) neewarana (niwana wahanawa)(sathwa santhanaye, athi nowechcha kusalayan athi nowana widihata, athi wechcha kusalaya nopawathina widihata wahala danawa)
	- kama chanda neewaranaya (lobaya)
	- wyapada neewaranaya (idweshaya)
	- theenamidda neewaranaya (chaithasika washayen theena+midda)
	- uddachcha kukkuchcha neewaranaya (chaithasika washayen uddachcha+kukuchcha)
	- wichikichcha neewaranaya (wichikichcha chaithasika)
	- methana enakan api igena gaththe pancha neewaranaya ne, namuth awidyawa akusalayakama tiyena handa 
	akusala sangrahayedi, awidya neewarana kiyala 6 weni neewaranayak gana katha karanwa.
	awidya neewarana (moha chaithasika)
	
	ethakota neewarana 6k, chaithasaika 8kin katha karanawa. upeksha bojjangaya wadana kota, me neewarna diha lanwela balanawa, ehema thamai neewarna dharma yatapath wenwa. oopanaika gunaya wadawana kiyala bodhi anga walidi pennennane menna me neewarna yatapath karana akaraya.

7) anusaya (anusaya->pariwuttana awassathawa -->weethikrama awassathawa, nidagena inne, karmayak awoth thamai nagitala enne. nidagena inna sobawayata thamai anusaya kiyala kiyanne. wenwenwa paramartha dharama washayen ipadila na anusaya washayen tiyenne aprakatai. athi bawa prakata wenne karanayak awoth witharai.)
	- kamaraga anusaya
	- bawaraga anusaya
	- patiga anusaya
	- maana anusaya
	- ditta anusaya
	- wichikichcha anusaya
	- awidya anusaya
	
	meka prahanaya karanne lokoththara marga nyanaya ipadaweemen.
		
	
8) sanyojana (ekathuwata)(sathwaya sansaraye bandala thabana rahan/lanu)
	- kamaraga sanjoyana
	- bawaraga
	- patiga
	- maana
	- ditti
	- seebbatha paramasa
	- wichikichcha
	- issa
	- majjariya
	- awijja

 9) klesha (sitha kilutu karana dewal)(klesha kiyala giya sare padame igena gaththa tika)
 
 wishayen keles 1500k hadenne 
 chiththa 1 + chaithasika 52 = dharma 53 hambenawa
 nama dharma 53 + nishpanna roopa (roopa 28n,anishpanna 10 ainkarala) 18 +lakkana roopa (upachaya,santhathi,jaratha anichchatha) 4 =  dharmatha 75
 me dharmatha 75 x2 (adyathmika,bahira washayen) = 150k
 e 150 aramunu kota thamai keles athi wenne.
 e nisa 150 x 10 = keleshayan 1500 hamu wenwa.
 
 
me okkoma tiyenne pudgala santhanayak aluthe. ( paramparawakata dena namak, chiththa santhanaya kiwwahama chichcha paramparawa gana thamai katha karanne.)

eka handa lokaye  7.9 billion minissu hitiyata.
pudgala jathi 12 habenne.
arya pudgalayo 8i. (ashta arya pudgalayan, sowan->sakada gami->anagami ->arahath ,maga/ pala washayen )
pruthakjana kattiya 4i. (meka thamai ada katha karanne)

1) dugathi ahethuka
2) sugathi ahethuka
3) diwi hethuka
4) thrihethuka 

api mehema kotas karanne , prathisandi chiththaya anuwai. (main point eka)

dugathi ahethuka,sugathi ahethuka kiyanna sith gonna kelinma kamawachara boomiya thamai aith wenne.
e kiyanne prathisandi chitthaya e jathiye dekak nam kelima kamawachara boomiyakamai ipadenne.

ehenam eka kohomada wenne kiyala poddak balamu.

kamawachara boomiya,

akusala wipaka upeka sahagatha santheerana sitha -> prathisandiya labanawa nam eka dugathi ahethukai
kusala wipaka upeka sahagatha santheerana sitha ->  prathisandiya labanawa nam eka sugathi ahethukai

me sith deken aniwaryayen kamawachara boomiyak mai.

iwi hethuka saha , thrihethuka gaththahama e walin,

maha-wipaka nyana wippayuktha sith 4n prathisandiya labena nam -> idwi hethukai. ( nyana wippayuktha kiyanne nyana yedila na enam praknaya (amoha kusalaya) yedila na. me hithaka aloba,adwesha kusal sith deka witharai pawathinne)

maha-wipaka nyana samprayuktha sith 4n prathisandiya labena nam -> aloba,adwesha,amoha thunama yedila.
e wage kusal sith thamai,

me sithuth kamawachara boomiyaka upaththiya labanna puluwan.
me anuwa kamawachara boomiye uppathiya labiya haki sitha 10k tiyenawa.

meeta amatharawa.

dyna kusal thrihethukai.

dhyana washayen katha krana kota
mahag-gatha wipaka sith 9k habenawa (roopawacha 5, aroopawacha 4)

mahag gatha wipaka sitha walin roopawacha aroopawachara prathisandi labanna puluwan.
e kiyanne,
marana mohothedi, dyana sitha pirihenne nathuwa tiyenna oni.
ehema tibuth pamanai adala thalayata wipaka labenne.
bariwela wath chuthi sithe adala maranasanna chiththa weethiya, 
wenas unoth eeta adala akarayata thamai prathisandiya

ex:
dyana sithen marenne na, maranaya sidu wenne maranasanna chiththa weethiyen.
aramunak aragena thamai marenne.
e aramuna thamai nimiththak washayen api ganne.
putuwen idagena idala nagittahama, e rasnaya thama putuwe pawathinawa wage,
nopirihunu dhyanaye gathi sobawaya, 
maranasanna chiththa withi aramune pawathinawa. (meka thamai api gathi nimiththa kiyala ahunwanne)
e gathi nimiththata adala uppathia wipaka lesa hamu wenwa.

e aramuna dyana nopirihunu dyana aramunak nam, adala wipakaya adala thalayedi labenawa.
me jeewithaye karapu dyana kusala -> eelaga bawayedi e kusalaya anuroopawa wipaka lesa lebenawa.
 
 
mahag-gatha sith apita hambenne dyna kusala wadawanna haki than waladi witharai.
e kiyanne 
kamawachara boomiyedi,
kamawachara,roopawachara, aproopawachara , lokoththara sith wada ganna puluwan.

methana lokoththara sith walata wipaka na.
e hinda ewa kusal, akusal washayen katha karanna ba.
e nisa kriya sith lesa adunawanwa.
me nisa 
roopawachara kriya 5k, aroopawachara kriya sith 4k habenawa.

lokoththara sith walata wipaka nathi nisa, prathisandi sith gonnata kriya sith aithi wenne na.
ehenam 
kamawachara boomiye sith paramaparawa athule,
hamu wana kriya sith walin, roopawachara, aroopawachara, kamawachara boomi thunama niyojana karanna puluwan.
habai thunatama aithi na , wipakath novie.
enam kriya sith digatama pawathwa ganeeme sobawaya thamai, rahath sobawayata lesa hadunwanne.
enam e sith wala kusal/akusal/wipaka na.

mahag-gatha kriya goden apita 
roopawachara kriya 5k, aroopawachara kriya sith 4k habuna

meeta amatharawa,
kaama boomiya gaththahama hambena sitha 54 thulin  kriya sith haduna ganna widiha balamu.

kaama boomiye - akusal sith 12, ( kusal sith 8, wipaka sith 8k, kriya sith 8k.) -> menna me set ekata kiyanwa sobana sith 24i kiyala. 
meeta amatharawa , thawa ahethuka sith 18 hambenawa.
ahethuka sith 18 + akusal sith 12 = asobana sith kiyala 30k.

ethkota sobana sith 24 + asobana sith 30 = kamawachara sith 54.

akusal walata -> adala wipaka pennum karanne ahethuka sith gonna thulin.
ennam akusala wipaka sith lesa ahuwena sith natha.
ewa pawathinne,
ahethuka akusala wipaka lesai.

e ai ?

ahethukai, hethu dharma yedila nathi nisa. (loba,idwesha,moha,aloba,awdesha,amoha)yedila. e nisai ahethuka kiyala kiwwe.
nathuwa ibe athi una kiyana adahasa nevi.

ahethuka gonnedi , kusal washayen wath , akusal washayen wath katha nokarana kriya sith 3k hambenawa.
kriya sith 3k, 
 - upeka sahagatha pancha idwara wajjana sitha (chiththa withi mathak wenna oni)
 - upeka sahagatha mano idwara wajjana sitha
 - somanassa sahagatha hasitha uppada sitha. (rahathan wahansela hina wenne sathutin, ehema hina wenakota use karana eka sithak thamai me sitha, meka janawa sithak)

ithuru ahethuka wipaka sith 15, kotas dekakata bedenawa
kusal/akusal washayen
kusal sith 8i,
akusal sith 7i.

kusala/akusala wipaka chakku/sotha/gana/jiwha wynana sith 8,
ethkota kusal walata 4i, akusal walata 4i.

kaya wynaya,

suka sahagatha kaya wyanaya
dukka sahagatha kaya wynaya

dan kusal walata 5i, akusal walata 5i.

eelagta,

kusala/akusala wipaka upekka sahagatha sampitijjana sitha
kusala/akusala wipaka upekka sahagatha santheerana sitha

dan kusal walata 7i, akusal walata 7i.

awasanaye,

kusala wipaka somanassa sahagatha santheerana sitha, ihalama ishta aramunak, (nikan budun hamuweema wage, itha uthkrushta kusala aramunak)- e nisa wisheshai.

dan kusal walata 8i, akusal walata 7i.


ethkota api mathaka tiya ganna oni ,
ahethuka kusala wipaka sith
misak,
ahethuka kusal kiyala jathiyak na.

kusal wipak sith- 16 ( 8k sobana sith walin, 8k ahethuka sith gonnen)
akual wipaka sith - 7 ( ahethuka sith gonne tiyena 7 pamanai)

me ahehutka wipaka 15n,
kusala/akusala uppeka sahagatha santheerana sith kiyana dekan pamanai prathisandiya laba de.

e hinda ara pruthakjana 4gen palamu deka me sith dekata sambandai.

sugathi ahethuka -> kusala uppeka sahagatha santheerana sitha
dugathi ahethuka -> akusala uppeka sahagatha santheerana sitha

summary eka gaththahama.

prathisandiya laba denne ,
ahethuka wipaka sith 2i,
maha kusala wipaka (sobana sith gonne) 8i. (iwihethuka 4, thrihethuka 4)

kamawachara prathisandiya labena wipaka sith 10.
mahag-gatha(roopa/aroopa) prathisandiya labena wipaka sith 9, (roopa 5,aroopa4)
  
enam prathisandiya denne,
total sith 19kin witharai.

ethkota , prathisandi, bawanga, chuthi kiyana kruthya 3ma karanne me sith 19n.
prathisandi, bawanga, chuthi akara 19k pawathinawa.

ethkota ,
wipaka kiyala kiyanne ,

kusala/akusal kala kenage santhanaye, ewa nisa anagathaye athiwana chiththa shaktheen.
(paramartha jathika dharama)


sith upadina isthaana 6k tiyenawa
indriya 5ka upadina isthana anuwa nam karala tibunata.
heart(herdaya roopaye) upadina sith gana etha wadi nisa,
e wata uppathi isthanaya anuwa nam denna ba.

ahethuka sith wala herdayen updina sith walata,
e e sithin upadina kruthya anuwa namak dee atha.

sampajjiana sitha - pili gannawa.
santheerana sitha - theeranayak gannawa
jawan sith - karmaya sidda karna sith (duwana sith)
 mewa okkoma herda wasthu ashithawa hataganan sith.
 e hinda kruthya mulikai.
 indiya 5n nam karanna ba.
 
harda roopaye pawathina bawanga chiththa paramparawata, api mano idwaraya kiyala kiyanawa.

kama roopa aroopa prathisandi laba denne sith 19kin.
meeta amatharawa asanyya thalaye prathisandi denne roopayen.
ehi sith natha.
ema nisa.

prathisandi sith 19ki, prathisandi 20ki.
roopawacha anthima dyanayen decide karanna puluwan sitha athuwa ho sitha nathuwa uppathiya labanna.
e anuwa asanyya thalaya yanna puluwan.


dan api balamu loka hadena widiha,
okkoma loka 31 (kama 11, roopa 16, aroopa 4)
eken roopawachara 16 , hewath brahma thala yedena hati.

roopawachara dyana sith anubawayen thamai wipaka sith lesa me than wala prathisandiya labanne.

roopawachara dyana wisthara karanawa akara 2k tiyenawa.
1)panchaka naya (naya kiyanne wistharaya kiyana eka)(5ka wishtharaya)
2)chathukka naya (4ka wistharaya)

mehema bedenna hethuwa,  roopawachara thala 16, kotas 4ta bedala katha karanne.
me thala 16ta yanna puluwan dyaana akara dekak 2k tiyenawa 
eka thamai panchaka naya, chathukka naya kiyala kiyanne.

onima dyanayak heena, madyama, praneetha washayen warga kerenawa.
meka gana wenama katha karanna oni. (dyanaya washi karana karama)
danata skip karamu. (practice eka adu,madyama,wadi) kiyala hithagena yamu.

mulin,
panchaka naya gamu (roopawachara dyana sith 5. gana katha karanawa)
dyana sith bedanne,
dyana anga (chaithasika) anuwai.
 
1 dyanaya (withakka,wichara,preethi,sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha. 
2 dyanaya (wichara,preethi,sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha.
3 dyanaya (preethi,sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha.
4 dyanaya (sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha.
5 dyanaya (upekka,ekaagratha) kusala sitha. (sukha wenuwata upekka enawa)


chathukka naya ta anukulawa. (roopawachara dyana sith 4. gana katha karanawa)

1 dyanaya (withakka,wichara,preethi,sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha.
2 dyanaya (preethi,sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha. (2/3 dekama ekata ganne)
3 dyanaya (sukha,ekaagratha) kusala sitha.
4 dyanaya (upekka,ekaagratha) kusala sitha. 

ex:
bada gala -> dana gala -> nagitinawa
dana gala -> nagitinawa


dan loka 16, thala washayen (chathukka naya washayen)
1 thalya (brahma loka 3)
	- bhahma parisajjaya (dhanaya heena nam, methana)
	- bhahma purohitha (dhanaya madyama nam, methana)
	- maha bhahma (dhanaya praneetha nam, methana)
enam methanaya yanna 1 dyananya pramanawath. (eke heena /madyama/praneed sobawaya anuwa ihalata yama)

2 thalaya (brahma loka 3) (deveni dyanaya)
	- pariththaabaya (abaya kiyanne alokaya tikai)(heena)
	- appa-maanaabaya(alokaya madyamai)(madyama)
	- aabassara (alokaya godai)(praneethai)

3 thalaya (brahma loka 3) (thun wena dyanaya)
	- pariththa suba 
	- appamana suba
	- suba kinhaka

4 thalaya (brahma loka 7)
	- eka laga tiyenawa dekak (bohoma kittuwen tiyenne)
		- wehappala
		- asanyya
	- ekakata ekak udin tiyennawa 5k. (stack wela)(mekata kiyanawa suddawasa 5 kiyala)anagami uththamyo upadina tan. (yata idala udata kiyanne)
		- awiya
		- athappa
		- sudassa
		- sudassi
		- akanita

me ankanita brahma lokaye idala yodun 55laksha8000k athin aroopa thala pihitala tiyenawa.
ethanath 4k tiyenawa

aroopa thala 4 (meka dyana bedeyen nevi yanne)(4 weni dyanayen/anithama tibba ewa witharai. upekka, ekagratha) (meka aramunu karanne aramuna anuwa)
		- akasananchayathanaya ( akasaya aramunu karala)(akasaya ananthai kiyala -ganna kasinaya )
		- wynananchayathanaya ( hitha aramunu karala)(akasaya dakinne hithen nisa, hitha gana aramunu karnawa)
		- akinchanyayathanaya (akasaya nathi bawa)
		-newasayyanasayyayathanaya (aramunak aththeth natha naththeth natha) (methanadi sitha harima balawath)(ekagrathawaya methana harima prabalai, budunta pera niwana kiyala salakuwe methanata. rahathan wahanse, niroda samapaththiya labanne methanin obbata gihin.) (nirodha samapaththi suwayen wada innawa kiyanne, me sobawayenuth ain wela.)
		
	
dan api katha kale brahma loka 20 gana. (roopa 16, aroopa 4)

mewa opapathika uthpaththi. iruthu prathyen awasha karana wimana washayen pahala wenawa.
e loka wala , prithiya thamai ahara washyen ganne.
e ayage sobawayan gana dana ganna oni nam,

deega nikaye bhrahmajala sutharaya,
aggannya suthra,loka winasaya -> anagathansa suthraya adiya thula hoya ganna puluwan.


me loka wala ayusha gana katha karanne kalpa walain awrudu walin nevi.

kalpa akara thunai,
- anthak kalpayak
- asankya kalpayak
- maha kalpaya

kalpa gana katha karanakota manussa ayusha walata sakepshawa thamai katha karanne.
kanussayage ayusha, 
awrudu 10 (1x^1) -> asankeyak wenakan yanna puluwan (asankeiyak -> 1x^140)
manussayek 
1x^1 -> 1x^140 -> 1x^1 apuwahama - api kiyanawa annakkalpayak kiyala kiyanawa.
me yanne adu wena kale.
roughly
awrudu 100ta sarayak, awruddak adu wenawa. 
budun kala awrudu 100. ethana sita awduru 100ta ekak adu wenawa.
dan awrudu 2600 gihin, awrudu 26 adu karanna oni.
dan parama ayusha 74k wage.
me rate anuwa. thawa awrudu 6400kin , manussa parama ayusha 10 bahinawa.
guna dharma prihenawa.
guna dharma anuwa ayusha wadi wenawa.

annakkalpa 20k tiyenawa -> asankeiya kalpayakata
asankeiya kalpa 4k tiyenawa -> mahakalpayakata
