aggannya suthra, anagathansa suthraya).
eka methana karala therumak na

giya sare loka gana arambayak gaththu handa e gana dana ganna oni nam 
interesting nam epaththa thawa goyanna puluwan.
ape awashathaya keles duru karala niwan desata yomuweema
eka sadaha 
awashya pasu bima sakas kara ganna
ada padama balanna kalin, 
ලෝකය හටගැනිම අතිපුජ්‍ය කොත්මලේ කුමාරකස්සප ස්වාමින්වහන්සේ deshanawa ahala enna.

ada api katha karanne,
lokaya thula danumen issarahata nirwana margaya galapa ganne kohomada kiyala.

ada padama mulin
>karmaya / karma pala wala pera gaman karu dhrushtiya bawa therum ganeema.
eeta passe 
> e dhrushtiya anuwa sansara pawathma thamai api katha karanne.
> e danuma chiththa withi thulin dakkinne kohomada kiyala api katha karamu.


loka pilibada wishaya naththam sansaraya budun wahanse warnana kale na.
ekata hethuwa, e wistharaya jara maranayen nidahas weekamk nokarana nisa.

dan me hethu kiyala kiwwahama
sathwayage pawathmata hethu kiwwahama
api igena gena tiyenne loba, idwesha, moha , aloba, adesha, amoha kiyana hethu 6.

namuth,
sammuthiyedi 
sammuthi hethu adara ganna oni.

ex:
ginnnak nisa dumak athi awei.

mehi ginna nisa dumak athi wenawa wage yam yam dewal athi weemata 
karunu wena dewal walatath hethu kiyala api kiyana.

e hethu sammuthi hethu, enam sammuthiya thula sathyak.

dharmayedi e adahasa nevi denne.
e kiyanne ihatha hethu 6n adahas karanne ehema deyak nevi.
e kiyanne yam kisi deyak athi weemata balapana / upakari wena hethu nevei.

ex:
gasak polewe rada pawathinna mul upakara wenawa wage.
chiththa chaithasikayan hata aramune pihita sitimata 
upakari wena hethu dharma tikak.

lobaya idwsha moha yana darmatha arambanayan thadin kawaddana shakthiya / hakiyawa
thamai e thula tiyenne.
me chaithasikayan ha samprayuktha wana anekuth chiththa ,saha chaithasika
adala, eka aramunaka nosali pihitimata udaw karai.

ema nisa samprayuktha dharmayan eka aramunaka nosali sitimata 
upakara karanu dharmayan thamai, dharmayedi hethu lesa hadunwanne.

mewa sammuthi hethu nevi.
mewa muula hethu lesa hadunwanawa. (gahak polowata set wela tiyena wage)

ahethuka lesa kiyawunu sith 18 , hethu 6 nathiwa hata ganna ewa.
muulahethun nathi nisa e namin hadin uwa. 

e nam, muula hethu athi ewa sahethuka kiwwa. (71 hambenawa)
muula hethu nathi ewa ahethuka kiwwa . (18k hamuwenwa)

methandi api aduna ganna oni de thamai.
aramunak nathuwa sith upadinne na.

aramuna saha hethu athara difference eka poddak balamu.

aramuna sama witama adyathmika ayathana 6ta gochara wana bahira dharmatha.
enam 
roopa, shabda, ganda, rasa, isparshaya, dhamma
mewa thamai aramunu (aarammana kiyanne paliyen aramunu walata) 
e nisa 
rooparambanaya, shabda-rambanaya..etc
lesa hambenawa.

ethakota hethu washayen api katha karanne,
me gaththu aramune, sitha nosali tiya ganna hethu wana 
chaithasika shakthin enam dharamatha.
mewa 6k lesa apita hambenawa,
loba , idwesha, moha, aloba ,adwesha, amoha lesa e aramune sith saha samprayuktha dharma pihita sitimata upakari wenwa.


ex:
ginnak nisa dumak athi wei.
sammuthiya athule , eka hethuwak.
meka dharmayen dakinawa nam
meka dakke rooparambanayak widihata,
dakapu rooparambanaye 
sitha pihitimata, hethu dharmaya 6n ekak ho keepayak upakara weema nisa.
sith param parawa e muulayanta anukoola wenawa.

loba chaithasikaya pradana unoth,
ginna aramunu wenne chanda ragaya mul karagena. 
ginna nisa athi wana rasnayata kamathi wenna puluwan.
ginna nisa pichchenawata baya wenna puluwan.
ginne alokaya nisa ginna tiyenawata kamathi wenna puluwan.
ginna nisa bathak uyaganna puluwan lesa upakaraka dharmayak lesa dakinna puluwan.

enisa ekama ginna , aramunu wana hethu dharama anuwa wiwida pathikada walin drushti gatha wenawa.

me widihata baluwahama,
apage siyalu karmayanta 
mulika padanama wenne 
dhrushtiyai.

ex:
awidagena yanwa kiyanne kriyawak, ehema naththam karmayak. (karumayak nevi :P)
sammuthiye karumayak kiyala kiyanne wipakayakata.
eka gain ekak issara karamayakata.

awidan yana kriyawa, ehemaththam karmaya
deman handiyak (junction ekak) hamba unoth ya yuththe mona paredi
kiyala theeranaya kalata passe thamai gamana yanne.
patan gaththe yanne koheda kiyala theeranaya karala.
enam dhrushtiya mul wela action ekata kalin.
enam dhrushtiya hageemak, sithe kriyakarithwayak.
enam sitha mul wela karma ipadila.

ethakota 
lokaye pawathma pawathinne karmaya, karma pala walin kiyana wishwasayak thamai apita tiyenne.
dharamya soya gena yana kenekuta,
karma saha karma pala athi wena hethu lesa 
me dhrushti / sithe mulikathwaya hambenawa.

sitha pradana wela karmaya sakas wena nisa,
ape chinthanaya wenas kirima thulin,
enam awabodaya thulin sasara jaya ganna puluwan bawa 
therum ganna puluwan.

budun deshana karanwa
"awijja niroda sankara nirodo" kirala.
enam 
awiddawa niroda karapuwahama automatically sankaraya niroda wenwa.
enam ape focus eka awabodaya wardanaya kara ganeematama wiya yuthui.
eka bana padayak ho , awabodaya wadi kara ganeema ekathu kara gannama oni.
awasthawa hambena sama thanama.

awidyawen, ape pera tibba bawa siyallama wahala tiyenne.
pera widipu duk,sapa. pera kal tibunu awabodayan kisiwak
ada api ta na.
me awdiyawa tiyena kan . 31 ek thalaya thula,
wipaka nawathwanna ba.
dewani wasara ganithaya, ipida mari, nathwa ipadena samawitama igena gannawa,
ekama karmaya nawatha nawatha sithu wenwa, ihatha bawaya gana nodanuwath kama nisa.

me lesa bawayen bawayata ekama karmayan api kochchara ras karagena athi da ?

desk, banku , putu adi bawthika sadaka ekama unath,
panthiyen panthiyata ape awbodaya wenas.
awabodaye wardanayak thamai api sidu karaganimin pawathinne.

awboda wardanaya , bawaya thula sama da karagena tiyenne.

budu rajanan wahanse  ge kalayata perath,
 wimukthi kami samajayak tibuna,
 e aya eya danna wimukthiya sadaha sitha meheyawuwaa.
 aageewaka, paribrajaka, nigannta, jatila lesa me aya apita hambenawa.
 eayata niwana hambune na. awabodaya sewwa , danuma pawathuna namuth niwana hamu une na.
 e ayage niwana newa-sanyya-naa-sanyaayathanata.
 ehema hithanna hethuwa sithin yanna puluwan ihalama thana ethana handa.
 sitha itha prabalai ethanai, ayusha kalpa asu-haradahak.
 niwana lesa e aya hithuwe ethana.
 
niwana sahanda,
awabodaye wardanaya, karana prathipadawa hariyata dana ganna oni,
eka puluwan wenne sath dharma awabodayen witharamai.
wena widihak na.
niwan magata yana awabodaya thamai wadawiya yuththe. 
"ajjewa kichchan aathappan" - ada adama wirya karanna 
lesa thamai budun deshan karanne.

ex tikak balamu.

ex:
kawru hari thuruwan wiwechanaya karana kota kipimak athi unoth
anththarawa katada ? thamuntamai.
boho agam thula, aagame mulika padanama wishwasayai.
e wishwasata kawru hari garahanawa nam
ehema naththam wishwasa nokarana sobawaya
papayak, akusalayak lesa thamai penwanne.

e nisa wiwechanaya karana aya agamata patahani wirudda wadeen lesa salakanawa.
me wiwechanya karana aya samaga gateemen, e ayage sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wenwa.
raga , idwesha , moha wadi wenwa.
sasare pawathma sidu wenawa.
eken thamanta wena antharawa danne na.
agame namayen thama sansara gatha wenawa. (akusala sangrahayama hodin sidu wela)

esema agame guna ganaya thula ipileema /sathuweema athi unoth
aththarawa katada ? thamuntamai.

ara agamata wada ape agama hodai, uthum, logical
ehema kiyala sathutu wenawa. enam mannayak athi kara gannawa.
ekath sansara gathai, 

enam raga idwesha moha niwanata adala wennema na.
enam hoda kiwwath sathutu wenna ba, waradi kiwwath duk wenna ba.

enema kohomada api niwana sadaha antharawak nowana widihata 
hasirenne?

meka karanne sanwegayak thulin. enam me sobawaya e dharmatha wala hati
meka podi dharmathayak lesa dakinna oni.

ex: 
marana gedarakata giya, lagama nyathiyek.
dan miniya dika balala hugak aya adanawa.
maranaya jeewath wena kenkuta uruma sobawayak
mamath me sobawya ikmawala na.
pawathina sobawayan ge hasirima ka prathipalayak pamanai.
lokayama duka matha pihita athi ba budun deshana karanne e nisa,

e nisa lokayama jara maranayen nidahas na.
e nisa duka urumai.
melesa sonwegaya upadawa ganna api purudu wenna oni.

e sanwegaya thula,
aleemak na, gateemak na, mulawak na
mohayak nowana madyastha sobawayak thamai pawathinna oni.
ethkota antharawak na.
meyai pilipadiya yuththe.

sanwegayakadi , pradana washyen upekka chaithasiyake aka akarayak thamai kriyathmaka wenne.
(upkesha chaithasika 10k tiyenawa - meka api katha karala tiyenawa)


me widihata,
aleema, udagu kama, uthdamaya, ipileema, manaya
mewa okkoma thanahawa thulin sadunu dewal.
thanawa = samudaya athyatai.
enam mewa dukata hethu.


dharmaya nodanna aya atharath,
usas chinthakawadeen, niwahal chinthayakan sitinawa.
me aya , kisiyam mathawadayak wuwaa nam e sadaha hethu prakasha kala.
boho wita mewa 
sasrutha hari uchcheda dhrushti thula thamai pawathinne.
methanath hethu pala sambanda pawathinawa.
namuth me siyalla 
lokaya thulai,
enisa 
budu rajanan wahanse mewa 
sammuthi sathya lesa penwa dunna.

ethkota kenek, ge wiwida dhrushtin matha 
karana prakasha, actions walin 
thamage sitha thula raga idwasha moha athi nowana widihata 
kriya kala yuthui.
enam akusalayata sangraha nokala yuthui.


muula padartha rasiyaka athi santhathiya. (ekata galaayaama)sobawaya
padanam kara gena thamai,
api roopa , wedana , sanyya, sankara , wynyana yana dharmatha wydyamana wenne.
(meka api paramartha jathika dharma waladi igena gaththa)
gathi sobawayan lesa mewa api haduna gaththa.


budu rajanan wahansege 
erdi wishayath
sathwa wishayath
loka wishayath
karma wishaya

yana dharmatha achintheeya dharmatha lesa hadun wanawa. ( e kiyanne sithala kelawak karanna ba)
 e nisa sama witama hithanna puluwan dewal gana witharai hithanna puluwan. (danna de gana pamanai hithanna puluwan.)
 kawadawath nohithapu ( ayathana 6ta gochacra nowu kisiwak apita hitha ganna ba)
 e nisa samawitama ape awabodaya ayathana 6 thulin thamai ganna hadanne.
 e nisa lokaya ayathana 6 wata pawathinawa.
 
 achitheeya wishayan, ayathana 6 thulin awaboda kara gatha nohakie.
 ewata atheen-indriya nyanaayan upadawa gath budda wachanayata ahukam denna oni.
 

ex:
sakwithi rajunta (shakra deviyo) , punyawantha erdi balayak tiyenwa
e kiyanne atham pudgalayanta pihitana suwusheshi shaktheen.
e kiyanne eyata punya shakthiya thulin erdiyen gaman yanna puluwan.
(ahasin gaman karanna puluwan
bawudda sahithye hambennawa , budun baha dakinna sharya deviyan manussa lokayata wadiya than
gana.
namuth meka ape danumata gochara na.
mokada methek kalayak dana gena hitapu hethu thulin meka withara karaganna ba.
e nisa meka prathihaariyak kiyala kiyanawa. (api laga tiyena facts walin describe karanna ganna ba)

dan kenek gena ahuwoth meka wenne kohomada kiyala eka bawthikawa pennanna ba
enam eka erdi wishayak. ( erdi wishaya gana awabodayak tiyenna oni)

ex:
budunta tibba arya erdiya , ( wyree aramunata erehiwa mythriya pathiraweeme hakiyawa)
nalagiri damanaya - math karapu atha damanaya.

ex:
manomaya erdiya ( manomaya shareera mawa penweeme hakiyawa)
budu rajanan wahanse erdiyen thawthisa diwaya lokayedi abidharmaya deshana kirima sadaha
mano maya shareerayak mawa pennuwa.


me widihata bawudda sahithyaye udaharana oni tharam hambenawa.
api therum ganna oni de 
erdi wishaya achinthayai, namuth e dharmatha awabodaya soya yama thula niwana na.
e hakiyawan gana thama thamage danum mattama anuwa maneemen,
sakaya, wimathiya, prathikshepaya  athi kara ganna hoda na.

mokada , sakaya, wimathiya, prathikshepaya thulin buddadi ata than kerehi athi wana sakaya nisa sowan margaya nyanaya wahenawa.

e nisa 
achinthaya wishayan,
apita hithanna puluwan saha hithanna bari lesa dharmatha athi bawa
awboda mattama anuwa wena karanawa.
me siyalla niwan dakimata adala na.

eelagata balamu, chanawa gana
drushtiya mathu karana chathana .

api katha kara , karmayata pradana wenne drushtiya kiyala. drushtiyata pradama wenne chathanawa kiyala.

chathana kotas 2i.
1) sahajatha chethana (siyalu sith walata athi wana chethana, sabba chiththa sadarana chaithasika lesa api katha kala. mokada sithak ekkama athi wenawa)
2) nanaththa chethana ( sugathi/dugathi wala sapa duk laba dena chethana) 


wipaka sith 32 + kriya sith 20 = sith 52
e sith 52 tiyena chethana mathu wipaka dena ewa nevei.
wipaka sithak kiyanne kalin karapu karamayaka wipakayak.
yali karmayak ein karanna ba.
e wagema 
kriya sithak kiyanne awyakrutha sith ( kusal / akusal katha nokarana sith)

ehenam me sith 52 ma mathu wipaka na.
enam me sith samaga shakthi kriya karithwayak sidu wenne.
chiththa , chaithasika dharmayan kriyakarithwayata pamunuwanne chethanawa wisin.
eya thamai hethuwa.
"chathana ham kamman wadami" - kiyala deshawadi pawasanne me dema thamai.

ethkota 
mathu wipaka dena chethana tiyenne 29k pamanai.
eka athi wenne 
akusal sith 12+ laukika sith 17 ( maha kusal 8, roopawachara kusal sith 5, aroopawachara kusal sith 4) 

ehenam , chethawa pradana kota  hata gath karmaya enam mathu wipaka dena shakthiya aththe
me sith 29ta pamanai.

awidya pachchaya sankara kiyala kiwwahama
sankaraya kiyala kiyanne menna me sith 29ta. enam sith wala pawathina chethanwata
api meka 
punyabi sansakara (maha kusal 8)
apunyabi sanskara (akusal sith 12)
anenjabi sansakara (roopawachara kusal sith 5, aroopawachara kusal sith 4)
kiyala beduwe. 

sansakarayai chethanawai athara sambandaya 
ehema naththam
awiddaya pachchaya sankara kiyana eka sith walin igena gaththa.

me awabodaya itha wadagath. dharamaya adunganna 
me sambandaya dana ganna oni 
meka apita abhidharmaya asuru kirima thulin.
enam abhidharamye watinakama pasak wenwa.
dharma awabodaye gabura, abhidharmaya thulinma thamai hamu wenne.

e nisa dharmaya gambeerai , durawabodai lesa hadunwanawa.

e wagema , abhidharamaya thawthisa diwya thalaye di , maathru diwya rajaya
athulu diwya pirisata thawthisa welawen, winadi 9k thula siyalla nonawathwa deshana kala. 
meya manussa lokaye kala nam dina 90k yanwa. minisunta ekadigata dawas 90 inna ba.
meka sidu kale thawsithawa thula budu ruwak mawala deshanawa karanna ida deela.
budun wahanse diwa aharaya sadaha sama dinakama , wadala 
budda upasthanaya sadaha wadapu sarayuth rahathan wahanseta deshan kala 
sarayuth rahathan wahanse golayo 500kata deshana kala.
e lesa abhidharmaya lokayata hambuna.

"eka una kohomada" kiyala ahathdima api 
me achintha wishaye alila , sakaye galila. mokada e dharmayo wada karana sobawaya gana 
nodanuwath kama nisa.

dan balamu 
chethanawa kohomata chiththa withiyakata sambanda wenne kiyala 

apita mathakai
aramunak gana katha karanakota 
pancha idwara chiththa withiyak ekka anubanda chiththa withi 4k yanwa kiyala 
aramuna dana ganna.
 
me mano idawarika chiththa withi 4re awasan chiththa withiyaedi 
lassanai, waninawa ... kiyala loba sithak nam pahala une
akusala chethanawa purnaya wela.
me widihata hata ganna chaithasikaya anuwa purnaya wena 
chethana sobawaya mathu wipaka janitha karanawa.

e 4 weni anubandaka chiththa withiyata api namak dunna 
"karma sadana chiththa weethiya kiyala"
mokada e 4weni mano idwarika chiththa withiya thamai
sobana sithak ho asobana sithak hadanna upakari wenne.
e nisa e chiththa withiya thula 
akusala ho kusala chethanawak purnaya wela.

 ex:
 cake gediyak marena mohothe mathak unoth.
 e gana dadi loba sithak awoth. enam kamashawak athi unoth.
 loba gathi sobawayak thamai athi wela tiyenne (paramarth jathika dharamyak)
 e nisa 
 hithe sahalluwa na wela, sitha bara gathiya wadi wenawa. pancha kamayata alila
 me sithe bara gathiya wisin
 e loba gathiyata adala , ebadu indriyan pawathinna puluwan thanak thamai 31 thalaya thula hambenne.
 api cake gediya aramu kale , e aramuna ganna puluwan wu indriya sobawayan ge pawathma thulamai. enam e gathi sobawaya athi wanna , e indriyan ge pawathma aniwaryen tibiya yuthui.
 e nisa 
 thirisan, pretha, asura, niraya (sathara apaya) thaka uthpaththiya janitha wenawa.
 
 dadi loba kamen, masuru kamen marenne , manussa bawayen unath
 marena mohothe manussa mattama athi kramanaya karala thirisan mattamata gihin.
 
 enam  dadi lobaya kiyanne thirisan mattamata aithi gathiyak.
 
 
 ex:
 budun kala sitiya , thodeiya bamuna kiyala masurek.
 eya hambena kisi deyak noka,nobi ithuru kala. winasa kale na.
 daruwatath loba kama purudu kala.
 karanna aya ayawath walakkuwa.
 meya maruna. budun kerehi pahadune na.
 meya pallek wela ipaduna. (thirisan apaye)(thirisan gathiya mulika wela)
 budun dakkahama , budunta buranna gaththa.
 budun ahanawa . "thodeiya oba ekaleth biruwa , adath buranwa neda"
 
 loba gathiya thulin apaya thula uthpaththiya labuwa.
 
 ex:
 e cake gediyama thawa kenek hithanwa ,
 mage kusaginnath niwa ganna puluwan 
 wena kenekge kusa ginnath niwa ganna puluwan deyak widihata.
 
 eka mona gathiyak da ? beda hadagena kana gathiyak.
 matath labayak, anuntath labayak.
 eka manussa gathi sobawayak 
 prarthakami sobawayan /chiththayan samawitama manussa gathiyak.
 e gathiyata anuwa uthpaththiya.
 
 ex:
  e cake gediyama mata nolabunath,
  dayawa karunawa pradana karagena wena kata hari laba dunnahama,
  sithe sahallukama wadi wenwa.
  dharma gochara, prakna gochara margaya wadana aya meya puja kara sithak athi unoth 
  eya sahallu sithak thamai athi wenne.
  sahallu sithak nam 
  thamawa athi kramanaya karapu gaheemakata
  enam e gathiya anuwa uthpaththiya diwya thalayak.
  
  ex:
  e cake gediye ma adinawa dakinawa.
  e cake gediyama kawoth meke wena kriyawa dakinawa.
  ekata tiyena pancha kama arasayen ath wenawa.
  e panchakamayen athwena gathiya nisa 
  eyata dyaana upadinawa
  enam pancha neewaran yatapath wenawa.
  ethkota uthpaththiya adala dyana thala wala upadinawa.
  
 ex:
 cake gediyath roopayak, me roopaya hamuwe
 niwana awaboda kara gannata 
 gatha yuthu prathipadawa
 desata yomu weema thamai karaganna oni.
 (meya prathyaksha kirimata nam budda wachanayata ahukam denna oni)
 (meka very important, ethenata thamai api enna oni e nisa eka 
 in detail wenama katha karamu.)
 
	
 me udaharanaya olarika udaharanayak pamanayai. arthaya allaganna balanna
udaharanaya nathuwa.

 summary eka gaththoth,
 
 mechchara wela katha kala karmaya saha chethanawa athara sambanadaya 
 saha achitha wishaya patha. wipaka awasath gana.
 
 wipaka awasatha gana katha karankota sith wala kruthya wadagath wenawa.
 
 (ahethuka sith 18n,
 upeka sahagatha santheerana sith 2) + maha wipaka 8 + mahag gatha wipaka 9 = sith 19
 karyaya (kruthya) thamai
 prathisandiya, bawanga, chuthi kiyana sith hadana eka. (enam kruthya 3k)
 
 enam me sith 19 thamai prathisandiya, bawanga, chuthi lesa apita hambenne.
 habai eka warakara ekai. (eka wadai/ eka kruthyai)
 
 pancha-idwara wajjana sithai +  mano-idwara wajjana sitha = sith 2-
 me sith 2 sidu karanne awarjana kruthya. eka warakata ekai.
 (kuburu kotana kenama schoole ugannawa, ekata karanna ba. multiple jobs karanna puluwan)
 
 chakku wynana sith 2i (ahethuka sith wipaka sith)(akusala  / kusala wipaka chakku wynanaya)
 me sith 2n karanne darshana kruthya.
 
 sotha wynana sith deken -> shrawana kruthya
 ghaana wynaana sith 2 -> aagrahana kruthya
 jwha wyaana sit h2 -> aswadana kruthya (rasaswadana kruthya nisa api kiyanawa aswadana kruthya)
 kaya wynyaana 2k -> isparshana kruthya (pottabba kruthya kiylath hadunwanawa)
 santheerana sith 3k tiynewa -> santheerana kruthya (kusala 2 (upeka/somanassa sahagatha santherana), akusala paththe 1 (upkka sahagatha withrai) santheerana kruthya
 
 mano idawara wajjana sith 1k -> woththapana kruthya. (junction ekak hambethdi decide karana sitha) (chiththa withi yedi kusala /akusala theeranaya kranne meya)
 
 akusal sith 12 + 
 hasitha uthpada sith 1+ 
 maha kusal 8 + 
 maha kriya 8+ 
 mahag gatha kriya 9 +
mahag gatha kusal 9 + lokoththara sith 8 = total eka 55 wenwa mekata kiyanwa jawana kruthya .


methana mathaka tiyaganna oni.

akusal sith 12 + 
hasitha uthpada sith 1+ 
maha kusal 8 + 
maha kriya 8+ 
mahag gatha kriya 9 +
mahag gatha kusal 9 = sith 47 me siyalu sith wipaka sith nevi.

lokoththara sith 8 gaththdi e thula keles na. e kiyanne ewa uparima pirisidui. me sith ata  (marga 4i, pala 4i lesa ganne) prathisandiya laba dena sith nevei. mewa niwan labana sith
sasaren ethara wena sith. 
wipaka prathisandiya labena saha nolabena lesa akara dekakin katha karanawa.
eka siyalu wipakasith 36k kiyala katha karanawa.
namuth lokoththra sith prathisandiyak nolabena wipaka sith enam pala sith lesa hadunawa. 
me pala sith walinuth 
jawan kruthya kala haka eka nisa thamai jawan sith gonnata danne.

ara sith 47 + lokoththara sith 8 = janan kruthya karana sith lesa gannawa.


maha wipaka 8 + santheerana 3  = sith 11 , thadarambana kruthya karanawa. (duwala duwala nawaththanna giyahama ath iwana sith)

methan tiyena santheerana sith 3thuna satheerana kruthya karanwa,
eken dekak prathisandiya laba denawa (upeka 2) kiyala api issella katha
 me thun thadarambana kruthyath karanwa kiyala api katha kala.
 
 e nuwa 
 upeka sahagatha santheerana sith 2n, kruthya 5k karanwa (prathisandi , bawanga, chuthi, santheerana , thadarambana)
 ewa ahethuka unata,
 karanna tiyena wade lokui.
 
 mahag gatha wipaka sith 9k -> prathisandi, bawanga ,chithi kruthya
 somanassa sahagatha santheerana sith -> santheera , thadarambana kruthya
 mano idwara wajjanayen -> woththapana, awarjana kruthya 

 summary eka gaththahama 
 ekama eka kruthyak pamanak karana sith
 
 jawan sith 55 + pancha idwara wajjana 1 + sampattijana sith 2 + depas wyaana sith 10 ( ahethuka gonne kusala/akusala 8 + somanassa/domanassa sahagatha kaya wyaanaya) = 68 sith
 
 me sith 68 thamai , thani kruthyak niyojana karanne.
 anith ewa kruthya dekathunak kirime hakiyawa tibbata 
 warakadi kranne eka kruthyak pamanai.
 
 ada api me anthimata igena gaththe kruthya sangrahayai.

 ---------------------- Budda wachanaya haduna ganeema ----------------------17/09/2021
 
  ape uthsahaya , pruthakjanan lesa me dharamaya wimanasa eka,
  ethkota lokaya thulin thamai me prathipawa gana katha karanna wenne.
  ehema katha karanakota , ohuta ethera weemak wenna oni.
  habai lagala inna ho ehema basa ganeemak memei. ( ehema wenna pudgala sobawayak tiyenne oni).
  enam kenek allala me deshanwa sidu kalata , e kenata , kenawa nirudda wela ethara weemak 
  pawathinna oni.(e kena ethana basa gaththoth, ethara weemak sidu wela na)
 
  anithya,dukka, anathma kiyana dharmatha yedethdi. ( hambawethdi novei)
  yedenawa kiyanneth hambewenawa kiyanneth dekak (hambenna mama inna epai)
  
  anithya,dukka, anathma kiyana dharmatha yedethdi, budurajanan wahanse
  e yedena akaraya/prathipadawa ismathu kala.
  

  
anna e wage sakkaya dittiya noridaya pilibanda nyanayak, nuwanak awadi weemak thamai gaweshanaya thula
sidu wiya yuththe.
e nisa,
ape prayathnaya, sakkaya dittiya mathu nowana akarayata , enam kenek,thanak,deyak,pudgalayek nowana lesa me dharmathawan desata yomu weemai. meka kara ganna kohomada kiyala thamai ada api katha karanna hadanne.

enam budu rajanwahanse deshanawa desata,  sakkaya dittiya mathu nowana akarayata yomu wenne kohomada kiyana eka thamai balanna hadanne.
meka wenne sakkaya dittiya noridaya pilibanda nyanayak awadi kara ganeema thulin.

e nisa ,
anithya,dukka, anathma kiyana dharmatha yedethdi (hamba wethdi novei)
budu rajananwahanse ismathu karapu prathipadawa practically adura ganna/dakinna hadamu.

budu rajanan wahanse apita penwala dunne,
lokaya kiyala haduna gaththa swabawaya thula, laga ganeemak hari ringa ganeemak hari 
ismathu novi,
lokayen etharaweema kiyana prayogika prathipadawak karaganne kohomada kiyala thamai
buduhamuruwo penwa denne.

ehenam lokaya therum gamu
lokaya kiyanne mama kiyana padanama samaga (e foundation eka uda)
mamen thorawa lokayak gana katha karanna puluwanda ?
katha kirima, wigraha kirima, hithana dewal. (lokaya pudgalayan karana kiyana hithana oni deyak)
lokaya ismathu wenne e dewal thulin.
lokaya athule e kriya eka eka widihata karana prathipada apita oni tharam hambela tiyenwa.
samaharu eka eka prathipada purudu karala ewata talent eka kiyala kiyanawa 
ex: music instrument ekak play karanawa wage. mal puja karanwa, gaman yanawa..

ehenam ehema ismathu wana yam prathipadawak (lokaya thula sakas karagath prathipada)
budun wahanse deshana kala prathipawak wiya nohaki.
kima da , 
lokaya thula athi wana prathipada, samawitama lokayathula hamuwana dewal samaga, naththam
mama kiyana padaname sita hamu wana dewal.)
mama samaga hamuwana dewal sakkaya dittiya poshanaya karanawa.
enam budda wachanayata idak na.

budda dharmaya thuladi , ethara wenawa kiyala karanaya athule
sithanna , katha krannata, idak nathi bawak
prathipadawen ismathu wenna oni.

eyai  budun penwu dharmaya thula nirodaya lesa widyamana wenne.
habai e nirodaya prathyaksha kara ganna loku nuwanak awashyai.
ethkota apita me dharmaye gabura awaboda wenna patan gannawa.

api hugak kamathi, niwaradi, hari deyak labenawata.
dharmaya thulath, eka eka deshana thulin me widihatama niwaradi , nirwachana ,
pahadili kirim, thamanta hamu wenawa nam thamai kamathi.
thamanta wena kenekuta meka wisthara karanna puluwan wena tharamata 
kamathie.

enam thama thaman, lokaye ringa ganna, bahaganna ehema naththam laga ganna 
thamai hama tissema kamaththa.
ethara wenna kamathi wela na.
ethara wemata wada ekathu karaganeemata kamaththa.

ese yamak ismathu nowana dharmayak pahadili karathdi
mukuth ismathu nowana nisa 
ekata kan yomu karanne na.

lokaye ethara wana dharmayama,
prayogikawa yedima thulin
api hoyanne, thawath ek wadapiliwelak. (prathipadawak, loka thula inna ekak)(ethara weema nevi)
anna e hageemata thamai kamaththa.
e nisa sitha namenne na budun ge deshanawa desata.

menna me widihata ape sithe pawathina abyanthara sidu weemak nisa.
monawa hari widihakata, thama thaman ta labenna thamai kamaththa.
me siyallen ikmenna oni kiyana adahasa thula hari 
innai kamathi. ethara wenna nevei.

enam ethula laga gena monawa hari thawa aluth deyak ganna thamai
kamaththa.

lokaya thula laga gena inna eka hoda na kiyana idea ,
eka thahawuru karanna inna thamai kamaththa.
me widihata 
eka eka ewa ain kara kara, prathipadawa wenas kara kara
awabodaye wenasa gana katha kara kara 
inna thamai kamaththa.
namuth 
lokaye inna eka ain karala na.

Budu rajanan wahanse lokaya pahala wela,
meme siyallama ikmawana dharmayak deshana kala
menna meyai durlabha.

prayogikawa ethara wena widihak kawadawath lokeyen ismathu wenne na.
habai,
atheethaye wimukthikaamin siti awadiyaka thamai mewani dharmayak pahala une.

ada samajaya thula e wimukthikaamin itha durlabhai.
jeewithaya athulen ena prashna hodata hithala,
monawa hari dekata kotu wela hitapu,  e atheetha pudgalayo
sapa , duka , thaman karapu deyak da kiyala ahala tiyenawa.

dan, niwaradi chinthayak tibuna kenek asiya yuththe,
sapa, duka labune ai ? misak karanne kawda kiyala nevi.

enam sapa duka thaman nisada , anith aya nisada , naththam api degollo nisada 
naththam ibe hata gaththu deyak da kiyala 

kenek, me question eka ahanne , e ayage anawabodaya handa.
namuth wimukthiya soyana , thama thulin wimukthiya soyanna nosagenna try karapu
kattiya.

budun deshana karanwa - mama ese wadaranne na.
sharima short answer ekak.

budun rajanan wahanse me awasthawe di asa, roopa , wynaana gana kathawak deshana kale na.
sarala uththarayak dunne.

e sarala uththaraye gabura haduna ganna puluwan praknawak tiyena ayata thamai me deshana karanne.
methana , 
wimukthikaamin,
question eka ahuwe e ayege awabodayata sapekshawa.
question hadila tiyenne e  aya danna dewal thulin.
sapa duka kiyanna matabena dewal, sapa duka athare
mama saha anun pawathinawa. ehenam sapa duka hamu wenna api okkoma handa da 
naththam ibe da.
me okkoma prashna , e kattiyege awabodaya anuwa wimasala,
ewa base kara gena thamai ahala tiyenne.

budun dena sarala uththara athule,
mama ese pawasanne na kiyala kiwwahama
question eka saha question eka athi unu base eka kiyana dekatama 
budu rajanwanhanse uththara sapayanawa.

e wage,
apith prashna ahanne ape base eke idala,
ape danumata sapekshawa, api igena gaththu subject eka haraha.
ape dharma question sakas wenne 
api danata allagaththu concepts anuwa.
e concepts ekka thamai api bana ahanne.

bana ahanawa kiyanne danna concepts confirm kara ganeemada ?

api danna wachana roopa, wedanaa, asa,wynaana...etc
kiyala danna wachana tikak dala , e tika anuwa hithanna / galapanna
purudu wela.
ethkota budun wadala dharamaya ahenne na.
mokada ahagena inna kota awadanaya deshanawa kerehi nevi,
api galapanna thamai awadanawaa,
dharmaya ahana oni kama tiyenne danna de wadi kara ganna 
ayeth lokaya thula.
enam 
dharmaya ahanna oni kama adura gena na.

e nisa apith 
ara wimukthikaamain wage (anya theerthikayo)
prashana aha aha innawa.
sapa duka jeewithe yedune naththam, ebadu prasha na,
mokada e sambanda puruddak nathi nisa.

enam 
niyama prashnaya api thulin mathu wena thak kal
apita hithanna sidu wenawa.
enam 
hithanna oni gathiya ain kara ganna hoda na.
(enam ahana hama dema hithanne nathu aseema thulin, drusthi gatha weema walakka ganna ba)
tak gala ena handa (hithanna idak na),
drushti prathyaksha karaganna hadana ratawak/puruddak witharamai api gawa tiyenne.
ekath ayeth lokaya thula mai.
laga ganeemak, basa ganeemak, padinchi weemak pamanamai.
ethara wela na.

budu himi pennuwe,
sapa duka pattichcha samuppannai kiyala.

meka ahuna gaman, api danna wachana set eka automatically apply karagannawa.
api danna pada uthum wela. ewa galapa galapa mathaya isthira karagannawa.
budun pawasana deta kan yomu wenne na.
hitha athule full gamak haganawa,
hitha athule wena witharka walata kotu wela.

budu rajanan wahanse penwa wadaale,
hethuwakin hata gannawa kiyalai pennuwe.
enam 
sapa/duka kiyana eka 
mamawath, anunthwath, degollanwath, ibe wath
nowa 
hethuwak nisa hata ganna bawa thamai pennuwe.

enam hata ganeemak kiyana dharamathawa thamai mathu kale.

ethkota sapa ho duka kiyana karnawa yedenne ai.
e prashnaya thama ismathu wenna oni.

ex:
oba swameen wahanse namak gen banak ahanawa.
swameen ahanse shrawakayan gen ahanawa 
"bana ahanawa" kiyana kaaranawa pahadili karala denna kiyala.
oyala mokada dena uththaraya.

youtube eken, radio eken, dharma sachchawakin ahanawa kiyala 
nirwachanayak dei.

e hama situation ekakama, oyabath innawa, swameen wahanseth wada innawa.
aheema sidu wena akaraya anuwa 
nirwachanayakuth tiyenawa. (zoom call ekakda , youtube da..etc)
methanadi bana ahanawa kiyana karnawa sidu wela da ?

inna mamai ahena banai ekka thamai wigraha karagaththe.
namuth prashnayata hari uththaraya deela na.

prashnaya : bana ahanawa kiyanne mokadda kiyala wigraha karanna kiyana eka.
namuth ape wigrahaya
inna mamai ahena banai ekakkai

ahanawa kiyana eka wisthara wela na.
aduma tharame ahanawa kiyana eka gana hithanawa hiya lan welawath na

ex:
api kama kanawa.
kanawa kiyana eka pahadili karanna.

atha paya holawala, age kriyakarithwayai,
bahira dewal, bath,kama
sambanda karala uththara denawa

eken kanawa kiyana eka pahadili karalada ?
math ekai thamunui wen karala tiyethdi
kanawa kiyana karnawa katha karanna puluwanda ?
mamai, bath ekai ekata ho wenama tibba kiyala kanawa kiyana eka
wisthara karanna puluwan da ? ba.
karnawa kiyana ekata nirwachanayak nathi handa 
eka wisthara kara gannawa api danna dewal walin.

menna me widihata thamai,
kanawa,
ahenawa,
dakinawa,
kiyanawa..etc
wage dewal api wisthara gena tiyenne.

namuth ewa hari nirwachana nevei.

kanne nathuwa innakota , kama piganath tiyenawa, kenath innawa
kanwa wigraha karanna ba.

kanawa kiyana eke api dunnu nirwachanaya hari nam.
e hethu wenama pawathiddi,
eka wisthara karana puluwan wenna oni.
but ehema ba.

namuth eke base eka balapuwahama,
api kanawa kiyana eka wishthara karan tiyenne 
ape base eka wechcha
tiyenawa innawa kiyana matha athulin.
e base uda idan thamai
ape nirwachanaya karagena tiyenne.

mama innakal, kama tiyena kal. 
mama deyak karana kal. 
ehema naththam
kaye kriyawai, bahira wasthuwai  wage monawa hari ekathu karan
kanawa kiyana eka wigraha karanne ai.

mewa thulin kanawa kiyana eka wigraha karanna ba.
kanawa kiyanne mekai, menna me widihatai
kiyala base ekak nathuwa wigraha karanna ba.

ehenam 
me mohothe idala, meka karanna ba.
wishthara karanne inna kenekui, tiyena dekui
ehema naththam , atheethaya thula pawathuna deyak (permanant)
sambanda karagena 

atheethaya thula permanant wechcha mamek, saha bath ekak padaka karagena 
me mohothe sidu wanna wu deyak wisthara kara gena.
me pachchuppanna kriyawata nirwachanayak, lokaya thulin na
namuth 
atha ossanawa , katata dagannawa 
aadi washayen , nithya karaaththu base uda idan 
nirwachanaya karagannawa.

mokada kanawa kiyana karnawata lan weemata wath bari nisa.

dan kanne nadda ? ahenne nadda ?
mewa wena dewal nevida ?

apita kan ahenawa, kama kanawa
e dekama sidda wena dewal.
habal apita ewa base walin pita wisthra karaganna ba.
nirwachanya base ekak pita deeganna hakiyawak aththema na.

dharmayen deyak igena gaththuhama,
e base eka uda idan , eke padinchi wela 
nirwachana gaha gannawa.

api lokaye tiyenne me widihata hitha gaththu base tikak. hithalu tikak.
namuth mularambaya eka nevi.

kenek, hodata me gana hithuwoth. (wiwida pathi walin)
eyata 
hitha athulen prashnayak enawa.
pennanna bari
labenna bari
pahadili karanna bari
siddyak tiyenawa.

kanawa ahanawa kiyala wachanayak tiyenawa.
e kriyadamaya mokadda kiyala kiyala hariyata danne na.

ethkota mokadda e , kohomada eka wenne kiyala 
oni kamak athi wenawa. (enthusiasam ekak)
soyanna oni kamak athi wenawa

jiwithaya gana melesa soyanna ,
me point eka upakaarayak wenawa neda.

melesa hithennath, ketharam tiyunu nuwanak awadi karagatha yuthuda ?
dharmaye siyum ba kethram balawath da ?

api karana siyalu sidu kirim, thula athi 
kriyawa ta pahadili kirimak na.
eka mokadda kiyala danne na.
habai sidu weemak tiyenwa.

menna me widihata hithanna gaththahama thamai , 
ai mehema wenne kiyala prashnayak mathu wenne.

ethkota thamai me dharmaya thawa thawath gaweshanaya karanna hitha denne.

ex:
punchi kale ipadichcha babek.
kirima deyak danne na.
eyage athule eyage tharka na.
eya language ekak igena ganne.
amma saha thaththa kiyana eka desata namila thamai ahunkam denne.
katha kirimata athi oni kama handa thamai language eka igena ganne.
e oni kama, soyana kota , eyata ena prashnaya thamai
ai ei,
ai ehema wenne,
ai ehema kiwwe.
amma ho thaththa dena mathayan, eyata therena widihata galapenawa nam,
eyath e matha thula idan , sithanna podda podda purudu wenwa.
amma putuwata putawa putuwa kiyanawa nam
lamayath ekata putuwa kiyala kiyanna patan gannawa.
eka putuwa kiyala thahawuru kara gannawa.
eke laga gannawa, padinchi wenawa.
ai ekata putuwa kiyanne kiyana prashnaya ahanne na.
e prashnayata ida kuth na.
mul kale e prashnaya ahuwath.
demapiyantath eka wishthara kara ganna bari nisa.
eka ehema thamai kiyala , 
dakka de dakka kena,
ahuwa de, haduna gaththa hageema kiyala sithara karagannawa.

jiwithe kriyawan, 
dakinawa, ahanawa, danenawa, hitha gannawa kiyana base eka 
wisthara karaganna yanne na.
mokada ethanata lan weematath 
hakiyawak na.

balanna kochchara asaranada kiyala.

dan ethkota hithanna pelabenawa 
mokadda me,
kohomada wenne,
ai mehema wenne.

kiyala hithanna pelabenawa 
habai uththara na

nirwachanayak nathi mebadu kriya kara kam mokadda ?
onna dan thamai api
e kale hitapu wimukthi kameen hithapu thanata awe.

uththara nathi asarana kama nisa thamai 
e aya budun ge dharmaya dihawata yomu wenne.

budun pahadili kara dharma pariyaaya ta yomu unata passe
e gollo hodata hitnawa,
kalpana karanawa 
thaman ge jeewithyata mula wenne nathuwa
hodata kalpana karana gathiya 
ismathu karagath ayata 
deshana kala karunu thamai,
budda wachanaya lesa hadinwenne.

e pahadili karana dharmaya thamai patichchasamuppa darmaya.
meka hethuwakin hata gaththu palayak.
e nisa 
prayogika patipadawak lesa yomu wenna oni.

lokaye ayata watahenawa nam, lokayata aithie neda ?
enema ekata lokoththara kiyanna ba neda ?
enam 
e pahadili kirima lokaya aithi wenna ba.

e nisa budda wachana api lokoththara lesa hadunawanawa.
e dharamya lokayen ethara weema sadaha pamanamai.

upadina, dirana, marena , leda wena , wayasata yana aadhi
siddi ,
jiwithaya athule hamuwana dharmathath
hethu pala dharamathawayata anukulai.

api nitharama mula wela nirwachanayak nathi mebadu kriya walata 
lokaya thulin nirwachana dapu nisa 
prashna athi kara gena .

ledak kiwwahama kenek matha kara gannawa
marenawa kiwwahama mama, danna kenek mathak karaganna
karanawa pudgalagek ekathu karagannawa
sathwa pudgala kalaya, ekathu karagena 
nirwachanaya denna bari ewa 
wisthara karaganawa.

leda weema kumak da ? kiyana prashnaya ahanne na.
leda une kawda , leda une ai, mokada wela tiyenne kiyala ahanwa.
ethkota 
leda weema kumak da kiyla hoyanna 
leda weema ilakkayak kara ganna oni.

enam api danna danaka idan thamai yanna oni.
me seweema 
danna thanen patan ganna puluwan.

practically prashaya ahanna kalin hariyata ahuna ganna purudu wenna oni.
lokaya thula leda weema kumak da kiyala ahanna widihak na
eka base walin thora handa.

hodata kalpana kaloth 
kawda marenne kiyala ahanna aithiyakuth na
marenawa kiyana eka wishthara karaganna baruwa
kanek wa sambanda karagena e ahana prashanya 
waradi bawa mulin therum ganna oni .

nirwachana nathi kriyawan walata lokayen hethu hoyala wadak na
ehema kaloth hambenne, piligath matha witharai.

me widihata api onima ekak ekka 
niruththara wenawa.
kriyawa wisthra kara ganna bari handa.
niruththara wenawa.
ese niruththara unata,
lokaya thula soyaganna bari me yathaa-arthaya
dana ganna oni nam, e athiwana kamaththa thulin
budu rajananwahanse gena dharma wachanaya desata naburu wenawa.
lokaya thulin dakeemata bari yathaa-arthya 
pennapu budurajana wahanse gana , achala shaddawa mathu wenawa.

leda weeme hethuwa -> buduhimi thamai niwaradiwa penwa wadale
leda weeme hethuwa pahadili karala dena dharmaya 
pachchicha samuppadayai.

lokoththara dharamayata naburu wenna nam
wimukthikaamin ahapu prashne waradda,
enam me mokadda, kageda kiyana prashanye waradda.
ape jeewithaya thulin dakinna oni.
ehema karala, 
wimukthikaamin ge awabodaya lagata wath api awe naththam
budun wahanse wadala wachana wala lokoththara arthaya apen gilihila.

nirwachanya nathi me asarana kama jeewithaya thulin dakeema
hariyata hiru uda wenna kalin
aruna nagenawa wage.
jeewitha aduren galawenna puluwan
alokaya aruna pitipassen pawathina bawa 
sakshath wenawa.....

---------------prathya yanu kumak da----2021/09/26------

dharmaye guna 
gambeerai, 
dura-awabodarai, 
dudasai (mage konaya thulin dakinna ba), 
panditha wedaneeyai (praknawanthyinta witharai penne)

ada kathawata issella, giya sare padame reference tika bala innama oni.
ethkota hodatama pahadilie.

manussayek gaththahama , ajiwi kotasakui sajeewi kotasakui.
marunama ithuru wena kotasa ajiwi,
sajeewi kotasa sith paramparawak pawatha ganna shakthiya.
ethkota body eke tiyena siyalu kotas upakarana.
sithata oniwidihata thamai hasurawanne. 

lokaye pawathmata me upakarana saha sitha pawathwagena yana shakthiya kiyana dekama tiyenna oni.
sitha / kaya. 
(sitha thulin hamunawa nama dharmayan)
kaya thulin hamuwana roopa dharamyan upakarayen
thamai lokaya pawathinne.
enam lokaya hamatissema pawathinne idwethawayak uda.
e nisa api chiththa,chithasika, roopa. lokaye pawathma niyojanaya karana paramaartha dharmathai.

api meka eg ekakin balamu.

1) nawak handa thamai minissu sagare gaman karanne.
e wage roopa kaaya nisa naama kaaya pawathinne. (balakaaya wage , kotas wala ekathuwak)  
nawa - roopa kaaya wage
minissu - naama kaaya wage
sansara sagare gaman karanna nam nawa saha minissu dennam inna oni.
roopa kaaya+ naama kaaya tiyena thak sasara gamane yedenna puluwan.

minissu nisa nawa saagare gaman karanne yam se da ? (minissu nathuwa nawa yanne nane)
naama kaaya nisa roopa kaya pawathie.

api katha katha kala - 
nawak handa thamai minissu sagare gaman karanne. (enam roopa kaya nisa  naama kaaya pawathinawa)
minissu nisa nawa sagare gaman karanawa. (enam naama kaaya nisa roopa kaya pawathinawa)
enisa roopa kaaya saha naama kaaya ownoun nisa pawathinawa.
enam ekinekata prathyai.
enam anyamanyai.
anyamanya prathyai.

roopa ipedena akara 4k api katha karala tiyenawa.
roopaye prathya gaththahama,
karma, chiththa , irthu, ahara yana prathyan gen
noyek akaraye roopayan, ipida, bidi, dira yanawa.
me roopayan athi une 
thamange (e roopaye) balapamakin thorawai, ( ee hethu prathya nisa hata gaththu roopa dharamayan)
(thamange balapamakin thorawai)/un hethuwakin upan me roopayata , e hethu dharama walata aithiyak prakasha kranna ba.
e roopayanta un himiyek kuth natha. (wena aithikarayakuth na) 

mama handa meka una nam , mata meka control karanna puluwan wenna oni.
ehema wenne na
roopayan ge wenas weema , ipida ,bidi,dira yama 
apita control karanna ba.
e nisa no-binda (unbroken) , no-diraa tiyagatha haki shakthiyak da natha.
api danna lokuma shakthiya tiyenne hithe,
me roopayan ge prathya sitha nevi
ehenam sithin mewa control karanna ba.
ex:
epa mage data watenne
epa mata leda wenna
epa mata wayasata yanna 

owa karanna ba.
mama kiyala kenek bahirin hada gaththanu nisa ,
eya nithya karagena hithanawa apita puluwan meka karanna kiyala

marena eka kal danna hadanawa
leda nathi kara ganna handanawa
konde sudu wena eka nawaththanna eka eka die ganawa.
bada wadi nam bada adu karanna wehesenawa.
methana idala wena thanakata hithuwoth yanna puluwan kiyala therena sobawayak allagena 
mata hithin meka control karanna puluwan kiyala mamathwaya thahawuru kara gannawa
bahira pothak / yamak mata allanna , ganna puluwan nisa 
mama pawathina bawa thahawuru kara gannawa.
namuth athule abyanthara sobawayan gana awabodayak na.

kriyawaliya gana awabodayak nathi nisa, 
upakalpanaya thulin sadanaya kala yuththa , thahawuru kara gannawa.

ex:
mata pothak alla ganna puluwan ahanda , potha tiyenawa , mama innawa kiyana sankalpaya prove kara gannawa.
potha nathuwath mama innawa kiyala mama kiyana drushtiya thahawuru kara gannawa.

science wala sampurna theory ekama mebadu upakalpana , repeated sadanaya kalayuthu dewal walin thamai 
prove karagena tiyenne.
samawitama ekama prathipalaya denawa nam eka aththa kiyala hithanawa.


kriyawaliya gana awabodayak nathi handa drushtiyen welenewa.
mama thahawuru wenawa.



prathya shakthiya nathi kisiwak lokaye hamu wenne natha. 

suka prathyan athi weemen suka wedanawada
dukka prathyan athi weemen dukka wedanawada 
suka dukka prathyan nolabeemen upeka wedanawada athi wei.

ape dorawal 6 ta aramunu muna gahena kota.
gahaniyek, pirimiyek, gasak, walak yanadi sanyaa pahala wenawa.
dorwal 6i + aramunui hamu unahama  -> sanyaa pahala wela.
sanyaa wa pahala une,hamuweema kiyana siddiya nisa
ehema nathuwa dorawal 6 ho aramunu wena wenama tibba kiyala sanyaawa hata ganne na.
enam me hamuweema enam 
un hethuwakin pahala woo e sanyyawata , aithikarayek na.
e wagema 
sanyawata aithiyakuth na. (sanyyawata swayan aithiyak na)

thamage hethuwakin nisa neve nam hatagaththe , eyata e hatagaththu dharamatha walata aithiyak na/ eyage kiyanna ba.
(apine mata aithi kiyala dagena inne.) (yakada deke gateema)
anathmai.

habai e hata gaththu dharmathawayata prathya shakthiyak tiyenawa. (hama dema pawathinne shakthiyak matha.)
lowa pawathina sama detama prathya shakthiyak aniwaryen pawathinawa.

roopa/wedana aadi dharamatha nisa,
yaam, eeim, ideem, siteem, deem, ganeem, kaam, beem aadiya sidu karana chethana wani sanskarayan da (chethanath ekak nevi collection ekak ne, ekatath wen wu prathya pawathinawa)
chethanawa ekak novu nisa, api mewata kiyanawa "chethana sankyaatha sanskaara" kiyala

aleem, kipeem adi sansakarayan da pahala wenawa.

thaman ge balayen nowa ,
un hethuwakin hataganna e sanskarayantada ewage aithiyak natha.
anathmai.

ex:
yakada dekak ekata gatunu wita ena saddaya yakadayata aithi na
gateema kiyana kriya prathyen hata gath dharmathawayak.
gabdaya yakadaye balayen, ehema thaththan
thaman ge balayen nowa 
un hethuwakin hata gath sanskarayak.
yakadayata e shabdaye aithiyak natha.
shabdaya yakadaya thulin awa nevi.
prathya shakthiya witharai methana tiyenne.

hamu weema kiyanne kriyawak.
eke kriyawaliye prathya shakthiya shabdaya bawata pariwarthana wela.

meka pahadili unada ? ehema wenna ba
kriyawak kiyana eka lokaya thula nirwachanayak denna puluwan deyak nevi ? nirwachanayak na
kriyawaliya, prathya shakthiya , hakiyawa
kiyana dewal, me lokadaya thula nirwachanaya karanna ba.
e nisa balawegayan (ithirawa nopawathina , wegayen wenas wana balayan) pamani.
mehew paramartha jathika dharma

nirwachanayak nathuwa thamai awaboda karagana oni.
nirwachanayak samawitama wynnanaya ashithawa thamai haduna ganne.
e nisa wynnanaya abibawa giya widharshana nyanak /hakiyawak me awabodaya sadaha awashayai.

marga nyaanaya athi wenne , mebadu , wynaanaya ikmawa giya widarshana nyaanayaka prathya shaktiyeni.
e hakiyawa naththam dharashana nyaanayapahala wenne na.
yakada deke gateema widu wanne na.
 
 
enam 
prathya shakthi prariwarthanayak pamanai pawathinne.
prathya shakthiye winaasa weemak na.
eke pramartha jathika dharmathawayak.
ehi anithya sobawayak pamanai aththe. (eka thanaka tiyenne na transfer wenawa)
api thamai wen karagena tiyenne 
yakada deka ekata gahuwa , eka handa shabdaya awa.
me depaththa pawathinne mama hitapu handa,
ekata wadeeme hakiyawa , mama handa hata gaththu ekak nevie.
parathya shakthi wenas weeme hakiyawa thula ekak lesa nothibeeme hakiyawa 
pawathina nisa 
anithya sobawaya wydamanai.

mese wynanaye pahala weemada ,
wisthara karanna puluwan.

roopa aadhi aramunu chakku idwaarayata hamu weemen, wynaanayan pahala wei.
me hamuweema, anya hethuwak.
enam 
wynaanaye pahala weema anya hethuwak nisa siduweemak,
enam 
pahala wu shabddayata , shabbadaya athi karapu hakiyawa athi na wage.
wynaanayatada , eya pahala weemata adala woo dharamathawayan ge aithi wasikamak natha.

e e prathyayen ipadila,bindee, diraa yana yam sanskarayan ( naththam naama roopayan)
thamange kamaththe hatiyata pawathwaa,
mamaya kiyala salakana athmayak novie.

bawayen bawayata yana no-marena athmayak da novie.

yaam, eem, aadhiya sidu karana athmayak da novie.
suwa duk widina athmayak da novie.
ee de sanwidana karana athmayak da novie
prathyen prathya hata gena 
ekenehima (e mohothema) diraa , bindee yana
dharma paramparawakin hata ganeemak pamanai.

e nisa iskandayan anathmayo ya.

dev, minis, sathwa samoohaya saha
siyalu wasthun, sadena
moola dhathu wana naama(sith 89,chaithasika 52), roopa (28)
kiyana 
paramartha dharma athi wenne kohomada ?

thawa gaburata yannai yanne :D

mewaa noyek hethun gen hata ganie.
e nisa sankatha / sanskaara kiyala hadunwanawa.
sanskara dharmayan athi karawana hethunta prathya kiyana namakin hadunwanawa.

prathya : sansakara dharmaya athi karana hethu walata.
budu rajanan wahanse, prathyan, krama 3nakata wisthara karanawa.
1) arya sathya karamaya
2) patichcha samuppaadha karamaya
3) pattaana deshana karamaya

melesa sanskarayan ge uppathi hethuun deshana kota wadala seka.

awidyawa athi kalhi sanskaraya hata ganie.

meka balamu,
prathya shakthiya hama ekema tiyenawa kiwwane
awidya wehi da prathya shakthiya wisheshayan (suwisi prathya washayen) pawathinawa,
ewaa ye yam yam shakthi walin,
yam yam aakaara walin 
awidyawa, sanskarayanta prathya we.

ehema nathuwa,
sanskaara upadawanawa kiyala iganweemak natha.

siyalu dharma wala athi , prathya shaktheen saha ,
hethu , arambana, sahajaatha wani suwisi prathya walinuth
e e dharama , e e dharmayan ta prathya wena widiha
budu rajanan wahanse uganwa atha.
meka mahaa pattanam prakaranaya kiyala hadunwanawa.
meka thamai, dharamaya thula pawathina prabalama kalla.

enam 
me kotas deka
1) siyalu dharma wala athi , prathya shaktheen
2) suwisi prathya
e e dharama , e e dharmayan ta prathya wena aakaraya.

uganwaaa atha.

me kotas deka gana igena ganeema
budu dharahama pilibada gana anga sampurna awabodayak upadawa ganeemata hethu prathya we. 

mebadu , gaambeera dharmayaka anawa-bodaya nisa 
dharmaya nodakapu nisa

widarshana nyanaya hewath praknawa no-wade.
sansara saagaraye athraman weemak pamanak sidu atha.

ese wenne 
mama kiyala kenek panawa gena 
mama thulin lokaya haduna gath bawa tharayee wishwasa kala nisa.

reference :
majjima nikaye , muula pannasakaye
palamu suthraya wana
siyaluma pariyayanta mulika wana 
moola pariyaaya suthraya anuwa
niwanada myyanaa karana bawak uganwamin
wisi aakara sakkaaya dittiyak.
penwa wadaala seka.

------------------ Hethu prathya thulin samudaya saha nirodaya  ---03/10/2021---------------
 
 giya sare katha kale prathya shakthiya gana
 api katha karanne hethu-prathya kiyana sambandaya gana.
 
 methana,
 hethuwa awenika wita, prathya dharmayo awenika novana lesa prathya wei.
 
 ex:
 nuga ataya kata palawenna oni nam jalaya , pas prathya dharma wenawa.
 pol atayata kata palawenna oni nam jalaya, pas prathya dharama wenawa.
 gas jathiya wenas unata,
 prathya podu wela.
 nuga beejaya hethuwen nuga palayak sadunata
 pol beejaya hethuwen nuga palayak hadenne na.
 hethuwa wenas wenawa prathya samana wenawa.
 nuga beejayata nuga gasak sadeeme prathya shakthiyak. pol beejayata tiyenne 
 pol palayak hadana shakthiya.
 
 prathya dharmayan eka unata , hethuwa wenas wena kota prathpalaya wenas. ( prathya kiyanne awasana prathipalaya nevi, upakarayai/ udawwak pamanai)
 enam hethuwa special.
 hethuwa matha palaya sakas weeme hakiyawa pawathinne.
 nuga beejayata nuga gasak weeme hakiyawa, eyata awenikai.
 enam nuga beejayata saha jaathai.
 pol beejayatath esemai.
 
 me saha jaatha hakiyata , pita tibunu prathayan
 anya jathika lesa hadun wanawa.

 enam hethu saha prathya ekinekata wenas wenne 
 me ayurin.
 hethu - saha jathaathai
 prathya - anya jathai
 dekenma karanne palaya hadenna udaw karana eka.
 pol palaya hadenna nam hethuwa saha prathya yana dekama tiyenna oni.
 naththam palaya hata ganeemak sidu wenna ba.
 
 
 hethuwa beejayata  awenikai
 prathya dharmayo beejayata awenika novei.
 
 budu rajanan wahanse, deshana samawitama sakkaya nirodaya ismathu karawanawa.
 e wage dharmayak kiyanna tiyennema nirodaya allagena mai.
 e nisa sium bawin balawath lesa hadunwanne.
 e nisa samudaya (hata ganeemak) gana katha karanna ba nirodaya nathuwa.
 eka pennawanne nyanayakin mai.

sothapanna marga nyanaya upadinne , ekthara keles dharmayan 
nirodaya weemath samaga mai.
e nisa sothapanna wenna dharmayak kohewath na.
samudaya (hata ganeema) sama witama nirodaya samagamai hamu wela tiyenne.

sothapanna marga nyanaya upadinna nam , sakkaya ditti,seelabbatha paramasa, wichikichcha yana akusala dharmayan samuchcheda washayen niroda wiya yuthui.
samma dittiya athi weemath , me wagemathamai
samawitama niroda nyanayak samaga thamai samudaya wanne(hataganne).

ehemanam nyaanaak gana katha karanna wenne margayak ekka mai.
suthra deshana karanne menna me marga nyaanayak upadinnai.
e deshana karna suthraya allagena wadak na. ehi allaganna deyak na.

ekama suthaya shrawanaya kirima thulin,
kenek sothapanna wana wita, thawa kenek uthum arihath bawata path wiya hakie.
eka ekkena ge hithapu paraasaya anuwa thamai prathipalaya labenne.
hithapu paraasaya theeranaya wenne , eya inna thana anuwa 
enam dharma awabodayata sapekshawa.

nyaanaya samudaya wanne nirodaya samaga mai.
e nisa eka eka mattam pawathinawa.
sowan marga nyaanaya
sakurthagami marga nyaanaya
anagami marga nyaanaya
arihath marga nyaanaya

me me mattam wala , wiwida keles sampurna washayen (samuchcheda washayen) nirodaya wei.
methana mathaka tiya ganna oni,
sowan waladi 3k prahanaya wenawa
sakurthagami mattame di keles prahanayak nowa, keles bara thunee weemak thamai sidu wenne.
(keles badeema thuni wela)
anagami mattame di, raga (kama ragaya pamanai) , patiga deka samuchchada washayen prahanaya wenawa.
me anuwa anagami mattama wena kota sanyojana 5k samuchchada prahanaya wela.
enam 
me 5ta kiyanawa 
oram baageeya sanyojana 5 kiyala. ( pahalata adina gathiya tiyenne me sanyojana wala)
(polawata gata gahala tiyenne yadam wage)
arihath mattame di,
uddam baagiya keles 5ma nirodaya wei. ( roopa raga, aroopa raga, maana, udachcha, awidya)


dasa sanyojana api igena gaththe palaweni padamen.
eka apply wena hati igena ganna 36 weni padamen.
palamu padame karunu dana sitiyata , apply kara ganna nam
35 weni padama dakwa igena ganeema kara tibiya yuthui.
naththam ewa thawath karanu ras kirimak, ehema naththam
keles barak pamanai.
dharma gaweshanya thula , prayogikawa apply kara ganna awashaya
samuchcheda prahanaya igena ganna awshai.

ex:
atha eka anthyak, natha eka anthyak
me dharmayedi e deka yedenne na kiyala 
api katha karanawa.
me deka yedenne na kiyala ahena kotama,
me dekama waradie kiyal alla ganna idak api wisinma hada ganna wa.
ethkota 
aththeth natha 
naththeth natha kiyala 
sithuwillak upaddawala, eka alla gaththahama
eyata adala woo, wipaka thalayak wana
newasayya-nasayya wipaka prathi sandiyakata karmayak sakas wela.
(aroopa thalayak)
sanyaawak aththeth na 
sanyaawak naththeth na
kiyana sium thana alla gannawa.
methanata boho aya niwana kiyala rawatenwa.
ekath thawa deyak alla ganeemak pamanai.
methan tiyena pradana fault eka 
sanyaawak aththeth na naththeth na kiyana sanyaawa labenna kenek inna oni.
ehenam sakkaya nirodayak wela na. 
enam niwanen thorai.

sakkaya kiyana dharmathwaya krama 3kata pawathinawa.
-chiththa
-sanyaa 
-ditti

me 3ma newasayya-nasayya thalayedi kadanna ba.
mokada dharmaya asanna kanak na. ( roopa na)
sithak pawathinawa, kayak na.
e nisa dana gaththu dharmaya pamanai use karanan puluwan. ( mano idwarika chiththa weethi pamanai)
aluthen sowan weemak kara gatha nohaka.
e nisa methanaya yana aya , dhaana mattam balayen giya namuth,
marga nyanaya soyana apita , abawya isthanayak. (noya yuthu thanak)

ethkota 
aththeth natha naththeth natha kiyala alla gaththoth
sakkaya nirodayak sidu kara ganna ba.
mamathwaye pawathma nisa.

sakkaya nirodaya sadaha,
indriya dharma wadila , e awashayathawaya ismathu wenna oni.
igena gena danuwath unahama dharma-dhara pudgalayeku athi wenawa misak
budun wahanse wethata naburu weemak wei da ?
mama iwath wela na neda ?

e nisa thamai
paratho goshayai
yoniso manikarayai 
me dharma nyanaya upadawa ganeemata mul wechcha hethu 2k wenne. ( sowan palayata hethu wana 4n, 2k)

eka nisa,
methuwak kal, dharmaya soyala 
ekathu karagath wishala dharma awabodayak api thula pawathinawa
namuth mama galawila na.
budun ge dharmaya samawitama mamathwaya ikamawala yamata deshana karapu
dharma pariyayak
namuth ape dharma gaweshanaya thula hamu unu
dharma poshanaya thula meya sidu wee na

ai e ?
api budda wachanaya lesa nam karapu, apita hamu unu de thula 
bubun ge wachanaya desata yomu weema hamu wela na.
enam 
api dara gena inna budda dharamya thula 
maththwaya poshanaya weema adu wela na.

samahara welawata ,
thamange awabodaya waradie kiyala api budda wachanaya desata nemennath try karanawa.
namuth namenna kenek innawa.
enam 
upaya (kittu wela), 
upaadana(lagata adagena)(upaya gaththu danuma atharinne na), 
abiniwesa(pandinchi wenawa), 
winibadda (ekata badda wenawa) 

kiyana karunu samaga sidu unu naweemak nisa, 
sakkaya poshana welamai pawathinne. ( me keles thamai pradana washayen sakkaya poshanayata hethu wenne)
me naweema, marga nyanata pramanawath na.  

marga nyana ye hethu , prathya monawada?

hethu - kalyana mithra sewanaya,sathdharma shawanayai, yoniso manikarayai, dhammanu damma prathipadawa
prathya - sakkaya poshanawa wana keles wala nirodaya.


ex:
lokaye wigraha wena widihata dharmaya kiyala denna puluwan.
api mechchara kal igena gaththu e dharama kotas,
eunata ewa lokaya thula pamani use kala hakke. dharama dara pudalayekuta
adala widihata, lokaya thula hamu wana dharmatha gana 
katha karanna awashaya loku knowledge ekak hada ganna puluwan.
e unata 
lokaye kisima kenekuta
ewa prathyan washayen wisthara karanna ba.
prathya shaktheen ge haath pasa thorathuru danne 
budu rajanan wahanse pamanai.
budda nyaanaya thulin hamuwu dharmatha.
ekata awasha hethu prathya sakas weema nisa 
danagaththu suwisheshi nyaana pariyayak.

prathya shaktheen, gana katha karanakota
e siyalu wisthara e adala budda nyaanata gocharai.

api mewa pramartha jathika dharama lesa katha kalata,
oyalata therenawada 
me kathwa lokaya thula dharma awabodayata sapekshai.
e danuma thulin , budda nyaanata gochara woo siyalu wisthara 
dana ganna ba.
e nisa e sampurna awabodaya soyanawata wada,
marga pala sadaha awashya awobadaya 
sakas kara ganeemata weerya karanna oni.
 
mewa budda nyaanayen prathyaksha karapu dharamatha.
-karma shakthiya
-ajatakashaya
-gathi lakshana
-thilakshanaya
-anishpanna roopa 10
kiyan siyalu
pramartha jaathika dharamathawayan 
budda nyaanayata prathyaksha woo dharma tha.

me dharama tha , lokaya thula ape nyaana mattamata 
gochara nowana nisa,
budda nyyanayen prathyaksha kala e dharmathwayan 
elasa daka gatha yuthui.
namuth ehi laga nogatha uthui.
mokada laga ganne thamanta theruna dharamaye.

budda darshanaya daraa gena 
margaya desata weerya kirimen 
lokaya thula laga ganeemen thorawa
nirodaya prathyaksha kara gatha hakiyawa athi wei
meyata prabala sathi math bawak/ shraddawak awshayai.

methan aakarawathee sharddawa, upadinne 
menna me budda nyaanaya thulin,
apita daka ganna bari, 
parama sathya penawa dunnu 
budda wachanaya desatama naburu weemen mai.

ex:
destination ekata lan wena widiha, 
pawanna puluwan giya kenekuta pamanai,
e giya kena ge instructions anuwa 
ethanata laga weemata nam
instructions walata garu karala , ese gaman karanna oni.

enam budda wachanaya desatama naburu weemen
marga nyaanaya upadawa ganeemata weeraya karanna oni.
sathiya,samadiya saha weerya thibiya yuthui.

e nisa ,
samma waayama, (waayama/wiyawamaya/weerya)
samma sathi,
samma samadhi, 
kiyana anithama 3 pradanawa
lokoththara washayen marga anga 8tama , eka wara yedena nyaanaya 
marga nyanayai.

lokoththara sithaka pamanai, marga anya 8ma eka wara yedenne.


me gaburu dharamya awaboda kara ganeemata 
withakshana sheeli bawak tiyenna oni. (sathya gaweshanayak/seweemak)
seweema pamanamai karanna puluwan.
labichcha dekata ringala laga gaththoth 
eka hari da ?
eka withakshana sheeli gathiyak da ?
withakshana-sheeli bawak kiyanne wimukthikaamai hageemak
e kiyanne sathya seweemak tiyenna uwamanai.

withakshana-sheeli sowabawaya lebena deyak nevi
labenawa nam hamuwena kenek sitima nisa.
laba gena ringala laga ganna a eka 
kenek sitina nisa wena deyak
sakkaya nirodaya nevi.
budda wachanaya ahila na.

budda wachanaya thula pawathinne 
sakka nirodaya sadaha awasha dharmayan.
withakshana-sheeli kiyana gathiya 
ehema labila ringaganna deyak nevi.
eka gathiyak.
enam pramartha jathika dharmayak.
anna e gathiya thula 
dharamaya hamu wanne.

ethkota ethara wena prathipadawakata enawa mai.
sakkaya dittiya poshanaya wana thanaka
enam anya arthyan gath wita,
withakshana-sheeli kiyana gathiyata wada 
withakshana-sheeli gathiya laba ganeeme oni kama ismathu wela
enam sakkaya poshanaya wela 
marga nyanaya upadawa ganeema pasaka thaba,
wachana tikak igena gena ,
eke laga gena innawa
dakkaya ditti niroda nyaanaye pihitanne naha.
pihitaganna ba.



budu rajanan wahanse, 
anithya, dukka kiyana dharamatha yededdi (paramartha jathika dharama)
hamba wethdi novie. ( e kiyanne laga ganna thanak nathi wenna oni, kenek nathi wenna oni, anathma sobawaya ismathu wenna oni, mage palanayata yatath na, ehema wenna mama inna epai)
enam
anithya, dukka kiyana dharamatha yededdi prathipadawa ismathu kala.

lokaye kenek allala katha karana kota , ohuta me dharmaya asenawa nam
ethera weemak sidu wiya yuthumai.
laga ganeemak novie.
ebadu sakkaya ditti nyanayak thamai awaboda kala yuththe.

marga nyaanayak thamai awadi wiya yuththe,
marga nyaanayatamai keles samuchcheda prahanaya wenne
me nisa lokaye kenek allala dharmaya katha karana kota 
e kena ikmawala , e sakkaya dittiya pilibanda nyaanayak awadi wela 
ethara weemak sidu wiya yuthui.
laga ganeemai novie.

meka therum ganna uthsaha kaloth, eka karanne oyage dharma danuma use karala.
ehema me sobawaya therum yanne na. 
eka therum ganeema nowa, enam laba ganeema nowa
e dharamayata anugatha weemai sidu wiya yuththe.

therum ganeemai, anugatha weemai dekak.

niroda nyanayak pahala karaganeema saha
label kireema yanu dekak.

awabodaya thamai awasha, therum ganeema / arthya seweema nevi ( definition ekak hoyanne 
therum ganeema sahada pamanai)
nirwachanayak nathi deyak awaboda karanawa kiyala kiyana kota 
eka definion eka ikmawala tiyenne
e kiyanne wynnanayen karaganna puluwan deyak nevie
enam wynaanaya ikmawala.
eya widarshana nyaana sobawayak.

refer note : eka balanna. ධර්මය-අසාගන්නතාක්-අවබෝධවනතාක්-ඉන්නේ-කලුවරෙමයි.docx

apita prasha athi une 
roopayak uawamana unu nisai.
naama roopa nomathi dewal nirwachanayen thorai,
shuthamaya lesa hamu wu dharmayata 
roopayak uwamana wu nisa , prashna athi wela .
nama dharmayan haduna ganna wynanayata bari nisa
meka therum ganna hadanakota kara ganna ba.
therum ganna hadanawa kiyannema pramadai.

e nisa soyanna oni gathiya hada ganne nathuwa 
therum ganna oni kiyana gathiya ismathu wela 
wyannayata thana awith
praknayata idak nathi wela
ringa ganna / laga ganna thanak ismathu wela
nirwachanayak upanna nam 
ekama thamai prashne,
nirwachanayak tiyena saama thanama 
soyanna oni gathiya nathi wenawa.
wyaanaya pramuka wenawa.

seweema thula, laga ganeemak, ringa ganeemak ta idak 
tiyenna ba.
nirwachanayak nomathi sobawaya 
elesin dakiya yuthui

nirwachanyak nomathiwa 
seweemak karanna nam
ese soyanna wenne 
thanhawe kruthyath samaga mai. ( apita awaboda wena mattamen thamai patan ganna wenne)
e kiyanne nirodaya dakkinna wenna samudaya sathya thula.
mokada samudaya katha karanne ma nirodayath ekka.

e mokadda kiyala soyana wita witharamai
marga nyaanayata ida hadenne.
"dittya suppati widya" kiyala kiwwe menna me awasthawata.
widyawa pahadili drushtiyen dakeema enam 
samma dittiya enam 
ethara weeme kruthya.

ethkota ex balamu.
 api karanna hadanne ,
 naveemak ekka seweemak karaganna .
 naveemak wenne danunu deyak ekkai. ( aduma tharama ahalawath tiyenna oni)
 apita danunu deyak widihata 
 thanhawa ganna puluwan.
 
 thanahawen thulin seweemak karaganna kota marga nyanaya ismathu wenna oni
ehenam 
thahawaka sewima misak roopayak seweema nevi.
apita pena roopaya gana soyanawata wada 
apita penne ai kiyana eka soyanna patan ganna oni.

nyaanaya tiyenne roopaya paththe nevie,
thanhawa upadinne roopaya paththe nevi, eka mano mulika dharamathawayak
nyaanayath mano mulika dharma thawayak.

prashnaya wisadanna oni , prashnaya tiyenawa thana.

ex:
ape jeewithaye roopaya paththa prabala wela.
mokada penawa kiyana eka given, eka danatama sidu wela iwara handa 
ethanin thamai api hithanna patan ganne.
eka tiyenawamai kiyana nithya sobawaya thula idan thamai 
lokaya patan ganne.
lokaye ganu denu , nithya wunu nisa pamanai pawathinne.
nyaanaya tiyenne roopaye paththe nevi,
enam bahira aramuna thula nevie
marga nyaanaya sadaha meya kada ganna oni.

bahiraya gana sithimen palak na,
marga nyaanaya sahada 
apita pena eka nevi
penne ai kiyana eka gana sitha yomu wiya yuthui.

melesa kirimen watina nuwanak pahala kara gatha hakie.
pancha upadana iskanada asuru wenawa nam 
ethana dukak mai.
pancha upadana iskanada asuru wenawa kiyala kiyana thana surraounding (wapasariya) eka
thamai,
ayathana 6 anuwa giya chiththa chithasika dharama  
saha
sabban roopan 
set ekata.
e nisa 
thun lokayama dukai. (kama,roopa,aroopa)
dukata namak thamai lokaya.
dukata hethuwa thanhawa.

-----------------sakkaya ditti nirodaya--------10/10/21----------------


meka katha karanna issella , 
mulin sakkaya ditti athi wena hati saha ehi nirodaya gana poddak
katha karala imu.

me lokaye, hithakin thorawa roopa tiyenawada ?

ex: onna gahak tiyenawa, gewal saththu innawa
mewa hithakin thorawada pawathinne ?

pruthakjanayo samawitama , hithakin thorawa
bahira lokayak tiyenawa kiyala ara gannawa.

e tiyena bahira lokayata ipaduna kiyala gannawa.
ex: 
mulin aiya ipadichcha loke man ipaduna.
me loke pawathuna, mama bihi una.

dan siddanthaya mehema nam eeta galapena saakshiya
kumak da ?
mama inna lokema thamai aiya inneth, mekata tiyena saakshiya 
mokadda ?
meka hithala neda kiwwe ? saakshiya hithe neda pawathinne ?
onna dan bahira pawathinne hithe neda kiyala dan aye hithanawa ?
ekath hithe neda ?
pawathina bawa therenne hitha pahala unahamai kiyala hithanawa.
meka harida ?
methana tiyena waradda thamai , hitha athule siyallama pawathinawa 
kiyala hithapu eka.
roopa,wedana,sanyaa,sankaara,wynaana kiyana iskanda 5 pawathinne hitha kiyana 
kulakayaka kiyala.
ex: hitha kiyna box eke me iskanda 5 pawathinawa kiyala neda 
therum aran inne ?
ekama kulakayaka thamai me okkoma tiyenne kiyala.

iskanda 5n thamai, ayathana 6 wisthara kara ganne.
ahen gaththath iskanda 5i, kanen gaththath ekamai.

meka hariyata ,
swimming pool ekata swimmers la 6k bahala innawa wage.
wathura tiyena handa peenanna puluwan.
e kattiya pool eke bahala inne e wathure peenanna puluwan hakiyawa nisa.

ethakota, peeneeme hakiyawata pradana wenne ,
peenime hakiyawa hethuwa saha wathura kiyana prathya tiyena nisa
peeneema sakas wenawa.
wathura ain kaloth, 6 denata peenanna ba.
wathura kiwwe mokatada ?
nodannakama kiyana wathura.
e kiyanne.
nodannakama kiyana wathura tiyena nisa thamai peenum karuwanta ehi
peenanna puluwan.

mulin api kathawa patan gaththe,
hithen thorawa roopa tiyenawai kiyana thana idala.
e kiyanne,
bahira lokayak tiyenawa, api ehi innawa.
kiyana thana idala.

bahira lokayak tiyenawa kiyana nodanuwathkama hindama thamai
api ehi innawa kiyana hageema athi wenne.
e mama innawai kiyana dadi nithya hageema thula thamai
ayathana walin lokaya ekka ganu denu karanne.
(pihinum karuwo wathure peenanawa wage)
ehenam mulu wishwayama randa pawathinne,
nodanuwathkama matha.
naththam awidyawa matha.

ehenam,
nodanuwathkama kiyana mulika prashnaya handa thamai
me siduweema sidu wenne.
ehema nathuwa sitha thula prashnak nevi.

dan me problem eka hithata awenika nam
hithe tiyena problem ekak nam
hithen me problem eka galawanna ba.
e kiynne marga pala laba ganna ba.

chathurarya sathya hamu unoth
eyata therenawa,
meka hitha thula athi waraddak nevi kiyana eka.
nodanuwath kama tiyena thaak
ayathana 6ta nodanuwath kama prathya karagena 
e hethu asuru karanna puluwan.

ehenam problem eka wathura saha peenum karuwo gawa nevi tiyenne.
wathura tiyena oni thanaka peenum karuwata peenanna puluwan.
wathura his karana job eka
wathurata ho peenum karuwanta aithi na.
habai wathura his thanaka, 
peenum karuwanta pawathmak na.

peenum karuwange peenime hakiyawa ain karanna haduwe na.
ehema karanna haduwoth sidu wela tiyenne, ayathana tiyethdi,
roopaya wenas karanawa wage wadak.
roopaya allaganna widiha wenas kala kiyala roopaya allaganeeme hakiyawa
nathi wela na.
e nisa
meka thulin ayathana pawathime hakiyawa adu wela na.

jalashaya his kaloth, enam nodanuwath kama iwath kaloth
pihinumkaruwanta pawathinna / pihitanna ba.
e hinda roopaya allaganna widiha wenas kara kiyala 
nodanuwath kama tiyena thak, 
pihineeme gathiya iwath karanna ba.

nodanuwath kama iwath karapu sanin,
roopaye alla ganeeme awshathawaya pawathinne na.

ehenam 
meya hithe parashnayak nevi,
moolika prashnaya samawitama awidayawe thamai pawathinne.

arya sathya hamu unoth,
eya therum gannawa 
hitha thula waraddak nevi,
nodanuwathkama thulin ahuwechchi dittiyak kiyana eka.

nodanuwath kama iwath kireema thulin,
nirodaya dakinna puluwan.

api ayathana gana hithanne, hariyata alibabai, horu 5 denai wage.
alibabath horek thamai. eya thama lokuma hora.
e gollo bihi wenne,
horakama pawathina nisa kiyala apita ahu wenne na.
horakama pawathina thek ali-baba saha horu 5 pawathina bawa dakkahama
enam 
horakama hethuwen karakam karana pudgalayan hamu wana bawa dakkama. enam
horakama pilisida dakkoth , kenek horek da nadda kiyana eka hoyala therumak na.
horakama iwath karanna puluwan nam, hoyakam karana aya hamu wenne na.

ayathanawala nodanuwathkame peenime hakiyawa handa thamai,
roopayak nithya washayen tiyenawa kiyana hageema hataganne.
e roopaya wiwida widihata allaganeema thulin 
roopayen galaweemak labanna ba.
ayathana wala kriyakarithya nodanuwathkama tiyena thek
pawathina nisa ( peenanna puluwan wathura tiyena thanak witharai)
nodanuwath kama iwath kaloth
roopaya ipadeemata awasha ayathanama nathi wela yanawa.

ex:
rassawa wisin mawa soya gannawada 
mama rassawak hoya gannawada ?

api ekaka training karala, hodata qualified wela hoda rassawak hoya gannawa kiyala api hithanawa.
rassawak hoyanna puluwan wenne kohomada ?

rassawak hoyanna puluwan wenne rassawal pawathina handa ne ?
ehenam api hithapu widiha waradie ne,
rassawak tibba handa thamai mata eka karanna oni dewal sakas karaganna wenne.
vacancy ekak naththam rassawak karanna ba neda ?
ehenam rassa tibba handa neda oyata job eka karanna puluwan.
nathuwa oya qualified handa nevi neda ?

podi horu tika allala deela loku hora hama dissema galawenawa.
maha hora eya berena widihata thamai sakshi denne.
eya gana saken baluwe naththam 
goda weemak na. 
hithanawa kiyannema maha horawa wishwasa kala kiyana eka.
hithanwa kiyana eka sidu wennema, lokaya thulin dunne siddi ekka
nodanuwathkama kiyana loku hora, e siddi sakshi washayen dunnahama
ewa balala podi horu tika alluwa kiyala 
horakama nawathinne na.
loku eka inna kam aluth podi eun hadenawa.

budu rajanan wahanse pennuwe 
yathartha waadi dharshanayak.

budunta pera,
sil rakka aya sitiya
mahana wechcha aya sitiya
budun yai kiya ganna aya hitiya
dharmaya sewuu kattiya hitiya 
wimukthi kaamain hitiya,

me siyalu dena roopaya eka eka akarayen allaganna, 
allaganna widiha gana gaburu wigrahan kara tibuna.
e roopayen midi aroopa thala walata yana hati pawa kiyala tibuna.

e kisidu karanayak thula saba wimukthiyak tibune na 
kiyala thamai budu rajanan wahanse pennuwe.

me widihata 
roopaya eka eka akarayen allaganna ditti gana 
katha kara inna eken,
budu rajanan wahanse pennapu
yatharatha wadi dharmaye watinakama
kochchara heena lesada aran tiyenne.
wimukthiya nosoyaa,
wimukthiya hamuwanawa kiyala sitha gaththu margayak soya soya
innawa.
"sabba daanam dhamma daanam jinaathi"
wanne, menna me wimukthiya ismathu karala dena daanayatai.
ebadu kalyana mithrayek hamunoth pamanai,
sathdharamya shrawanaya wenne.
thama thula pawathina 
ikshana sampaththiyen prayojanayak ganna puluwan wenne.


e kalaye hitapu wimukthikaamin tibbichcha 
anya woo dharashana nyanaya.
unu wiwida roopayan saha iskandayan 
e iskandayan thora kirimen roopa aroopa thala uppaththi
diwyathala , sansaraye pawathma hodata sak karana krama
hoda naraka, pin paw
aadi dewal
apita aluth.
eka hinda ewa hoyanna pelabenawa.
eka nisa e danuma soya yanawa
e danuma nisa athmawadayata kotu wenawa.
giya athme sitapu mama thamai me ada inne
giya athme karapu pin paw nisa ada mata karmaya balapala kiyana 
wisthraya isthira kara gannawa.
apita me lokaye dewal wadara widiha
modern loken hamu wenne nathi handa 
e gana kagena hari ahana welawata 
ewa soyanna handawa.
thamangema soya yaame ramuwakata, enam iswakeeya raamukata kotu wenawa.

api mechchara kalayak,
dharmaya soya yanawa kiyala karagena gihin tiyenne 
wimukthi kaamin eda hitapu thanata ena eka.
iswakeeya raamukata kotu wela thamai meka hoyala tiyenne.
iswakeeya ramuwa tiyenawa kiyalawath api danne na.

wimukthiya seweema, samawitama e nisa 
kalyana mithraya mathama thamai pawathinne
kalyana mithraya matha 
sath dharmayata yoniso manasi karaya yedeemen
jeewithayama prathipadawak karaganna puluwan.
ethkota thamai etharaweema 
penna hari patan ganne.

thamage raamuta galapena ho nogalapena sobawaya
ramuwa athulemai pawathinne.
ramuwen eliyata yame sobawaya kalyana mithrayek nathuwa 
kara gannama ba.
e nisa wimukthikaami pudgalayek bawata 
path weeme hakiyawa, thama thulin seweemen 
pudgala sobawayen ethara weemak sidu karaganna ba. 
ekata kalyana mithra ashrayak awashamai.

ese kala hakke dedenukata pamanai. ( budu saha pasee budu rajanan wahanselata pamanai), 
maha rahathan wahansela athulu ithuru siyaluma kattiya 
shrawakayan pamanai.
kalyana mithrayek ge asura nathuwa 
ramuwen eliyata enna ba.
enam
sowan marga anga 4 wadenne na.
(kalyana mithra sewanaya, sathdharma sharawanaya, yoniso manasikaraya,
dammanu damma prathipadawa)

sil aragaththata,
dana,seela, bawana kalata,
mal pahan puja kalata 
wandana mana, sath gayana kalata 
dharama karunu ek ras kalata
epamanakin witharak
nirodaya sakshath karaganna ba.
nirodaye hethu saha prathyan sakas weema sidu wiya yuthui.

me siyalla api kara gena tiyenne,
eda hitapu wimukthikaamingen awaaboda mattamata 
pamineema sanda pamanai.

nirodaya dakkinna nam,  thamage ramuwen
eliyata paminiya yuthui.
ese paminiya haki wabath
eya karana margaya prathipadawa lesath.
awabodaya thula nirodaya pawathina bawath
kalyana mithrayan ge asurakin shakshath kara ganna puluwan.

buddadi pramuka kalyana mithrayan wahanselage 
wachana desata naburu wenna oni.

ex:
robots la dennek innawa, kannadi nathuwa penne na
e denna kannadi dekak maru kaloth, 
penne thamange drushtiyata , ehema naththam kannadiye pata anuwa 
kiyana eka awaboda wenawa.
nil paata kannadiyak dagathtoth loke penne nil pata drushtiyakin
habai.
kannadiya galawala,
kannadiya gana katha karoth.
eka kannadiya gana kathwak pamanai.
kannadiya da gaththahama nilpatin penawa kiyalawath
galawapuhama , wena widihata penawa kiyala kiyanawa wath nevei.

ewage,  
eliye tiyena de ahen balanawa wath
hithe tiyena de eliyen penawa wath 
kiyana depaththa hamu wanne,
peneema pawathinawa pamanai.
api kannadiya gana witharak nam katha karanne
ethana tiyenne kathawak pamanai. 
peneema pawathina nisa depaththak pawathinawa.
peneema pawathinawa kiyala haduna gaththe,
penunu deyak tiyenawa kiyana hageema thula neda
pawathunu deyak penuna kiyana , anawabodaya nisa neda
peneema saha penuna de thahawuru wela tiyenne.
ehenam
peneema saha penuna de aniwabodaya/awidyawa thulama sakas wechcha deyak neda.

ehenam 
eliye tiyena de ahen balanawa wath
hithe tiyena de eliyen penawa wath
kiyana depaththen ma 
peneema saha awidyaawa athara tiyena sambandaya haduna ganna ba.
ehenam 
e dekatama podu nowana,
mada sobawaya enam
madyama widihata
peneema pawathina nisa me pathi deka pawathina bawath
peneema samawitama anawabodaya nisa ismathu wena bawath
daka ganna puluwan.
enam
prathipadawa madyama woo wita 
awidyaawa namathi wathura thula peneema kiyana pihinum karu ge pawathma 
pawathina bawa 
awaboda wiya yuthui.
 

 

 








 





    
  
 

------------------- Next session------------------------------
----thanhawen upan anyanamanya prathya--------------



nikkanthi thanahawa gana thamai katha karanna oni.

apita lokaye tiyena dekata tiyena kamaththa 
thanhawa kiyala therenawa.
e unata 
lokaya hadenne thanhawen kiyana eka 
jeewithyen balanna therenne na. e gana echchara therumak na
e nisa 
bahira roopayen thanhawa iwath karanna try karanawa.
mata oyawa penawa, lassana dewal pariharanaya karanna puluwan.
e hinda ewa ehema une ai kiyala 
hoyanna uwamanawak enne na .
sithuwillak wath enne na.

habai roopayak uwamana nisai , siyalu prashna athi une.
roopaya hamuwanna tiyena hakiyawa thula idan thamai me siyalu sellam damme.
 
ahen roopayak balanawa = iskanda sobawayan = wipaka sithe dharmatha tikak
dakkata passe , 
wena aramunakata yana wita , e kiwwa dewal athi bawata manasa paththe 
nimiththak athiwenawa.
e kiyanne dakapu dewal tiyenawa kiyala danenawa.
eeta passe penunu, ahapu, dakapu paththata,
sitha thahawuru wela, tiyena de balannath yanna puluwan.
(lankawe tiyena ge gana hithuwoth , e dakapu de tiyenawa kiyala hagenawa)
wipaka naama roopa dakinna pera, (naama roopa sambandaya chakku wynanayen daka ganna issella)
manase gathiya kiyana karama wynaanaya pahala wela.
(atheetha bawanga -> bawanga chalana -> bawanga upachcheda -> pancha idwara wajjana sitha -> chakku wynaanaya enne)
methana karama wynaanaye pahala weema chakku wynaanayata pera sidu unu deyak.

ex:
oya gedaraka plan ekak adinna hithapuwahama, hithanne nathuwa adinna puluwan da ? ba
sitheema mulikai,
1) palamu piyawara lesa sitha mulikawa naama,roopa hata gannawa, naama-roopa athi kalhi mano-wynaanaya anyamanya prathya lesa hata gannawa. (karma wynanaya)(me karya sidda karanna awashaya wana prathya shakthiya). me set ekama wipaka mattame tiyenne
apita penne nathi starting point eke siddiyak ganai me katha kale.

2) menna me wipaka pancha upadana iskandaya,
anyamanya lesa karama bawa upadanayata sambanda wenawa.
e nisa yamak tiyenawamai kiyala hithenne me point ekedi.
(lankawe geya tiyenawamai kiyala hithenne me nisai)
enam upadana iskandaya pawathina kan, upadanaya pawathinawa.
enam e deka anyamanyai.

e nisa iskanda tikak ( penena bawa) <-> manasa paththe (thanha,upadana , keles)
enam thanhawa thamai naama,roopa deka ekata badala yaa karana katayuththa karanne.
thanahawa tiyena kam lokaye duka pawathinawa.
mese sithe awarjanaya kirima sithema sobawayak.
ese sihi karana aramuna , thanha upadanaya yedunata passe 
keles tika duru nowuna nam 
chethana bawooo wenawa.
   
karmayak karanna sithak pahala wenna oni neda.
karmaya sidu karana wynanaya pahala une koheda ?
eka pahala une manase. e 

thunkalayaka pawathmak tiyena bawa hamuwanne kohomada balamu.
